PART I: Teachings from bSod nams dbang po (1559-1621); vol. ka, text no. 6, pp. 555-618/ /dharmA sya swA mi shrI mansadgu re bhyassadharmA ya thA shU ta sya na yassu bha gi
ta gambhi ra puShTiM dharmA ssarba kA sha sya surYa nA ma bi ha ra tisma// /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par
bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed las rje btsun grub pa'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba dpal sa skya pa chen po 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga nas kyis rjes
su bzung ba'i sarga ces bya ba bzhugs so/ /

rgya gar skad du/ dharmA sya swA mi shrI mansadgu re bhyassadharmA ya thA shU ta sya na yassu bha gi ta gambhi ra puShTiM dharmA ssarba kA sha sya surYa nA maH bod skad du/
chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba/ rje btsun bla ma
bka' drin can rnams kyi zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su mchi'o/ /tshe rabs thams cad du rjes su gzung du gsol/ sngon tshe grangs med bskal pa'i dus nas yan
lag bdun ldan sku brnyes kyang / /gdul bya drang phyir 'phags pa'i yul du mdzad pa bcu gnyis ston mdzad pa'i/ /lha mi'i mgon po zas gtsang sras dang des gsungs lung rtogs
dam pa'i chos/ /rgyal sras bstan 'dzin dge 'dun tshogs la byang chub bar du skyabs su mchi/ 1 /rgyal bas gsungs

pa'i mdo dang sngags kyi bka'/ /mkha' mnyam gdul bya'i don du bsdud mdzad pa'i/ /gsang ba'i bdag dang dgra bcom byang sems tshogs/ /rim par byon pa rnams la bdag cag dad/ 2
/rgyu dang 'bras bu'i theg pa'i gsung rab kyi/ /dgongs pa rang dbang 'grel ba'i skyes chen mchog /'phags yul mdzes par byed pa'i 'gro ba'i gnyen/ /paN grub dbang po de dag
phyag gi gnas/ 3 /bod yul mtha' 'khob mun pa'i gling chen por/ /dam chos nyi mas kun tu gsal mdzad pa'i/ /'jig rten mig gyur sgra bsgyur lo paN rnams/ /bka' drin dran
pas yang yang phyag bgyi 'o/ 4 /gangs can ljongs 'dir mdo sngags phyogs re ba'i/ /bstan 'dzin mang yang yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag /'jam pa'i dbyangs dang mthu stobs mgon
po yis/ /mngon sum rjes

bzung sa skya'i bla chen rgyal/ 5 /de sras thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rtse/ /bod yul rdor 'dzin gtsug rgyan grags pa'i mtshan/ /thub dbang gnyis pa sa skya paN chen dang
/ /dpal ldan 'phags pa'i yon tan bsam bzhin 'dud/ 6 /de lta'i skyes chen rnams kyi bstan pa'i rgyun/ /snyigs ma'i dus 'dir ches cher gsal ba la/ /gzhan dang mtshungs pa
med pa'i mdzad pa can/ /sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gtsug na mdzes/ 7 /gang sku nyi ma 'bum gyi gzi 'bar zhing / /de gsung lugs gnyis 'dod pa 'jo ba can/ /khyod thugs
byis pa'i blo yis dpag dka' ba'i/ /grub mchog dbang po'i mtshan gyis bdag skyongs shig 8 /snyigs dus dmu rgod 'dul dka'i sems can rnams/ /'jam des zhi ba chen po'i 'phrin
las kyis/ /'dul mkhas ji mdzad bstan 'gro'i don gyur pa'i/ /yab

rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas gang des srungs/ 9 /dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi spyi gzugs mchog /mchog dang thun mong dngos grub stsol ba'i lha/ /lha mchog dkyil 'khor gtso bo rigs
brgya'i bdag /bdag gi skyabs gcig rje btsun mus par 'dud/ 10 /gzhan yang rgyal ba'i bstan pa gces 'dzin pa'i/ /'gro kun dga' mdzad don gnyis lhun grub dang / /sbyin sogs
phar phyin spyod pa mthar son pa'i/ /snyan pa'i grags pa gsal de bsngags par 'os/ 11 /zab yangs man ngag kun la dbang phyug pa'i/ /rim gnyis ting 'dzin zab mor rab brtan
dang / /ngag dbang lha dang dbyer med thams cad mkhyen/ /chos kyi grags pa srid na gsal de bsngags/ 12 /de sogs rtsa rgyud bla ma'i bka' drin las/ /dam chos thos tshul
legs par bshad pa'i gtam/ /zab rgyas

chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed 'di/ /'chad par 'gyur gyi don gnyer dga' bas nyon/ 13 /'dir skal ba dang ldan pa'i skyes bu rnams shin tu rnyed par dka' ba'i dal 'byor gyi mi
lus rin po che lan cig tsam thob pa'i dus 'dir/ rang dang pha ma rigs drug gis bsdus pa'i sems can thams cad rnam par grol ba rin po che'i gling du phyin par byed pa'i thabs
la dus 'khor mo yug tu 'bad par bya dgos pa yin te/ ji skad du/ mi yi gru la brten nas ni/ /sdug bsngal chu bo che las sgrol/ /gru 'di shin tu rnyed dka' bas/ /rmongs
pa dus su gnyid ma log /ces gsungs pas so/ /ji ltar 'bad par bya ba'i tshul yang / chos mngon pa las/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ /bsgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /zhes
gsungs pa ltar thog ma nyid du legs pa'i yon tan thams cad kyi gzhir gyur pa lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rin po che la gnas dgos pa yin pa las/ tshul khrims de
yang / rgyud rdo rje rtse mo las/ so sor thar dang byang chub sems/ /rig 'dzin rang gi ngo bo 'o/ /zhes dang / bde mchog gi gzhung las/ gong nas gong ma'i sdom pa ni/ /bu
khyod kyis ni gzung bya ste/ /grol ba'i rgyu ni de las gzhan/ /thabs ni cung zad yod ma yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gzhi sdom pa gsum thob la ma nyams par byas nas/ de'i
'og tu brgyud pa dri ma med pa las 'ongs pa'i gsung rab rnam par dag pa'i tshig don rnams/ thos pa dang bsam pa dang bsgom pa'i tshul la brtson 'grus dang nan tan snying
por bgyid pa'i sgo nas dal 'byor gyi rten lan cig tsam

thob pa 'di don yod par bya dgos pa las/ bdag cag gis yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi zhabs kyi padmo la gtugs te dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi ji ltar thos pa'i tshul mdo tsam
zhig brjod na/ gang gi zhal gyi dkyil 'khor mthong tsam gyis/ /'gro kun dbang du bsdu ba'i mthu stobs can/ /padma 'byung gnas dus mthar dge slong tshul/ /grub mchog bsod
nams dbang por snying nas 'dud/ /ces pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa bdag cag gi 'dren mchog /sa gsum gyi bla ma dpal sa skya pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs byams pa dpal ngag
dbang bsod nams dbang po grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ba'i drung du/ rang lo bcu bzhir slebs pa 'phags pa'i yul na thun mong zhes grags pa lcags pho khyi'i lo dbo
zla ba'i yar ngo'i gral tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin dpal sa skya'i dbu rtse rnying mar bstan pa'i rtsa ba so sor thar pa dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i dbang po/ shI ri pu tra/rgyal po'i khab shing thag can du 'khrungs pa/ sras sgra gcan 'dzin/grong
khyer ser skyar/ bram ze sgra gcan 'dzin/rA Dar 'khrungs pa'i sa ra ha yin/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/lho phyogs bai ta'i yul/ gu Na mi Ta/'dis dbu ma rtsa shes la 'grel
pa mdzad/ rin chen bshes gnyen/lam 'bras kyi lo rgyus su dharmA mi trar bshad/ dpal ldan chos skyong /zla ba'i grong du 'khrungs pa'i bi ru pa yin/ gu Na pa ri/ chos kyi
phreng ba/ 'byung gnas sbas pa/dran pa nyer bzhag phyis 'gyur gyi paNTi ta/ paNDi ta chen po shAkya shrI/kha che khri brtan gyi grong khyer sra lwa rang

rar 'khrungs pa/ sa skya paNDi ta chen po/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ chos rje mnyam med pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs dpal/ chos rje dge bzang pa/ chos rje A nanda pa/ grub
chen chos kyi rin chen/ sems dpa' chen po brtson 'grus rgya mtsho/ chos rje chos rgyal dpal 'byor/ mkhan chen nam mkha' dbang phyug dpal sa skya pa chen po 'jam mgon grub
pa'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/dus phyis dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i khur
'di mi bya ba mthu med byung ba nas/ dge tshul dang tshangs spyod dge bsnyen gyi bslab pa 'bul tshogs bgyis te yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ming btags tsam
du gnas pa lags/ /yang na kha che paN chen gyi rjes su/ mkhan chen rdo rje dpal/ mkhan chen 'od zer dpal/ mkhan chen bsod nams dpal/ mkhan chen bkras tshul/ shar pa ye
rgyal/ ngor chen kun bzang / byams chen rab 'byams pa/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang / spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/
/yang rje de nyid kyi drung du/ dbu sems kyi lugs las khyad par du 'phags pa'i rgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi cho ga'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa thob nas/ de'i yig cha rje dkon
mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang nos so/ /dbang gi skor la/ thog mar grub chen dzAe ta ri'i lugs kyi mgon po tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba
thob pa'i rgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ dze ta ri dgra las rnam

rgyal/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ bla chen bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis 'od zer/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ye/ grags pa dpal/ sru lung
pa kun smon/ brag phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun dga' bzang po/ chos rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ yongs
'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang
po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang na ngor chen mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin man sngar bzhin no/ ! /yang ma gcig grub
pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dpag med kyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba thob pa'i rgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti pu pa/ ras chung
ba/ mi la ras pa/ dwags po lha rje/ tha tsa ba/ 'bri gung pa/ spyan snga ba/ yang dgon pa/ spyan snga rin chen ldan/ rje zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal/ chos
rje bde legs rin chen/ kun dga' dpal bzang / dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang po/ drin chen dpal ldan mgon po/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen

pa/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang bla med rdo rje theg pa'i smin byed kyi thog ma rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos lhad
med dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bka' rnam par dag pa smin rgyas su thob pa'i rgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje
sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab yon tan/ 'khon rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong
/ 'khon ston bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ kha 'ub pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ dga' ldan pa kun
bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun rgyal/ theg chen kun bkras/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rgya dkar shes rab
rgyal mtshan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang na chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi rjes
su/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo chen po man gong
dang

'dra/ yang na rje btsun pa/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa rin rgyal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man
gong dang 'dra/ yang na rje sa paN/ glo bo lo tsA ba/ 'phags pa/ mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal man 'dra'o/ /phur pa rtsa dum gyi rgyud chos rje sa
skya paNDi ta'i 'gyur/ dkyil mchog las rim slob dpon padmas mdzad pa de nyid dang mnyam dznyA na ku mA ras bsgyur ba/ sgrub thabs bklags pas don grub/ sa chen gyis mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs/ phur pa'i sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma rje btsun pas mdzad par grags pa rnams thos/ ! /dpal kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du
dbang bskur ba thob pa'i ring rgyud ni/ spyi dang 'dra la/ sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud bar la ma chad pa'i nye rgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ bla ma sa skya
pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ bla chen kun rgyal/ theg chen
rin po che/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang
po/ /des bdag la'o/ ! /nang zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni gsung ngag dang 'dra bas 'og nas 'byung ba ltar yin la/ ! /rje
btsun rdo rje bdag med ma

lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ Da ma ru pa/ a wa dhu ti pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog
mi shAkya ye shes/ bla ma se mkhar chung ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ bla ma ne tshe sbal ston/ slob dpon bye ba lung pa/ bla ma shes rab grags/ gnam
ba 'phar chos shes/ mngon pa dbu dkar ba/ dbang phyug brtson 'grus/ de la 'phags pa rin chen dang / paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ de gnyis ka la zhang dkon mchog dpal/ de la
chos rje brag phug pa/ de la bla ma dam pa dang / ri khrod pa gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de la chos rje shar pa dang / grub chen buddha
ba gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma rdo rje 'chang / de la sems dpa' chen po/ de gnyis ka la rje btsun dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug pa dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng
ge de gnyis char la 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo chen po/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang
na 'dren mchog rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chen po man 'dra'o/ /yang na mngon pa ba/ 'phags pa/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ dkar po brag pa/ bla ma dpal ldan
pa man chad gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang chos rje de nyid kyi drung du/ mdo rgyud thams cad kyi bcud phyung ba gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag yongs
su rdzogs pa legs par thob pa'i chos kyi

rnam grangs la/ thog mar sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid dang rjes su 'brel bar brgyud pa'i rnam thar rnams thos pa la/ rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i bla ma rgya bod kyi lo
rgyus/ bod kyi lo rgyus rgyas pa dmar gyis mdzad pa/ sa chen gyi rnam thar rje btsun gyis mdzad pa/ rje rtse mo'i rnam thar tshangs spyod ma dang / khyod nyid ma mchan ma
rje pas mdzad pa/ rje btsun gyi rnam thar mnal lam ma sbal ston gyis mdzad pa dang / chos rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa gnyis/ rje sa paN gyi rnam thar 'phags pas mdzad pa dang
/ lho pa rin chen dpal gyis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa'i rnam thar shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa dang / byang gzhon bo dhi ku ma ras mdzad pa/ tshogs bsgom pa'i
rnam thar dang nyan chen pa'i rnam thar bar ston gyis mdzad pa'i lo rgyus las btus pa/ nyan chen pa'i rnam thar dkar po brag pas mdzad pa/ zhang pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan
pas mdzad pa/ brag phug pa'i rnam thar ri khrod pas mdzad pa/ bla ma dam pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas mdzad pa dang / karma byams chos pas mdzad pa kha skong dang bcas
pa/ ri khrod pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ dkar po brag pa'i rnam thar rang nyid kyis mdzad pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa'i rnam thar sems dpa' chen pos mdzad
pa/ grub chen buddha shrI'i rnam thar ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ shar chen ye rgyal gyi rnam thar rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar
kha skong dang bcas pa mus chen gyis mdzad pa/ mus chen gyi rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa rtsa

'grel kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen gyi rnam thar rje sangs rin gyis mdzad pa/ rje dkon mchog 'phel gyi rnam thar mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen dang / rje dkon mchog
lhun grub kyis mdzad pa gnyis/ rje sangs rin gyi rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa sa los mdzad pa/ sa lo chen po'i rnam thar ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/
rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi rnam thar dkon mchog dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar rgyas pa ljags steng nas gnang zhing / bla ma bsten
pa'i thabs shlau ka lnga bcu pa rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i dka' 'grel dang bcas pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i snang gsum mdzes rgyan gyi lung rnams dang
/ brgyud pa gnyis las 'ongs pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga rnams legs par thos/ lam gyi dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi sgo nas dkri ba la/ thog mar yab kyi
rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba rtsa sngags AShTa'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ lus dkyil gyi
khrid kyi sngon 'gror thabs rgyud kyi gtso bo lam dus kyi dbang bskur ba gsang sngags yi ge brgya pa'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ gsang dbang gi lam gyi sngon 'gror rje btsun
rdo rje bdag med ma'i sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor dang / bla ma'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams par bskur ba lam dus kyi dbang dang bcas pa/ lam
zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi khrid dang byin rlabs/ phyi'i bar chad srung thabs rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug

gi srung ba thun mong ba'i byin rlabs rnams legs par thob nas/ de rnams kyi rgyab rten tshad ma bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i yig sna rnams kyi lung thob pa la/ thog mar bstan
bcos rdo rje'i tshig rkang / de'i rnam 'grel rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa bcu gcig nang nas tshig nyung la don rgyas pa gnyag ma yig chung dang bcas pa la deng sang
lam 'bras glegs bam zhes mtshan du grags pa 'di'i nang na bzhugs pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi rnam 'grel gnyag ma dang / /gsal byed kun gzhi rgyu
rgyud gdan sogs dang / /lus dkyil 'chi bslu bum dbang 'da' ka ma/ /thig le'i rnal 'byor phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid dang / /bzhi pa'i 'da' ka bar do'i gdams ngag dang /
/lam dbang tshad ma bzhi dang gdams ngag drug /rten 'brel lnga dang grib sel yig chung gnyis/ /thig le srung ba yig brgya'i 'don thabs dang / /rlung sbyor bha ga'i yi ge
'khor bzhi'i rgya/ /dbang phyug don brgyad sa phyed mngon rtogs dang / /don bsdus ma ste nyi shu rtsa bzhi ni/ /bstan bcos nyid kyi steng du bshad bya 'o/ /de dag las 'phros
gud du gsungs pa'i chos/ /'khor 'das dbyer med dbang bzhi'i man ngag gnad/ /mchog dbang bskur tshul bskyed rim bsdus pa dang / /ril bu'i sgrub thabs yum gyi byin rlabs
dang / /gegs sel bzhi dang dbang chu sgrub thabs gsum/ /rtsa ltung 'khrul spong tshogs 'khor sbyin sreg ste/ /rtsa ba las 'phros chos sna bcu bdun pa las/ /phyi ma bdun
po logs su bzhugs kyang rung / /'bring bsdus lam

gnyis gzhung shing chen po bzhi/ /rtogs bskyed chos lnga lam zab bla ma rnams/ /nyams myong tshad ma'i chos sna nyer dgu yin/ /lung gi tshad ma lung sbyor rnam pa bzhi/ /bla
ma tshad ma rgya bod rnam thar gnyis/ /man ngag phra mor bcas pa drug bcu 'o/ /zhes pa ltar glegs bam dkar chag tu thebs pa'i chos sna drug cu las/ glegs bam 'dir cis kyang
bzhugs dgos pa'i chos sna zhe dgu las/ dang po pa dang / thun mong du logs su bzhugs kyang rung ba'i chos sna bdun dang bcas pa legs par thos/ man ngag phra mo'i rkang
grangs logs su bsgrigs pa mtshan po ti dmar btus su grags pa thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ thog mar bla ma tshad ma'i skabs su/ bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rje pas mdzad
pa/ de'i kha skong shar pas mdzad pa/ sa bir mjal ba'i lo rgyus rje pas sga thang la gnang ba/ nyams myong tshad ma'i skabs su gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba'i khrid yig

pa/ bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub thabs 'phags pas mdzad pa/ dbang gi rab dbye rje pa'i gsung las zhang btsun gyis bris pa/ rje pas sga ston la springs pa/ phyi nang gsang

med ma'i byin rlabs rje pas mdzad pa/ gtum

mo 'khor lo bzhi pa/ gtum mo'i dmigs pa nyer dgu/ gegs sel gsang bdun ma/ bar chad gsum sel/ bka' rgya ma/ nyams che chung / gleng gzhi ma/ rlung reng lnga bcos pa sogs 'byung
ba lus 'khrugs sogs sel ba/ gegs sel gyi yi ge bzhi'i gsal byed rnams sa paN gyi gsung 'gros yi ge rnying pa/ 'phrin las so gnyis kyi sdom tshig dang de'i zhal shes buddha

su gnad du che ba drug gi yig rnying / rten 'brel lnga sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ lam bsdus pa dmar gyis mdzad pa/ phyag chen gyi dbye ba sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ tshogs sbyor

pa/ gsal byed buddha shris mdzad pa/ bir srung gi

ga mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i man ngag shes rab 'khor lo'i dngos grub mchog gi sgrub thabs/ chos kyi dung gi ting nge 'dzin 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ 'phags pa mtshan
yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ yi ge gcig pa'i rab tu sbyor ba'i sgrub thabs/ gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs cho ga dang bcas pa 'od
zer 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ yang gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs sangs rgyas kyis gsungs
pa/ sgrol ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs/ mchog sbyin sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ dbang byed sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje'i myu gus mdzad pa/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs
tshul mi 'dra ba gsum las/ gcig slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ yang rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta slob dpon chos 'byung zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol ma dug
sel ma'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma nor sbyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'od dpag med kyi snying po'i rgyud las 'phags ma sgrol ma'i rtogs pa gsungs pa/ ngan song las sgrol ba'i sgrol
ma'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'chi ba bslu ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ sna tshogs yum gyi sgrub thabs/ don thams cad rab tu sbyin pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub
thabs/ de'i gzungs/ yang dug sel ba'i sgrub thabs/ de'i rigs sngags sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa/ 'phags ma dug sel ma'i rtogs pa dzaM gu ma'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje sgrol
ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta'i

rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ de'i man ngag yang sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta chen po gnas brtan dpe med kyis mdzad pa/ 'jigs pa brgyad las skyob pa'i sgrub thabs/
rgya nag rim pa'i 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgya nag chen po'i rim pa'i 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon brtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad/ yang 'chi ba bslu
ba'i sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug gi slob ma thu bos mdzad pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal pos mdzad
pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs/ ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs che chung mi 'dra ba lnga las gcig slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ tsunda'i sgrub thabs
mi 'dra ba gsum/ rtogs pa las phyung ba'i 'od zer can phyag bcu ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang rtogs pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od
zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ rtogs pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'od zer can ser mo phyag brgyad ma'i
sgrub thabs/ au Di ya na'i 'od zer can phyag bcu gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs/ au Di ya na'i 'od zer can dmar mo phyag bcu gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i
rol pas mdzad pa/ 'od zer can dmar mo phyag bcu ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i jag 'chings/ rtog pa las gsungs pa'i
'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon snying po'i zhabs kyis mdzad

pa/ 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ 'od zer can pi tsu ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ de'i gzungs bklags pa'i man ngag ri khrod lo ma can
gyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ sher phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ ri khrod lo ma can gyi gzungs/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma sku mdog ser mo'i sgrub thabs rgyas
bsdus gnyis/ sher phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dge 'dun sbyin gyi bus mdzad pa/ yang shes phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta padma 'phel gyis mdzad pa/ gser mdog
can gyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ shes phyin gyi sgrub thabs/ yang gser mdog can gyi shes phyin gyi sgrub thabs/ shes phyin gyi sgrub thabs 'phags pa thogs med
kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags ma rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ dbyangs can ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs
gnyis/ rdo rje pi waM ma dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs gshin rje nag po las gsungs pa/ yang rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub
thabs/ 'phags ma khro gnyer can gyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ sgrol ma'i rtog pa las phyung ba ku ru ku lle'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma'i rtogs pa las byung ba rig byed ma'i
sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ de'i dbang du byas pa'i man ngag yang rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ u rgyan nas byung ba'i rig byed ma'i
sgrub thabs/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa rol pa'i

mdzad pa'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ kyai rdo rje'i rim pas rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ kyai rdo rje'i rgyud nas phyung ba'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ rig byed ma phyag drug
ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ rig byed ma phyag brgyad ma'i sgrub thabs intra bhu tis mdzad pa/ yang rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i man ngag gi rim pa/ rig byed
ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ ku ru ku lle'i las rab tu bskyangs pa'i sbyor ba/ rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ gdugs dkar
can gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje tsa rtsi ka'i sgrub thabs/ so sor 'brang ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gsum/ stong chen mo/ gsang sngags rjes 'dzin/ rma bya chen mo/ bsil
ba'i tshal zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo lnga'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa/ phyir bzlog ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan gyi sgrub thabs/ gzhan gyis
mi thub pa'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje ghanda ri'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ srung ba lnga'i cho ga rdo rje lcags sgrog gi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ paNTi ta chos kyi 'byung gnas
blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan gyi sgrub thabs/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ lha mo nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gsum/ de'i
gzungs kyi man ngag phag mo shes rab gsal byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ byams pa'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ paNDi ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa'i mdzad pa'i dzambha
la nag po'i sgrub thabs/ dzambha la ser po'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gsum/ ser po phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs

tsantra go mis mdzad pa/ ser po lha pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rgyas bsdus gnyis/ de la chu rgyun du 'bul ba'i man ngag gi rigs mi 'dra ba gsum/ slob dpon tsantra
go mis mdzad pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ rtog pa bdun pa las gsungs pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ paNDi ta shardha ka ras mdzad pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ 'jig
rten gsum las rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje me dang nyi ma 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs/ rta mchog gi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje gshed dmar gyi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje nag po'i
sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ yang dgra nag gi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje mthar byed kyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ bgegs mthar byed kyi sgrub thabs/ stobs po che'i sgrub
thabs slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ yang stobs po che'i sgrub thabs/ hU~M mdzad kyi sgrub thabs/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs/ kyai rdo rje'i phyag gnyis pa'i
sgrub thabs tA ra shrIs mdzad pa/ bdag med pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs/ de'i cho ga dam pa thams cad 'dren pa'i 'jig rten gsum
gyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ yang nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs te lha 'di rnams kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ a bhya ka ra/ shu bhaM ka
ra gupta/ pu dza ti/ ratna rakShi ta/ go taM shrI/ kirti paNDi ta/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rgyal mtshan rin chen/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ ka bcu pa gzhon nu seng
ge bla ma mgon po 'bum/ bla ma dpal ldan

tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rgyal
ba lha mchog seng ge thar rtse ba sangs rgyas seng ge mkhan chen chos 'od zer/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ mus chen/ 'dren mchog man
gong dang 'dra/ yang na ngor chen/ 'jam dbyangs shes rgyam pa/ 'dren mchog man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen/ dpal rdor ba/ 'dren mchog man gong dang 'dra ba'o/ ! /sgrub thabs
brgya rtsar grags pa sgrub thabs dgu bcu go drug paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'i rjes gnang thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ dang po thub pa rdo rje
gdan gtso 'khor gsum/ gnyis pa brtan pa'i 'khor lo bha wa kantas mdzad pa/ gsum pa yang brtan pa'i 'khor lo/ bzhi pa tshig lhug pa'i brtan pa'i 'khor lo/ lnga ba tshig
lhug pa'i a ra pa tsa na dkar po padmas mdzad pa/ drug pa a ra pa tsa na dkar po lha lnga mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ bdun pa 'phags pa 'jam dpal zhal gsum phyag drug
pa/ brgyad pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje gtso 'khor lnga/ dgu pa ngag gi rgyal po gtso 'khor gnyis/ bcu pa rgyal po rol pa/ bcu gcig pa rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod nas gsungs pa'i
'jam dpal/ bcu gnyis pa rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod nas bsdus pa'i 'jam dpal/ bcu gsum pa yang 'jam dpal/ bcu bzhi pa yan lag med pa'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ bco lnga pa 'jam
dbyangs chos dbyings

gsung dbang / bcu drug pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'jam dpal/ bcu bdun pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa/ bco brgyad pa 'jam dpal shes rab 'khor lo/ bcu dgu pa 'phral
du nyams su myong ba'i a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ nyi shu pa gshin rje nag po zhal drug pa/ nyer gcig pa gshin rje nag po zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ nyer gnyis pa gshin rje
pu dza na bha dras mdzad pa/ nyer gsum pa rdo rje chos/ nyer bzhi pa seng ge sgra/ nyer lnga pa ha la ha la lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ nyer drug pa kharsa pa Ni lha
lnga rnyog pa med pas mdzad pa/ nyer bdun pa yi ge drug pa gtso 'khor gsum pa lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ nyer brgyad pa ha ri ha ri la bzhon pa/ nyer dgu pa ha la ha la
lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ sum cu pa padma gar dbang sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ so gcig pa sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i spyan ras gzigs dgra las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ so gnyis
pa sgrol ma rdo rje myu gus mdzad pa/ so gsum pa sgrol ma dkar mo gtso 'khor gsum pa yid bzhin nor bu rgyal pos mdzad pa/ so bzhi pa seng ldeng nags sgrol gtso 'khor
gsum pa sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ so lnga pa sgrol ma dkar mo ngag dbang grags pa'i sras kyi thu bos mdzad pa/ so drug pa o rgyan gyi 'od zer can/ so bdun pa rtog pa las
gsungs pa'i 'od zer can/ so brgyad pa rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can dkar mo/ so dgu pa mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od zer can/ bzhi bcu pa o rgyan gyi 'od zer can
lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ zhe gcig pa yang o

rgyan gyi 'od zer can/ zhe gnyis pa tsundha/ zhe gsum pa gnod gnas ser po tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ zhe bzhi pa dzambha la nag po dag pa byin gyis mdzad pa/ zhe lnga pa nor
rgyun ma/ zhe drug pa khro gnyer can/ zhe bdun pa byams pa/ zhe brgyad pa shes phyin dkar mo sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ zhe dgu pa shes phyin dkar mo dge bsnyen gyi bus mdzad
pa/ lnga bcu pa shes phyin dkar mo/ nga gcig pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ nga gnyis pa mdor bsdus pa'i shes phyin/ nga gsum pa mi g.yo ba sngon po pra bha ka
ra karti dang gzhon nu sbas pas mdzad pa/ nga bzhi pa gtum po chen po/ nga lnga pa rdo rje hU~M mdzad/ nga drug pa ri khrod lo ma can ma/ nga bdun pa dbyangs can ma dmar
mo/ nga brgyad pa bgegs dgra nga dgu pa ral gcig ma/ drug cu pa dug sel ma/ re gcig pa rig byed ma/ re gnyis pa rtog pa las gsungs pa'i rig byed ma/ re gsum pa o rgyan gyi
rig byed ma/ re bzhi pa o rgyan nas 'byung ba'i rig byed ma/ re lnga pa khams gsum dbang du byed pa'i spyan ras gzigs sa ra has mdzad pa/ re drug pa gnod gnas dang nor

rje gshed dmar po yab yum/ bdun cu pa so sor 'brang ma/ don gcig pa gtsug tor rnam rgyal/ don gnyis pa rma bya chen mo/ don gsum pa stong chen rab 'joms/ don bzhi pa gsang

mdzad pa/ lha mo'i gson cig ma bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ las mkhan gyi bskul/ dam can mon bu ma bdag chen rgya dkar bas mdzad pa/ rdo rje phur pa'i bzlog
pa 'khor lo

rtsibs bcu ma/ ltas ngan brgyad cu'i bzlog pa/ phur bsrung dam can bcu gnyis kyi bskul slob dpon padmas mdzad pa rnams thos/ gsung rab de rnams kyi lung grub mchog dbang po'i
zhabs kyis sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po la gsan gsungs/ ! /slob dpon dze ta ri'i thugs kyi yang snying rje btsun sa skya pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i tshe sgrub kyi gdams
pa zab mo sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yan chad snyan brgyud kho nar bzhugs pa sngags 'chang de nyid kyis grub rgya gling pa pad rgyal gyi don du yi ger 'god pa mdzad
pa'i tshe sgrub kyi man ngag zab mo'i bsgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ dze tA rI dgra las rnam rgyal/ slob dpon byang chub
bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ bla chen bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya pa
paNDi ta/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis 'od zer/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ye/ grags pa dpal/ sru lung pa kun smon/ brag
phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun dga' bzang po/ chos rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog
'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/
! /paNDi ta chen po nags kyi rin chen gyis slob dpon

chen po padma 'byung gnas la dngos su gsan pa'i tshe sgrub zab mo'i bsgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas/ mahA paNDi
ta nags kyi rin chen/ lo chen manydzu shrI dznyA na/ mtshan ldan 'od zer seng ge mnyam nyid rin chen rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin kun dga' lung rigs/ grub mchog bsod nams
dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ /tshe sgrub kyi yi ge rje nyid kyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ /paN chen nags rin nas brgyud pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug gi tshe sgrub zab mo'i
bsgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa chen po/ rnal 'byor pa sa ka pa la/ paNDi ta chen po nags kyi rin chen/ lo tsA ba chen po manydzu
shrI/ mkhas btsun 'od zer seng ge mnyam med rin chen rgya mtsho/ grub chen kun dga' lung rigs/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ /tshe sgrub kyi yi ge rje
nyid kyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ ! /yang bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta gnyis pa sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal
snga nas kyis mdzad pa'i gsung rab rnams thos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar gsan yig thos pa rgya mtsho padma rA ga'i phreng ba/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub
kyi rnam thar blo gsar klu'i dbang po gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi rnam thar dge legs rin chen gter zhes bya ba/ de'i kha skong utpa
la'i chun po/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas

pa byin rlabs kyi chu gter zhes bya ba/ yang bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang mchod pa'i cho ga bsdus pa/ byin rlabs bla ma'i rnal 'byor utpa la dkar po'i cod pan zhes bya ba spyan
ras gzigs la sbyar ba lha cig sangs rgyas skyabs ma la gnang ba/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi lam rim gyis sgo nas bla ma'i gsol 'debs/ rje btsun sa skya pa rnams la bstod pa
thugs rje'i char 'bebs/ rtsa ba'i bla ma yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po rnams
la bstod pa re/ rje rang gi bdag bstod/ rtsa ba'i bla ma gnyis dang / rje nyid rang la gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa nus ldan dbang mo shrI de wa'i don du mdzad
pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen dang / zhwa lu lo chen gnyis kyi bstod pa/ rje rang gi bdag bstod rnams skad gnyis/ lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ spros med brgyud
pa'i gsol 'debs/ sbyor drug brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ de'i gsham na rin chen rgyal mchog zhabs la gsol ba 'debs zer ba'i shlau ka gcig dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i lam zab rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi khrid yig ngo sprod dang bcas pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rnal 'byor pa rol pa'i rdo rjes
mdzad zer ba'i nyis 'bigs/ kun rig brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ mi 'khrugs pa'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rdo rje phur pa'i stod las kyi dbang gi brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ smad las
drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang gi

bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kha skong / yang rdo rje phur pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs bsdus pa/ bde mchog bla brgyud kyi gsol 'debs kha skong / snar thang dpe khang
gi srung ma spe ha ra la 'phrin bcol shlau ka gnyis/ rta mgrin yang gsang bla brgyud kyi gsol 'debs/ gu ru drag dmar/ bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bla ma dam pa la shugs
ring dad pa'i rgyang 'bod thugs rje'i chu skyes zhes bya ba btsan la dbon po shes rab rgyal mtshan la gnang ba/ yon tan rgya mtsho ma'i tshig don gyi dogs dpyod ma rig
mun sel rgya nag rgyal po la phul ba'i zhu yig mnga' ris rdzongs khar mnga' bdag rgyal po la gnang ba/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub la phul ba'i zhu yig nyis 'bigs
gcig dang bzhi/ zhwa lu lo chen la phul ba'i zhu yig e waM chos ldan gyi 'bul bsdud pa dge 'dun dpal bzang la gdams pa/ yig mkhan zla grags la gnang ba'i bka' shog gnyis/
lo dgon pa'i spyan snga la gnang ba'i bka' shog sdeb sbyor med pa gcig dang yod pa gnyis te gsum/ bla ma sgra tshad pa dkon mchog rgya mtsho la gnang ba'i bka' shog
byang pa chos rje rin chen bzang po la gnang ba'i bka' shog gnyis/ thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi mkhan po chos rje blo gros rab yangs la gnang ba'i bka' shog rab 'byams pa kun
tshe la gnang ba'i bka' shog smin drug lo tsA ba la gnang ba'i bka' shog gdong dga' ba kun spangs tshe ring grags pa la gnang ba'i bka' shog lhun grub rtse mkhan po thams
cad mkhyen pa la gnang ba'i bka'

shog 'dol kha rgyal po la gnang ba'i bka' shog rgyal mkhar rtser gnang ba'i bka' shog gnyis/ seng ge rtse pa la gnang ba'i bka' shog dge legs kyi tshigs su bcad pa gcig dang
bzhi/ gzhis dga' rin spungs pa dpon sogs la gnang ba'i bka' shog dgu dang / snar thang pa'i rtsom grogs zhus pa gcig tshong 'dus pa la gnang ba'i bka' shog gnas gsar pa
la gnang ba'i bka' shog gnas pa la gnang ba'i bka' shog gnyis/ rtsed pa nam mkha' la gnang ba'i bka' shog rin chen rtse'i gnyer pa dkyil 'khar seng sding la gnang ba'i dris
lan bka' shog khams kyi 'bul bsdud pa bla ma sgra tshad pa dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ dge slong nam mkha' rtse mo/ rta 'bul ba mdo sngags rab 'byams pa kun dga' dpal 'byor
rnams la gnang ba'i lam yig sde tshan gsum/ yig mkhan zla grags la gnang ba'i gdams pa/ mkhar spe rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal gyi dris lan gnyis/ rab 'byams pa dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan la gnang ba'i gdams pa/ gdong dga' ba kun spangs chos la bskul ba'i gtam/ byas 'gyur pa'i sgrub chen rnams la dge sbyor bskul 'debs/ snar thang stong
dpon dpon blon la gdams pa gnyis/ rigs drug 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyi snang tshul rtsom 'phro gcig rje nyid rang gi thugs dam smon lam tshigs bcad ma/ dbu rtse rnying ma
dang / sgo rum dpe khang gi rten gsum rnams kyi dkar chag tshigs bcad ma gnyis/ tshe lha dang nor lha'i tshigs bcad shlau ka gnyis/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od

'bar ba'i drung du rje nyid kyi snam sbyar phul ba'i kha yig gser khang na bzhugs pa'i yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su rje nyid kyis bzhengs pa'i
bla ma rin 'byung gi snyan dar kha yig rje sangs rgyas rin chen gyi nang rten gling dga' na bzhugs pa'i thub pa'i snyan dar kha yig sgo rum dang nang so'i dgon khang du
gzhis dga' rin spungs nas gtor gsos gnang skabs kyi snyan dar kha yig le tshe dgu rtsed pa nam mkhas chos skyong thun mong du phul ba'i snyan dar kha yig gcig srub na bzhugs
yod/ chos rje dkon mchog tshul khrims pa'i gdung rten rgyal rtse na bzhugs pa'i dngul gyi mchod rten la bsngags pa bkra shis kyi mgrin dbyangs zhes pa gcig dpal dus
kyi 'khor lo la bstod pa/ gur mgon la bstod pa shlau ka gcig dmar po skor gsum la bstod pa shlau ka gcig mnga' ris rgyal po la gnang ba'i bstod pa/ rje nyid kyi bu slob sogs
dad ldan so sos bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa la/ byang pa bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis pa la bstod pa/ gu ge bzhi sde ba nam mkha' brtan pa la bstod pa/ dpal 'khor bde chen
gyi mkhan po dkon mchog tshul khrims la bstod pa/ lo dgon pa'i spyan snga la bstod pa/ blo gros rab gsal la bstod pa shlau ka gcig chos rje mgon po dbang phyug la bstod
pa shlau ka gcig thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi gdan sa bkra shis brtan pa la bstod pa/ chos rje dpal ldan rgyal mtshan la bstod pa/ thub bstan yangs can gyi gdan sa pa grags
pa rgyal mtshan la bstod pa/ skye rtsa mkhan

po rdor 'dzin la bstod pa/ gting skyes pa chos rje kun dga' bkra shis la bstod pa shlau ka gcig chos rje rdo rje seng ge la bstod pa shlau ka gcig nyag re gser mdog pa'i bla
ma la bstod pa/ jo nang mkhan po dpal ldan rin chen la bstod pa/ chos rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la bstod pa shlau ka gcig chos rje kun dga' rgya mtsho la bstod pa shlau
ka gcig yang jo nang mkhan po la bstod pa shlau ka gcig sgrub pa ba sangs rgyas dpal la bstod pa gcig ste tshan pa bco brgyad/ sgrub thabs skor la bla ma rin 'byung gi
sgrub thabs/ bir srung thun mong ma yin pa'i bsgom tshul/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i sgrub thabs nges don zla ba'i 'od zer/ sngags phreng phyag bris ma las zhal
bshus pa/ rnal 'byor ma'i rgyun gyi nyams len/ dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs grol ba'i thig le/ rdo rje bdag med ma'i lus dkyil zur 'debs/ yang dag me gcig gi sgrub
thabs nor bu'i phreng ba/ dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i khro bo'i sgrub thabs/ dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i bsnyen sgrub gsal byed bdud rtsi'i 'od can/ gu ru drag dmar gyi sgrub
thabs/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ srung ma drug cu'i gtor chog gshed dmar dpa' gcig gi sgrub thabs/ spros med rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i
sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang byed tshul/ mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs/ phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed/ seng gdong ma/ spyan ras gzigs rnams kyi sgrub thabs chung ngu
gsum/ rjes gnang gi tho gnyis mchan du yod pa/ tshe dpag med grub

pa'i rgyal mo'i sgrub thabs/ tshe dpag med dze ta ri lha dgu'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi rgya mtsho lha cig sangs rgyas skyabs ma la gnang ba/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi sgrub thabs/
'chi med sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ dpal gur gyi mgon po khro bcu'i srung 'khor khams gsum bdud las rnam rgyal/ mgon po dpa' gcig gi sgrub thabs bdud
'joms rdo rje rnams so/ /nyer mkho la rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg sa skya pa'i dkar gtor cha bzhi gtong tshul gsung rgyun ma/ gtor chen zur 'debs/ rnam rgyal stong mchod
kyi chog sgrig 'chi med dpal ster/ khro bo rme brtsegs kyi bstod pa grib sel kun grol/ bkra shis shlau ka gcig myur rtsis rnam dag skyon med nyer mkho kun gsal/ thub
shing bgod bzhi'i yig chung / 'khor lo bde mchog gi 'chad thabs/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi sa bcad rtsom 'phro/ rdo rje phreng ba'i zin bris/ gnas yul rtsa khams kyi dbye
ba/ zhal gnyis ma'i byin rlabs byed tshul/ dbang bshad mdor bsdus/ smon lam shlau ka gcig mgon po lha lnga'i dbang bshad/ byang pa bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis pa che 'don
mdzad dus gnang ba'i mol gtam dgos pa skabs don/ rtse gdong pa'i sger gyi gdung rabs/ bsngo ba gcig rdo rje 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor gyi dbang gi brgyud pa la
nang mchod 'bul ba'i tshigs bcad/ nag po chen po phyag gnyis pa'i bstod pa phreng 'dzin chos kyi nyin byed kyis mdzad pa la 'gyur gnang ba'i skad gnyis/ rje btsun sgrol ma'i
mtshan

brgya mchan ma/ 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po mchan ma/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi gzungs ring gleng gzhi phan yon dang bcas pa 'di la skad gnyis med/ gtsug tor rnam
rgyal gyi gzungs mchan ma/ rdo rje'i glu mchan ma/ bi ru pa'i sngags anggu ri mchan ma/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi sngags phreng mchan ma/ uShNi Sha mchan ma/ sgra mi snyan gyi
gzungs mchan ma/ tshe dpag med kyi gzugs ring thung gnyis mchan ma/ sgrol ma'i yi ge bcu pa mchan ma/ he ru ka'i yig brgya mchan ma/ bha ya na mchan ma/ kyai rdor gyi
gtor sngags mchan ma/ mgon po'i yi ge bcu gnyis ma dang / bdun ma mchan ma/ mkha' 'gro spyi gtor gyi gtor sngags mchan ma/ bcu gcig zhal gyi gzungs mchan ma/ tshul khrims
rnam dag gi gzungs mchan ma/ rdo rje sgrol ma/ so so 'brangs ma/ stong chen mo/ rma bya chen mo/ gsang sngags rjes 'dzin/ bsil ba'i tshal/ ri khrod ma/ sna tshogs yum rnams
kyi gzungs mchan ma/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa mchan ma/ rdo rje sems dpa'i yi ge brgya pa mchan ma/ ngan song sbyong ba'i gzungs mchan ma/ mi 'khrugs pa'i
gzungs mchan ma/ 'chi 'joms 'khor bcas kyi sngags mchan ma/ gtsug tor dri med/ gsang ba ring bsrel/ byang chub rgyan 'bum/ rten 'brel snying po rnams kyi gzungs mchan ma/
mchod pa'i sprin gyi gzungs mchan ma/ mchod rten bskor ba'i gzungs mchan ma/ yon sbyong ba'i gzung mchan ma/ sman byin gyis brlabs pa'i sngags mchan ma/ 'byung po 'dul byed
kyi sngags mchan

ma/ gshin rje gshed kyi sngags mchan ma/ gnod sbyin pho mo'i sngags mchan ma/ rnam thos sras 'khor bcas kyi sngags mchan ma/ byin dbab pa'i sngags mchan ma/ gzungs gra lnga
rgya dpe las dag par bshus pa/ tshe dpag med kyi mdo rnams la zhus dag dang 'gyur sogs mdzad pa'i skad gnyis ma/ bde mchog dkar po'i khrid yig zur 'debs gsal ba'i sgron
me/ gshed dmar gyi khrid yig gsal byed nges don rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi them skas/ ku ru ku lle'i rdzogs rim utpa la'i lcags kyu/ rdo rje phur pa'i 'cham bshad/ rdo rje
phur pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i gsal byed rin po che'i do shal/ sbyin sreg rdo rje'i me 'od/ gtor zlog dgra bgegs kun 'joms kyi lhan thabs gsal byed gnam lcags rdo rje'i
dbal/ mahA kA la'i gtor chog 'phrin las lhun grub/ mahA kA la'i gtor chog bdud las rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa'i bka' srung rnams kyi gtor chog rgyun gyi nyams len bklags
pas grub pa/ dpal sa skya pa'i yi dam chos skyong rnams la gtor ma 'bul ba'i tho snar thang dpon mo la gnang ba/ rdo rje nag po chen po'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dpal sa
skya pa'i bka' srung rnams kyi bskang gso mnyes byed 'chi med sgra dbyangs/ dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i bskang gso dngos grub rol mtsho/ dpal mgon 'khor
dang bcas pa la bstod pa dgra bgegs srog gcod kyi 'khor lo/ /dpal sa skya pa'i chos skyong rdo rje gur gyi mgon po'i las tshogs gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa'i man ngag
drug cu pa'i

cho ga dgra bgegs gnad gcod kyi spu gri/ chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu gsum gyi bskyed chog dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi gtor chog rdo rje phur pa'i srung ma dkar bdud lcam dral
dang dam can gyi gtor chog dngos grub bsam 'phel rnams thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/
des bdag la'o/ /yang na sa lo chen po/ mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /snyigs dus bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa dpal
sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa'i gsung rab rnams kyi lung thos pa'i tshul ni/ skyes
chen gang gi ngo mtshar rnam thar cha/ /gang la bsams kyang dpyod ldan yid 'phrog pa'i/ /snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang rje/ /ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen rgyal
gyur cig /ces pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i gsung rab dri ma med pa
rnams/ de'i bka' 'bangs kyi brgyud 'dzin gyi grangs mar gtogs pa sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bdag gis 'bad pa cher byas nas lung rgyun zhus shing
phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar bka' 'bum po ti dang po la sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa la bstod pa rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse ma/ rje dkon
mchog lhun grub la bstod pa dkon mchog gdung

'dzin ma/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi bdag bstod shlau ka gcig gur mgon lha brgyad kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ dge sding mgon khang du phul ba'i mda' dar kha yig lam zab
rgyun gyi nyams len/ lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi khrid byin rlabs bya tshul/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i sgrub thabs/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi lung byin rlabs
bya tshul/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i lugs kyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod kyi cho ga'i gsal byed gsar bu'i blo can rtogs par sla ba/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi sngags phreng
phyag bris ma las 'bru len byas pa shin tu dag pa/ slob dpon spyod pa'i rdo rje'i lugs kyi slob ma dbang bskur gyi mtshams sbyor slob dpon las dang po pa la nye bar mkho
ba'i phyag len gyi rim pa gsal ba/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rgyun gyi nyams len/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs rgyas pa ma rig mun sel/ rje btsun rdo rje
rnal 'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor du slob ma rjes su 'dzin pa'i cho ga shin tu gsal ba/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs kyi bshad pa zin bris/
grib ma chung ngu khrus kyis sel ba'i cho ga thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu bsgom tshul bla ma'i rnal 'byor la sbyar ba/ bdud rtsi'i ril bu sgrub
tshul las dang po la mkho ba bdud rtsi'i 'byung ba/ man ngag lugs kyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor/ kyai rdo rje rgyu dus kyi dbang gi rtogs pa bskyed/ lam dus kyi dbang bskur
tshul kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa la mchan gnang ba/ lam dus nyams su len pa'i rim

pa/ rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ bsgrub pa lung sbyin gyi gsal byed snying gi ze 'bru/ gshed dmar dpa' gcig gi sgrub thabs gtor bsngo dang bcas pa/
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i sgrub thabs gzhan phan don yod/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i phyag mtshan gzhan phan rgyas byed/ dpal gsang ba 'dus
pa 'phags lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du slob ma dbang bskur ba'i mtshams sbyor gzhan phan lhun grub/ gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen po thub bstan lha chen
gyi bca' yig bslab pa kun 'dus/ mkhan chen dpal ldan bzang po mdo khams la 'bul bsdud bskul la gnang skabs kyi spyi 'gro/ yang bla ma kun dga' dpal bzang mdo khams la 'bul
bskul la gnang ba'i spyi 'gro/ deb gter rin chen bang mdzod/ dus mdos chen mo'i deb bris rnams bzhugs/ bka' bum po ti gnyis pa la/ 'jam dpal a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub pa
byed tshul/ mol gtam yid bzhin nor bu/ sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po de nyid kyi sras mchog sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po las rim par 'phel
te/ dpal sa skya'i gdung brgyud dri ma med pa rgyun ma chad pa 'byung ba'i rten 'brel du/ dus mchod pa sger gyi gdung rabs bsgrigs par mdzad pa'i yi ge nyung ngu / rab gnas
don gsal gyi gsal byed dngos grub 'byung ba/ dpal yang dag mar me dgu pa'i sgrub thabs rim pa gsal ba/ yang dag me dgu'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rim pa gsal ba/ yang dag
me dgu'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga blo

dman dga' ba skyed byed/ yang dag me dgu'i rdul tshon la brten pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub mchod byed tshul ngag 'don gyi tho/ rdo rje phur pa'i rnga byin dbab kyi brda sprod
mthong ba rang grol/ rdo rje phur pa'i bsnyen sgrub kyi gsal byed bdud rtsi'i nyi 'od can zhes bya ba sa los mdzad pa la sngags 'chang chen pos mchan gnang ba/ rdo rje
phur pa'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho gas rang gzhan smin byed kyi phyag len shin tu gsal ba yid 'ong blo gros kha 'byed/ rdo rje phur pa'i dbang gi
mtshams sbyor blo gsal dga' ba skyed byed/ drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang gi gsal byed rin chen phreng ba/ rdo rje phur pa'i dngos grub char 'bebs kyi 'cham gyi brjed byang
snang ba 'gyur thub/ stong ra chos rje kun dga' legs grub pa'i dris lan/ dam can bstan ma bcu gnyis kyi sku mdog phyag mtshan rgyan cha bzhon pa rnams bstan pa/ dpal
rdo rje nag po chen po'i sku bzhengs tshul yid bzhin nor bu mthong ba rang grol/ sgrub lnga'i nang gzungs 'bri tshul/ gur gyi mgon po'i khro bcu'i srung 'khor/ rdo rje brag
rdzong ma bar chad kun sel/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i bsnyen sgrub gsal byed gdams pa rin chen 'bar ba/ mgon po'i lus dkyil rdzogs rim bsgom tshul gyi khrid yig kha
gsal gzhan phan rgyas byed/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyag len gyi rim pa ji lta ba'i gtor chog dpal sa skya'i bka' srung rnams kyi gtor chog rgyun gyi nyams len shin
tu gsal ba'i phyag len ma 'bring po/ gtor chog bsdus pa shin tu nyams len

bde ba bar chad kun bcom dngos grub mchog stsol/ rang srung rgyas pa 'bri tshul shin tu gsal ba/ dpal ldan sa skya'i chos skyong khyad par can rnams kyi dus gtor gyi phyag
len rol yig gson po'i skra dang sen mo la tsha tsha btab pa'i yig chung / bdag chen kun legs pa la gnang ba'i bka' shog rnams bzhugs/ bka' 'bum po ti gsum pa la/ ka mad sum
bcu la gras pa'i gsung mgur/ dngul chu chos rdzong gi rgyal sras thogs med pa'i sku 'dra la snyan dar phul ba'i kha yig ka mad sum bcu la gras pa'i sa lo la gsol 'debs/
byas 'gyur gnas bstod/ dbus phyogs su mdzad pa'i nyams mgur mkhyen brtse ma/ byas 'gyur sgrub chen dge slong kun dga' la gdams pa'i nyams mgur che chung gnyis/ yang byas
'gyur du gnang ba'i mgur ma gcig bsod nams chos kyi dpal 'dzoms la gnang ba'i nyams mgur/ skyid sdug med pa'i nyams dbyangs/ ye shes mkha' 'gro la gdams pa'i zhal gdams/
chos kyi rgyal po la gdams pa'i zhal gdams/ gong dkar dbon po mkhyen rab la gnang ba'i bka' shog gdong dga' chos rje la gnang ba'i bka' shog gu ru drag po'i dbang chog
mthong ba rang grol/ gu ru drag po'i las mtha' gsal byed dgra bgegs tshar gcod kyi dpe/ mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa dze ta ri lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor sgrub cing mchod pa dang
'jug cing dbang blangs te slob ma la dbang bskur ba'i mtshams sbyor dang bcas pa/ tshe sgrub zab mo sa skya pa'i gdams pa thun mong ma yin pa/ ma gcig

grub pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dpag med kyi dbang chog rje btsun ma sgrol ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i tshe khrid bklag
chog ma/ rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma'i rjes gnang bya tshul shin tu zab pa/ thub pa gnas brtan chen po bcu drug dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ mgon po lha brgyad
kyi rjes gnang bya tshul shin tu gsal ba/ tsa turmu kha'i rjes gnang bya tshul bklag chog ma/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang byed dus lung byed pa'i yi ge dmag zor rgyal mo'i rjes
gnang bya tshul/ dpal dur khrod kyi bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang bya tshul sa lo'i gsung bzhin bkod pa/ pu tra ming sring gsum gyi rjes gnang bya tshul/ pu tra'i rjes
gnang zur bka' byed tshul/ bran bdud gshin rje nag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang bka' gtad bya tshul/ dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang bya tshul shin tu gsal ba/ mgon po lho
nub pa'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ dzam dmar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang byed tshul bklag chog ma/ grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ grub thob brgyad
bcu rtsa bzhi'i rnam thar/ gur gyi mgon po'i las mkhan ru 'dren dang bcas pa'i 'cham dpe/ dpal sa skya'i chos skyong gur gyi mgon po'i las tshogs gtor ma la brten nas
dgra bsad pa'i man ngag drug cu pa'i cho ga dgra bgegs gnad gcod kyi spu gri zhes bya ba sa los mdzad pa la sngags 'chang chen po'i mchan bu gnang ba/ gtor ma brgya rtsa'i
ngag 'don/ bum gter gyi lag len/ chu gtor gtong ba'i

rim pa blo gsar dga' ba bskyed byed/ klu gtor gtong tshul gsal byed sgron me/ dkar bdud kyi bskang gso/ dmag zor rgyal mo'i bskang gso'i yi ge rnams bzhugs so/ /de rnams kyi
brgyud pa ni/ snyigs dus rgyal ba'i bstan pa la rgyal ba gnyis pa ltar grags pa'i skyes chen dam pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin
chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de'i thugs sras grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ des bdag la'o/ /gsum 'bum de dag gi khrod nas grub thob brgyad cu'i rnam
thar sogs dpe sna 'ga' re'i lung rgyun ni sngags 'chang nyid kyi dngos kyi slob ma 'jun pa chos rje la thug pa spyan snga rin po che/ dang brgyud pa'i slob ma gzhan dag
las kyang nos mod kyi 'dir brjod bde ba'i phyir gsung 'bum gyi dkar chag bzhin phyogs gcig tu bris pa yin no// ! //'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo padma'i rnam 'phrul bsod nams
dbang po'i zhal snga nas kyi gsung rab rnams kyi lung thob pa'i tshul ni/ mthu stobs dbang phyug padma 'byung gnas dang / /gang thugs ye shes ngo bo ro gcig pa'i/ /grub
mchog ded dpon bsod nams dbang po'i zhabs/ /gus pas 'dud do brtse bas gzung du gsol/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa snyigs dus kyi grub pa'i dbang phyug mthu stobs
kyi mnga' bdag chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs byams pa dpal ngag dbang bsod nams dbang po grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa'i gsung rab rnams/ de'i slob bu'i tha chung
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis phyogs

gcig tu bsgrigs pa la gsung 'bum po ti gnyis byung ba'i glegs bam dang po'i nang du bzhugs pa'i rim pa la/ rdo rje phur pa'i brgyud 'debs bar chad kun sel/ zab lam brgyud 'debs
dgos 'dod kun 'byung / lam 'bras brgyud 'debs byin rlabs myur 'jug yang lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dngos grub bsam 'phel/ yang lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs
bsdus pa byin rlabs myur 'jug dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dad pa'i pho nya/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs bsdus pa/ gur drag
bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ brgyud 'debs bsdus pa 'dod don myur 'grub/ zhal bzhi pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs bar chad kun sel/ mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug sngags
'chang chen po la bstod pa byin rlabs dngos grub kyi char 'bebs/ yang sngags 'chang chen po la nang gi rnam thar dang mthun pa'i gsol 'debs/ rang rig bla ma'i gsol 'debs
mthong ba rang grol/ bla ma'i bstod pa phun tshogs dge legs kun gyi 'byung gnas/ 'dren mchog dam pa gzhon nu blo gros kyi sku bstod byin rlabs myur 'jug gdams pa zab mo
khyad par can/ bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga bsdus pa 'phrin las bsam 'phel/ mon bu pu tra'i drag bskul dam nyams tshar gcod dpa' bo'i 'brug sgra/ srung ma spyi'i dmod bcol gyi
bskul dam nyams tshar gcod rdo rje'i me dbal/ rten rdo rang byon lung bstan/ rol mo'i bstan bcos myong grub kyi lag len 'khrul med

gcig shes kun grol/ ja mchod phun tshogs dge legs ma/ dam pa'i chos kyi dbye ba/ skyabs 'gro'i rnam bshad blo gsal dang ba skyed byed/ rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa
shin tu bde ba/ bshes gnyen rnams kyis dris pa'i lan bstan pa rgyas byed/ dam tshig rdo rje'i sgrub thabs dam tshig gong 'phel/ tshe sgrub 'chi med lhun grub/ rig 'dzin
tshe'i sgrub pa yid bzhin nor bu/ tshe sgrub 'chi med rdo rje/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs sdig sgrib kun 'joms/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs shin tu bde
ba/ gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa 'phrin las lhun grub/ khro bo'i rgyal po rme ba brtsegs pa'i sgrub thabs bar chad kun sel/
'phags pa seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs nad kun sel byed/ gsung ngag rin po che'i dmigs rim nyams su len tshul shin tu bde ba/ lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid yig gi yang
snying bsdus pa tshig nyung don rgyas/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas par bskur ba'i cho ga grol lam mthar phyin/ dpal kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi mngon par rtogs pa yan
lag drug gi rnal 'byor nyams su len tshul gyi bsgom don rnams phyogs gcig tu dril ba nyams rtogs gong 'phel/ rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig yid bzhin
nor bu/ rten bskyed kyi yi ge mgon po'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ mahA kA la'i nyams len nyon mongs rang grol gyi gdams pa/ rig 'dzin brgyud pa'i ja mchod ci bsam kun 'grub/
gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid yig

shin tu go bde gsung rgyun gyi rim pa gsal ba dngos grub rgya mtsho 'di 'phro can yin/ rnams bzhugs so/ /de rnams kyis glegs bam dang po'i dkar chag bstan zin nas/ gsung 'bum
po ti gnyis pa na bzhugs pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin brlabs bya tshul gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu/ mahA kA la 'khor bcas kyi bstod
pa khams gsum zil gnon/ bstan srung 'khor bcas kyi bstod pa bar chad kun sel/ dben gnas byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong gi gnas bshad dngos grub rgya mtsho/ bya btang ku
sa li'i brtul zhugs la gnas pa ri khrod dbang po'i nyams mgur bde chen phun tshogs/ dben gnas ngo mtshar can phur ri rdo rje'i brag rdzong gi gnas bshad ngo mtshar rgya
mtsho dgos 'dod kun 'byung / nyams dga' blo bde'i mgur/ nged rang la gnang ba'i zhal gdams dgos 'dod kun 'byung / bla ma rgyang 'bod kyi tshigs bcad dgos 'dod kun 'byung
/ bya btang ri khrod pa pu nya indras rang la rang gis gros 'debs kyi tshigs su bcad pa snying gtam yid bzhin nor bu/ mchog dman gyi gang zag kun la zhu ba'i phrin yig don
gnyis lhun grub/ smon lam gyi tshigs bcad ci bsam chos bzhin 'grub pa dang / bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad bkra shis don grub gnyis/ rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po
padma 'byung gnas kyi rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar phun sum tshogs pa'i rgya mtsho/ rang rig dbang bskur gyi bsgom tshul gcig shes kun grol/ slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung
gnas dang rje 'bangs nyer

lnga la gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa dngos grub kun stsol/ grub chen shrI singha dang mjal tshul phyag bris ma las zhal bshus pa/ slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung
gnas kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyams su len tshul grub gnyis bsam 'phel/ rdo rje phur pa'i las thig gdab tshul ma rig mun sel rnams bzhugs so/ /gsung rab de rnams kyi nang
nas slob dpon chen po'i rnam thar sogs dpe sna 'ga' zhig gi lung rgyun ni grub mchog dbang po'i mtshan can de nyid kyi dngos slob dang brgyud pa'i slob ma sogs gzhan las
kyang nos mod kyi/ 'dir brjod bde ba'i phyir gsung 'bum gyi dkar chag bzhin phyogs gcig tu bris pa yin la/ de las gzhan pa'i gong bkod bzhin gyi gsung rab rnams yongs su
rdzogs par ni 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid las dngos su thos so/ /'dir smras pa/ de bA su ra mu ku Ti gi ri a gra/lha dang lha min gtsug rgyan sa 'dzin rtser/
pA da ra dza surYa a darsha dzi ga/zhabs rdul nyi ma'i me long la 'tsho ba/ /hi ta su khaHrasmi lakShi na sa shrI//phan bde'i 'od zer 'bum phrag bzhad pa'i dpal/ /siddhi
shwa ra pu Nya indra na ma/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams dbang por 'dud/ /de ltar grub mchog ded dpon bka' drin las/ /zab dang rgya che'i chos dang thun mong gi
/dngos grub mi zad nam mkha' mdzod kyi gter/ /stsol mdzad gang gi rnam thar bsam bzhin dad/ /gzhon nu'i dus nas khyed dang mjal re bzhin/ /thugs rje gting nas g.yos pa'i
dge mtshan gyis/ /'dzum pa'i zhal bstan mdzes pa'i spyan gyis gzigs/ /lugs gnyis bslab byas yang yang blo

mig phye/ /bka' drin de tsam kho nar ma zad kyi/ /nam yang 'bral med thugs rjes nyer dgongs te/khyod rab tu byung phyin chad nged dang 'bral med lhan cig tu gnas dgos shing
nga'i chos dang zang zing gi bdag po khyod kho na 'os yin no gsungs pa sogs/ /thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa'i snang tshul rnams/ /dran pa'i mod la spu ldang mchi ma g.yo/ /bla
ma padma 'byung dang dbyer med thugs/ /thugs dang rang sems ro gcig lhan skyes ngang / /ngang de blos byas ma yin gnas lugs mchog /mchog de rtogs nas don kun lhun grub
shog /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las rje btsun
grub pa'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba dpal sa skya pa chen po 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga nas kyis rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te dang po'o// //gcig zhus// ! mkhan
chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//

PART II: Teachings from Grags pa blo gros (1563-1617); vol. ka, text no. 7, pp. 619-670/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul
legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang mtshungs med grags pa blo gros kyis rjes su bzung ba'i
tshul gyi sarga bzhugs so/ /

rgya gar skad du/ dza ga tau nA tha shrI wan sanggu ru pu Nya dhwa dza shrI bha dra nirmma Na kA ya mantra dha ra gu ru a dhya nu kampa ma hatsa twaM na maH bod skad du/ 'gro
ba'i mgon po dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i sprul sku sngags 'chang bla ma sems dpa' chen po'i zhabs la mgos phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhi ba 'tsho
yi rnam sprul 'gro mgon rje/ /dga' ldan gnas nas slar yang gangs khrod 'dir/ /gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i skur sprul pa'i/ /sngags 'chang mtshungs med grags pa blo
gros rgyal/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa lhar bcas 'gro ba'i bla ma dus gsum rgyal ba'i yab cig mkhyen rab dang thugs rje tshad med pa'i bdag nyid 'phags pa 'jig
rten dbang phyug dang gnyis su ma mchis pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan

dpal bzang po pa'i drung du dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin ji ltar nos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar grub chen dze ta ri'i lugs kyi mgon po tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba thob pa'i rgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang
po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ bla chen bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla
ma bkra shis 'od zer/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ byang sems ye rgyal/ grags pa dpal/ sru lung pa kun smon/ brag phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal
ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun dga' bzang

po/ chos rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin
chen/ bka' drin mtshungs med yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa blo gros/ des bdag sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ kun dga' dbang
phyug 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/
mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag
la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ gu ge paNDi ta/ glo bo

mkhan chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na gu ge paN chen/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen/ mkhas grub dpal
ldan rdo rje/ 'dren mchog man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge rgya zhang phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma cha rgan/ grags
pa dpal man 'dra/ yang na rgya zhang phug pa/ 'jad pa rin shes/ e pa 'khon ston man 'dra/ yang na grags pa dpal/ chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen seng ge bu ston/
lo tsa ba byang chub rtse mo/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs/ dkyil chog bstod
pa rnams slob dpon dze ta ri dgra

las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rgya gar gyi paNDi ta 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang / bod kyi lo tsa ba lce dga' ba'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba rnams kyi lung dang / sngags 'chang chen
pos mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /yang ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dpag med kyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag
med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti pu pa/ ras chung ba/ mi la ras pa/ dwags po lha rje/ tha tsa ba/ 'bri khung ba/ spyan snga ba/ yang dgon pa/ spyan snga rin chen ldan/
rje zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal/ chos rje bde legs rin chen/ kun dga' dpal bzang / dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang po/ drin chen dpal ldan mgon po/ rje sangs rgyas
rin chen/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ bka' drin mtshungs med yab rje sbas pa'i sras grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ ! /bla med rdo
rje theg pa'i smin byed kyi thog ma bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang bskur ba rnam par dag pa lan
mang du thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ shrI dharmA kA ya sa manta bha dra/ dpal chos sku kun tu bzang po/ sambho ga kA ya badzra satwa/longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ nirmma Na kA
ya padma ka ra/sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ nA gantra rakShi ta/'khon klu dbang po bsrung ba/ badzra ratna/rdo rje rin chen/ pra dznyA gu Na/shes rab yon tan/ shi la rA
dza/tshul khrims rgyal po/ badzroShNa Sha/rdo rje gtsug tor/ shu bha sha ra Na/dge skyabs/ shu bha bA shya/dge mthong / ne pA la/bal po/ shAkya ma ti/shAkya blo

gros/ pradznyA shi la/shes rab tshul khrims/ /ratna ra dza/dkon mchog rgyal po/ mahA bhu mi paNDu/sa skya pa chen po/ A nanda garbha/kun dga' snying po/ A tsarYa pu Nya gra/slob
dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ bhaTTa ra ka ya sha dhwa dza/rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bhu mi paNDu paNTi ta nanda dhwa dza shrI bha dra/sa skya paNTi ta kun dga' rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ ArYa ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dra/'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ pra bha wAn shrI/kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/ A nanda badzra/bu lung
ba kun rdor/ wa ra wantu ma ti/lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ A nanta pu Nya/dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ ratna dhwa dza/gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sanggu ru pu Nya
dhwa dza shrI bha dra/bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ gu ru shrI win shi la/bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ badzra dha rA nanda bha dra/rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta kirti dhwa dza/paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ ma ho sa dhya pu Nya nI ra bho ga su bha ka ra dhwa dza shrI bha dra/mkhan chen bsod nams lhun
grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bhu mi paNDu manydzu gho Sha/sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ wa gindra A nanda ratna manggalaM ya sha dhA dza
shrI bha dra/ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ shrI wan bhu mi paNDu mahA mantra kirti ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dra/dpal ldan sa
skya pa sngags 'chang chen po grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ta ma ma shAkya u pa sa ka paNDi ta wa gindra A nanda pu Nya kirti dhwa dza shrI bha dra ya/
des bdag shAkya'i dge bsnyen mkhas pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la'o/ /yang na bla ma dam pa'i rjes su/ mahA gu ru A nanda dhwa dza/bla
ma chen po kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mahA ya na dharmA rA dza A nanda maM ga laM dhwa dza shrI bha dra/theg chen

chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ manydzu gho Sha ka sha dhwa dza shrI bha dra/'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ tsakra na tha
pradznyA dhwa dza shrI bha dra/'khor lo'i mgon po shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bhu mi paNDu lo tsA ba sa skya lo tsA ba/ man 'dra'o/ /yang na/ bhaTTa ra karje
btsun pa/ pa kuTTi de sha na/gan pa ston dar/ pa kuTTi dharmA rA dza/gan pa chos rgyal/ pa kuTTintra ratna/gan pa dbang rin/ pa kuTTi ratna dhwa dza/gan pa rin rgyal/ dharmA
swA mi sanggu ru chos rje bla ma dam pa man gong du 'dra'o/ /yang na/ rje btsun gan pa ston dang / gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin rgyal man gong dang
'dra/ ! /yang na 'khon ston dkon mchog rgyal po/ glo bo rdo rje srin po/ glo bo rdo rje 'dzin/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ bla chen 'phags pa man chad 'dra'o/ ! /yang
bka' drin mtshungs med yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
ba thob pa'i brgyud pa la bka' babs bdun ldan sogs su yod pa las/ sa lugs kyi dbang bka' rnying pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / indra bhu ti/ klu las
byung ba'i mkha' 'gro ma/ rgyal po bi su kalpa/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ de la 'phags pa lha/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa dang bzhis zhus pa las slob
pa'i rdo rje/ nag pa spyod pa/ sa 'dres pa/ de la mar me mdzad/a ti sha/ de wa ka ra/btsun mo can/ birYa bha dra mngon shes can/ gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum la 'gos khug pa
lhas btsas kyis

gsan pa las/ dbus pa dge ser/ gnam kha'u pa/ sa chen/ kha'u pa rdo rje bdud 'joms/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug
pa/ brag phug pa blo brtan/ chos rje dpal ldan pa/ grub chen buddha ba/ rje rdo rje 'chang / sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/
sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ bka' drin mtshungs med yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag la'o/ ! /sa lugs kyi dbang bka' gsar ma'i nye brgyud
ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ ma taM gi pa/ ra hu la shrI/sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen/ bakSha ta de wa/ kha che paN chen/
sa skya paNTi ta/ 'od zer shAkya/ dar ma shes rab/ rin chen dpal/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sru lung pa kun smon/ don ri grags pa dpal/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun
mkhyen bu ston/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man sa lugs kyi dbang bka' snga ma'i brgyud pa dang 'dra/ yang brgyud pa'i
bka' babs bdun dang ldan pa'i lugs ltar na/ thog mar rdog lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhu ti/ klu las gyur pa'i rnal 'byor
ma/ rgyal po bi su kalpa/rgya gar lho phyogs o dhe'i sha bram ze chen po sa ra ha/ na gardzu na/rgyal bas lung bstan pa'i dge slong dpal ldan/ de la slob ma'i mchog
arYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen

dang / klu'i byang chub dang / zla ba grags pa dang bzhis zhus/ des slob pa'i rdo rje dang / nag po spyod pa ba/ sa 'dres pa/ des mar me mdzad di paM ka ra/ dang paN/ de wa
paN dkar a ka ra btsun mo canka ra tsandra dang / paNbirYa bha dra mngon shes can gsum las/ gsum pos 'gos khugs pa sngags pa jo rog can lhas btsas la gsungs/ gzhan yang
za hor gyi mkhas pa btsun mo can/ ma yul rdzong gi na ga ko Ti/ bi kra ma la shi la'i thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis par grags pa'i di paM ka ra/ rdo rje gdan gyi mkhas pa chen
po nag po pa/ kongka la'i mkhas pa chen po rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can/ rgyal po'i khab kyi mkhas pa chen po dza hu zhes bya ba zhi ba bzang po/ kha che khri brtan gyi
mkhas pa chen po tsaNDa ha ri la sogs pa paNDi ta bdun cu/ mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis dang bcas pa la lo tsA ba chen po 'gos kyis gsan/ de la 'jad pa so rong gi mang ra
ba seng ge rgyal mtshan la/ de'i 'jad brag ltag gi rdog ye shes btsun pa seng ge de'i dbon po rdog mu ni rab tu byung ba'i mtshan nyi ma btsun pa seng ge des bres chu bar
gyi klan btsad nyi ma co rig lcam/ de gnyis la mu ni'i sras ArYa de wa/ de zhar chos pa skyi mkhar 'jugs gres/ kha dbon tsha'i ltag pa rin chen grags pa/ de la bla ma thams
cad mkhyen pa chos 'od kyis rgyud 'grel gyi bshad bka'ang thob/ yang rdog chen pa dang klan btsad tsha gnyis la snyi mo'i phug ka ba 'bum skyabs/ rong lha steng gi gtsang
ston smra seng / nyang stod sri chung gi lce mdo seng / yang brag ltag pa chen po la cha gar mon mo brag gi mi nyag rdo rje

grags/co reg de la lce mdo sde seng ge co reg de la bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa dge sding pa chos 'od/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ yang klan btsad tsha la thang spe ba/ grub thob gser
sding pa/ bla ma chos 'od/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ yang na thams cad mkhyen pa lce blo ldan seng ge bla ma 'phags pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu phag re
'gag chen pabsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i
rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ ! /mar lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sgro 'dogs nang nas chod pa grub
thob nyams brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / indra bhu ti/ DA ki bde ba'i zhabs/ Dombhi he ru ka rdo rje dril bu pa/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ kambha la pa/ nag po spyod pa/ ti
lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/sngags pa lcang lo can/ tshur dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kirti/ mgar ston shes rab rgya mtsho/ grangs so khro bo la rtsar ang khug pa rin chen
seng ge rong pa shes rab seng ge ston mo lung pa ye shes 'bar/ bla ma chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ khyung po/ chos rje shar pa/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ buddha ratna/ sa
lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / byang sems blo gros rin chen/ 'phags pa klu
sgrub/ mtshan gsang

ba ma taM gi pa/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba/ 'tshur dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kirti/ mkhan po bya khang pa bsod nams rin chen/ mkhan po thur la pa tshul khrims
skyabs/ mkhan po thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ grub thob gser sding pa gzhon nu 'od/ thams cad mkhyen pa chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od man 'dra'o/ /mkhas pa paNDi ta'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhu ti/ klu las gyur pa'i rnal 'byor ma/ rgyal po bi su kalpa/ bram ze sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ de'i thugs sras bzhi/
nye sras gsum ste bdun ni/ 'jam dpal zhal mthong shAkya mi tra/ sgrol ma zhal gzigs nA ga bo dhi/ sa brgyad non pa arYa de wa/ spyan ras gzigs zhal mthong ma tingga pa/ nye
ba gsum ni/ sangs rgyas bskyangs/ legs ldan 'byed/ slob dpon dpa' bo dang gsum mo/ yang ma tanggi pa/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa'o/ /yang klu sgrub kyis ma tanggi pa/
zla grags/ rig pa'i khu byug a wa dhu ti pa/ spyod pa'i rdo rje/ nag po zhabs/ dri med blo gros/ dpal ye shes snying pos mar pa la gdams te/ mar pa la 'phags skor gyi rgyud
'grel pa dang / rgyud rkyang / bshad rgyud lnga gzhung phran dang bcas pa dang / ye shes zhabs lugs sogs dang bcas pa la rgya gar na 'grel pa nyer gsum/ jo bos nyer lnga
tsam gsan gsungs skad/ bod na bdun zer yang mang du snang / mar pa la dza ya na/ tha ga na/ snyim tog gsum yod/ spyir rgya gar du lan gsum/ bal por lan bzhi ste bdun/
shar nub lho byang kha

che/ bal po'i paNDi ta dang / ku sa li grags tshad la bla ma brgya rtsa/ brgyud pa 'dzin nges lnga bcu rtsa brgyad/ snang ba 'gyur nges bcu gsum/ 'dus pa la mkhas pa'i bla
ma bdun gyi nang nas nub khu la kShe tra'i gtsug lag khang na gnas pa dpal ye shes snying po las 'dus pa'i dbang rgyud gdams pa'i bka' babs/ khyad par du mar pa'i bu bzhi'i
nang nas 'tshur dbang la nA ro pa'i dbang dang rgyud rkyang gdams par bcas pa gdams/ de'i rjes gad pa kirti/ de la mi nyag thur la pa/ dbus pa mgar dge grub thob zhang
gzhung pa/ des thugs sras gsum la/ gang bar gser kha'i rin chen gling pa la tshul khrims mdzes/ bla ma rgya rnal 'byor pho ba lung pa/ dge slong chos grags dpal bzang /
bla ma shAka gzhon/ bla ma blo ldan/ bla ma 'phags pa/ bu ston sogs man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /jo bo'i lugs kyi dbang bka'i brgyud pa ni/ /rdo rje 'chang bdag indra bhu ti
che/ /nA gar dzo gi bram ze sa ra ha/ /nA gardzu na zla ba grags pa dang / /ku sa li gnyis jo bo a ti sha /rong pa mgar dge lha rje stod pa dang / /shes rab rgyal po shes
rab gtsug tor dang / /lha rje chen po thang stod chos kyi 'od/ /bla chen klog kya bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / /kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal ldan grags pa dpal/ /'dus pa'i
dbang dang gzhung phran lung thob byas/ /phyis ni bla ma bsgom ye'i zhabs drung du/ /bde dges gsang 'dus rgyud 'brel phran bcas thob/ /khong la 'phags pas rgyud 'grel phran
bcas gsan/ /de la bu ston man chad gong

dang 'dra'o/ ! /chag lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ klu sgrub/ sras kyi thu bo shAkya bshes gnyen/ ArYa de wa/ 'phags pa rta dbyangs/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal
zhabs/ dza landha ri pa/ dpe med dpal/ gambhi ra ma ti pa/ niska langka pa de ba/ ra wendra pa de wa/ chag lo tsA ba/ 'u yug kung ra ba bla ma dpal/ yang klu'i byang chub
kyis Dombhi pa/ bi ra Di pa/ ma taM garbha/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ra wantra pa/ chag lo tsA ba/ yang zla grags kyis rol pa'i rdo rje/ skal ldan grags pa/ 'od zer 'byung gnas
grags pa/ 'od mdzad lha/ chos kyi 'byung gnas zhi ba/ rnam par grags pa'i lha/ rnyog med lha/ ra wendra pa/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/ 'u yug dpal la/ bla ma grags chen
pa/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston man chad gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ mgon po klu sgrub/ ArYa de
wa/ shAkya dge bsnyen/ zla ba grags pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ skal ldan grags pa/ 'od zer 'byung gnas grags pa/ 'od mdzad lha/ chos kyi 'byung gnas zhi ba/ bi khye ta de wa/
kha che shAkya shrI bha dra/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'od zer shAkya/ kha'u dar shes/ se mo dar pa rin chen dpal/ bla ma ra gnyis pa rgyal rin/ sro lung nags phug pa kun smon/
bla ma grags chen pa/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston man chad gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /dpyal lugs kyi dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ jo bo dang 'dra'o zhes zer bu ston rin po che'i gsan
yig la snang yang / dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos kha che

paN chen la zhus par snang bas/ kha che paN chen yan sa lugs dang 'dra/ de'i rjes su dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po/ rje btsun sga lo/ bla ma dpal gyi rgyal mtshan/ bla
ma don ri grags chen/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston lo tsA ba/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams man 'dra'o/ /sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang lan mang du thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ lho brag pa byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ ka bzhi pa grags gzhon/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ chos
rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog
dkon mchog 'phel/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan
chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang nos/ mkha'
'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i 'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ma/ a
bhya ka ra/ shu bhaM ka ra gupta/ pU dza ti gupta/ ratna rakShi ta/ go taM shrI/ karti paNDi ta/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/lo tsA ba 'dis lo brgya dang bdun thub/ rgyal mtshan
rin chen/ gar

thig pa bsod rgyal/ ka bcu pa gzhon nu seng ge bla ma mgon po 'bum/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun
dbang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des
bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ kun dbang / 'dren mchog rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen kun bzang / 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya
mtsho/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
