mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po mgur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang sgo rum bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi drung dang / rdo mgon yid
bzhin nor bu'i drung sogs su lan gsum thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shardha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin bzang / brag steng pa/
mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ bla
ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo chen po/ sngags
'chang chos

kyi rgyal po/ bka' drin mtshungs med yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa rin po che yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas rgyal tsha
lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ paNDi ta grags pa rdo rje/ sa skya lo tsA ba man 'dra'o/ /yang na dam pa kun grags kyi rjes su/ dga' ldan pa kun
bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ ! /gur gyi mgon po lcam dral
gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shardha kA ra warma/ jo bo/ rin chen
bzang po/ gu rub rin chen bsod nams/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam
mkha' dpal

bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gur gyi mgon po'i srung 'khor mdun gang ma dang / ser ba srung ba/ mdun gang ma 'phags pa'i srung 'khor gyi zhal shes
rnams dang / mgon dkar gyi tshe khrid zab mo'i lung yang thos so/ ! /yang rje btsun thugs rje can de nyid kyi drung du sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i gur gyi mgon po
khro bcu'i srung 'khor bar chad kun sel gyi lung dang / de'i dgongs don rnams ljags steng nas shin tu rgyas shing zhib par nos shing / yang dpal rdo rje nag po chen po
gur gyi mgon po 'khor dang bcas pa mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub kyi tshul du sgrub pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag nang khrid du grags pa 'jam sgrub rtsub sgrub zhar byung
gi man ngag dang bcas pa'i khrid yig sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i gzhan phan rgyas byed kyi lung khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/
bde ba'i rdo rje/ shaddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi
ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa dpal ldan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin
chen/ spyan tshab pa tshul khrims bzang po/ 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra

shis/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ rgyal tshab dkon mchog dpal ldan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/
des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po/ sngags 'chang chen po man 'dra/ yang na rje 'jam
dbyangs/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chen po man 'dra/ yang na rje 'jam dbyangs/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' bzang man
'dra/ khrid yig de nyid kyi lung gi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ sngags 'chang chen mo/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngor pa bha danta a wa dhu ti/ mus pa bha danta
ku sa li/ de las kyang bdag gis thos so/ ! /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang sgrub thabs rgya gzhung gi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal sde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna kirti/
ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba chen po/ bla ma gnam kha 'ub pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
'jam dbyangs

nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan yan sngar
dang 'dra ba las/ de nas dpal tshul/ shar chen dang grub chen buddha shrI gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal/ rgyal tshab kun dbang
/ kun mkhyen bsod seng / 'dren mchog rje sangs rgyas rin pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang dang / zhal bzhi pa
bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang gi yig cha sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang nos so/ ! /'phrin las rab tu myur pa'i dam can pu tra chen po'i rjes gnang zur bka' thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paNDi ta dharma pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/
bla ma mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya
paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub

chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ sa lo
'jam dbyangs chen po/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor grub chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/
des bdag la'o/ /pu tra'i rjes gnang zur bka' rgyas bsdus bya tshul gyi yi ge sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang nos so/ ! /bran bdud gshin rje nag po yab yum gyi
rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ sha ddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa
yon tan tshul khrims/ mal gyo lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi
ta/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ tshem bu pa dpal
ldan blo gros/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ kun bzang rtse pa/ lo chen rin chen chos kyi rgyal po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje
sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /bran bdud kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang nos so/ ! /dpal nor
skyong gi bdag po dur khrod kyi bdag po

yab yum gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'khor lo bde mchog rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ padma badzra/ badzra ra hu la/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dam tshig gi rdo
rje/ 'chi med blo bzang / bai ro tsa na/ khams pa sga lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yar bsgom/
rgyal tsha chos dbang / mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ yar klung seng rgyal/ bla chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam rgyal/ 'khon ston blo
gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas mchog dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po/ 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal
po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na sa lo yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug sngags
'chang chen po man 'dra/ 'di'i rjes gnang gi yi ge sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub skor yar klung pas mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gtor
chog chom rkun bsrung ba'i las tshogs dang bcas pa rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ ! /sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur gnyis kyi srung ma dkar
bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ klu'i dbang po srung ba/ rdo rje
rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal

po/ rdo rje gtsug tor/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / bal po/ shAkya blo gros/ shes rab tshul khrims/ dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ 'od ldan dpal/ kun dga' rdo rje/ mchog ldan legs pa'i blo/ kun bsod/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA/ 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i rjes gnang gi yig cha sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa
dang / bskang gso che chung gi lung yang thos so/ ! /dpal ldan dmag zor rgyal mo'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / paN chen la ba dmar po/ 'byung gnas
bzang po/ sgrub ston rgyal ba ye shes/ shes rab bla ma/ saM gha bha dra/ dpal chen 'od po/ zhang ston nyi ma/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba/ 'jam dbyangs
'khon ston/ rin chen mgon/ nyi ma bshes gnyen/ dkon mchog bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs mgon/ 'jam dbyangs ral gri/ nam mkha' snying po/ nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ sgrub chen byas
'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang

grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i rjes gnang gi yi ge mchod gtor 'bul tshul/ bskang gso rgyas bsdus rnams sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /yang
yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal mo lugs kyi snyung gnas kyi cho ga thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs/ dge slong ma dpal mo/ paNDi ta zla
ba gzhon nu/ ye shes bzang po/ bal po'i paNDi ta pe nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nying phug pa/ sru pa rdo rje rgyal po/ /zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ rtsi
'dul ba/ bde ba can pa/ chu bzang pa/ rin po che shes rab 'bum/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ kun spangs chos kyi rin chen/ byang sems bsod
nams rin chen/ mtshungs med ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje btsun dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang
grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /'jig rten dbang phyug gi gzhung bzhi nyams su len tshul kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa dang / bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan
gyis mdzad pa'i snyung gnas chog bsgrigs kyi lung yang thos so/ ! /gdon sgrol gyi man ngag zab mo'i cho ga thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ shaddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen
bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ bla ma mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ gnyan gtsug tor rgyal po/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ shar pa ye 'byung / shar pa dus
'khor ba/ kun dga' byang

chub/ mkhan po rgyal bzang pa/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug pa/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/
rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen thams
cad mkhyen pa/ paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /gdon sgrol gyi cho ga thar rtse nas
nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i rin chen phreng mdzes kyi lung yang nos so/ ! /slob dpon chen po a bhya ka ras mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor
bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyi sgrub thabs rnal 'byor rdzogs phreng / dkyil chog rdo rje phreng ba/ sbyin bsreg 'od kyi snye ma ste rgya gzhung gsum gyi lung thos pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ 'jig med 'byung gnas sbas pa/ dpe med bsrung / rnam par grags pa'i lha/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ de'i dbon chung bhu mi/ de
sras mi ba la shrI bha dra/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba byang chub seng ge skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol bu/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge chos rje rdo rje seng ge mkhas grub shAkya 'od zer/ rje buddha singha/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal
bzang / yab rje sbas

pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang rgya gzhung de gsum gyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ a bhya ka ra/
na ya ka pA/ da sha pa la shrI/ bikSha ra de wa/ shrI bha dra/ la li ta badzra/ dharmA gupta/ ratna ka ra/ padma badzra/ ratna kirti/ sangs rgyas dbyangs/ paN chen nags
rin/ 'gos lo tsA ba/ lhun sde rab 'byams pa/ dge slong rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs chos grags/ rje bkra shis mtshan can/ rje padma ba/ rje wa gindra/ chos rje buddha
ba/ zhwa lu mkhas grub rin chen rgya mtsho/ bha danta ku sa li/ de las kyang bdag gis thos so/ /rje thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng ba'i
sgrub dkyil gyi yi ge rdo phreng mdzes rgyan gyi lung yang thos so/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos mdzad pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs bya tshul gsang
ba yid bzhin nor bu'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po yan lam 'bras dang 'dra la/ de nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang
po/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ ! /'jam dbyangs nag po'i sgrub thabs man ngag dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa/ rje btsun chen po/ sa skya paN chen/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya/ mnyam med
pa/ bla ma shAkya 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ chos rje kun dga' bzang

po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas
pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs gu ge paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /bslab bsdus nas gsungs pa'i lus
srung ba'i rigs sngags sgra mi snyan pa'i rang gzungs su grags pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ma ti shrI/ ha ngu tsandra/ dar ma grags/ dpal chen rgyal ba don grub/ ye shes
rgyal po/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas
pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i yig cha rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /bde mchog dkar po'i tshe
sgrub zab mo'i khrid lung dang bcas pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'khor lo bde mchog paN chen shAkya shrI/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa sangs rgyas ye shes/ rin chen bsod
nams grags pa/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rin po che grags tshul ba/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ chos rje kun dga' bzang po/ bo dong pa bla
ma chu srin dpal/ mkhas btsun dpal rgyal ba/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal

bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /de'i yig cha sangs rgyas rin chen pas mdzad pa dang / rgyal tshab dkon mchog dpal ldan
pas mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ /yang jo bo rje'i thugs dam chos chung brgya rtsar grags pa thob pa'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs ni/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma dge blo'i
'gyur/ 1 spyod btus sgron ma nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 2 bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ 3 dbu ma'i man ngag nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 4 snying po bsdu ba tshul
khrims 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/ 5 snying po nges par bsdu ba nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 6 byang chub sems dpa' nor bu'i phreng ba/ 7 byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams
ngag tu byas pa de gnyis la 'gyur byang mi snang / 8 'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i klu rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur la nag tshos bcos
pa/ 9 spyod pa'i glu badzra pa Ni dang chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 10 chos kyi dbyings su lta ba'i glu nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 11 dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag nag tsho'i 'gyur/
12 byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug pa bstan pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 13 skyabs su 'gro ba bstan pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 14 theg pa chen po'i lam sgrub thabs
yi ger bsdus pa dge blo'i 'gyur/ 15 theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa dge blo'i 'gyur/ 16 rang gi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ba dang bcas pa yi ger bris pa
dge blo'i 'gyur/ 17 mdo sde yi don kun las

btus pa'i man ngag nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 18 mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 19 las rnam par 'byed pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 20 ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u
shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 21 'jig rten las 'das pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga 22 /kha ston dang glegs bam bklag pa'i sngon du bya ba'i cho ga 23 /pha rol tu phyin pa'i tsha
tsha gdab pa'i cho ga 24 /bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa 'di bzhi la 'gyur byang mi snang / 25 sems bskyed pa dang sdom pa'i cho ga'i rim pa dge blo'i 'gyur/ 26 de rnams jo
bo rje nyid kyis mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i cho ga byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ 27 pu Nya shrI mi tra dang dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ byang chub tu sems bskyed
pa'i cho ga klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 28 pu lentra bo dhi dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang yi dam blang ba'i cho ga dgra las rnam rgyal gyi
mdzad pa/ 29 su ma ti kirti dang blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ las dang po pa'i sa sbyang ba byang chub sems dpa'i dgra las rnam rgyal gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/
30 kriShNa pa dang chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ sems rin po che sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i 'phrin yig dgra las rgyal ba'i gsang bas mdzad pa/ 31 A tsarYa du lo pa
dang / chos she'i 'gyur/ bshes pa'i springs yig slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 32 sarba dznyA de wa dang / dpal brtsegs 'gyur/ slob ma la springs pa tsantra go mis mdzad
pa/ 33 sarba dznyA

de wa dang / dpal brtsegs 'gyur/ rgyal po ka ni ka la springs pa ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ 34 bi dya ka ra pra bha dang rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/
dri ma med pa'i dris lan rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba rgyal po dang snyan ngag mkhan la gdams pa/ don yod 'char gyis mdzad pa/ 35 ka ma la gupta dang / rin chen bzang
po'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis dge slong rab gsal gzhon nu la springs pa/ 36 sarba dznyA de wa dang / dpal brtsegs 'gyur/ shes rab brgya pa klu sgrub
kyis mdzad pa/ 37 sarba dznyA de ba dang / dpal brtsegs 'gyur/ dran pa nyer bzhag gi tshig le'ur byas pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyi mdzad pa/ 38 dharmA ka ra dang
/ gtsang de wendra'i 'gyur/ mi dge ba bcu'i las lam bstan pa rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 39 a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang / shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ dge ba bcu'i las lam bstan
pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 40 buddha ka ra dang / chos shes 'gyur/ mya ngan bsal ba rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 41 a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang / shAkya 'od
kyi 'gyur/ gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs brjod gsang ba'i byin gyis mdzad pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 42 yon tan bdun brjod pa'i gtam dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ 43 ga~M ga dha
ra dang rin bzang 'gyur/ tshul khrims kyi gtam dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ dza landha ra dang rin bzang 'gyur/ tshogs kyi gtam dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa gangga dha ra dang
rin bzang 'gyur/ 45 mi khom pa

brgyad kyi gtam rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 46 a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ legs par bshad pa rin po che'i za ma tog lta bu'i gtam dpa' bos mdzad pa/ 47
ru tra dang shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ phyin ci log bzhi spangs pa'i gtam ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ 48 buddha bha dra dang rin bzang 'gyur/ rtsod dus kyi gtam ma ti tsi tras mdzad/
49 a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ dben pa'i gtam chos byin gyis mdzad pa/ 50 di paM ka ra dang dge blo'i 'gyur/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga tshigs bcad
nyi shu klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rin chen phreng ba las phyung ba/ 51 ba tshwa'i chu klung gi mdo las phyung ba'i sems can mgu ba'i tshigs bcad/ 52 buddha ka ra warma dang
chos shes kyi 'gyur/ smon lam bdun bcu pa gzhan la phan pa'i dbyangs dgon pa bas mdzad pa/ 53 dharmA shrI bha dra dang dpal gyi lhun po'i sdes bsgyur ba/ don dam byang
chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i rim pa dang / 54 kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i rim pa gnyis ka rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 55 padma ka ra warma dang rin bzang 'gyur/
sangs rgyas rjes dran/ 56 chos rjes dran/ dge 'dun rjes dran gsum mdo las phyung ba/ 'dod yon lnga'i nyes dmigs bshad pa dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ 57 dharmA shrI bha dra
dang rin bzang 'gyur/ rtogs pa chen po yongs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde las phyung ba'i sdig bshags kyi cho ga 60 /de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa'i srung ba dang / 61 sdig
bshags zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i

bslab btus nas phyung ba/ 62 mdo sngags gnyis kyi thun mong ba'i maNDal bya ba'i cho ga sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 63 maNDal 'bul ba'i cho ga dgra las
rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ 64 a du lo pa dang chos shes kyi 'gyur/ maNDal gyi cho ga rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ 65 maNDal gyi cho ga rnyog med rdo
rjes mdzad pa/ 66 a du lo pa dang blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ maNDal gyi cho ga kaM pa las mdzad pa 'gyur rnying ngo / 67 /ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u gnas brtan byang
bzang gis mdzad pa/ 68 bi nA ya tsandra dang chos shes kyi 'gyur/ ting nge 'dzin tshogs le nag po pas mdzad pa/ 69 de nyid dang chos shes kyi 'gyur/ bsam gtan gyi chos
drug a ba dhu ti pas mdzad pa/ 70 de'i 'grel bshad dA na shi las mdzad pa/ 71 dharmA shrI bha dra dang rin bzang 'gyur/ ting nge 'dzin gyi mi mthun phyogs rnam par gzhag
pa mdo las phyung ba/ 72 hwa shang zab mo dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i 'gyur/ rnam par rtog pa'i gegs bsal ba sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa 'gyur rnying / 73 rnal 'byor
gyi mtshan nyid bstan pa byang bzang gis mdzad pa 'gyur byang med/ 74 rnal 'byor bsgom pa la 'jug pa ka ma la shi las mdzad pa/ 75 pradznyA warma dang ye shes sde'i 'gyur/
rnal 'byor bsgom pa'i lam ye shes snying pos mdzad pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 76 rnal 'byor la 'jug pa phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ 77 dharmA shrI dang rin chen bzang po'i
'gyur/ mi sdug pa bsgom pa'i rim pa dge ba'i go chas

mdzad pa 'gyur rnying / 78 lus yongs su spyad pa'i bsgom pa'i rim pa nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 79 de nyid dang chos shes 'gyur/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i bsgom pa'i
rim pa'i man ngag dpal ye shes grags pas mdzad pa/ 80 padma ka ra warma dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med pa bsgom pa mahA ma tis mdzad
pa/ 81 bi na ya tsandA dang chos shes kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor la 'jug pa chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa/ 82 shes phyin bsgom pa'i man ngag rin po che'i 'byung gnas zhi bas
mdzad pa/ 83 shanti bha dra dang 'gos kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i bsgom pa'i don mdor bsdus te bstan pa ye shes zla bas mdzad pa/ 84 pradznyA warma dang ye shes sde'i
'gyur/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gzhung rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa dze ta ris mdzad pa shanti bha dra dang 'gos kyi 'gyur/ 85 yon tan bdun bstan pa'i gtam dbyig
gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ 86 ka ma la gupta dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bslab btus kyi rtsa ba zhi ba lhas mdzad pa/ 87 bslab btus kyi mngon par rtogs pa mar me mdzad ye
shes kyis mdzad pa/ 88 de nyid dang nag tsho'i 'gyur/ theg chen nyi shu pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 89 kha che a nanta dang grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa sa lu
ljang pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 90 dharmA shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba legs pa'i blo gros dang dznyA na ku ma ra'i 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos
pa/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung

ba'i snying po'i tshig le'ur byas pa dang / 91 rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i snying po'i rnam par bshad pa gnyis ka klu sgrub gyis mdzad pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 92 rmi lam
yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 93 kha che shrI tha ra tha dang grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ byang chub sems 'grel slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa
rab zhi bshes gnyen gyis bsgyur ba la gzhi byas/ 94 go rub chos kyi shes rab dang / seng dkar shAkya 'od dang / shes rab grags dang / mar pa chos dbang dang / pa tshab nyi
ma grags dang / grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams las don gang bzang rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa/ bla na med par bstod pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 95 shAkya 'od kyi
'gyur/ srid pa las 'das par bstod pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 96 shrI tha ra tha dang grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ yon tan mtha' yas pas bstod pa dkon mchog 'bangs kyis
mdzad pa/ 97 sarba dznyA de wa dang rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/ yon tan mtha' yas pa'i bstod pa'i 'grel pa phyogs glang gis mdzad pa/ 98 lo
paN snga ma de rnams kyis bsgyur cing bcos pa/ yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa'i don gyi tshig ler byas pa phyogs glang gis mdzad pa lo paN 'dra/ 99 khyad par 'phags bstod
tho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/ 100 lha las phyung du byung bar bstod pa bde byed bdag pos mdzad pa gnyis ka sarba dznyA de wa dang rin chen mchog gis bsgyur ba la dpal rtsegs
kyis bcos pa/ skyabs 'gro bdun

cu pa zla ba grags pas mdzad pa jo bo rje dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ skyabs 'gro yan lag drug pa bi ma las mdzad pa 'gyur byang med pa/ dri ma med pa rin po che'i 'phrin
yig ces bya ba dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang tshul khrims rgyal po'i 'gyur te rjes dran gsum so sor byas pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs brgya dang gsum
yod pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ pu to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan grags/ chu mig pa shes rab grags/
gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ sangs rgyas bsgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchim nam mkha' grags/ rgyang ro byang chub 'bum/ mchims blo bzang grags pa/brgyud yig gzhan las gyang
ro byang chub 'bum mkhan chen blo bzang pa'i rjes la 'byung yang / mchim gyi rnam thar ltar na 'di bzhin yin/ yol ston bsod nams lhun grub/ slob dpon grags pa rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ rgya ston tsantra de ba/ ri khrod pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ 'dren mchog dkon
mchog 'phel/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ yab rje grags pa'i mtshan can/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo

gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa'i rjes su rje shar pa kun dga' bkra shis/ rgyal tshab ganggA na buddha/ bla ma dharmA ba/ chos kyi rje maho sAddha
ya ratna/ des bdag a nanda la'o/ /yang gso byed kyi chos skor la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u drug dang / bshad pa'i rgyud le'u sum bcu so gcig dang / man ngag gi brgyud pa le'u
dgu bcu go gnyis dang / phyi ma rgyud la le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga dang / mjug don yongs su gtad pa le'u gnyis te yongs su dril bas le'u brgya dang lnga bcu nga drug yod pa
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ buddho Sha dhi gu ru/sangs rgyas sman gyi bla/ bi dya ku ma ra/'tsho byed gzhon nu/ bI Na dznyA/rgyun shes/ bu na rbe su dza/nam so skyes/ anta
de ba dzwa la/thang la 'bar/ pa dA dwi tsarYa/rkang gnyis spyod/ ga ta pA la pu tra/'gro skyong / hasta ra pra brta nam/me bzhi 'jug a Ta ka hna/lug nag bandhu na/rgya skyegs/
sha ra sa ra/mda' yi mchog la ba na hasta/lan tshwa'i lag pa/ shrI manda mA la/dpal ldan phreng ba/ shrI manda lakShmi/dpal ldan phun tshogs/ ka retpanta/yid las skyes/
sU ra garbha/nyi ma'i snying po/ inu garbha/zla ba'i snying po/ tsantra pra bhaHzla ba'i 'od zer/ ArYa na gardzu na/'phags pa klu sgrub/ shrI wan shu ra/dpal ldan pha
gol/ so ma nanda/zla dga'/ bai ro tsa na/rnam par snang mdzad/ dharma rA dza bhi bhu pa ti/chos rgyal mnga' bdag khri srong lde btsan/ ko Na bha dznyA/grwa pa mngon shes/
dzi ba ka ratna sha ra Na/'tsho byed dkon skyabs/ bai ro tsa di nA tha/g.yu thog mgon po/ dznyA nA nanta/ye shes kun dga'/ lakShi mi/'bum me/bu ston/ be ro tsA ni nA tha
ratna/g.yu thog mgon po rin chen/ bu ra ka de sha na shAkya nA tha/phag ston shAkya mgon po/ shrI wanda dzi pa ka ra/brang ti dpal ldan 'tsho byed/ shrI manda dhwa dza/brang
ti dpal

ldan rgyal mtshan/ a nanda bha dra/brang ti kun dga' bzang po/ bya ghra de ba shrI/brang ti stag lha dpal/ badzra shrI bha dra/rdo rje dpal bzang / dharmA rA dza mangga laM/brang
ti chos rgyal bkra shis/ de wa swa mi a nantarthA siddhi/lha rje kun dga' don grub/ bikShu ga ga na shrI bha dra/brang ti dge slong nam mkha' dpal bzang / mahA bo
dhi sa twa kirti ma ti dhwa dza/byang chub sems dpa' chen po grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bhu mi paNDu ka waka gindra a nanda pu Nya ya/des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rje nam mkha' dpal bzang po'i rjes su/ rje don grub mtshan can/ chos rje buddha ba/ bla ma dharmA shrI/ chos kyi rje ma ho pA dhya ya ratna/
des ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang sgrub thabs kun btus sam/ rgya mtshor grags pa lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'i rgya gzhung gi lung thob
pa'i rnam grangs la/ dam tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ paNTi ta ku mu ta 'byung ba'i blo gros zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dam tshig gsum gyi rgyal
po'i sgrub thabs rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje gdan gyi man ngag gi cho ga dpal rdo rje gdan gyi sgrub thabs/ yang dpal rdo rje gdan gyi sgrub thabs/
yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ za ma tog bkod pa'i man ngag gis mdzad pa'i yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ dpal ldan 'jig rten mgon po'i sgrub
thabs/ yang yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ kharsa pa Ni 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs rnyog pa med pas mdzad pa/ po ta la kharsa pa Ni'i

sgrub thabs slob dpon padma 'byung gnas blo gros zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ kharsa pa Ni'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bde byed kyis mdzad pa/ dpal ldan mkha' spyod 'jig rten dbang phyug
gi sgrub thabs a nu pa ma rakShi tas mdzad pa/ dpal ldan mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs paNTi ta 'jigs med rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'jig
rten mgon po'i sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ yang seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs/ dpal ldan seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug ha la ha la'i
sgrub thabs/ ha la ha la'i sgrub thabs lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ rdo rje chos kyi sgrub thabs cho ga bsdus pa/ padma gar gyi dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs sangs
rgyas kyis gsungs pa/ yang padma gar gyi dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs ha ri ha ri la bzhon par gyur pa'i sgrub thabs/ ha ri ha ri la bzhon par gyur pa'i sgrub thabs sangs
rgyas kyi gsungs pa/ 'jig rten gsum po dbang du byed pa'i 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs sa ra ha'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gsum dbang du byed pa'i 'jig rten
dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug dmar po'i sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gis lhag par dbang du bya ba'i cho ga 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug
mgrin pa sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ padma'i phyag gi gzungs/ nye bar spyod pa dang bcas
pa sran ma ma sha'i zhal gyi gzungs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug don yod zhags pa'i sgrub

thabs/ dpal ldan 'jig rten gsum po dbang du byed pa/ 'phags pa bhukma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon shu nya ta sa mA dhi badzra sA da'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dpal ldan 'jig rten mgon
po'i sgrub thabs/ brtan pa'i 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bha wa kandhas mdzad pa dang / tshig lhug pa'i brtan pa'i 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam dpal seng ge sgra'i
sgrub thabs/ 'jam dpal ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs paNTi ta yid bzhin nor bus mdzad pa/ dpal ldan ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/ yang ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/
'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sgrub thabs/ dpal ldan 'phags pa ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ shes rab 'phel ba'i
gter ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan 'phrog byed 'joms pas mdzad pa/ tshig lhug pa'i a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ rje btsun 'phags pa 'jam dpal bsgom pa'i man
ngag a ra pa tsa na 'phral du nyams su myong ba'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ yan lag med pa'i sgrub thabs/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ chos dbyings
ngag gi dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ sems can dbang du bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin/ yang chos dbyings ngag gi dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ yang a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/
ngag gi sgrub thabs/ dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ chos dbyings kyi dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs kyi dbang du bya ba'i cho ga yang ngag gi sgrub thabs/ 'jam dpal
rgyal po rol pa'i sgrub

thabs/ yang 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ yang dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ bung ba myos pa'i sgrub thabs/ lhag par
dbang du byed pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ yang 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod las bsdus pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ rig pa 'dzin pa so so nas
bsdus pa'i 'jam dbyangs kyi sgrub thabs/ shes rab 'phel ba'i cho ga mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i man ngag shes rab 'khor lo'i dngos grub mchog gi sgrub thabs/ chos kyi
dung gi ting nge 'dzin 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs/ 'phags pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ yi ge gcig pa'i rab tu sbyor ba'i
sgrub thabs/ gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs cho ga dang bcas pa'i 'od zer 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ yang gtum po chen po'i sgrub thabs/
seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa/ sgrol ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs/ mchog sbyin sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ dbang byed sgrol ma'i sgrub
thabs slob dpon rdo rje'i myu gus mdzad pa/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub tshul mi 'dra ba gsum las gcig slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ yang rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs
paNDi ta slob dpon chos 'byung zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol ma dug sel ma'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma nor sbyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'od dpag med kyi snying po'i rgyud las 'phags
ma sgrol ma'i rtog pa gsungs

pa/ ngan song las sgrol ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'chi ba bslu ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ sna tshogs yum gyi sgrub thabs/ don thams cad
rab tu sbyin ma'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i gzungs/ yang dug sel ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i rigs sngags sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa/ 'phags ma dug sel ma'i rtog pa dza~M gu
la'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ de'i man ngag yang sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta chen po gnas brtan dpe
med kyis mdzad pa/ 'jigs pa brgyad las skyobs pa'i sgrub thabs/ rgya nag rim pa'i 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgya nag chen po'i rim pa'i 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub
thabs slob dpon brtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ yang 'chi ba bslu ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'chi ba bslu ba'i sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug
gi slob ma thu bos mdzad pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal pos mdzad pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs/ ral gcig ma'i
sgrub thabs che chung mi dra ba lnga las gcig slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ tsunda'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gsum/ rtog pa las phyung ba'i 'od zer can phyag bcu ma'i
sgrub thabs/ yang rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can dkar
mo'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje dbyings kyi

dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'od zer can ser mo phyag brgyad ma'i sgrub thabs/ au Di ya na'i 'od zer can phyag bcu gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol
pas mdzad pa/ 'od zer can dmar po phyag bcu ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od zer gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i jag 'chings rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can
gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon snying po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ 'od zer can gyi pi tsu ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs rgyas
bsdus gnyis/ de'i gzungs bklag pa'i man ngag ri khrod lo ma can gyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ shes phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ ri khrod lo ma can gyi gzungs/ shes rab
kyi pha rol tu phyin ma sku mdog ser mo'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ shes phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dge 'dun sbyin gyi bus mdzad pa/ yang shes phyin dkar
mo'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta padma 'phel gyis mdzad pa/ gser mdog can gyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ shes phyin gyi sgrub thabs/ yang gser mdog can gyi shes phyin
gyi sgrub thabs/ shes phyin gyi sgrub thabs 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags ma rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ dbyangs
can ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ rdo rje pi waM ma dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i

sgrub thabs gshin rje nag po las gsungs pa/ yang rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags ma khro gnyer can gyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ sgrol ma'i rtog pa las phyung
ba ku ru ku lle'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma'i rtog pa las phyung ba rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ de'i dbang du byed pa'i man ngag yang rig
byed ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ u rgyan nas byung ba'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ kyai
rdo rje'i rim pa'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ kyai rdo rje'i rgyud nas phyung ba'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ rig byed ma phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/
rig byed ma phyag brgyad ma'i sgrub thabs indra bhu tis mdzad pa/ yang rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i man ngag gi rim pa/ rig byed ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon nag
po pa'i mdzad pa'i rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ ku ru ku le'i las rab tu brkyangs pa'i sbyor ba/ rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ gdugs dkar can gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje tsa rtsi
ka'i sgrub thabs/ so sor 'brang ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gsum/ stong chen mo/ gsang sngags rjes 'dzin/ rma bya chen mo/ bsil ba'i tshal zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/
lha mo lnga'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa/ phyir bzlog ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan gyi sgrub thabs/ gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje ghanDa
ri'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ srung ba lnga'i cho ga rdo rje lcags sgrogs ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ paNDi ta chos kyi 'byung gnas blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i

rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan gyi sgrub thabs/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ lha mo nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gsum/ de'i gzungs kyi man ngag phag mo
shes rab gsal byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ byams pa'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ paNDi ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa'i mdzad pa'i dzambha la nag po'i sgrub thabs/ dzambha
la ser po'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gsum/ ser po phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs tsaNDa go mis mdzad pa/ ser po lha pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i sgrub thabs rgyas
bsdus gnyis/ de la chu rgyun du 'bul ba'i man ngag gi rim pa mi 'dra ba gsum/ slob dpon tsantra go mis mdzad pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ rtog pa bdun pa las gsungs pa'i
rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ paNDi ta shaddha ka ras mdzad pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje me dang nyi ma 'bar ba'i
sgrub thabs/ lta ba mchog gi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje gshed dmar gyi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje nag po'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ yang dgra nag gi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje
mthar byed kyi sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ bgegs mthar byed kyi sgrub thabs/ stobs po che'i sgrub thabs shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ yang stobs po che'i sgrub thabs/
hU~M mdzad kyi sgrub thabs/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs/ kyai rdo rje'i phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs tA ra shrIs mdzad pa/ bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ 'byung
po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs/ de'i cho ga dam pa thams cad 'dren pa'i 'jig rten gsum gyi rdo

rjes mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ yang nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs te lha 'di rnams kyi sgrub thabs kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ a bha ya ka ra/ shu bhaM ka
ra gupta/ pU dza ti/ ratna rakShi ta/ go ta~M shrI kirti paNDi ta/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rgyal mtshan rin chen/ gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal/ ka bcu pa gzhon nu
seng ge bla ma mgon po 'bum/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun
mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas
sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ mus chen/ 'dren mchog man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen/ 'jam dbyangs sher rgyam pa/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog
'phel/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rgyal tshab dkon mchog dpal ldan/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ chos rje shar pa/ bha danta
ku sa li/ des bdag la'o/ /rje thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i lha tshogs rnams kyi mngon rtogs rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i yi ge
'dod dgu'i ljon shing rin po che'i snye ma'i lung yang thos so/ ! /yang rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i sgrub skor logs na bzhugs pa ser pod du grags pa thob pa'i
chos kyi rnam grangs

la/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje gur dang gur rgyan las phyung ba/ sngags 'don bshad pa/ lcam dral gyi rtsa sngags la 'gyur mchan dang / rtsa sngags kyi bod skad tshigs
bcad du stob pa ma tis mdzad pa/ rtsa sngags kyi 'gyur mchan dpang los mdzad pa/ lcam dral gyi rjes gnang 'phags pas mdzad pa/ lo rgyus cung zad gcig lcam dral gyi
rjes gnang 'gro mgon bsod nams pas mdzad pa/ pu tra ming sring gi rjes gnang dam pas mdzad pa/ mgon po'i sgrub thabs bram ze mchog sred kyi mdzad pa shaddha dang lo chen
gyis bsgyur ba/ las byang lo chen gyis mdzad pa/ lcam dral sbags sgrub 'phags pas mdzad pa/ bris sku dang lder sku bzhengs tshul/ sbyin bsreg bkra shis dpal gyis mdzad pa/
gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa/ gzhan gyi rig sngags dang rbod stong bzlog pa/ rmi lam ngan pa dang mtshan ma ngan pa bzlog pa/ byad sha spag pa/ kha zas la brten nas
dgra bsad pa dang / dgra bgegs tshogs su bza' ba ste gces pa'i shog ril drug dam pas mdzad pa/ zab gtad ting nge 'dzin gyi shes rab kyis bris pa/ srung 'khor shAkya grags
kyis mdzad pa/ bsrung bzlog bsad gsum gyi zhal shes tshigs bcad ma 'phags pas dam pa la gnang ba/ rtsa gsum la brten pa'i bsam gtan gyi las sbyor/ rten gtor gyi man ngag
'khor lo lnga la brten pa'i bsam gtan gyi las sbyor/ gsang rten lus la bcangs ba/ 'khor lo bcangs thabs/ gtor ma'i man ngag gtor ma bca' thabs/ ngag mnan/ ngag srung /
sku gsung thugs

mi 'gyur ba'i gdams pa dang bcas pa dam pas mdzad pa/ mnan pa'i thun sgrub/ mnan pa dngos/ zor gyi gdams pa/ 'jam zhing zhi ba'i sgrub pa/ pho rkyang du sgrub pa dang / me
yi gdung ba dang / pho rkyang gi bsnyen sgrub sbrags pa/ lha mo nag mo'i gzungs/ bstod pa rkang pa brgyad pa mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs lo ka shrIs bsgyur ba/
pho rkyang mo rkyang gi sgrub pa gsal bar byed pa pu Nya badzras mdzad pa/ zangs gri can gyi sgrub yig pu tra ming sring gi gzhung gter me mon pa ming sring gi sgrub thabs/
pu tra ming sring gi lo rgyus sgrub thabs dang bcas pa/ pu tra ming sring gi bstod pa/ gtso 'khor sbags sgrub gzungs kyis pas mdzad pa/ sgrub pa'i gnad dril ba/ mgon po'i
sgrub thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa paN chen shAkya shrI nas brgyud pa/ gsang sgrub spu gri skor gsum kha che paN chen nas brgyud pa 'khor bcas kyi rjes gnang
zhang dkon mchog dpal dpon slob nas brgyud pa'i yi ge gnyis rnams thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po yan rjes gnang dang 'dra/ de nas gu ge paNDi
ta/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/
des bdag la'o// ! //yang rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag gi lo rgyus/ rjes gnang / rwa zor/
rtsa ba'i 'khor lo/ rab gnas/ gnad

'bebs/ skong zor kha sbyor dbye ba/ sngags ring / sngags kyi them yig sngags kyi gnad/ g.yab pa dar thogs/ nor bsgrub/ dbang bsdud/ spos sbyor/ rang dang slob ma rdzas sogs
gtad pa/ gtsug lag khang sogs gtad pa/ gnas mal dang nor rdzas sogs bsrung ba/ gsang rten byed thabs/ bskang bshag spyod lam dang dbang du bya ba/ de la mkho ba'i gnad/
dam tshig gi gso ba/ zhal gdams don drug ma/ rten bca' thabs/ chos skyong rten thabs/ rten gzugs/ yang rten gyi man ngag sngags ring thung gi man ngag bsnyen sgrub las gsum/
sbyin sreg ma nyan na tshod lta bya tshul/ dmod bskul/ 'go ba'i thabs/ 'khon nag bza' ba/ bskyod gnas srung gsum/ ltas ngan gtong thabs/ gnyan gyi shog dril/ chig brgyud
ma/ bskrad chog sre'u gso ba/ shwa ldog bskang ba bsdus pa/ bstod pa gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ yang ltas ngan gtong thabs/ sbas pa'i gdams pa/ 'gab 'dre mnan pa/ rakShi ta'i
man ngag bstod pa kha'u pas mdzad pa/ sgrub dus kyi gdams pa/ gzungs pas mdzad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i zhal gdams te yig sna lnga bcu rtsa gsum thos pa'i rgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal sde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna kirti/ ri sul gyi
rnal 'byor ma/ bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba chen po/ bla ma gnam kha'ub pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon chen rin po che/ chos rje sa skya

paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye
shes rgyal mtshan/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge bla ma rdo rje seng ge rje shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ /des bdag la'o/ /bka' drin mtshungs med sngags 'chang
grags pa'i mtshan can nyid kyi gsung rab rnams thos pa'i tshul ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi/ /rnam par sprul pa sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan/
/gang gi gsung rab yid 'ong padma'i tshogs/ /lhan cig bzhugs pa'i rnam grangs 'di ltar ro/ /de la 'dir bka' drin gzhal du med pa'i sngags 'chang bla ma sbas pa'i sangs rgyas
grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po de nyid kyi gsung rab dri ma med pa rnams mgon de'i slob bu'i tha shal za nyal 'chag gi rnal 'byor pa sngags 'chang ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs la thog mar sngags 'chang chen po la mtshan bstod kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs su
bcad pa/ bar do'i gdams pa zab mo/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i rnam thar 'ja' sa drug pa tshigs bcad du mdzad pa'i gsung rtsom 'phro can/ chos dung dkar po
rgyang grags kyi lo rgyus sngags

'chang chen po'i gsung rgyun bzhin bkod pa/ bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi lo rgyus snyan brgyud ma/ gur gyi mgon po'i las tshogs gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa'i man ngag
gi skabs su med thabs med pa'i man ngag dam pa/ gsung mgur bla ma rgyang 'bod/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i sbyin sreg gi ngag 'don dang phyag len gsal bar bkod
pa las dang po pa la nye bar mkho ba dngos grub myur stsol/ rdo rje phur pa dang kyai rdor gyi sbyin sreg gi phyag len zhal shes mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog gsung ngag rin po
che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid yig dang po'i blo can gyi rtogs par sla ba gsung rgyun gyi rim pa gsal ba/ dug srung zab mo/ rje rgyal ba mus pa chen po dang nged rang
la lung bstan gyi tshul du gnang ba'i bka' shog tshan pa gsum/ nged rang sku mched la gnang ba'i gsang gtor byed tshul gyi yi ge dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i sgrub thabs 'bring
po gzhan phan bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun rnams bzhugs pa'i glegs bam yongs rdzogs kyi lung rnams nos so/ /'dir smras pa/ ku la asdyi lakShi de ba lya pantha nri hi kha raM/rigs
rus phun tshogs lha yi lam la gar mdzad cing / /driShTa na saM to Sha ling ga nu pa la maNDa pa ri purNa/lta bas mi ngoms mtshan dpe'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs/
/aM bhu sa dznyA na da ma dra sha shaHru pa la nu ha ra/rmad byung mkhyen brtse'i ri bong gzugs kyis yid 'phrog pa/ /mantra tsantra kirti pra bha pi ta skandha dza ya/sngags
'chang zla ba grags pa'i 'od dkar phung po rgyal/ /gang gi zhal dkyil zla ba rgyas pa yi/ /utpal 'dab 'dra'i spyan gyi 'gro kun la/ /dal bur gzigs nas mdzes pa'i 'dzum
zhal

gyis/ /kun la rtag tu yid bde'i dga' ston stsol/ /sras kyi tha chung bdag la'ang mjal re bzhin/ /dges pa'i bzhad sgras bsus nas lus kyi gnas/ /phyag gis nyed sogs brtse bas
nyer dgongs te/ /thugs phebs byams pa'i gsung gis lan brgyar bskyangs/ /khyad par dpal ldan sa skya'i chos srid kyi/ /ma 'ongs bstan pa'i bdag por khyod 'gyur zhes/ /lung
bstan ji bzhin kun gyis mngon gyur pa'i/ /dus gsum sgrib med gzigs der snying nas dad/ /sprul pa'i skyes mchog khyed kyi bzhed pa'i don/ /sa skya'i sde dang bstan pa gdung
brgyud bcas/ /yar ngo'i zla ltar 'phel zhing rab rgyas nas/ /bdag gzhan 'di phyi'i don kun lhun grub shog /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos
ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags
pa blo gros kyi zhal snga nas kyis rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te gnyis pa'o/ / gcig zhus// ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//

PART III: Teachings from Mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan (1542-1618); vol. kha, text no. 1, pp. 1-136/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar
thos tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan gyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ sa de badzra garnA tha sha ra NaM sad dzi naH badzra dha ra mahA buddha dhwa dza pA da ma mi de he wAnma ti bhikta banda kraM taM/ bod skad du/ lha dang bcas
pa'i 'gro ba'i mgon skyabs dam pa rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan zhabs la bdag lus ngag yid gsum gus pas 'dud par bgyi'o/ /'khor 'das brtan
g.yo'i bdag po rdo rje 'chang / /gzhan ngor ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i skur sprul nas/ /mchog dang thun mong dngos grub kun stsol ba'i/ /rje btsun mus pa chen pos rtag skyongs
shig /ces pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa bdag cag rnams kyi 'dren pa dam pa khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas/ srid pa gsum gyi bla ma/ sku gsum gyi
bdag nyid/ dkon mchog gsum gyi ngo bo/ 'jig rten gsum gyi mig gcig pu/ lha dang bcas

pa'i 'jig rten na rje btsun mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan zhes yongs su grags pa'i ston mchog thub pa chen po'i rgyal tshab dpal ldan bla ma dam pa de nyid kyi drung
du zab pa dang rgya che ba dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi ji ltar thos pa'i tshul mdo tsam zhig brjod na/ thog mar bstan pa'i rtsa ba so sor thar pa dge bsnyen dang / dge
tshul dang / dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag pa thob pa'i tshul ni/ 'phags pa'i yul na singga la zhes bya zhing / rgya nag lugs la dmar ser can du grags pa me mo sbrul
gyi lo nag pa zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi snga dro'i cha la babs pa na/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba sras dang slob mar bcas pa thams cad kyi spro ba dang / bsdud pa'i byed pa
po/ don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te rgyal ba gnyis pa rje btsun mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi drung du mkhan po zhus

shing / las kyi slob dpon mtshungs med chos kyi rje thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi gdan sa pa bzod pa rgya mtsho ba/ gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon pa mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug
yangs can gdan sa pa chos kyi rje 'jam dbyangs chos bzang ba/ grib tshod pa gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa gling dga' zur 'chad pa chos rje chos skyong rdo rje/ dad pa'i dge
'dun bshes gnyen kun dga' lhun grub/ lung rigs smra ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan la sogs pa kha skong bar 'os pa'i dge slong du ma dang bcas pa'i dbus su yon tan rin po che
du ma'i 'byung gnas gling dga' bsam gtan phug gi bla ma gong ma rdo rje 'chang dang dbyer ma mchis pa rnams kyi gzim phug chos kyi pho brang chen po ga la ba der bsnyen par
rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thub pa'i dbang

po/ sha ri pu tra/rgyal po'i khab shing thag can du 'khrungs pa/ sras sgra gcan 'dzin/grong khyer ser skya/ bram ze sgra gcan 'dzin/ra Dar 'khrungs pa'i sa ra ha yin/ 'phags
pa klu sgrub/lho phyogs be ta'i yul/ gu Na mi Ta/'dis dbu ma rtsa sher 'grel pa mdzad/ rin chen bshes gnyen/lam 'bras kyi lo rgyus su dharmA mi trar bshad/ dpal ldan chos
skyong /zla ba'i grong du 'khrungs pa'i bi ru pa yin/ gu na pa ri/ chos kyi phreng ba/ 'byung gnas sbas pa/dran pa nyer bzhag phyis 'gyur gyi paNDi ta/ paNDi ta chen po
shAkya shrI/kha che khri brtan gyi grong khyer sra wa rar 'khrungs pa/ mkhan chen rdo rje dpal ba/tsho mtha' ba jo gdan/ mkhan chen 'od zer dpal/rgyal ba gser khang pa/
mkhan chen bsod nams dpal/snye mo bong ra ba jo/ mkhan chen bkra shis tshul khrims/yar 'brog sbrang mda' ba yin/ kha cig 'di 'od zer dpal ba'i sdom phrug rtsib pa shes mgon
pa'i sdom phrug tu 'dod/ shar pa ye shes rgyal

mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug spyan
snga rin po che dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ thub dbang gnyis pa rje btsun sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /de ltar rang nyid lo gzhon nu'i dus nas rigs kyi bag chags
sad pas rab tu 'byung 'dod kyi blo bcos min zhig yod pa la brten/ de nyid 'grub pa'i thabs tshul sna tshogs shig bgyis kyang / yab yum gnyis kyis dgongs pa ma 'khrol bar
yun ring 'gyangs pa la/ rang lo bcu bzhi lon skabs rtsom pa thams cad kyi thog mar gyur pa'i 'jam dbyangs sa paN gyi sku bstod de brtsams nas myur du rab tu 'byung bar
gsol ba btab pas/ lo de kho nar bsam don 'bad med du 'grub ste grub mchog 'jam dpal dbang po'i mtshan can las so sor thar pa dge bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa legs par
mnos shing / slar rang lo nyer gcig lon skabs rje btsun rgyal ba mus pa chen po'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag pa thob pa'i skal ba
mchog dang ldan par gyur mod kyang / dus phyis gangs can gyi 'gro ba ma lus pa'i bde skyid kyi rtsa ba dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i khur 'di rang
ngos nas ngal ba lhur len ma bgyis na sa skya pa'i bstan pa mtshan gyi lhag mar nye bar dogs pa 'di kho na sems kyis ma bzod pa'i dbang gis/ rang nyid la lung rtogs kyi
yon tan gang yang med kyang / rtsa brgyud kyi bla ma gong ma ye shes kyi

spyan ldan rnams kyi thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir dang / spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa/ sems can gyi bde skyid/ lhag par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa sde gdung brgyud dang
bcas pa snying khong bcangs pas rang nyid gcig pu zhi bde don gnyer gyi blo rgyang ring du spangs/ theg chen sems bskyed kyi go bgos te lhag bsam bzang pos kun nas blangs
pa'i nyan thos 'dul ba nas bshad pa'i bsnyen par rdzogs pa dang / dge tshul dang / tshangs spyod kyi bslab pa ji srid 'tsho'i bar du bsrung bar khas blangs pa de nyid de
las nyams pa dang / phyis blang du med pa sogs kyi nyes pa mi 'byung ba'i phyir dam chos 'dul ba rang nas gsungs pa ltar gyi bslab pa 'bul chog tshul bzhin du bgyis te/
de yang gang la 'bul ba'i yul rang gi mkhan po'am/ bslab pa bgres pa'i dge slong la bya bar bshad kyang / sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos dpal sa skya'i dbu rtse
rnying ma'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i drung du 'bul bar mdzad 'dug pa bzhin/ ye shes sems dpa' dngos dang khyad par med pa'i 'jam dbyangs kyi sku brnyan de nyid kyi
drung du/ chos rje sa paN gyis dbu'i gtsug phud phul ba'i thub dbang rdo rje gdan chung ma sngar rang gis dge tshul sgrub dus skra phud phul ba'i ston pa'i sku de nyid bzhugs
su gsol ba bdag cag gi mkhan po dang ngo bo gcig par mos pa'i blos de nyid kyi drung du gsol bzhi'i cho ga las thob cing khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi bdag
nyid dge slong gi sdom pa dang / rang sdom bcu phyogs mthun dang bcas pa'i dge tshul

gyi sdom pa/ mi tshangs spyod spongs pa'i dge bsnyen gyi bslab pa rnams phul te/ rtsa ba bzhi chang dang lnga spong pa'i yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen du bzung bar gsol nas/ de phyin
chad dge bsnyen rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ming btags tsam du khas 'che ba'i sdom rgyun gyi brgyud pa ni gong du bshad pa de dag gis shes so/ /'bul chog de ni bu ston rin po
che'i 'dul TIka chen mo/ 'phags pa rin po che'i dngos slob rgya byang seng gi 'dul TIka shin tu gsal ba dang / sgra pa shes rab rin chen gyi 'dul TIka ngo mtshar can sgra
TIka tu grags pa rnams la zhib tu dpyad cing / gzhan yang 'dul ba'i spyi TIka tshad thub du ma la brten nas mtha' chod par byas pa yin no// ! //yang rgyal ba gnyis pa rje
btsun thugs rje can mus pa chen po buddha'i mtshan can de nyid kyi drung du/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa mnos pa'i tshul ni/ mngon par rtogs pa rin po che'i ljon shing
las/ bla ma gong ma rnams dbang gi sngon du thun mong ma yin pa'i skyabs su 'gro ba dang sems bskyed pa tsam mdzad ces gsungs pa de'i phyag len zur du phyung ba'i/ dbu
sems kyi lugs las khyad par du 'phags pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyi rjes 'brangs jo bo nA ro ta pa la sogs pas bde mchog gi dbang gi sngon du mdzad pa dang / rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gi rjes 'brangs jo bo ga ya dha ra la sogs pas kyai rdo rje'i dbang gi sngon du mdzad pas brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed ces bya ba/ lta ba'i
sgo nas dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed du bsdud pa tsam las/ theg chen thun mong ba'i mdo yi rjes su 'brangs pa ni ma yin

pa'i rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bde kye sogs kyi smin grol gyi brgyud pa gzhan dang 'dra'o// ! //yang khyab bdag
'khor lo'i mgon po rdo rje 'chang mi'i sku gzugs can rje btsun sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan de nyid kyi drung du/ rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa thob pa'i tshul ni/ thog
mar dpal 'khor lo bde mchog slob dpon nag po spyod pa'i lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur rnam par dag pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha ra/rdo rje 'chang / badzra
pA Na/phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/mda' 'dzin/ nA gardzu na/klu sgrub/ sha wa ra/ri khrod pa/ lU hi pa/nya lto ba/ dha ri kasmad 'tshong ma'i khyo/ badzra ghaNTa/rdo rje
dril bu/ kurma la da/rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra/dpal dra ba 'dzin/ kr-iShNa tsarYa badzra/nag po spyod pa'i rdo rje/ gu hya/gsang ba pa/ bi dza ya pA da/rnam par
rgyal ba'i zhabs/ anta ra ba/bar ma/ te lo pa/til brdung ba/ na ro pa/'di bram ze'i rigs kyi ming yin/ a bha ya kIrti/'jigs med grags pa/ gcen/ kA la tsakra/dus 'khor ba/
gcung / pra dznyA ku Ta/shes rab brtsegs/ ma ti kIrti/blo gros grags pa/ shrI bhu mi paNDu A nanda garbha/dpal sa skya pa kun dga' snying po/ AtsarYa ratna pu Nya gra/slob
dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ bhaTTa ka ra ratna kIrti dhwa dza/rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bhu mi paNDu paNDi ta nanda dhwa dza shrI bha dra/sa
skya pa lnga rig kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ arYa ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dra/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ratna shrI/dkon mchog dpal/ pu Nya
shrI/bsod nams dpal/ sha wa ra ma ti sdyi ra/ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ sanggu ru pu Nya dhwa dza shrI

bha dra/bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ shrI wan shI la dharma swA mi dznyA na dhwa dza shrI bha dra/dpal ldan tshul khrims chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po/ badzra dha rA nanda bha dra/rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mahA satwa ratna dhwa dza/sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ paNDi ta kirti dhwa dza/lnga
rig grags pa rgyal mtshan/ ma ho sa bhya ya sarba dznyA pu Nya nI ra bho ga su bha ka ra dhwa dza shrI bha dra/mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub legs
pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bhu mi paNDu lo tsa manydzu gho Na nanta pu Nya kirti dhwa dza shrI bha dra/sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod
nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ wa gindra a nanda maM ga laM ya sha dhwa dza shrI bha dra/ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po/ shrI wan bhu mi paNDu ma hA mantra kirti ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dra/dpal ldan sa skya pa sngags 'chang chen po grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ shrI tsakra
saM wa ra buddha dhwa dza/dpal 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ ta ma ma shAkya u pa si ka paNDi ta wa gindra a nanda pu Nya kirti dhwa dza shrI bha dra ya/des
bdag shAkya'i dge bsnyen mkhas pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la'o/ /yang na sems dpa' chen po'i rjes su/ dharma swA mi buddha
shrI bha dra/chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / pa Tu siddhi shrI wan ra dza/mkhas grub dpal ldan rgyal po/ bhaTTa ra ka bha dra shrI/rje btsun bzang po dpal ba/ mahA paNDi
ta gangga na shwa ra/mkhas pa chen po nam mkha' dbang phyug siddhi shwa ra dharma shwa ra/grub pa'i dbang phyug chos dbang phyug bhaTTa ra ka badzra dha ra buddha dhwa
dza/rje btsun rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ ta ma ma bhu mi paNDu u pa si ka wa gindra a nanda pu Nya ya/des bdag sa skya ba dge bsnyen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ /yang

na rje sems dpa' chen po/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ 'khor lo sdom pa sangs
rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs sangs rin/ sa lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra// ! //dpal 'khor lo bde mchog grub chen lU hi pa
lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa thun mong ma yin pa sa lugs ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/mda' 'dzin nam mda' bsnun ces pa'am/
yang na sa ra mda'/ ha ni bsnun pa'o zhes shar ba rdo rje 'od zer gsungs/ klu sgrub/ sha wa ri pa/ lU hi ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra/
nag po spyod pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/kun tu bzang po/ nam mkha'i snying po/ snyan grags bzang po/ na ro pa/ ye shes dngos grub/ rtsa bshad pa
rnams nA ro pa'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs yin zer te dpyad do/ /pham thing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab brtsegs/pradznyA ku Da/ mal lo tsa ba blo gros grags pa/ sa chen/
rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang ston/ brag phug pa/ de la chos rje bla ma dang ri khrod pa gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma dpal ldan pa/ shar
chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje 'jam dbyangs/ rje dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje bzang po dpal/ paN chen nam dbang / rje chos
dbang / 'khor lo sdom pa

sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rje 'jam dbyangs/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen buddha'i mtshan can la bdag gis thos so/ /yang
na mus chen gyi rjes su/ zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang / rje dpal ldan rgyal po man 'dra'o/ /yang brgyud pa'i bka' bab bdun ldan ltar na/ thog mar sa lugs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ sa paN yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas bsod nams seng ge'u yug pa/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ dbus pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen
grub/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang
/ mnga' ris paN chen dpal ldan rgyal po/ chos rje bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje btsun chos dbang phyug 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/
des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgyal
po/ rdo rje 'chang buddha'i mtshan can/ des bdag la'o// ! //mar do lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/bde mchog u hi pa lha bcu gsum ma'am/ yang na bde mchog la lwa pa yang zer/ ye
shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ DeM ki pa/ la lwa pa/ indra bhu ti/ ka tsa Ta pa/ dril bu pa/ dza landha ri pa/ nag po pa/ ku sha la/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mA na ka shrI dznyA na/
bal po bha

danta/ mar pa do pa/ gze ba blo ldan/ gze ba jo bde/ slob dpon khu ba/ lho tshad pa/ lo mchog dpal ldan seng ge bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man gong dang 'dra'o// ! //jo lugs kyi dbang bshad/ brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ lU hi pa/ dha ri
ka pa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ jo bo rje/ shanti pa/ rong pa 'gar dge lha rje stod pa/ steng zla gsal/'u yug spen phug shong nyi ma kha dro/ gcen shes rab rgyal po/ gcung shes
rab gtsug tor/ lha rje chen po/ chos 'od/ zhing chen grags pa dpal/ bde gshegs dpal/ bla ma sgom pa ye shes/ bla ma grogs chen/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ mkhas grub
gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o// ! //paN chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bde mchog rdo rje phag mo/ lU hi pa/
ri khrod zhabs/ kandha pa/ 'dren mdzad zhabs/ bikSha ta de ba/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ bi bhu ta tsantra/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba/bsod nams bzang po/ mnga' ris pa sangs rgyas ye
shes/ze dmar ba yang zer/ bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man dang 'dra'o// ! //pu hrang lo chung
lugs kyi dbang bshad gnyis ka'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ lU hi pa/ DeM ki pa/ dha ri ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ dza landha ri

pa/ nag po spyod pa ba/ dge ba'i mgon po/ rus sbal zhabs/ bhu wa pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ma na ka shrI/ pra dznyA rakShi ta/ phaM thing pa gsum/ yang na ma
na ka ri dang / pra dznyA rakShi ta gnyis ka la na shrI de dang phaM thing pa la bha danta pa/ lo chung su ra pa/ grags mchogla stod srib kyi gad logs su/ dmar chos kyi
rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris skyi ston/ thur la pa/ thang dpe ba/ gser sding ba/ bla ma chos 'od/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes
rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man gong dang 'dra// ! //mar lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ pham thing pa yan chad sa lugs dang 'dra la/ de nas bal po bha danta/
lo chung grags mchog shes rab/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan chen po/ dbon po shes rab rdo rje/ thub pa shes rab/ brtson 'grus rdo rje/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma
shAkya gzhon nu/ lce blo ldan sengge/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po man sngar bzhin no// ! //dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ mai tri pa/ nya ka pa/ kandha pa/ bikSha ta de wa/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ grub thob
rdo rje gdan pa/ paN kShi ti garbha/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos bzang / rje btsun sga lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge gru ma chos skyong dpal/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos
rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun bzang man

gong dang 'dra'o// ! //sbal spang sna lugs lU hi pa jo bo lugs kyang zer/ kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ slob dpon chen po tsaNDi ka pa/ bram ze
chen po me ko ba/ lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ sdom pa bzang po/ jo bo rje/ de la lo chen rin bzang dang / nag tsho lo tsa ba gnyis kas gsan/ de gsum ka la bla ma rnam gnyis kyis
gsan/ de la 'al pa 'phan yul/ ston mgon/ 'al pa 'phan/ jo btsun/ sgom pa mang sgom/'phan yul rgyal ba/ sbal spang sna ba/drang srong srin po ri pa/ me rag dar byang /spong
zho brag nag rin chen rgyal po/de'i dbon po/ bla ma grags pa dpal/don ri pa/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ mkhas grub chos rje/ ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po man sngar bzhin no// ! //dpal 'khor lo bde mchog slob dpon dril bu pa lugs kyi zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba brgyud pa'i bka' bab gnyis dang
ldan pa thob pa las/ thog mar sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dpal chen he ru ka rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bar 'dzin zhabs/ nag po spyod pa/
gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ dpal ldan 'jigs med grags/ dus 'khor ba/ mal gyo lo tsA ba/ rje brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po
che/ chos kyi rje/ 'gro ba'i mgon po/ zhang ston chos rje/ grub chen brag phug pa/ de la chos rje ri khrod pa dang / chos rje bla ma dam pa gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka
la bla ma

dpal ldan tshul khrims kyis gsan/ de nas rje rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ chos rje zha lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mnga' ris paN chen dpal ldan rgyal po/
chos rje dpal bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje btsun dam pa chos dbang phyug mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang
na mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa
buddha'i mtshan can/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na sa paN/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ de la brag phug pa/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla chen kun blo dang gsum gyis gsan/ de
gsum la bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan pa man 'dra/ yang na sa paN la 'phags pa dang / bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rjes gsan/ de gnyis la khro phu bsod seng / yang brtse ba
rin chen seng ge de gnyis la kun mkhyen bu/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen pa/ rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na sa paN/ nyan chen pa/ de la bla ma dam pa dang / dkar po brag
pa gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis las bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa/ 'jam dbyangs rin rgyan/ bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/
'dren mchog phyogs las rnam rgyal/ lo chen byang rtse/ shar chen pa man 'dra/ yang na brag phug pa chen po/ brag phug pa dkon rgyal/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rje rdo rje
'chang man 'dra// ! //bka' bab

gnyis pa kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dril bu pa/ dga' ba'i rdo rje/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ 'byung gnas sbas pa/ de wa pUrNa/ kha che
paN chen/ spyi lhas pa seng dpal/ zhang ston 'bri lugs pa/ khro phu ba bsod seng / yang rtse ba/ kun mkhyen bu/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen pa man 'dra// ! //nye brgyud ni/
dril bu pa/ de wa pUrNa/ kha che paN chen man 'dra// ! //sa lugs kyi phag mo skor gsum gyi nang nas grub chen nA ro ta pa'i lugs kyi rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa/ DeM ki pa/ anta ra pa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ phaM thing pa gcen 'jigs med grags
pa/ gcung dus 'khor ba/ klog kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang ston/ brag phug
pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ chos rje ri khrod pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ zha lu ba sangs
rgyas dpal bzang / mnga' ris pa rgyal po/ chos rje bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje btsun dam pa chos dbang phyug 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen nA ro pa/ phaM thing pa sku mched man gong dang 'dra'o// ! //yang khyab bdag 'khor
lo'i mgon po de

nyid kyi drung du/ dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i sgo nas/ rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa rgyu dus kyi
dbang bskur ba mtshan nyid dang ldan pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thog mtha' med pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / /ma skyes mi 'gag shes rab bdag med ma/ /stobs
bcu'i dbang phyug dpal mgon bi ru pa/dmar ser me sbrul la bltams nas/ rnam byung 'brug la grub pa brnyes zer/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug shar phyogs nag po pa/ /rten 'brel
zab mo'i don gzigs DA ma ru/ /gzung 'dzin gnyis spangs a wa dhu ti pa/ /mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa ratna shrI/ /sgra bsgyur rgyal po shAkya ye shes dang / /snyan brgyud
gdams pa kun rig rje btsun se/ /zab don chos kyi snang ba 'bar ba'i mtshan/ /ang gir chu spre'i lo 'khrungs sa skya pa/bag yod ces pa chu mo glang gi lo dpal ldan sa skya
btab nas lo bcu dgu 'das pa/ /rnga chen chu khyi lo 'khrungs rje btsun rje/yab nga bzhi pa/ /rab byung me yos 'khrungs pa grags pa'i zhabs/de las lngas gzhon pa/ /dge
byed chu stag lo 'khrungs paNDi ta/de las sum cu rtsa lngas gzhon pa/ /myos byed shing lug lor 'khrungs 'phags pa'i zhabs/de las lnga bcu nga gsum gyis gzhon pa/ /kun ldan
lcags byi lo 'khrungs zhang ston rje/de las lngas gzhon pa/ /dbang phyug me glang lo 'khrungs brag phug pa/de las so bdun gyis gzhon pa/ /yongs 'dzin chu byi lo 'khrungs
'gro mgon rje/de las so lngas gzhon pa/ /agni me 'brug la 'khrungs ri khrod pa/de las bzhis gzhon pa/ /dpal gdong chu bya lo 'khrungs dpal ldan pa/de las bcu bdun gyis
gzhon pa/

/myos ldan sa yos lo 'khrungs buddha shrI/de las drug gis gzhon pa/ /rnga chen chu byi lo 'khrungs rdo rje 'chang /de las zhe gsum gyis gzhon pa//rnam byung sa 'brug lo 'khrungs
mus pa che/de las drug gis gzhon pa/ /khro bo shing glang lo 'khrungs dkon mchog 'phel/de las nga bdun gyis gzhon pa/ /dmar ser me sbrul lo 'khrungs lhun grub zhabs/
de las nga gnyis kyis gzhon pa/ /rab myos lcags rta lo 'khrungs dkon rgyal ba/de las lo bcu gsum gyis gzhon pa/ /dge byed chu stag lo 'khrungs buddha'i sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ mtshan/de las lo so gnyis kyis gzhon pa/ /gser 'phyang me bya lo skyes bdag la'o/de las lo nga bzhis gzhon pa/ /de ltar kyai rdo rje phyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor
du thabs rgyud kyi thog ma rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba dang / nang zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du thabs rgyud kyi gtso bo lam dus kyi dbang dang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag
med ma'i lus dkyil gyi byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ brag phug pa yan chad gong dang 'dra ba las/ de la bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / ri khrod
pa blo gros brtan pa gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ de nas grub chen buddha shrI/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man chad gong
dang 'dra'o/ /yang na chos rje sa paN/ tshogs bsgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal man gong bzhin/ yang na nyan chen pa/ dkar
po brag pa rin chen seng ge bla ma dpal ldan pa/ grub chen buddha shrI/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal

mtshan/ de gnyis char la 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge bla ma phyi ma de lnga
char la 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po dkon mchog 'phel/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /dbang byin rlabs de rnams kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs
bsgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ kun mkhyen gangs pa grags pa dpal/spang khang pa'ang zer/ ma ti paN chen/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis/ gu shrI nam mkha' bzang
po/nyi lde ba/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje man gong bzhin/ yang na chos rje sa paN/ grub thob yon tan dpal/ la ru ba bsod nams seng ge kun mkhyen gangs pa man gong bzhin/
yang na 'phags pa/ zhang pa brag phug pa chen po/ brag phug pa dkon rgyal/ sa skyabu ston dbang phyug dar/ chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis man gong bzhin/ yang
na bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims yan chad gzhan dang 'dra ba la/ de nas bla ma nam mkha' dpal bzang /de'i dbon po/ gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/
'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man gong bzhin// ! //yang lugs gcig ni/ mus chen yan sngar dang 'dra ba las/ khro mo shing 'brug lo 'khrungs rgyal
tshab rje/de las nyi shu rtsa drug gis gzhon pa/ /'dzin byed me byi lo 'khrungs legs 'byung zhabs/de las so gnyis kyis gzhon pa/ /dmar ser me sbrul lo 'khrungs dkon lhun
rje/de las zhe gcig gis gzhon pa/ /rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho man chad

gong dang 'dra/ /yang na sa skya paN chen nas/ rab myos lcags rta lo 'khrungs tshogs bsgom pa/sa paN las nyer brgyad kyis gzhon pa/ /rnam 'gyur lcags stag lo 'khrungs nyan
chen pa/de las nyi shus gzhon pa/ /inggir chu sprel lo 'khrungs ratna'i mtshan/de las zhe gnyis kyis gzhon pa/ /bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang
na sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man gong dang 'dra// ! //yang na chos rje sa paN nas/ tshogs bsgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan
chen bsod nams brtan pa/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge bla ma dpal ldan pa man gong dang 'dra// ! //yang na nyan chen pa nas/ brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa/ bla ma dpal ldan
pa man gong dang 'dra// ! //yang na rje sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ de gsum ka la rje
sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o// ! //yang na bla ma dpal ldan pa yan chad sngar gyi rnams dang 'dra ba las/ de nas shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/
rje kun dga' bzang po/ de la rje mus chen/ kun mkhyen rin po che/ grub chen dkon blo gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum ka la rje sangs rgyas rin chen pas gsan/ de nas rje dkon mchog
lhun grub man 'dra'o// ! //yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ bla ma 'phags rgyal/ bla ma rin chen dpal bzang / 'gro

mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa man gong gi rnams dang 'dra// ! //yang na zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ brag phug pa chos rje
rnam gnyis/ dpal ldan pa man 'dra// ! //yang na nyan chen pa/ bang mo zhu ba gzhon nu dpal/ 'gro mgon bsod nams pa/ bla ma dpal ldan pa man 'dra'o// ! //yang na brgyud pa
lugs gcig ni/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug pa yan 'dra ba las/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba kun dga' bsod nams/ rje dkon mchog lhun
grub man 'dra/ ! /yang na chos rje sa paN nas/ tshogs bsgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge bla ma dpal ldan pa man gong
dang 'dra/ ! yang na mus chen/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ de gsum ka la 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal pos gsan/ de la sa lo tsA ba kun dga'
bsod nams man chad sngar bzhin no/ ! /yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge de gnyis la 'dren mchog dang rje sangs rgyas rin chen gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis la sa
skya lo tsAs gsan/ de la rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ ! /yang na mus chen/ grub chen dkon blo/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang na ngor
chen/ mus chen/ kun dga' dbang phyug mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa skya lo tsA/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man

'dra'o/ ! /yang na ngor chen yab sras/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ ! /yang na ngor chen/
mkhas grub gzhon nu seng ge de gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba lha 'bri ston pa shes rab rdo rje/ paN chen mi nyag pa sogs gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang na ngor chen/ mus chen
gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba spyan snga kun dga' rdo rje dang / gung ru shes rab bzang po gnyis la mi nyag paN chen gyis gsan/ sa lo man sngar dang 'dra/ ! /yang na sa paN/
grub thob yon tan dpal/ la ru ba bsod nams seng ge gangs pa grags pa dpal/ paN chen ma ti/ theg chen chos rje/ gu shrI nam bzang / mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ paN chen mi nyag
pa sogs gong dang 'dra'o/ /yang na gu shrI nam bzang / ngag dbang grags pa/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa skya lo tsA ba man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang na 'gro mgon
bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ nya dpon kun dga' dpal/ grub chen kun dga' blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang
na 'gro mgon chos rje/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge theg chen chos rje/ grub chen kun dga' blo gros sogs snga ma dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang na rje kun dga' bzang po yan gong
bzhin las/ mus chen/ kun dbang / dpal rdor ba/ kun mkhyen/ 'dren mchog rje sangs rin pa/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub man

'dra/ ! /yang rgyu'i dbang bskur rkyang pa'i brgyud pa gzhan ni/ rje bla ma dam pa yan gsung ngag dang 'dra ba las/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal/ rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/
mtshungs med rgyal mtshan dkon mchog byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo ba tsA ba man 'dra/ ! /rje btsun rdo rje bdag
