med ma lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa chen yan chad yab dang 'dra ba/ de nas ne tse sbal ston/ bla ma shes rab grags/ gnam
pa rwa chos shes/ mngon pa ba dbang phyug brtson 'grus/dbu dkar ba/ de la 'phags pa rin po che dang / paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ de gnyis la zhang dkon mchog dpal/ de la
chos rje brag phug pa/ de la bla ma dam pa dang ri khrod pa gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de la chos rje shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan dang
/ grub chen buddha ba gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka la bla ma rdo rje 'chang / de la sems dpa' chen po/ de gnyis la rje btsun dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug pa dang / kun mkhyen
bsod nams seng ge de gnyis ka la 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ de la 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub man yab dang 'dra/ ! /yang rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo
rje 'chang kyai rdo rje de nyid kyi drung du/ mdo rgyud thams cad kyi don gyi bcud phyung ba gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag yongs su rdzogs
pa legs par thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar sngon 'gro snang ba

gsum gyi khrid dang rjes su 'brel bar lam 'bras brgyud pa'i phyag mchod chen mo kha skong dang bcas pa/ brgyud pa'i rnam thar zhib mo rdo rje/ rje sa skya pa chen po nas/ rje
rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bar gyi rnam thar thor bu ba thun mongs su grags pa rnams thob pa la/ rje sa chen gyi rnam thar rje btsun gyis mdzad pa/ rje btsun rtse mo'i rnam
thar bstod pa mchan bu dang bcas pa rje pas mdzad pa/ rje pa'i rnam thar chos rje pas mdzad pa rnam thar man lam ma sbal ston gyis bris pa/ chos rje pa'i rnam thar lho
pa kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa dang / rnam thar gsung bgros ma bla ma rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa'i rnam thar ye chen pos mdzad pa/ tshogs nyan gnyis kyi rnam thar
bar ston gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud pa'i lo rgyus las btus pa/ nyan chen pa'i rnam thar dkar po brag pas mdzad pa/ zhang pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ brag phug
pa'i rnam thar ri khrod pas mdzad pa/ chos rje bla ma dang ri khrod pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ dkar po brag pa'i rnam thar khong pa rang gis mdzad pa/ dpal ldan
pa'i rnam thar mus chen pas mdzad pa/ buddha'i rnam thar bla ma rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ chos rje shar pa'i rnam thar dad pa rgyas byed ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ rdo
rje 'chang gi rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa mus chen gyis mdzad pa/ rnam thar dngos grub dbang gi rgyal po gu ge paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ mus chen gyi rnam thar gsung
bgros ma gung rus mdzad pa/ rnam thar ngo mtshar chu rgyun kha skong dang bcas pa kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa/ rje kun

dbang pa'i rnam thar rin po che'i phreng ba mkhan chen legs 'byung gis mdzad pa/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba'i rnam thar mi nyag paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen gyi rnam thar
rje sangs rgyas rin chen pa/ glo bo mkhan chen pa/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan pa rnams kyis mdzad pa/ rje 'dren mchog gi rnam thar yon tan mtha' yas pa rje sangs rin
pas mdzad pa/ rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba'i nyin byed rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ rje sangs rin pa'i rnam thar dge legs rin po che'i gter kha skong dang bcas
pa sa skya lo tsAs mdzad pa/ de'i rnam thar 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi yon tan rnam par bkod pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho'i rnam thar
rje byang pa rab brtan pas mdzad pa/ bla ma bsten pa'i thabs shlau ka lnga bcu pa mkhan chen legs 'byung gi mchan bu dang / rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i dka' 'grel dang
bcas pa/ brgyud pa gnyis las 'ongs pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga rnams legs par thos/ ! /dngos gzhi la thog mar yab kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du
dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba rtsa sngags aShTa'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ lus dkyil gyi khrid kyi sngon 'gro thabs rgyud
kyi gtso bo lam dus kyi dbang bskur ba gsang sngags yi ge brgya pa bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ ! /gsang dbang lam gyi sngon 'gro rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i sindhu ra'i
dkyil 'khor dang / bla ma'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams par dbang bskur ba

lam dus kyi dbang dang bcas pa/ ! /lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi khrid dang byin rlabs/ ! /lam zab nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len/ ! /bla ma rin chen 'byung
ldan gyi rnal 'byor/ ! /phyi'i bar chad bsrung thabs rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi bsrung ba thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs/ ! /nang gi bar chad bsrung thabs dbang bzhi'i
brda don gyi man ngag chig brgyud ma/ thun mong gi bar chad bsrung thabs la phan 'dogs pa rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/ ! mtshon par bya ba gsung ngag rin po che'i
lam thams cad mtshon par byed pa bir srung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas pa/ ! /gsung ngag rin po che'i don bsdus te nyams su blang ba'i tshul ston
pa brda don gsal ba'i nyams len gyi man ngag dang bcas pa/ ! /gsung ngag stan thog gcig tu nyams su blang ba'i tshul ston pa lam bsdus te bsgrub pa'i lung sbyin pa/ ! /rnal
'byor dbang phyug gi zab chos lam sbas bshad kyi khrid 'khrul 'khor lag len dang bcas pa/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi bye brag tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs yan lag dang
bcas pa/ chos skor 'di'i bka' srung rdo rje nag po chen po dpa' rkyang gi rjes gnang rnams legs par thob nas/ de rnams kyi rgyab rten tshad ma bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i
yig sna rnams kyi lung thob pa/ thog mar bstan bcos rdo rje'i tshig rkang / de'i rnam 'grel rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa bcu gcig gi nang nas tshig nyung la don rgyas
pa gnyag ma'i yig chung dang bcas pa deng sang

lam 'bras glegs bam zhes mtshan du grags pa 'di'i nang na bzhugs pa'i rnam grangs la/ rdo rje'i tshig gi rnam 'grel gnyag ma dang / /gsal byed kun gzhi rgyu rgyud gdan sogs
dang / /lus dkyil 'chi bslu bum dbang 'da' kha ma/ /thig le'i rnal 'byor phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid dang / /bzhi pa'i 'da' kha bar do'i gdams ngag dang / /lam dbang tshad
ma bzhi dang gdams ngag drug /rten 'brel lnga dang grib sel yig chung gnyis/ /thig le bsrung ba yig brgya'i 'don thabs dang / /rlung sbyor bha ga'i yi ge 'khor bzhi'i rgya/
/dbang phyug don brgyad sa phyed mngon rtogs dang / /don bsdus ma ste nyi shu rtsa bzhi ni/ /bstan bcos nyid kyi steng du bshad bya 'o/ /de dag las 'phros gud du gsungs
pa'i chos/ /'khor 'das dbyer med dbang bzhi'i man ngag gnad/ /mchog dbang bskur tshul bskyed rim bsdus pa dang / /ril bu'i sgrub thabs yum gyi byin rlabs dang / /gegs sel
bzhi dang dbang chu sgrub thabs gsum/ /rtsa ltung 'khrul spong tshogs 'khor sbyin sreg ste/ /rtsa ba las 'phros chos sna bcu bdun las/ /phyi ma bdun po logs su bzhugs
kyang rung / /'bring bsdus lam gnyis gzhung shing chen mo bzhi/ /rtogs bskyed chos lnga lam zab bla ma rnams/ /nyams myong tshad ma'i chos sna nyer dgu yin/ /lung gi tshad
ma lung sbyor rnam pa bzhi/ /bla ma tshad ma rgya bod rnam thar gnyis/ /man ngag phra mor bcas pa drug cu 'o/ /zhes pa ltar glegs bam dkar chag tu thebs pa'i chos sna drug
bcu las/ glegs bam 'dir cis kyang bzhugs dgos pa'i chos sna zhe

dgu/ las dang po dang thun mong du logs su bzhugs kyang rung ba'i chos sna bdun dang bcas pa legs par thos/ man ngag phra mo'i rkang grangs logs su bsgrigs pa mtshan po ti

bir 'jam pa'i lo rgyus rje pas sga theng la gnang ba/ nyams myong tshad ma'i skabs su gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba'i khrid yig rje pas gra ston la gnang ba/ smin byed

pas mdzad pa/ dbang gi rab dbye rje pa'i gsung las zhang btsun gyis bris pa/ rje pas sga ston la springs pa/ phyi nang gsang gsum gyi maNDal sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ de'i

buddha shrIs mdzad pa/ dbang bzhi'i ngo sprod rtsa 'grel sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ brda don gsal ba rtsa 'grel sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ lho pa'i zin bris/ bstan bcos tshad ma'i skabs
su gnad du che ba drug gi yig rnying / rten 'brel lnga sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ lam bsdus pa dmar gyis mdzad pa/ phyag chen gyi dbye ba sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ tshogs sbyor
gyi mngon rtogs 'phags pas mdzad pa/ 'khor bzhi'i rgya sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ lam bsdus pa'i bshad pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ bsgrub pa lung sbyin sa paN gyis mdzad pa/

pa/ gsal byed buddha shrIs mdzad pa/ bir bsrung gi man ngag rnying pa gsum/ bir bsrung gi man ngag byin rlabs byed tshul dang bcas pa 'phags pas mdzad pa/ rnam 'joms

la tshar gsum khug pa che rje pas mdzad pa/ yi ge brgya

pa'i gdams ngag gi yig rnying sgo drug chos 'brel du grags pa la/ shanti pa'i mdo rgyud bsre ba/ shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa dang / dznyA na shrI dang / rin chen rdo rje gsum
gyi bar chad gsum sel/ ngag dbang grags pa'i gnyug ma dran gsal/ nA ro pa'i sdug bsngal gsum sel rnams thos/ de rnams kyi kha skong rje bla ma kun dga' bzang po yab sras

chen po mi bskyod rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa la/ ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i cho ga mngon par rtogs pa yan lag drug pa/ lus dkyil lam dus kyi dbang
len tshul/ gtor chog bar chad kun sel/ khrid kyi zin bris che chung gnyis/ lam zab kyi nyams len byed tshul rnams thos/ mdor na gsung ngag rin po che dang rjes su 'brel

dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ kun mkhyen rin po che lnga pas rjes
