skya ba ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ 'dren mchog gsum kas rjes su bzung ba rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog
lhun grub man 'dra/ ! /yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang pa/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ ! /yang na bla ma dpal ldan
tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man gong dang 'dra/ ! /bla ma rin 'byung gi brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun dbang pa/
'dren mchog sa skya

lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ ! /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge man 'dra'o/ ! /yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje sangs rgyas rin
chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya ba a nanda la'o/
! /rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi byin rlabs dang / bir bsrung thun mong ba'i brgyud pa lam zab dang 'dra'o/ ! /bir bsrung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje kun dbang ba/ 'dren mchog sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ ! /yang
na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang na mus chen/ grub chen dkon blo/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba man 'dra'o/
! /yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang / mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /gsung ngag rin po che'i man ngag gi don thams cad bsdus pa brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs nyams
len gyi gnad zab mo du ma dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bi ru pa/ sa chen/ rje btsun sa paN/ bla ma lung phu ba/ nam mkha' bsod nams/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu
grub/ dga' ldan pa kun

bsod/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ blo gros brtan pa gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba rgyal tshab kun dbang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/
rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa a nanda la'o/ ! /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge man 'dra/ ! /yang
na mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ rje sangs rin/ sa lo tsA ba man 'dra/ ! /yang gzhung bshad sras don ma/ gzhung bshad dmar ma gnyis kyi steng nas rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi bshad
bka' rgyas shing mtha' chod pa dang / yig cha de gnyis kyi lung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje sa chen/ rje btsun sku mched nas/ rje sems dpa' chen po yan chad lam
'bras dang 'dra/ de nas rje zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang / paN chen nyi zla seng ge grub chen nam mkha' shes rab/ rje zhe dgon pa bsod nams rtse mo/ rje rin chen chos
'phel/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun bsod la'o/ /gzhung bshad dmar ma rkyang ba'i brgyud pa ni/ dmar chos kyi rgyal
po/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen
po dkon

mchog rgyal mtshan/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang gzhung bshad de gnyis kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rje mus pa chen po'i gsung las 'khrungs pa'i bikShu
ku sa li pa las kyang bdag gis thos so/ ! /zhar byung gi man ngag thob pa la dag pa gsum gyi khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi he
ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa/ mi thub zla ba/ dge slong dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon
dgra lha 'bar/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ dga' ldan pa/ bkra shis dpal/ kun dga' bsod nams/ chos rje rnam gnyis/dpal ldan bla ma dang ri khrod pa blo
gros brtan pa gang rung / byams pa chos legs/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des sa skya pa a nanda la'o/ /khrid kyi yi ge chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa thos/ ! /rang byin rlabs kyi dmigs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa
rin po che yan chad dag pa gsum gyi khrid dang 'dra/ de nas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ chos rje brag phug pa man chad gong dang 'dra/ khrid yig rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad
pa thos/ ! /lam sbas bshad kyi thugs

rdo rje'i khrid/ 'khor lo/ grub chen bcu/ phra mo brgyad dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa a nanda la'o/ ! /sbas bshad 'khor
lo so gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ nyan chen pa nas gnyag snying po rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rgyal mtshan 'od/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan pa man 'dra/
! /pho brang lnga'i sbas bshad 'phrul 'khor dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ nyan chen pa/ dkar po brag pa/ bla ma dpal ldan pa man 'dra/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnam 'joms/ birWa pa/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ skyo ston dri med/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal tshul pa/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ rje sangs rin/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya
mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun bsod la'o/ /yang na skyo ston dar ma ye shes/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul
rgyal/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims man gong dang 'dra/ yang na rje btsun/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos

rin/ gan pa rin rgyal/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan sogs sngar bzhin no/ ! /tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs yan lag drug dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan chad lam
'bras dang 'dra ba'am/ yang na 'brog mi nas/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ gzhon nu grub/
zhang byang chub shes rab/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ rje buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun bzang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ rgyal tshab kun dbang
pa/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya
ba a nanda la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /sgo drug chos 'brel du grags pa las/ mdo rgyud bsre ba'i brgyud pa
ni/ slob dpon shanti pa/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ se ston kun rig zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ lung phu ba/ sgom pa nam bsod/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub/ zhang
ston byang shes/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal tshul ba/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ grub chen dkon mchog
blo gros/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag

dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /bar chad gsum sel gyi brgyud pa ni/ dznyA na shrI/ shes rab 'byung gnas/ rin chen rdo rje gsum la 'brog mis gsan/ de la sgom chen se rog gnyis
kas gsan/ de la gnyos/ yer pa bsgom seng / grub thob lha 'bar/ kha rag sgom pa/ lung phu ba sogs snga ma ji bzhin no/ ! /gnyug ma dran gsal gyi brgyud pa ni/ sgrol ma/
ngag dbang grags pa/ 'brog mi/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa chen/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ lung phu ba sogs sngar bzhin no/ ! /sdug bsngal gsum sel gyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun
nA ro pa/ 'brog mi/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ gsal ba'i snying po/ sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ rje btsun la sogs gong bzhin no/ ! /mgon po dpa' rkyang rjes gnang gi brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po yan chad gsung ngag dang 'dra/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal
ba lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
/yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /mgon po dpa' rkyang gi sgrub thabs gur rgyan las 'byung ba dang / sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang
gi yi ge kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ /kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad/ man

ngag gi gsal byed/ lus dkyil gyi rnam bshad bde chen bcud kyi snying po/ gsung ngag bstan pa rgyas pa'i nyi 'od/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen pas mdzad pa'i dam tshig gi bshad
pa/ khrid yig dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter chen/ dbang gong ma'i khrid yig lam zab bsdus pa/ bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrub pa'i phyag len gyi yi ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas
mdzad pa'i snang gsum mdzes rgyan/ sems bskyed kyi cho ga slob ma rjes 'dzin/ lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len gsang ba'i nye lam tshar gsum khug pa gsung ngag rin
po che'i dmigs rim dang mthun pa'i gsol 'debs zab don snying po/ de'i lam 'khyer gyi smon lam bdud rtsi snying po/ man ngag gi brda 'grol zab don snang ba/ gzhung ji lta
ba bzhin dkri ba'i gzhung shing la 'phros pa'i dri ba tshigs bcad ma/ rgyud gsum mdzes rgyan rnams kyang thos so/ /de ltar gsung ngag rin po che gnang ba'i skabs der/
bsags sbyangs kyi dus dang / rgyu dbang / lam dbang / lam zab phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung / bir bsrung thun mong ba/ brda chig brgyud/ bir bsrung thun mong ma yin pa/ brda
don gsal ba/ sgrub pa lung sbyin sogs kyi gsung rgyun phyag len gal che ba rnams zin bris kyi tshigs su bcad par bsdebs pa ni 'di lta ste/ skabs der bsags sbyangs skabs
kyi lag len la/ /skyabs 'gro sems bskyed rdor sems sgom bzlas dang / /de rjes bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen du/ /bskyed la maNDal so bdun ma nyid dang / /bdun ma gnyis po
lan mang phul rjes su/ /bla ma rang la

bstims te mnyam bzhag skyong / /de rjes dge ba bsngo ba rnams bya zhes/ /bla ma'i gsung de brjed dogs bris pa yin/ /snang gsum skabs su khog phub bshad pa mdzad/ /sngags lam
tshugs nas rtsa ltung rgyas par 'chad/ /de yang bla ma'i phyag len bris pa lags/ /rgyud gsum tshugs nas lag len byed dgos la/ /bsgrub pa'i maNDal bsham zhing rang nyid
kyi/ /mdun du maNDal 'bul yul rnams bsam la/ /maNDal mang du phul rjes rang la bstim/ /der rjes rdor sems sgom bzlas de yi rjes/ /bla ma'i rnal 'byor byed cing 'khor 'das
khrid/ /tshugs nas bla ma kye rdor dbyer med pa/ /spyi bor bsgoms nas de nyid snyoms 'jug gis/ /zhu nas rang la bstims te lta ba'i mchog /'khor 'das dbyer med bsgom pa yin
no zhes/ /bla mas gsungs pa de bzhin bris pa'o/ /sngags lam tshugs nas slob ma kun 'dus te/ /rgyun du maNDal so bdun ma re dang / /thos rgya ma re phyag len la mdzad do/
/rgyu dbang gnang ba'i skabs der 'jug pa'i dus/ /nang bsrung bdud rtsi ster dang rig pa yi/ /dbang lnga'i mchod pa sogs la nyer mchod lnga'i/ /mjug tu shapta byed pa mus
pa che/ /dkon mchog rgyal mtshan phyag len yin no zhes/ /bdag gi bla ma gsungs shing mdzad kyin 'dug /skabs der dgos pa'i skur byed nam mkha' yi/ /dkyil 'khor bsgom tshul
dmigs pa 'di lta ste/ /pho brang yod med gang ltar lha rnams kyi/ /dbus su gar bu de yis dbus nyid dang / /phyogs bzhir yo ga nas bshad rigs lnga dang / /mtshams

bzhir yum bzhi lha rnams phyogs bzhi ru/ /sras chen brgyad dang de mtha' khro bo dang / /mchod pa'i lha mo bsgom pa yin no zhes/ /bla mas gsungs de brjed dogs bris pa yin/
/gsol gdab dus su rigs lnga kyai rdo rje/ /zhal brgyad bcu drug phyag can du gyur bsgom/ 'di yang gsung rgyun yin no// ! //lam dbang gnang skabs phyag len 'di lta ste/ /thog
mar rten dang mchod gtor legs bshams nas/ /gnas yo byin rlabs dbang chu mdzes rgyan bzhin/ /byas la de nas lam dus nyams blangs te/ /dkyil 'khor bsdus rjes rnam rgyal
bum pa bsgrub/ /bsgrub tshul dbang chu mdzes rgyan ji bzhin las/ /skabs 'dir las bum med phyir de der ro/ /de nas skur byed nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor gyi/ /lha tshogs snying
kha'i 'od kyis spyan drangs te/ /dbang bskur dkyil 'khor gtso bo bla ma dang / /tha dad med pa'i sku lus de nyid la/ /gdan gsum tshang bar mos te maNDal phul/ /gsol gdab
rgyun bshags sdom bzung byas rjes su/ /mig dar 'ching tshul me tog lag len cing / /bgegs bsang dri ba dri lan sems bskyed bsgom/ /bsgoms pa de nyid brtan par byas pa'i
rjes/ /gsang bar gdams la hU~M dzaHhU~M zhes pa'i/ /'jug pa bya zhing dam bzhag rnam bzhi bya/ /de nas byin rlabs rim lnga zhu ba yis/ /maNDal gsol 'debs byas rjes byin rlabs
kyi/ /rim pa lnga bya tiShThas brtan par bya/ /me tog 'bul tshul mgor bzhag mig gi dar/ /bsal tshul byas la sku dkyil mthong bar bsam/ /de nas dngos gzhi chos yon maNDal
phul/ /gsol btab

byur bsal de nas rig pa yi/ /dbang lnga nas brtsams dbang bzhi rdzogs kyi bar/ /lam dus bzhin bya 'on kyang dbang gi rdzas/ /bum chu 'thung dang dbu rgyan gyon pa dang / /rdor
dril lag tu 'dzin rnams lam dus kyi/ /dus der bsgom bya yin mod skabs 'dir ni/ /dngos su byed la dbang rnams rdzogs pa dang / /chos skyong rnams la gtor 'bul byas pa'i
rjes/ /bskangs pa rgyas bsdus gang yang rung ba dang / /bstod pa byas rjes rdo glu bkra shis dang / /smon lam de yis sangs rgyas myur thob shog /ces pa'i bar bya de nas
slob ma rnams/ /khrus byas gral la 'khod de dbang bskur bya/ /rigs lnga'i dbang dang rdo rje brtul zhugs dbang / /rdo rje slob dpon dbang rnams slob ma yi/ /phyi nang gnyis
ka'i rten la bskur ba yi/ /gsang dbang de dang 'dra la sher dbang ni/ /phyi yi rten dang nang gi 'khor lo lnga'i/ /gtso bo rnams la bskur gyi gzhan la min/ /lam dbang
bskur ba'i skabs der skur byed kyi/ /dkyil 'khor slob dpon dbang gi rjes su bstim/ /nyams len dus su dbang bzhi rdzogs par mnos/ /rig pa'i dbang lnga'i dbang rdzas bum pa'i
chu/ /ster dang dbu rgyan 'ching dang rdor dril gnyis/ /lag tu gtad dang ming dbang bskur ba dang / /brtul zhugs dbang gi dbang rdzas rdo rje de/ /gtod dang slob dpon
dbang dus rdo rje dang / /dril bu sbyin dang chu yi dbang bskur ba/ /rnam sogs de dag mdzad po skur byed kyi/ /dkyil 'khor nyid kyi gtso bo'i thugs kha nas/ /zhal gcig phyag
gnyis ldan pa'i he ru ka /byon par

bsam la de dang rdo rje yis/ /slob dpon gnyis kas mdzad par bsam pa yin/ /lam dbang thob nas chu rgyun mi nyams phyir/ /dbang bskur zab mo thun drug bzhi gsum gnyis/ /gang
byas na yang rung la thun gcig la/ /nges par rgyas par bya dgos thun gcig ni/ /shin tu bsdud par 'dod na skyabs sems dang / /rdor sems sgom bzlas byas la rdor sems bstim/
/tshogs zhing spyan drangs de la mchod pa dang / /yan lag bdun pa la sogs byas pa'i rjes/ /tshogs zhing rang lus bstims nas lus dkyil bsgom/ /de nas dbang bskur rnams ni
len pa yin/ /de lta'i lam dbang gnang skabs phyag len gyi/ /rim pa rnams dang dus der mkho ba yi/ /dmigs pa 'ga' sogs gsal bar bshad pa 'di/ /bla ma dam pa'i gsung rgyun
phyag len rnams/ /shin tu nges par byas nas bris pa 'o/ ! /lam zab phyi ma 'di nyams len/ /dus kyi rang lus dum bu ru/ /gtubs tshe rang gi spyi bo nas/ /rnam shes he ru
ka'i rnam pas/ /thon nas tha mal pa'i lus de/ /gtubs par bsgom zhing he ru ka /de ni zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /bsam par bya 'o yin no zhes/ /bla ma'i gsungs de brjed dogs
bris/ ! /nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyid/ /gnang skabs phyag len 'di lta ste/ /mdzes pa'i stegs la chu rnam bzhi/ /sngon 'gro'i nyer spyod lnga dang ni/ /zlum gtor gsum
bsham bla ma yis/ /gdan la 'dug ste lam dus blangs/ /de rjes nang gi bla ma yis/ /rnal 'byor bsgom la gtor bsngo bya/ /de nas slob ma rnams bsdus la/ /bla mas gsal

btab/ sems bskyed sogs byas nas/ /slob ma maNDal 'bul gzhug gang drin ma/ /sogs kyi rjes zlos byed 'jug go /de yi rjes su slob dpon gyis/ /skyabs su 'gro ba nas brtsams te/
/nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi/ /ngag 'don gong dang 'dra ba las/ /khyad par ye shes pa slob ma/ /rnams la bstims nas de'i rkyen gyis/ /slob ma'i lus dkyil gsal 'debs
so/ /legs par rdzogs nas gtang rag gi /maNDal sogs bya de'i rjes su/ /slob dpon gyis ni mjug chog rnams/ /bya 'o de lta'i lag len gyi/ /rim pa 'di ni bla ma yi/ /gsung rgyun
phyag len legs zin pa'i/ /lugs su byas nas bris pa yin/ /bla ma rin 'byung gnang dus phyag len ni/ /stegs la zlum gtor gsum dang chu rnam bzhi/ /sngon 'gro nyer spyod
lnga bsham slob dpon gyis/ /thog mar lam dus blangs la de yi rjes/ /nyid la bla ma rin 'byung legs par bsgom/ /de nas gtor bsngo byas la slob ma bsdus/ bla mas/sems bskyed
gsal btab sogs bya maNDal dang /slob mas/ /gang drin la sogs gsol btab byar bcug la/ /de nas bla ma rin 'byung nyid/ /gong du bsgom pa bzhin du skyabs 'gro nas/ /brtsams
te ngag 'don rnams brjod sems bskyed bsgom/ /de rjes slob ma rnams la bsgom tshul sogs/ /spog la gtang rag maNDal yon 'bul rnams/ /byas nas bla mas mjug gi cho ga bya/
/de bzhin lag len rim 'di bla ma yi/ /phyag len zin pa'i lugs su byas nas bris/ ! /bir bsrung thun mong ba 'di nyid/ /

nyams len byed tshe rang gi mdun/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug bskyed dgos pa/ /de la ye shes pa 'jug dus/ /bla ma rnams ni birWa pa'i/ /rnam pa thim zhing sangs rgyas dang / /byang
sems thams cad kyai rdo rje'i/ /rnam pa mdun bskyed de'i thugs kar/ /zhugs par bsgom pa yin zhes pa'i/ /bla ma'i gsung de 'dir bris so/ ! /chos zab gdams pa chig brgyud
ma/ /gnang skabs phyag len 'di lta ste/ /chu bzhi sngon 'gro mchod lnga dang / /zlum gtor gsum rnams stegs la bsham/ /de nas bla mas lam dus blangs/ /dkyil 'khor bsdus
te chos skyong la/ /gtor 'bul byas rjes slob ma bsdud/ /bsdud gong yol bas slob dpon dang / /slob ma 'dug pa'i bar bcad la/ /slob ma 'dus nas maNDal dang / /kun mkhyen
ye shes sogs byed 'jug /de yi rjes su bla ma yis/ /sems bskyed gsal btab sogs bya 'o/ /de nas dpon slob thams cad kyis/ /bsrung 'khor bsgom zhing uShNi Shi/ bzla ba'i/ngang
nas slob ma rim pa bzhin/ /yol ba'i phyi slob ma 'dug pa nas nang du slob dpon gyi drung du yong bcug la/ bla mas/brda rnams bstan la kun rdzogs nas/ /de nas dpon slob
thams cad kyis/ /bsrung 'khor gyis mjug rdzogs par bya/ /de rjes gtang rag maNDal sogs/ /byas la slob dpon gyis mjug chog /rnams bya de lta'i lag len gyi/ /rim pa 'di yang
bla ma yi/ /phyag len zin pa'i lugs byas bris/ ! /thun mong min pa'i bir bsrung nyid/ /gnang skabs phyag len 'di bzhin te/ /zlum gtor lnga dang nyer spyod lnga/ /chu bzhi
dang

bcas stegs mdzes pa/ /cig la bshams nas slob dpon gyis/ /lam dus blangs shing birWa pa'i/ /bsrung ba thun mong min pa bsgom/ /de yi rjes su chos skyong sogs/ /rnams la gtor
'bul legs par bya/ /de nas slob ma rnams bsdus nas/ /maNDal gsol 'debs rgyun bshags dang / /sdom bzung rnams ni byed du bcug /de rjes bla ma birWa par/ /bsgom zhes brda
sbyar de'i sku gsung / /thugs dang lte ba brla rtsa yi/ /yi ge rnams la brten nas ni/ /slob ma byin rlabs de'i rjes su/ /slob ma rnal 'byor dbang phyug tu/ /bsgom du 'jug
rnams slob dpon gyis/ /gsal por brjod la de nas ni/ /gtang rag maNDal sogs byas la/ /bla mas rjes chog rnams bya'o/ /'di lta'i lag len rim pa 'di/ /bla ma'i phyag len de
zin pa'i/ /lugs su byas nas bris pa lags/ ! /brda don gsal ba'i gdams pa 'di/ /gnang skabs phyag len 'di lta ste/ /rab mdzes stegs la maNDal steng / /tshom bu dgu bkod de
drung du/ /chu bzhi sngon 'gro nyer spyod lnga/ /zlum gtor gsum dang bcas legs bsham/ /de nas bla mas lam dus dang / /maNDal bsgrub mchod tshul bzhin bya/gling dgar tshes
bcu la byed pa bzhin/ /de yi rjes su gtor ma rnams/ /chos skyong sogs la 'bul byas nas/ /slob ma bsdus te bla ma yis/ /man ngag gleng gzhi brjod rjes su/ /slob ma rnams
la maNDal dang / /gsol 'debs gang drin sogs byed 'jug /maNDal gsol 'debs byin rlabs kyi/ /sngon 'gro chos yin dngos gzhi la/ /slob mas

bla ma kye rdo rjer/ /mos pa mdzod ces slob dpon gyis/ /brda sbyar de nas slob ma yis/ bla mas /lag tu brda don gsal ba'i rdo/ /gtad la byin rlobs de bstan bya/ /de nas rgyas
bshad rtsa tshig gis/ /'bru gnyer sogs bya de'i rjes su/ /byin rlabs rjes kyi bya ba ni/ /slob ma rnams la gtang rag gi /maNDal 'bul sogs mdzod cig ces/ /brjod la byed
'jug de grub nas/ /slob ma slog la bla ma yis/ /rjes chog ma nor legs par bya/ /'di lta'i lag len rim pa 'di/ /bla ma'i phyag len brjed dogs bris/ ! /sgrub pa lung sbyin
gnang skabs phyag len ni/ /zlum gtor lnga gsum gang rigs nyer spyod lnga/ /chu bzhi dang bcas bsham la bla ma yis/ /lam dus blang zhing chos skyong la sogs la/ /gtor bsngo
de nas slob ma rnams bsdus la/ /bla mas bshad pa rgyas bsdus ci rigs bya/ /de nas slob mar chos yon maNDal dang / /gang drin sogs kyi gsol 'debs byed 'jug go /de rjes
rten 'brel sgrig dang bar chad bsal/ /gzhan don bya ba mthu dang ldan pa'i lung / /sbyin pa rnams la slob mas gsol 'debs dang / /bla mas brjod dgos rnams bya de'i rjes su/
/dam bzhag rnam pa bzhi po slob dpon gyis/ /bya 'o dus der phan yon dang nyes dmigs/ /gnyis ka dam bzhag la dgos bum chu de/ /sgrub pa'i lung sbyin 'di nyid gnang skabs
kyi/ /dus su sgrub pa'am yang na de gong du/ /sgrub pa'i chu lhag yod na des rung ngo / /dam bzhag grub nas bla mas de sba zhing / /dam du spel zhes sogs kyi bshad pa bya/
/de nas slob ma gtang rag

maNDal sogs/ /byed 'jug de rjes bla mas gtor 'bul sogs/ /bya 'o de bzhin lag len rim pa 'di/ /bla ma'i phyag len zin pa'i lugs byas bris/ ! /yang chos kyi rje dus gsum sgrib
med du gzigs pa de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid zab mo rnams mnos pa'i tshe/ /de dag gi sngon 'gror byang chub kyi sems rin po che
sbyong ba'i man ngag blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral du grags pa'i khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga'
snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/
na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems
dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug pa/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyal ba
mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ ra ston yon tan dpal bzang / mkhan chen bsam grub lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub

dpal ldan rdo rje/ mtshungs med ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ de ltar sngon 'gro'i chos su sa skya pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i blo sbyong
du grags pa'i zhen pa bzhi bral gyi gdams pa nyams khrid du bstsal nas/ ! /dngos gzhi bde mchog gi khrid rnams gnang ba'i thog mar grub chen nag po spyod pa'i lugs kyi
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bskyed rim gyi bshad pa shin tu zhib pa sems 'dzin gyi khrid dang bcas pa smin rgyas su thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/
sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ri khrod pa chen po/ lU hi pa/ dhA ri ka rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra/ nag po spyod pa'i rdo rje/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ anta
ra pa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ gcen 'jigs med grags/ gcung dus 'khor ba/ shes rab brtsegs pa/ blo gros grags pa/ dpal sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse
mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dkon mchog dpal/ bsod nams dpal/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
zha lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan rgyal po/ chos rje bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje btsun chos dbang phyug 'khor lo sdom pa sangs
rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag

sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'khor lo bde mchog lU hi pa'i lugs kyi bskyed rim gyi bshad pa dka' gnas mtha' chod dang bcas pa sems 'dzin
gyi dmigs khrid kyi gnad zab mos brgyan pa/ de'i rdzogs rim gyi khrid bsdu ba gsum sogs nyams khrid du mnos shing / ! /yang 'khor lo bde mchog dril bu pa lugs kyi lus
dkyil gyi bshad pa shin tu mtha' chod sems 'dzin gyi khrid zab mo dang bcas thob pa de dag gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang chen/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub
zhabs/ sha ba ri pa/ lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bur 'dzin pa/ nag po pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ phaM thing pa/ shes rab
brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ zhang ston/ brag phug pa/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje buddha'i mtshan can/ dpal ldan rgyal po/ bzang po dpal ba/ rje nam dbang ba/ mkhan chen chos dbang ba/ mus
chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang gong gi brgyud pa de nyid las 'ongs pa'i dpyid dang thig le zhal sbyor

gyi man ngag zab mo yang thos shing / lU hi pa'i sgrub thabs dpal mngon par rtogs pa/ lo chen gyi 'gyur la 'gos dang / mar dos bcos pa/ de'i 'grel pa rngog gi 'gyur/ phyi rol
mchod pa'i cho ga dang / lag mchod gnyis/ dpyal chos bzang gi 'gyur/ gtor ma'i cho ga rngog 'gyur/ phyi ma bzhi pra dznyA rakShi tas mdzad pa ste lU hi pa'i smad lngar
grags pa thos/ slob dpon nag po spyod pas mdzad pa'i 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs dang / dkyil chog lo chen gyi 'gyur la 'gos kyis bcos pa/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga rig pa
gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ dpyid kyi thig le mar do'i 'gyur/ gsang ba de kho na nyid gsal ba 'gos 'gyur la mar dos bcos pa/ o la pa ti grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur te/ bskyed rim
skor gsum/ rdzogs rim skor gsum dang bcas pa'i gzhung drug ka thos/gzhung drug 'di la/ sa paN gyis 'gyur bcos mchan bcas mdzad/ de'i mjug tu/ rin chen bzang pos dag par
bsgyur ba las/ /mar pa do pas ma dag pa yang byas/ /de la kho bos jo bo'i lugs bzhin du/ /dag par bcos te 'gyur mchan dag kyang bgyis/ /zhes 'byung zhing / sngon gyi dus
su sa chen gyi nag 'bum yig sna bco lnga spel nas/ sa gzhung spyi don so sor bkral/ gzhung don mchan bu'i 'bru re re nas bsnan pa'i zhib bshad gnang ba'i rgyun bzang po
byung ba yin gsungs/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs mal 'gyur/ dkyil mchog bandhe chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rdzogs rim rim pa lnga pa blo ldan shes
rab kyi 'gyur te dril bu skor gsum du grags pa ste/ lU nag dril gsum gyi gzhung de rnams rje btsun sa skya pa gong ma'i mchan bu dang bcas pa thos

so/ /gzhan yang nyung ngu mtshams sbyor/ su ma ti kirtis mdzad pa grags mchog shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rgyun bshags bhu ri pas mdzad pa dang / bod gzhung la/ rje sa skya pa chen
pos mdzad pa'i rtsa rgyud kyi le 'grel dang / dka' 'grel gnyis/ man ngag nag 'bum du grags pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa'i lo rgyus/ gzhung drug
spyi'i rnam gzhag dkyil chog sgrub thabs/ sbyin sreg gsang ba de kho na nyid gsal ba/ o la pa ti/ dpyid thig rnams kyi sa bcad re re/ ras bris la brten pa'i dkyil chog
mngon rtogs kyi TIkka/ sbyin sreg gi TIkka/ de'i lag len/ ro sreg gsang ba'i de kho na nyid gsal ba'i Tikka/ de'i tshig don bsdus pa'i go 'byed o la pa'i rnam bshad/ dpyid
thig gi Tikka ste chos kyi rnam grangs bcu bdun yod pa dang / gnyan gyi mdzad pa'i lU hi pa'i 'bru 'bum/ dril bu pa'i dbang gi bya ba rje btsun rtse mos mdzad pa/ rje btsun
gyis mdzad pa'i he ru ka'i byung tshul/ lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs kyi don 'grel chen mo/ nag po dkyil chog gi sa bcad 'khrugs can dang 'khrugs med gnyis/ nag po pa'i sgrub
thabs dang / sbyin sreg gi sa bcad/ nag po dkyil chog gi 'grel pa bshad sbyar du grags pa/ dkyil mchog lag tu blang ba'i rim pa/ dril bu pa'i sgrub thabs/ tshes bcu'i
mchod pa bya tshul/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus dkar shAkya grags dang / shar pa rdo rje 'od zer gyis mdzad pa/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i bde mchog bla ma mchod
pa'i chog chos dang bsod nams

rab rgyas/ mus chen sems dpa' chen pos mdzad pa'i lU nag dril gsum rim pa bzhin nyams su blang tshul/ dkyil 'khor rgyal mchog gi ngag 'don/ lU nag dril gsum gyi bum bskyed/
bde gshegs sa bzung / kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa'i bde mchog chos 'byung / bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad/ lU nag gnyis kyi mngon rtogs/ bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa/ kha
che rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa la 'phags pa rin po ches bcos shing dag par mdzad pa dang / paN chen nyi zla seng ges mdzad pa'i bde mchog nag po lugs kyi bskyed rim gyi
rnam bshad/ rje bzang po dpal bas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lU nag dril gsum gyi bskyed rims kyi rnam bshad chen mo rnams dang / rje de nyid kyi mdzad pa'i dpyid dang thig le
zhal sbyor gyi rdzogs rims kyi khrid yig rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ ! /rdzogs rim zab mo nag po rim bzhir grags pa'i khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag
na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ri/ lU hi pa/ dhA ri ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra pa/ nag po spyod pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/
ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ klog kya ba/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje pa/ 'phags pa/ zhang
dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ blo brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ kun mkhyen
bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin

dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje man 'dra/ yang
na ngor chen/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa man gong dang 'dra/ rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa'i rim bzhi lam slong mchan bu dang bcas
pa'i lung bshad zhib mo dang / rje kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig gi lung yang thos so/ /yang 'khor lo bde mchog rdzogs rim dril bu rim lngar grags pa'i khrid sngon
'gro'i byin rlabs dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bar ba 'dzin pa/ nag po spyod
pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ phaM mthing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paN chen/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ bo dong brtson rdor ba/ khro phu bsod seng / yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge mnyan mkhar ba bkras bzang / khyung
lhas gzhon nu'i mtshan can/ shar chen ye rgyal ba/ ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge de gnyis kas rjes
su bzung

ba yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /khrid yig rje btsun chen po dang / chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs bla ma rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa rnams
thos shing / dmigs pa'i gnad rnams mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub kyi khrid yig nang bzhin gnang ngo / ! /yang rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod kyi bskyed
rim rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i rdzogs rim zab mo rtsa dbu ma kha 'byed pa'i man ngag yum la sbyar ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo
rje rnal 'byor ma/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ DeM ki pa/ a nanda ra pa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal gyo lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ bsod
rtse/ grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa/ blo gros brtan pa/ dpal tshul ba/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon
rgyal/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / paN chen
grags rgyal/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo

'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i rjes su/ zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mnga' ris pa dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje
bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje chos dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /de rnams kyi nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang
/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen nA ro pa man gong bzhin no/ /nA ro pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gong ma'i mchan dang bcas pa/ sgrub thabs rnal 'byor bcu gcig ma/ phyi mchod
mdor bsdus/ mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ byin rlabs kyi cho ga tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ tshogs 'khor/ sbyin sreg mar me'i sbyin sreg pra se na dbab pa/ gnod sbyin mo bsgrub
pa'i man ngag sogs dang / sman chen po'i bcud len rnams rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ bdag 'jug tshogs 'khor/
sbyin sreg rnams dang / sgrub thabs dang / bstod pa bla ma rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i mkha'
spyod sgo 'byed/ rje bzang po dpal ba dang / rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi rnam bshad kyi lung dmigs pa'i zab gnad du ma dang bcas pa thos shing / yang nA
ro mkha' spyod kyi zab chos kyi nying khu mkha' spyod bsgrub pa'i nye lam gyi gtso bo thun mong ma yin pa'i bsam mi khyab kyi man ngag zab mo sa skya pa'i gser chos kyi
yang snying de nyid thob pa'i

brgyud pa ni gong dang 'dra ba la/ ! /yang zab mo'i yang rtse mkha' spyod bsgrub pa'i 'pho ba chig brgyud ma thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/
paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang / rje dpal ldan rgyal po/ chos rje bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang
phyug rje chos dbang pa/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /de thams cad kyi rgyab rten du/ 'khor lo bde
mchog gi rtsa rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa/rtsa rgyud ma la mchan/ rtse mos mchan sna bsrings pa/ Tikka mu tig phreng ba'i steng nas stsal cing 'di dag dang gong gi
nag 'bum/ rim bzhi lam slong rnams kyi mchan rtse mo'i 'di yin zhing / mu tig phreng ba'i mi gsal ba rnams nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyi Tikka rje btsun gyi gsung bgros ma
dang / sa paN gyi dngos slob zhang bya rung ba'i bde mchog gi bshad mtshams gnyis las kha skong byed lugs 'di ltar yin dang / lhag par rtsa rgyud nag po'i skor/ zhes grags
pa dang mthun par gzhung drug gi bshad 'grel rang du sbyor na 'di ltar byed tshul rnams kyi rnam gzhag zhib tu gsungs pa thos so/ /paNDi ta su ma ti kirti dang / lo tsA
ba mal gyo blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po'i sa bcad dang / TIkka mu tig phreng ba'i steng nas dang / de'i bshad rgyud rnal 'byor ma kun spyod/ mal
'gyur rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i sa bcad 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i steng nas lung bshad kyi bka' drin mtha' chod pa stsal cing / de'i dus rje'i gsung las/ 'di'i rtsa rgyud
kyi le'us skabs so so nas bstan pa'i sngags btu'i byin rlabs rnams ni kho bos ma thos

pas/ da lta de 'dra'i rgyun thob pa chos rje sman mgur ba yin te/ khong gis paN chen nam dbang pa nas brgyud pa'i rgyun zhe dgon pa rje chos rgyal mtshan la zhus nas deng sang
khong la bzhugs nges yin pas/ khyed sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i khur bzhes nas byin rlabs de dag kyang gsan par mdzad nas rgyun ma chad pa spel dgos so zhes gsungs byung
ba bdag gis snying la bcangs nas/ dus phyis chos rje sman mgur ba las brgyud pa/ lo nas spyan snga rin chen gsan pa de nyid bdag cag gis mnos pa'i tshul ni 'og tu 'byung
ngo / /de ltar bde mchog gi rtsa bshad kyi rgyud de dag gi bshad bka' thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ri/ lU hi pa/
dha ri ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra pa/ nag po spyod pa'i rdo rje/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/
klog kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal gyo blo gros grags/ dpal sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun sku mched/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod
nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ rje btsun legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ 'khor lo sdom pa sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa

ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / rje sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje dkon mchog
lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na rje sems dpa' chen po'i rjes su/ zha lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / rje dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje bzang po dpal ba/ paN chen nam dbang / rje chos
dbang phyug rje 'khor lo sdom pa man 'dra/ ! /'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i khrid 'chad dus kyi phyag len ni/ slob dpon drung du zlum gtor gcig /chab bran nas bzhag slob
ma bsdud/ /'du dus bla mas bcom ldan 'das/ /rdo rje sems dpa' he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes brjod de nas dpon slob thams cad kyis/ /yig brgya mang brjod de'i rjes
su/ /stobs bzhi tshang ba'i bshags pa bya/ /rdo rje sems dpa' rang la bstim/ /de nas phur bu gdab pa dang / /bsrung 'khor bsgom pa rnams de ni/ /bde mchog nag po pa'i lugs
kyi/ /sgrub thabs ji bzhin dpon slob kun/ /gyis mdzad de rnams grub rjes su/ /khro bo 'bar ba'i tshogs rnams kyi/ /sogs dang gzhan yang smon lam dang / /bkra shis tshigs
bcad 'ga' re rnams/ /dpon slob kun gyis mdzad rjes su/ /bla mas gong bsham gtor ma de/ /sngags dang phyag rgyas byin brlabs la/ /gtor mgron 'bar ba'i phyag rgya dang /
/pheM zhes bya bas spyan drangs nas/ /lag pa rdo rje thal mo kha/ /gyen du phye la gtor ma nyid/ /sngags kyis a khaM sogs kyis/ phul la phyi mchod dang / /nang mchod byas
la lha tshogs

rnams/ /zhes nas 'dod pa kun 'grub shog /ces pa'i bar bya de grub nas/ /gtor mgron gshegs gsol de nas ni/ /sems bskyed gsal btab sogs byas la/ /khrid dang lung gi thun byed
do/ /bla mas gtor 'bul mdzad skabs su/ /slob ma rnams kyis maNDal 'bul/ /de lta'i lag len gsal ba 'di/ /bde mchog nag po'i khrid chen nyid/ /gnang dus bla ma'i phyag len
de/ /brjed de 'jigs nas 'di bris so/ /rim bzhi gnang skabs phyag len ni/ /gong du bshad pa de dang 'dra/ ! /lU hi lugs kyi bde mchog gi /khrid gnang dus kyi phyag len ni/
/gzhan rnams nag po pa bzhin las/ /srung 'khor lU hi pa rang gi /sgrub thabs bzhin du bsgom pa yin/ ! /dril bu lugs kyi bskyed rdzogs kyi/ /khrid 'chad dus kyi phyag len
ni/ /gzhan rnams nag po pa dang 'dra/ /srung 'khor lU hi lugs bzhin mdzad/ /de lta'i lag len rim de dag /bla ma'i phyag len zin pa yis/ /lugs byas don gnyis bsgrub phyir
bris/ ! /dpyid thig skabs kyi ma ning gi /yi ge bzhi ni r-i r-i dang / /l-i l-i la zer yin no zhes/ /bdag la bka' drin mnyam med pa'i/ /rje btsun mus pa chen pos gsungs/
/gsung de brjed dogs 'dir bris lags/ ! /yang chos kyi rje byang chub kyi sems rdo rje de nyid kyi drung du/ rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i brjod don thams cad
gcig tu 'dus pa'i rim lnga'i khrid zab mo 'gos lugs su grags pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang dang / kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig zung 'jug gsal

sgron dang / mang mkhar ba blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i gsung la zin bris mdzad pa sogs kyi steng nas sa bcad dang / bsgom pa'i dmigs pa rgyas bsdus
ji ltar yod pa kun cha tshang ba so sor go don mtha' chod bla ma'i gsung bgros kyis brgyan pa smin rgyas nyams khrid du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / gsang
ba'i bdag po/ rgyal po indra bhu ti/ klu'i rnal 'byor ma/ bi su kalpa/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa/ slob pa'i
rdo rje/ nag po pa/ sa 'dres pa/ brtson 'grus bzang po/ 'gos lo tsA ba/ mang ra ba/ rdog ye shes seng ge nyi ma seng ge nyi ma lcam/ thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ gser
sding pa gzhon nu 'od/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rje rdo rje
'chang / rje sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge paN chen kong ston/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje sangs rin/ de gnyis la bdag chen ngag dbang grags pa/
'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ chos kyi rje byang chub kyi sems rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang
na bu ston/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na bu ston/ lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/
grub chen buddha shrI/ rje rdo rje 'chang man

gong dang 'dra/ rje rdo rje 'chang dang / kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig zung 'jug gsal ba yang thos so/ ! /dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs kyi bskyed rim gyi bshad
pa rgya gzhung rnams dang / paN chen gung ru sogs kyis mdzad pa'i rnam bshad mang po'i steng nas/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi sgrub thabs dngos grub rgya mtsho dang sbyar ba shin
tu rgyas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje chos/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ rgya gar lho phyogs kyi o Di sha'i rgyal po bi su kalpa/ bram ze sgra gcan
'dzin bzang po/ rgyal pas lung bstan dge slong dpal ldan/ de la slob ma mchog bzhi ste/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ 'phags pa lha/ klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa/ de bzhis
slob pa'i rdo rje la/ des nag po spyod pa la/ des dri med blo gros/ sa 'dres pa chen po/ des paN chen birWa bha dra/ de wa a ka ra tsaNDa/ ratna a ka ra shanti/ dpal sbas/
mar me mdzad de lnga las/ rje rin po che 'gos kyis shan ti pa dang / dpal sbas gnyis ma gtogs/ sa 'dres pa'i slob ma gsum/ rgya gar shar phyogs na rgyal po sprin gyi shugs
can/ rdo rje gdan gyi nag po pa/ kha che khri brtan gyi tsaNDa ha ri/ bal po rdzong gi nA ga ko Ti/ bal po mthil gyi tsa hung / sa ra ha pa rnams la zhus pa las/ 'di
paNDi ta mngon shes can/ btsun mo can/ nag po pa gsum gyi lugs gtso che'o/ /rje 'gos la slob ma rgyud kyi ka ba tshugs pa bzhi/ man ngag gi gdung theg pa brgyad/ las tshogs
dang 'phrin las la mkhas pa lcam dang dral ma

gshibs pa ltar dpag tu med pa yod pa las/ 'dir 'jad pa so rong gis mar ston seng rgyal/ des rngog ye shes seng ge des sras po nyi ma seng ge des klan btsad tsha/ des rdog mu
na'i sras po arYa de wa/ de la ltag pa rin chen grags dang / gtsang smra seng / mi nyag rdo rje grags rnams kyis gsan/ yang rdog nyi ma seng ge la/ gzhu'i phug ka ba/ phug
ston shes rab grags kyis gsan/ de la'ang mi nyag rdo rje grags kyis gsan/ yang klan btsad tsha nyi ma lcam la/ rgya mkhar thang spe ba'i mkhan po 'phags pa skyabs kyis
gsan/ de la gser sding pa gzhon nu 'od kyis gsan/ de la skyi mkhar 'jug bre kha'i ltag pa rin chen grags kyis gsan/ de la bla ma chos sku bas gsan/ yang rong lha sdeng
gi gtsang smra seng dang / cha dkar mon mo brag gi mi nyag rdo rje grags gnyis la lce ston mdo sde seng ges gsan/ de la bla ma chos sku ba/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen
bu ston rin chen grub/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen
bsod nams seng ge de la paN chen nyi zla seng ge kong ston dbang phyug grub pa/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen dang bzhi las/ rje sangs
rin pa'i drung du 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtshos gsan/ de las bdag cag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa buddha'i mtshan can/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /

'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i mdor byas lo chen gyi 'gyur/ de nyid rtsa rgyud kyi lugs dang sbyar ba mdo dang bsre ba lo chen gyi 'gyur/ mdor byas kyi skabs skabs su
mi gsal ba gsal byed kyi kha skong klu byang gis mdzad pa'i rnam gzhag rim pa lo chen gyi 'gyur/ klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog dang / rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed
pa'i rgyu dbang rdul tshon du bskur tshul klu byang gis mdzad pa'i cho ga nyi shu pa/ pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ rdzogs rim 'phags pas mdzad pa'i rim lnga lo chen
gyi 'gyur/ 'di'i rim pa gnyis pa'i/ 'khor ba'i gzeb las rnam grol/ zhes pa yan chad kyi sems dben bsgom pa'i 'bras bu bstan pa yar bcad 'phags pa'i gsung yin la/ de las
'phros pa'i gsung bgros mang po byung ma byung ba shAkya bshes gnyen gyis chad dogs nas 'phags pa'i gsung rab la mthud nas bris pa ni/ shes rab ngo bo 'di nyid ni/ zhes pa
man chad do/ /de rnams kyi rim pa lnga rgyas par bstan pa'i don bsdoms pas nyams myong skye ba/ ngo sprod pa arYa de bas mdzad pa'i spyod bsdus sgron me lo chen gyi 'gyur
las 'gos kyis bcos pa/ paNDi ta mngon shes can gyi gdams pa/ paNDi ta btsun mo can gyi gdams pa/ nag po dam tshig gi rdo rje'i gdams pa ste 'gos kyi shog ril gsum du grags
pa/ mngon shes can gyi bskyed rim gyi khrid/ nyi ma lcam gyi zin bris/ gser lding pas mdzad pa'i skor la/ rim lnga don bzhi ma/ rim lnga don lnga ma/ dmar khrid 'khor
lo can/ cig char ba'i man ngag 'khor lo med pa

yi ge tshan gnyis/ sems dpa' sum brtsegs/ mnyam bzhag sgyu ma'i rnal 'byor/ rmi lam sgyu ma'i man ngag bar do sgyu ma'i gdams pa/ le lo can 'chi khar sangs rgya ba 'pho ba'i
gdams ngag btsan thabs kyi 'pho ba/ rnam shes grong du 'jug pa'i man ngag srog rtsol la brten nas gtum mo bsgom pa lam rim pa lnga dang sbyar ba/ 'khor lo 'jug ldog la
brten nas ma rig pa rtsad nas bcad pa'i man ngag chags can 'og sgo la brten nas bde ba lam du blangs pa'i man ngag bsre ba drug gi man ngag 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi bzhugs
tshul bstan pa/ rdo rje sems dpa'i gsang lam/ sdig po che btsan thabs su sangs rgyas pa'i man ngag mgrin par rmi lam la brten nas sgyu ma btsan thabs su bzung ba'i man
ngag snying khar mi shigs pa'i thig le la brten nas ma rig pa rtsad nas bcad pa'i man ngag gsang ba thugs rgyud kyi rim pa lnga'i man ngag rim lnga'i dbang gong ma'i man
ngag pha rgyud yang snying / spyir rgyud thams cad dang / bye brag tu ma rgyud he badzra gyi gdams pa'i bcud bsdus te 'di rnams gser sding pas mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags
'od kyis mdzad pa'i ngo sprod/ yu mo khugs/ bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i rim lnga'i smar khrid yid bzhin nor bu'i za ma tog ces bya ba rim lnga mar lugs gtso che ba'i khrid yig
gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad paN chen nyi zla seng ges mdzad pa/ de thams cad kyi rgyab rten du/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/ rgyud phyi
ma dang bcas pa'i le'u bco brgyad pa/ lo chen gyi

'gyur/ de'i 'grel chen sgron ma gsal ba dpal ldan zla ba grags pas mdzad pa lo chen gyi 'gyur/ kun mkhyen bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i sgron gsal gyi 'grel bshad mtha' drug rab
gsal/ 'chad thabs kyi man ngag gsang ba'i sgo 'byed rnams kyi lung bshad zhib tu thob pa'i/ sgrub thabs mdo byas mdo bsre sogs rgya gzhung phal cher dang / 'gos kyi shog
ril gsum sogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ gong gi rim lnga 'gos lugs kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra la/ bu ston gyi khrid yig dang mthun pa gtso che ba'i rim lnga mar lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / byang sems blo gros rin chen/ klu sgrub/ ma taM ki pa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA/ dbang gi rdo rje/ rje gad pa/ bya khang pa bsod rin/ mi nyag
thur ba la tshul khrims skyabs/ rgya mkhar thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ grub thob gser lding pa gzhon nu 'od/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin
chen/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ bla ma dam pa buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge paN chen kong po
dbang phyug grub pa/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje sangs rin/ de gnyis ka la bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ chos kyi rje byang chub
kyi sems rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /gser sding pa'i man ngag yig skor phal che ba sogs de dag gi brgyud
pa lugs

gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ bi su kalpa/ sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ zla ba grags pa/ slob pa'i rdo rje/ nag po spyod pa/ dri med blo gros/ ye shes
snying po/ mar pa lo tsA man sngar dang 'dra ba las/ de nas bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rjes su/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che byang chub rgyal mtshan/
sku zhang rin chen bkra shis/ sku zhang sangs rgyas dpal 'byor/ dus zhabs pa shAkya dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs chos kyi grags pa/ kun spangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen
padma'i mtshan can/ rje ngag dbang pa/ sprul sku chos kyi ljon shing / rje dge 'dun dpal bzang / mkhas grub rin chen rgya mtsho/ bikSha ku sa li pa/ des bdag sa skya pa
ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud/ 'grel chen sgron gsal dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang phyag na rdo rje/ bram ze chen po
sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ arYa de wa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA/ tshur dbang nge / 'khon gad pa kirti/ mgar ston jo sras/ ang phug ri ston/ seng ge rdzong pa/ khung ston
zhig po/ mkhan po tshul snying / chos sding mkhan po rdo rje snying po/ chos sding pa 'og ma/ shrI zur phug pa dar ma bzang po/ mkhan po bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ ma ti
paNTi ta/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ ri khrod pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ chos rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ chos rje dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha mchog seng ge
chos rje dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shar khang pa shes rab

rgyal mtshan/ rje thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje dpal ldan don grub/ rje ga gdan buddha/ bikShu paNDi pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
/paN chen nyi zla seng ge'i rnam bshad kyi lung gi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rje nyi zla seng ge rje dkon mchog dpal bzang / grub chen nam mkha' shes rab/ rje bsod nams rtse
mo/ rje rin chen chos 'phel/ chos rje bsod nams sangs rgyas/ bikShu ku sa li pa/ des bdag sa skya pa la'o/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du rdo rje nag po chen
po gur gyi mgon po 'khor dang bcas pa mkha' 'gro sbrags sgrub kyi tshul du bsgrub pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag nang khrid du grags pa 'jam sgrub rtsub sgrub sogs
zab mo'i man ngag rnams nyams khrid du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/
brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon
tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/
bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ bdag chen nam mkha' tshe brtan/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/
rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal

mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i nang sgrub kyi khrid yig 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyis mdzad
pa'i khrid yig gnyis/ 'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang bya tshul/ mgon po gzi brjid bskyed pa'i man ngag rmi lam ngan pa dang mtshan ma ngan pa bzlog pa'i man ngag srung ba brag
rdzong ma'i zhal shes kyi snyan brgyud zab mo rnams ma lus pa thob cing / mgon po khro bcu'i srung 'khor dkar shAkya grags kyis mdzad pa dang / kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad
pa gnyis kyi lung yang thos so/ /gnyan mgon chen po zhal bzhi pa'i tshe sgrub zab mo srung 'khor gur bdun mar grags pa'i man ngag gi khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna rakShi ta/
kharsa pa Ni/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ gnam kha 'ub pa/ de gnyis ka la sa skya pa chen pos gsan/ rje btsun rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/
'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal ba/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ gling dpon
chen chos sku 'od zer/ rje byams pa shes

rab bzang po/ chos kyi rje bsam gtan rin chen/ rje 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ /'di'i man ngag gi yi ge rnying ma'i lung yang thos/ ! /yang snga ma de las kyang ches zab pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i tshe sgrub zab mo srung 'khor
gur bdun dang bcas pa'i man ngag gi khrid/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang bas mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas zhal shes kyi zab gnad du mas brgyan pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna rakShi
ta/ kharsa pa ni/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ gnam kha 'ub pa/ de gnyis ka las sa skya pa chen pos gsan/ rje btsun rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje
sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo ring pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje tshul khrims mtshan can/ rje rin chen chos
'phel/ rje rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /tshe sgrub bsrung bzlog dang bcas pa'i yig cha rje nam mkha'
dpal bzang pa'i

lung yang thos// ! //yang chos rje rnam par snang mdzad de nyid kyi drung du/ sbyong rgyud nas bshad pa'i ngan song sbyong ba kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sarba dznyA buddha/kun mkhyen sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/phyag na rdo rje/ rA dza pra ka sha tsandra/rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ pra bhu ti pA mi ta/rab
'byor bskyangs/ a nanda garbha/kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA pA li ta/shes rab bskyangs/ shanti garbha/zhi ba snying po/ shu bhi ni mitta mi tra/dge mtshan bshes gnyen/
su kha badzra/bde ba'i rdo rje/ shra dha ka ra warma/dad byed go cha/ paNDi ba ratna bha dra/lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ she lo pa ti/brag steng pa/ paNDi ba ma ti
kirti/mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ ma hA bhu mi/sa chen/ bhuTTa ra ka kIrti dhwa dza/rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bhu mi paNDu paNDi ta/sa skya paNDi ta/ a nanda
shrI/tshogs bsgom kun dga' dpal/ pu Nya sdyi ra/nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ A nanda ma ti/ti shrI kun dga' blo gros/ sanggu ru puNya dhwa dza/bla dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ ma ti sdyi ra/blo gros brtan pa/ gu ru shrI wanni la/bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ dharma swa mi dznyA na dhwa dza/chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ badzra dha ra
A nanda bha dra/rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mahA satwa ratna dhwa dza/sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bhaTTa ka ra budha ratna/rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen/ bhaTTa ra ka ga ga na shwa ra/rje nam mkha' dbang phyug dharmA swa mi dharmA shwa ra/chos kyi rje chos dbang phyug bai ro tsa na buddha dhwa dza/rnam par snang mdzad
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bhu mi paNDa ka wa gindra A nanda la'o/sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' la'o/ ! yang kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa'/
dpe med bsrung ba/ shanti pa/ 'jigs med

'byung gnas sbas pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ bikSha ta de wa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ bi bhu ta tsaNDa/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba/ zhang ston dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ ri khrod
pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ ! /chag lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan
'das kun rig slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ shAnti pa/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ a bhya ka ra/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ niska la~M ka rdo rje gdan pa chung
ba/ ra wentra/ chag lo tsA ba chos kyi dpal/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge paNDi ta rdor she/ zhang dkon mchog dpal man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na g.yag sde lo tsA
ba nas/ lo mchog bag ston/ tshul rgyal/ bla ma dpal tshul/ shar chen/ ngor chen man 'dra'o/ ! /smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag
na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ de'i slob ma mchog lnga ni/ pad dkar ye shes/ ye shes rdo rje/ rgyal po sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ nyi ma'i snying po/ rgyal rigs pa
sa ra ha pa'o/ /de gnyis ka'i slob ma kun dga' snying po/ ta thA ga ta badzra/ shaddha ka ra warma/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ sum ston ye
shes 'bar/ gnyan ston tshul khrims 'bar/ thod pa dben rtsa grags/ thod pa 'od zer/ slob dpon chos mgon/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ paNDi ta rdo rje shes
rab/ bla ma 'phags

rgyal/ bla ma rin chen bzang po/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /kun rig gi cho ga'i rnam bshad chen
mo zin bris ma dpag bsam ljon pa'i steng nas cho ga'i bshad pa shin tu rgyas pa mtha' chod du ma dang bcas pa/ phyag rgya rnams kyi phyag len brda sprod dang bcas zhib
tu bstsal cing / rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i gzhan phan skor gsum dang / rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i bsnyen rgyas/ rdul tshon kha skong / gzhan phan mtha' yas/ cha gsum
gtor ma'i yig cha rnams dang / rnam bshad dpag bsam ljon pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ /sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ bram ze dzi na mi tra/ swasti pha la/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ pradznyA wa li ta/shes rab bskyangs/ ye shes rdo rje pra hi ta/rab
tu phan pa/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ kha che dharmA phA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gnyal pa nyi shes/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ gshen rdo rje
seng ge rgya gsar pa/ 'bro dzi ti pa/ snye mdo pa bsod nams dpal/ gnyal pa chos grags/ bya rin chen 'od/ 'dzin pa blo chen/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul
rgyal ba/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ byang sems kha char ba/ byang sems blo rin pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen dkon mchog rin chen/ 'jam
dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rnam par snang mdzad sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/

des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'dzin pa blo chen/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma bsod dbang / kun mkhyen seng ge 'bum/ paN chen ma ti/ sa bzang
'phags pa/ ngor chen man gong dang 'dra'o/ /dkyil 'khor phyi ma bcu gcig gi bdag mdun sgrub tshul/ dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len/ de'i sta gon
gyi zur 'debs dang bcas pa rje sangs rin gyis mdzad pa thos so/ ! /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud chen po rin chen mchog gi 'gyur/ sa bcad mchan bu spyi don
rnams rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa'i Tikka dang bcas pa'i steng nas bshad bka' lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje sa chen yan chad
kun rig sa lugs kyi dbang dang 'dra/ de nas gnyag ston dbang rgyal/ rje btsun chen po/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang ston chos rje/ na bza' brag phug pa/
blo gros brtan pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams
seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rnam par snang mdzad sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /rje btsun dang kun mkhyen gyi gzhan phan skor rnams dang / sbyong rgyud rkyang pa'i lung sogs ni slar yang rje btsun de nyid

kyi dngos kyi slob ma rnams las kyang yang yang thos so/ ! /yang thugs rje chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan de nyid kyi drung du/ smar khrid tshem bu lugs thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen tshem bu pa/ spyi bo lhas pa/ brag dmar ba/ dgon gsar ba/ kun spang rje/ ra ga brag pa/ rin chen dpal/ bla ma dam
pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan legs pa/ ratna shrI/ nam mkha'i mtshan can/ phun tshogs rdo rje/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ gnyan lo chen po/ thar rtse nas sangs rgyas seng
ge thugs rje chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs tshogs gnyis mthar phyin ma dang / khrid yig
rje sangs rgyas seng ges mdzad pa rnams thos so/ ! /yang chos kyi rje jo bo rin po che sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi drung du/ theg pa chen po'i blo sbyong don bdun mar
grags pa'i khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa chen po/ mi pham mgon/ 'phags pa thogs med/ rgyal sras dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa rnam grol sde/ gu
na mi tra/ slob dpon seng ge bzang po/ gang pa spel/ ku sa li pa/ ku sa li gnyis pa/ gser gling pa/ mar me mdzad/ 'brom ston pa/ pu to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan
grags/ 'chad ka ba ye shes rdo rje/ se ston 'od zer gzhon nu/yar klung jo bo'i chos 'byung na chos kyi rgyal mtshan zer bar snang / kha cig dar ma shes rab zer/ lha ston
'od zer bla ma/jo bo'i chos 'byung na byang chub rin chen

zer/ lha sding pa byang chub 'bum/ lha sding dbon po/ yon tan dpal/ bde ba dpal/ ka bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med bzang po
dpal/ 'gro mgon tshul khrims dpal/ mkhan chen gzhon nu rgyal mchog mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ paN chen nam mkha'
dbang phyug chos kyi rje dpal 'byor rin chen/ jo bo chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na thub dbang / byams
pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ blo brtan/ ku sa li che chung / gser gling pa/ mar me mdzad/ dpal 'brom ston/ glang thang pa/ pu to ba/ sha ra ba/ 'chad ka ba/ se ston spyil
bu/ lha ston spyil bu ba man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas bsgom pa/ seng ge skyabs/ byams gling pa/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub/ kun dga' tshul khrims/ gangs
pa grags pa dpal/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rje kun dga' bzang po/ rje sems dpa' chen po man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na rgyal sras thogs
med pa/ lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/ de gnyis ka la lo tsA ba skyabs mchog bzang po/ de nas ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa man chad sngar dang 'dra/ rgyal sras chos
rje pa'i khrid yig 'gro mgon dpal ldan ye shes kyis mdzad pa'i zin bris/ de'i sngon 'gro dang dngos gzhi'i kha skong mus chen sems dpa'

chen pos mdzad pa dang bcas pa thos so/ ! /rten 'brel snying po'i khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa chen po/ spyan ras gzigs/ byams pa mgon po/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/
a ti sha 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ pu to ba rin chen gsal/ rgya ston lcags ri ba/ rnal 'byor ba chos kyi g.yung drung / snyi phu ba sgyer sgom zhig po/ rgya
sgom ri ba/ bo dong rin po che/ nyan chen pa bsod nams brtan pa/ rin po che shes rab 'bum pa/ rgyal sras thogs med/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ sems dpa' chen po dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug man blo sbyong don bdun dang 'dra/ yang na nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ mus chen rgyal mtshan/
mus pa rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ rje sems dpa' chen po man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na nyan chen pa/ mus pasher bum pa/ mus palo tsA ba nyi ma
rin chen/ nam mkha'i rnal 'byor man 'dra/ yang na nyan chen pa/ mkhan chen byang chub sems dpa'/ mus pa'bro bsgom nam mkha' dpal/ nam mkha'i rnal 'byor man 'dra ba las/ khrid
yig chen mo mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang gis mdzad pa yang thos so/ ! /skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ lo chen byams
pa'i dpal/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ lho brag pamkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen grags pa bshes gnyen/ chos lung pa bsod nams rin chen/ chos rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog
mus chen sems dpa' chen

po/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug man rten 'brel snying po dang 'dra la/ yang na mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen ka bzhi pa grags pa gzhon
nu/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ byang sems tshul khrims dpal/ rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog man 'dra/ khrid yig rgyal sras thogs med pas mdzad pa
dang bcas pa thos so/ ! /yang theg pa chen po blo sbyong gi man ngag rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i pod chung gi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ jo bo rjes rgyal
srid spangs te thar pa bsgrubs pa'i rnam thar/ jo bo dang gser gling pa mjal ba'i lo rgyus/ blo sbyong don bdun ma'i gzhung mchan yod med gnyis/ de'i 'grel pa mtshon
cha 'khor lo rma bya dug 'joms/ gyer bsgom rdo rje glu/ byams pa'i rnal 'byor pa'i blo sbyong / blo sbyong sems dpa'i rim pa/ rang rgyud ngan pa dma' dbab pa/ zas dge ba'i
stobs bskyed pa/ gser gling pas jo bo la mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i ched du gnang ba/ nyon mongs lam du blangs pa'i man ngag bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ sdig sbyong / theg chen 'khon
sbyong / rnal 'byor ma gnyis kyis jo bo la gnang ba'i blo sbyong / ku sa li'i tshogs bsog skyid sdug lam khyer/ sum pa lo tsA ba'i snyan brgyud/ kun tu bzang po'i blo
sbyong / blo sbyong thun brgyad ma la/ zas la brten pa/ dbugs la brten pa/ rigs drug gi sdug bsngal dang du blang ba/ sha khrag la brten pa/ gtor ma la brten pa/ 'byung
ba la brten pa/ lus yid

bzhin nor bur bsgyur ba/ 'chi kha ma'i blo sbyong ste brgyad dang / gegs sel blo sbyong / ma 'ongs pa'i 'gal rkyen spong ba/ jo bo'i don bdun ma/ mchim gyi blo sbyong / birWa
pa'i blo sbyong / rnam dag gtsug nor la gnang ba'i tshig rkang brgyad ma lo rgyus dang bcas pa/ de'i 'grel pa/ mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i blo sbyong gi nyams len/ theg chen
blo sbyong don bdun ma/ ratna gu ru'i tshogs chos/ yang dgon pa'i blo sbyong / rten 'brel snying po'i khrid yig rnams kyi lung dang / blo sbyong thams cad kyi lus lta bu
don bdun mas gtso bor byas/ gzhan rnams so so nas dmigs par dril nas nyams su len tshul dang bcas pa zhib tu thob pa las/ jo bo'i bla ma dharma rakShi ta'i blo sbyong mtshon
cha 'khor lo'i brgyud pa ni/ dharmA rakShi ta/ jo bo/ 'brom/ pu to ba/ sha ra ba/ 'chad ka ba/ se spyil bu ba/ lha spyil bu ba/ lha 'gro mgon/ 'od 'jo ba/ mkhan po dmar
ston/ mkhan po shes rab rdo rje/ don zhags pa sangs rgyas rin chen/ bla ma grags pa tshul khrims/ chos rje rgyal ba bzang po/ nub chos lung pa bsod nams rin chen/ chos
rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya ba ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams pa la'o/ ! /rma bya dug 'joms kyi brgyud pa de dang 'dra/ ! /gyer bsgom rdo rje'i glu'i brgyud
pa ni/ byams mgon/ byams pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ jo bo

man gong dang 'dra/ ! /blo sbyong sems dpa'i rim pa'i skor rnams kyang de dang 'dra/ ! nyon mongs lam du blangs pa dang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/
byams pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ ku sa li gnyis/ gser gling pa/ jo bo/ 'brom/ pu to ba/ sha ra ba/ 'chad ka ba/ spyil bu ba/ slob dpon lha/ lha lding dbon/ dharma singha
/ rgya ston byang rgyal/ mkhan po gzhon byang / rin chen 'byung gnas dpal/ don zhags/ sangs rin man 'dra/ ! /sdig sbyong dang / theg chen 'khon sbyong yang de dang 'dra/
! /rnal 'byor ma gnyis kyis gnang ba'i sems sbyong gi brgyud pa ni/ sgrol ma khro gnyer can/ jo bo/ 'brom/ spyan snga ba/ bya yul ba/ gtsang pa rin po che/ glang lung pa/
rgyas bsgom pa/ rin sangs pa/ sgom pa byang skyabs/ ye shes zhabs/ shi la badzra/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ ku sa li'i tshogs bsog kyang de dang 'dra/ ! skyid sdug lam khyer
gyi brgyud pa ni/ kha che paN chen/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ lho brag pa byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen grags pa bshes gnyen/ chos lung pa bsod nams rin
chen man dang 'dra/ yang na mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ rin chen bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ byang sems tshul khrims
dpal/ chos rje rgyal mchog man 'dra'o/ /sum pa lo tsA ba'i snyan brgyud kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje phag mo/ sgrol ma/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma

yon tan/ chos rje sa paN/ grub thob 'dar 'phyar/rin chen bzang po/ mkhas grub chos rje/ ri khrod ras chen/ pra dznyA bo dhi/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN nas 'phags
pa zhang pa/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ rgyal sras thogs med man skyid sdug lam khyer dang 'dra'o/ ! /kun tu bzang po'i blo sbyong gi brgyud pa ni/ jo bo/ dgon pa ba
'dzed dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ sne zur ye 'bar/ sgyer bsgom rgya ma ba/ sangs rgyas dbon ston gzhon 'byung / zangs dgon pa/ mkhan po chos ldan/ slob dpon shAkya bkra shis/
rgya ma bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ ! /thun brgyad ma'i brgyud pa ni/ gser gling pa/ jo bo/ 'brom/ spyan snga tshul 'bar/ glang thang pa rdor seng
/ slob dpon zhang zhung pa/ phyas jo bo/spyan yas yin nam snyam/ lung nang mkhan po/ brag ston shes rin/ slob dpon gzhon bsam/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ ! /gegs sel blo sbyong
dang / 'gal rkyen spongs pa gnyis kyang de dang 'dra/ ! jo bo'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ dpal mchog Dombhi pa/ jo bo
rje/ 'dzeng dbang rgyal/ pu to ba/ rgya lcags ri ba/ lha ri rtsa brgyad pa/ dwags po lha rje/ phag mo grub pa/ rgya sgom ri pa/ rgya mkhar ri pa/ brag dmar ba/ zhang brag
dkar ba/ bla ma dkon mchog byang chub/ gzhon nu grags/ slob dpon zhang / shes rab bsod nams pa/ slob dpon brtson 'grus/ slob dpon chos mchog don zhags pa man 'dra/ rnam
dag gtsug nor

la gnang ba'i blo sbyong gi brgyud pa ni/ jo bo nas/ mkhan po dmar ston gyi bar mtshon cha 'khor lo'i brgyud pa dang 'dra/ de nas jo gdan klu gshong ba/ bshes gnyen shes rab
dbang po/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ ! /birWa pa'i blo sbyong gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / birWa pa/ Dombhi ba/ dpal 'dzin/ ma ti ba/ niska lam ka ra wentra/ chag chos
rje dpal/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ma ti shrI/ ye shes zhabs bzang po/ don zhags pa man 'dra/ tshig rkang brgyad ma'i brgyud pa thun brgyud ma'i glang thang pa man dang 'dra'am
snyam/ ! /mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i blo sbyong gi nyams len dang / theg chen blo sbyong gi brgyud pa ni/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ 'brom ston pa/ pu to ba/ sha ra ba/ mal
gro ba/ brag dmar ba man jo bo'i don bdun ma dang 'dra'o/ /jo bo'i rnam thar rgyas pa/ lam yig chos kyi 'byung gnas 'brom gyis mdzad pa dang / yang jo bo'i rnam thar chen
mo dge bshes zul phu bas bsgrigs pa/ rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong legs bshad kun 'dus rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ ! /blo sbyong pod chung dang
blo sbyong legs bshad kun 'dus/ jo bo'i rnam thar lam yig blo sbyong dpal ye ma sogs kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas
rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ chos rje rdo rje dpal 'byor/ jo bo chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ bikShu ku sa li pa/ ma ho pa dhya ya/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun

dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang chos rje de nyid kyi drung du/ bka' gdams lha bzhir grags pa'i khrid thob pa'i lha khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa/ byams pa/ seng ge bzang po/
ku sa li che chung gnyis/ gser gling pa/ a ti sha 'brom/ pu to ba/ glang ri thang pa/ rgya lcang ri ba/ dwags po lha rje/ rnal 'byor chos dbang phyug sgyer bsgom/ rgyas
bsgom/ bo dong rin po che/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ pra dznyA'i mtshan can/ gu ru bzang po dpal/ mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ grags pa bshes gnyen/ rgyal ba phyag
na/ kun dga' blo gros/ paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lo pa spyan snga ba ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum pa'i khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs/ ra hu la gupta badzra/
dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ nag tsho lo tsA ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba/ wa yu ba shes rab tshul khrims/ lce bsgom shes rab rdo rje/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa/ chos kyi
seng ge gnyan ston chos kyi shes rab/ chos rje ston pa brtson 'grus seng ge 'gro mgon shangs pa tshul khrims 'bum/ gnyan ston chen po rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ nam mkha'
dbang phyug nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ rje btsun mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug
rdo rje 'chang sangs

rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /thugs rje chen po'i khrid kyi brgyud pa 'di/ skyer sgang lugs kyi rigs gtad kyi brgyud pa dang
mthun pa zhig yin nam snyam ste de'i lugs bzhin bris pa yin la/ da dung khrid kyi brgyud pa khungs thub cig btsal bar bya'o/ ! /sgrol ma rjes dran lnga'i khrid kyi brgyud
pa ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas/ 'phags ma sgrol ma/ jo bo yab sras/ rngog legs she/ mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ phul chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor pa dar

pa sangs rgyas/ dga' ldan lha yul du byams pa mgon po/ ri

pa 'pho ba/ drug pa

/mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ paNDi ta a bhya ka ra gupta/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa/ paNDi ta dA la shI la/ sa skya paNDi ta/ slob dpon 'u yug pa/
