rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams lo/ /yang lugs gcig ni/ rje btsun mi g.yo ba/ 'od byed 'byung gnas dpal/ kha che paN chen/ paNDi ta dA na shI
la/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ 'dul 'dzin byang sems/ rgyal tsha chos dbang / gzhon grags mchog dbyangs/ g.yag ston sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shes bya kun rig paNDi ta grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /rgya gzhung mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i yig rnying ma lus pa/ de'i zhal shes

gsum yar klung pas mdzad pa/ mkhan chen g.yag pas mdzad pa'i sgrub skor mi zad pa'i gter mdzod rnams thos so/ /mi g.yo ba sngon po'i rjes gnang chu bsrung dang bcas pa thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin
po che/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa chen po/ blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal tshul ba/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun
dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya
mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'di'i rgya gzhung dang / gsal byed kyi yi ge rje btsun bsod nams
rtse mos mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa rnams thos so/ ! /gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes
rgyal

mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ mus chen/ 'dren mchog sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub
man 'dra/ yang na mus chen/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ rnam rgyal gyi rtog
pa dang 'grel pa bsod nams rtse mos mdzad pa/ bstod pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ sgrub skor chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa/ sa los mdzad pa'i stong mchod kyi lag len/ rje
dkon mchog lhun grub gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs stong mchod dang rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa'i yi ge bdud rtsi chu rgyun zhes bya ba yang thos so/ ! /rdo rje rnam
'joms kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug rin chen dpal/ byang chub gzhon
nu/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge shar pa man gong dang 'dra'o/ /sgrub thabs/ bum chog sbyin sreg dang bcas pa 'phags pas mdzad pa/ ba ri ba nas brgyud pa'i gtor chen
gyi cho ga rje btsun rtse mos mdzad pa lo

rgyus dang bcas pa/ dpang gzugs bla ma rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ rnam 'joms kyi sgrub thabs bum chog rjes gnang dang bcas pa rje btsun dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa
rnams thos so/ ! /dzaM ser gyi rjes gnang thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon dzAe ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa mched gnyis/ bla ma ba ri lo
tsA ba/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ tshogs bsgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ bsod nams skyabs/ bla ma gzungs kyi dpal ba/ bla ma dpal tshul/
shar chen/ rje kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/
ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi cho ga rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ /dzambha la nag po'i rjes gnang gi brgyud
pa ni snga ma dang 'dra/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ ! /'jig rten dbang phyug seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang gi brgyud
pa ni/ seng ge sgra/ tsandra go mi/ de'i slob ma a tsa ra gciggrub chen dpal 'dzin yin gsungs/ jo bo nA ro ta pa/ phaM thing pa sku mched/ asdyu la badzra/ bha man tsa gling
pa thugs rje chen po zer/ ro phyag rdum/ de

gnyis ka la bla ma mal lo tsAs gsan/ de nas sa chen/ gnyan gtsug tor rgyal po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ shar pa ye 'byung / shar pa dus 'khor ba/ kun
dga' byang chub/ mkhan po rgyal bzang / bla ma grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug pa/ 'dren
mchog ratna wardha/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun
grub man 'dra'o/ ! /gdon sgrol gyi brgyud pa ni/ shaddha ka ra warma/ lo chen/ brag steng pa/ mal lo man gong dang 'dra/ sgrub thabs tsandra go mis mdzad pa mal 'gyur/ rmi
lam brtag pa/ gtor chog klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ bstod pa ti la ka dang / tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ gdon sgrol gyi cho ga dkar shAkya grags dang / 'khon rin rgyal gyis mdzad
pa/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi cho ga rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa yang thos so/ ! /grub chen mi tra dzo gi nas brgyud pa'i tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes gnang
gi brgyud pa ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas/ lo ki shwa ra/ grub chen mi tra dzo gi paN chen buddha shrI/ chag lo dgra bcom/ grum ston dar ma shes rab/ grub thob legs ldan 'od/
chos rje dpal chen bzang po/ chos

rje ye shes dpal bzang / rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya
mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
mdzad pa thos so/ ! /mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen dzAe ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa sku mched/ ba
ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ bla ma kun bkras pa/ rje ngang tshul bzang po/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma blo gros bzang po/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'gos lo tsA ba chos
skyong bzang po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /las tshogs kyi yi ge rnying ma yongs rdzogs dang / sa los mdzad pa'i mngon rdzogs chung ngu rjes gnang gi thob yig dang bcas pa thos/
! /yang seng ge'i gdong can gyi sgom bzlas kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rgyal 'phags pa yan chad gong dang 'dra/ de nas bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/
'gro mgon

bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal tshul ba/ shar chen ye rgyal ba/ ngor chen kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen
dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs
las tshogs dang bcas pa'i yi ge rnying ma'i lung yang thos/ ! /rme brtsegs dud kha'i sgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun 'jam dpal/ slob dpon dzAe ta ri/ rdo rje
gdan pa mched/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ bla ma grwa thang pa/ bla ma kun bsod/ bla ma blo gros dpal/ bshes gnyen seng ge

rin chen/ dar ma bzang

po/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rgyal mtshan don grub/ gtsang pa rin rgyal/ bya btang bo dhi'i mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs rin grags/ bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos
grags/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /phyag na rdo rje atsya'i
rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ nA ga dzu na/ padma badzra/ tsandra go mi/ rA dza dharma/ zangs gling pa/ khams pa a seng
/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ jo sras stag la me 'bar/ ston pa grags pa/ don zhags pa/ slob dpon lha rtse/ chos grags/ e pa 'khon ston/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma rgyal 'od/

dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa thos so/ ! /yang phyag na rdo rje u tsarYa me dbang ma thob pa'i

smos

mkhar ba/ skyi ston ru zhang / dkon mchog blo gros/ chos kyi grags pa/ e pa 'khon ston/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma rgyal 'od/ slob dpon smra seng / mkhan chen byang seng
ba/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang / gu ge paNDi ta/ snyug la paN chen/ 'di'i gong gi brgyud rim la 'ga' zhig brtag par bya'o/ /rje dpal ldan rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang

pa gso ba/ steng gdon gzir ba/ lus bsrung ba/ ser ba bsrung ba/ phyir bzlog rnams kyi yi ge rnying ma'i lung thos so/ ! /thugs rje chen po skyer sgang lugs kyi rigs gtad
kyi brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs

dbang phyug ra hu la gupta/ dI paM ka ra/ nag tsho tshul rgyal/ phyag sor ba shes rab 'bar/ wa yu ba shes tshul/ lce bsgom 'phags sras/ skyer sgang chos seng / gnyan ston chos
shes/ ston pa brtson seng / 'gro mgon tshul 'bum/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal/ nam mkha' dbang phyug pa/ nam mkha'i rnal 'byor pa/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam
dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs dI paM ka ras mdzad pa/ rigs gtad kyi cho ga skyer sgang pas zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan pa'i
sgrub thabs rnams thos so/ ! /'jig rten dbang phyug bcu gcig zhal gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs dbang / dge slong ma dpal mo/ paN chen zla ba
gzhon nu/ ye shes bzang po/ bal po pen nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nying phug pa/ rdo rje rgyal po/ zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ rtsi 'dul chen po/ bde ba
can pa/ byang sems chu bzang pa/ shes rab 'bum pa/ rgyal sras rin po che/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo

rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /dpal mo lugs kyi snyung gnas kyi cho ga thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs
dbang / dge slong ma dpal mo/ paN chen zla ba gzhon nu/ ye shes bzang po/ bal po pen nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nyin phug pa/ spru pa rdo rje rgyal
po/ zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ rtsi 'dul ba chen po/ bde ba can pa/ byang sems chu bzang pa/ de nas gnyag chen pa/ chos rje bsod nams bzang po/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/'di'i
gong gi bla ma 'ga' brtag par bya'o/ /rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rje rdo rje dpal 'byor/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams la'o/ /gnyag ston bsod nams dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i snyung gnas/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar/ chos rje bsod nams bzang pos mdzad pa'i snyung gnas cho
ga'i lung yang thos/ ! /ye shes khyung nag gi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgya gar gyi a tsa ra dmar pos rje btsun sa skya pa chen po la dngos su gnang / des rje
btsun bsod nams rtse mo la/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rong mi nyag grags dpal/ rong mi sba ba can sangs rgyas dpal/ rong mi dar ma grags/ rong mi sangs rgyas rgyal

pa dpal bzang po/ shar sbu chu ba dpal ldan

grags pa/'di gnyis kyi bar du brgyud rim 'ga' zhig btsal lo/ /'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'di'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa'i yi ge sbu chu ba dpal ldan grags pas mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ ! /gur mgon bla ma dbyer med gung chen
bkra shis dpal bzang nas brgyud pa'i dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i gtor dbang bar chad kun sel thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje mkha'
'gro ma/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ paNDi ta shardha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya
pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dkon mchog dpal ba/ na
bza' brag phug pa/ 'gro mgon chos rje/ gung chen bkra shis bzang po/ grags pa bshes gnyen pa/ sangs rgyas bshes gnyen pa/ byams pa chos legs pa/ rje thugs rje dpal ba/ 'jam
dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /shrI badzra mahA kA la gur gyi mgon
po lcam dral lha gsum gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ shardha ka ra warma/
lo chen rin chen bzang

po/ gu rub rin chen bsod nams/ mal lo blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang ston chos rje/ na bza' brag phug pa/ puNya mtshan can/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus
chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje nam sangs/ mkhan chen chos dbang / rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /gtor dbang dang rjes gnang gnyis ka la gtor ma zlum gtor mdzad/ ! /gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ shardha ka ra/ lo chen rin bzang / gu rub rin chen bsod nams/ mal lo blo gros grags/
sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal
tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs

rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/
rje spyan snga rin po che/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na/ dam pa kun dga' grags kyi rjes su/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo ring pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/
mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan pa/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /pu tra'i rjes gnang zur bka' thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paNDi ta dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/
bla ma mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rje sa skya
paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla

brgya

rtsar grags pa sgrub thabs dgu bcu rtsa drug paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'i rgya gzhung gi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ dang po thub
pa rdo rje gdan la gtso 'khor gsum/ gnyis pa brtan pa'i 'khor lo bha ba skandhas mdzad pa/ gsum pa yang brtan pa'i 'khor lo/ bzhi pa tshig lhug pa'i brtan pa'i 'khor lo/
lnga pa tshig lhug pa'i a ra pa tsa na dkar po padmas mdzad pa/ drug pa a ra pa tsa na dkar po lha lnga mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ bdun pa 'phags pa 'jam dpal zhal
gsum phyag drug pa/ brgyad pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje gtso 'khor lnga/ dgu pa ngag gi rgyal po gtso 'khor gnyis/ bcu pa rgyal po rol pa/ bcu gcig pa rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod
nas gsungs pa'i 'jam dpal/ bcu gnyis pa rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod nas bsdus pa'i 'jam dpal/ bcu gsum pa yang 'jam dpal/ bcu bzhi pa yan lag med pa'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje/
bco lnga pa 'jam dbyangs chos dbyings gsungs dbang / bcu drug pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'jam dpal/ bcu bdun pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa/ bco brgyad pa
'jam dpal shes rab 'khor lo/ bcu dgu pa 'phral du nyams su myong ba'i a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ nyi shu pa gshin rje nag po zhal drug nyer gcig pa gshin rje nag po zhal gsum
phyag drug pa/ nyer gnyis pa gshin rje gshed du dza na bha dras mdzad pa/ nyer gsum pa rdo rje chos/ nyer bzhi pa seng ge sgra/ nyer lnga pa ha la lhan skyes rol pas
mdzad pa/ nyer drug pa kharsa pa Ni lha lnga rnyog pa med pas mdzad

pa/ nyer bdun pa yi ge drug pa gtso 'khor gsum pa lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ nyer brgyad pa ha ri ha ri la zhon pa/ nyer dgu pa ha la ha la lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/ sum
bcu pa padma gar dbang sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ so gcig pa sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i spyan ras gzigs dgra las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ so gnyis pa sgrol ma rdo rje myu gus
mdzad pa/ so gsum pa sgrol ma dkar mo gtso 'khor gsum pa yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal pos mdzad pa/ so bzhi pa seng ldeng nags sgrol gtso 'khor gsum pa sangs rgyas kyis mdzad
pa/ so lnga pa sgrol ma dkar mo ngag dbang grags pa'i sras kyi thu bos mdzad pa/ so drug pa u rgyan gyi 'od zer can/ so bdun pa rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can/ so
brgyad pa rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can dkar mo/ so dgu pa mya ngan med pa'i shing gi 'od zer can/ bzhi bcu pa u rgyan gyi 'od zer can lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa/
zhe gcig pa yang u rgyan gyi 'od zer can/ zhe gnyis pa tsunda/ zhe gsum pa gnod gnas ser po tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ zhe bzhi pa dzambha la nag po dga' ba'i byin gyis mdzad
pa/ zhe lnga pa nor rgyun ma/ zhe drug pa khro gnyer can/ zhe bdun pa byams pa/ zhe brgyad pa shes phyin dkar mo sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ zhe dgu pa shes phyin dkar
mo dge 'dun gyi bus mdzad pa/ lnga bcu pa shes phyin dkar mo/ nga gcig pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma/ nga gnyis pa mdor bsdus pa'i shes phyin/ nga gsum pa mi g.yo
ba sngon po pra bha ka ra kirti dang gzhon

nu sbas pas mdzad pa/ nga bzhi pa gtum pa chen mo/ nga lnga pa rdo rje hU~M mdzad/ nga drug pa ri khrod lo ma can ma/ nga bdun pa dbyangs can ma dmar mo/ nga brgyad pa bgegs
