brul gtor/ chos spyod dang gtor ma'i rim pa/ byang sems rin chen mgon gyi nang rten gyi dkar chag bsod nams 'od zer la gdams pa/ g.yung

drung dpal la gdams pa/ yan lag bdun pa spyod 'jug lugs/ shes rab grub/ gshin rje rab brtse/ nam mkha' lhun grub/ shAkya bzang po rnams la gdams pa re re/ shAkya bzang po la
gdams pa chos brgyad lam du blang ba/ shAkya bzang po la gdams pa'i blo sbyong sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang ba/ ka drug pa la phul ba/ dpon chen byang pa la phul ba/ chos
nyid rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ gnod lan du phan 'dogs pa'i dam bca' dang smon lam/ dam chos tshul bzhin sgrub thabs/ lta sgom spyod 'bras/ gzhi lam 'bras bu'i ngos 'dzin/
chos rje kun mkhyen pa'i dris lan/ shAkya bzang po la gdams pa/ sangs rgyas dpal la gdams pa/ slob dpon chen po nam mkha' rin chen la gdams pa/ phar phyin drug gi ngos
'dzin/ dkon mchog gsum gyi ngos 'dzin/ khyi thul can la gdams pa/ mkhan chen byang rtse ba'i dris lan/ nad sogs lam du blang ba/ shAkya bsod nams la gdams pa/ nam mkha'
dpal la gdams pa gnyis/ rgyal dbang / grags rin/ ldong ston rnams la gdams pa re re/ chos blo dbon po la gdams pa gsum/ gro sa mkhan po la gdams pa/ chos mchog la gdams
pa gnyis/ bla ma po thog pa/ rtogs ldan bsod rin/ 'od zer bzang po/ ri pa gzhon rgyal/ brtsibs ri pa gzhon byang / sgom chen bsod rgyal/ khams pa blo gros dpal/ mi nyag
rgyal mtshan 'bum/ mi nyag rab ston/ rin po che skyobs pa dpal rnams la gdams pa re re/ rgyal sras lag len gyi pha yul spong ba'i

skabs kyi zhal gsal/ nam mkha' bzang po dang / chos dbang rin chen grogs mched gnyis rnams la gdams pa re re/ bshad gsar ba'i don du mdzad pa'i mol gtam/ ma Ni ba'i drang gtam/
bsngo ba byed tshul/ dpon rin dang khams pa ma Ni pa'i don du mdzad pa'i smon lam re re/ ras rkyang pa'i zhal chems dris lan/ bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad dpon rin gyi
don du mdzad pa ste chos kyi rnam grangs brgya dang bdun gyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje
'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /'jig rten dbang phyug sprul pa'i sku rgyal sras rin po che thogs med bzang po
dpal gyi bka' 'bum gyi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma'i bstod pa/ yang bla ma'i bstod pa/ lo tsA ba blo brtan gyi gsol 'debs/ bu ston
gyi gsol 'debs/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi bstod pa/ smar khrid brgyud pa'i bstod pa/ sum pa lo tsA ba'i snyan brgyud kyi gsol 'debs/ snying po don gsum
gyi brgyud pa/ smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi brgyud pa'i phyag 'tshal/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed brgyud pa/ byang sems sdom brgyud/ yang byang sems sdom brgyud/ blo sbyong
brgyud

pa/ rten 'brel snying po'i bla ma brgyud pa/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi bla ma brgyud pa/ bsnyung gnas brgyud pa/ chos la bskul ba'i gtam rin po che'i phreng ba/ chos la bskul
ba'i gtam rin po che'i rgyan/ dam bca' rnam gsum/ gdams pa gnyis/ rgyal sras lag len/ rang gis rang la bskul ba/ rang la gdams pa/ gdams pa ang drug rang la gros 'debs/
bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan brgyud/ jo bo'i gsol 'debs/ spyan ras gzigs la bstod pa tshig rgyan me tog phreng ba phan bde'i 'byung gnas/ thugs rje chen po'i phyag 'tshal/ 'jam
dbyangs kyi phyag 'tshal/ byams pa'i bstod pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ slob dpon zhi ba lha'i smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi cho ga sems tsam lugs kyi smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi
cho ga jo bo lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga chos spyod rab gsal/ gser gling pa nas brgyud pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid yig rten 'brel snying po'i khrid yig skyid
sdug lam khyer gyi khrid yig bcu gcig zhal gyi snyung gnas/ don zhags lnga'i bstod pa/ thugs rje chen po'i sgom bzlas/ thugs rje chen po'i gtor ma/ sgrib sbyong / dzambha
la/ nor rgyun ma'i mngon rtogs/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas la bstod pa/ sman bla'i rjes gnang / byang chub sems dpa' bcu drug gi bstod pa/ g.yung drung dpal gyi don du mdzad
pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ rtse thang gi slob dpon chen po grags pa rin chen la gdams pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i drung du zhu yig byang chub rtse mo'i dris lan/ skal ldan
bsod

nams 'od zer la gdams pa/ ldong ston la gdams pa/ chos blo dbon chen la gdams pa/ chos blo dbon po la gdams pa/ chos blo dbon po la phul ba/ chos kyi blo gros la gdams pa/
nad las sogs pa lam du khyer ba/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen shAkya bsod nams la gdams pa/ slob dpon chos mchog la phul ba/ yang slob dpon chos mchog la phul ba/ nam mkha' bzang
po'i dris lan/ skyobs pa dpal gyi dris lan/ blo gros dpal la gdams pa/ rtse thang pa sangs rgyal la gdams pa/ mi nyag rgyal mtshan 'bum la gdams pa/ snar thang phu'i bla
ma po tog pa la gdams pa/ bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa/ rab don 'jam dbyangs grags pa la gdams pa/ slob dpon gzhon nu grub pa la gdams pa/ sgom chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan
la gdams pa/ chen po bsod nams bzang po la phul ba/ 'od zer bzang po la gdams pa/ byams chen pa la phul ba/ ri pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ shAkya bzang po
la gdams pa gnyis/ bon po khyi thul can la gdams pa/ mkhan po dro sa pa la gdams pa/ nam mkha' rin chen dpal bzang po la gdams pa/ yang nam mkha' rin chen dpal bzang la gdams
pa/ slob dpon nam mkha' dpal ba la gdams pa/ gnas rnying pa rgyal dbang la gdams pa/ rdzogs chen pa chos nyid rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ dpon chen shAkya bzang po la
gdams pa/ dge slong chos dbang rin chen grogs mched la gdams pa gnyis/ chos blo

dbon po la gdams pa/ shes rab grub pa la gdams pa/ ka drug pa la gdams pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen shAkya bzang po la gdams pa/ stag lung pa sangs rgyas dpal la gdams pa/ shAkya
bzang po la gdams pa/ bshes gnyen nam mkha' grub pa la gdams pa/ dbon po byang pa la gdams pa/ bsod nams dpal la gdams pa/ ras rkyang pa rgyal mtshan dar ma la gdams pa/
slob dpon dpal ye shes kyis bskul ba'i dam bca' dang smon lam/ dam chos tshul bzhin bsgrub pa'i man ngag bshes gnyen rab rtse la gdams pa/ pha jo g.yung drung dpal la
gdams pa/ rten gyi dkar chag lo rgyus gnyis/ nang gi lo rgyus/ mdo sde rgyan/ rgyud bla ma/ spyod 'jug gsum gyi Tikka'i dbu zhabs kyi tshigs bcad/ zla bzang gi don du mdzad
pa'i bsngo ba smon lam bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa rnams so/ /de rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ 'gro mgon tshul khrims dpal/ mkhan chen gzhon nu
rgyal mchog mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug chos rje dpal 'byor rin chen/ rdo rje
'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /rgyal sras pa'i rnam thar 'gro mgon dpal yes mdzad pa'i lung yang thos/ ! /dpal
ldan bla ma dam pa 'dren mchog chos kyi spyan ldan sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' 'bum gyi lung thob pa'i rnam

grangs la/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la bstod pa gsum/ sdom gsum brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kyi kha skong snga phyi gnyis/ gsung ngag sogs kyi brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong
tshan pa lnga/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog dpal la bstod pa gnyis/ dkon mchog gsum bstan bsrung dang bcas pa la bstod pa/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa/ rgyal po khri
srong lde btsan/ jo bo rje rnams la bstod pa re re/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa'i rnam thar/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i rnam thar/ zab mo bla ma'i rnal
'byor/ gsung ngag rin po che khrid kyi zin bris che chung gnyis/ kyai rdo rje'i mngon rtogs/ de'i gtor chog lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs snga phyi gnyis/ dbang chu gsal
ba'i me long / sa chog gi lag len/ so shing sogs kyi dgos pa bshad pa/ bskyed rim gyi grub mtha'i shan 'byed/ de las 'phros pa'i rno cha/ dril bu lus dkyil gyi bshad pa/
lU nag dril gsum gang zag gcig gis nyams su len tshul/ nag po pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyal mchog gi skabs kyi gsal byed/ lU nag dril gsum gyi bum bskyed/ bde gshegs sa bzung gi
lag len/ 'dus pa 'phags lugs kyi dkyil chog gi gsal byed/ 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim gyi bshad pa 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i bsnyen pa dang / tshe sgrub kyi man ngag sgrub thabs
brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho'i gsan yig gtsug tor dri med kyi cho ga'i lag len/ tsha tsha'i rab gnas mdor byas pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gtso 'khor gsum pa'i sgrub thabs/
rang

gis rang la gros 'debs/ bde ba can na bzhugs pa'i dge bsnyen rnams la gnang ba'i bka' shog bla ma nam mkha' dpal bzang la gdams pa snga phyi bzhi/ bla ma blo rin la gdams pa/
slob dpon chos kyi rgyal mtshan la gnang ba'i bka' shog bla ma rin chos la gdams pa/ dpon po kun dga' chos skyong la gdams pa/ byams chen rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas 'phel
la bstod pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs
dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rje btsun bla ma dam pa thugs rje chen po dang
ldan pa sangs rgyas rin chen dpal bzang po nyid kyi gsung rab rnams kyi lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ rnam rgyal bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng
ge'i rnam thar/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros pa'i rnam thar bstod pa 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba'i rnam thar/ rje sems dpa' chen po sogs kyi
bstod pa thor bu ba 'ga' dang / lam zab bsdus pa'i nyams len/ gsung ngag gi khrid yig dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter chen/ de'i kha skong / 'khrul spong gnad kyi gsal byed/
rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi rnam bshad/ kyai rdo rje'i bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad snying po don gsal/ rtsa sngags kyi bshad pa/ bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrub pa'i phyag len/ dpal mngon
par rtogs pa'i

gsal byed/ spyod pa'i rdo rje'i lugs kyi sgrub thabs ma nor gsal sgron/ lU hi pa'i sgrub mchod kyi zur 'debs/ mchod phreng gi lhan thabs/ bde mchog dkar po'i tshe sgrub/ 'dus
pa 'phags lugs kyi sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs/ de'i bkra shis/ sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor phyi ma bcu gcig gi bdag mdun sgrub
tshul/ dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len/ de'i sta gon gyi zur 'debs/ 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'phrin las kun khyab/ tshe dpag
med lha dgu'i dbang gi cho ga rin chen phreng ba/ rong ston chen po nas brgyud pa'i tshe sgrub khyad par can/ tshe dpag med grub pa'i rgyal mo'i lugs kyi dbang chog sgrol
ma dkar mo'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ don yod zhags pa'i bsnyen sgrub bya tshul/ seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang mngon rtogs/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes
gnang bya tshul/ u tsarYa'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ 'byung po 'dul byed kyi mngon rtogs dang rjes gnang bya tshul/ mgon po lcam dral gyi rjes gnang bya tshul/ mgon po'i
man ngag rtsa gsum la brten pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum 'jam rtsub gnyis/ 'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang bya tshul man ngag zab mo 'ga' zhig dang bcas pa/ dur khrod bdag po'i
rjes gnang bya tshul gtor chog dang bcas pa/ dud sol lha mo'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ de'i gtor chog de'i thugs dam bskangs pa'i cho ga gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i sgrub yig gsan
yig

mdor bsdus/ nyin zhag phrugs re'i thugs dam nyams len gyi tho/ gcod khrid gdan thog gcig ma'i nyams len/ gling dga' bde ba can gyi bca' yig mdo khams la 'bul bsdud gnang ba'i
yi ge dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa 'bog pa'i cho ga bsngo ba smon lam bya tshul rnams so/ /de dag gi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya
mtsho/ rje btsun dam pa chos dbang phyug phyi ma gnyis ka la bdag cag gi bla ma 'brel tshad don ldan sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /yang brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje btsun chos dbang pa/ chos rje dge 'dun dbang phyug
rje mus pa chen po'i thugs sras dam pa bikShu paNDi pa ta/ de dag las bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis thos pa'o/ /'dir smras pa/ shrI mAn tri lo ka na
thA hi ta su kha ni dhiM/dpal ldan 'jig rten gsum mgon phan bde'i gter/ /dza ya sha sa na pa ri pUrNa bha Sha pA dha ka ma hA ra tha/rgyal bstan yongs rdzogs bshad sgrub
shing rta che/ /tsakra shwa ra na ya ka wa ra badzra dha ra/'khor lo'i dbang phyug 'dren mchog rdo rje 'chang / /bhaTTa ra ka buddha dhwa dza pA da na ma/rje btsun sangs
rgyas rgyal mtshan zhabs la 'dud/ /1 a haM ba na antar a ra Nya na tha ta ba/bdag rang nags nang dben par mgon khyod kyi/ /pA da ra dzA hrI da ya sya padme pa ta shA ha
ta/zhabs rdul snying gi padmar rtag bkod de/ /sa kha bi la makShe ke ba la di bA ra tri tra/bsam yas rnam thar 'ba' zhig nyin mtshan du/ /u pA tsi tA sa ma ti sha ta mu kha
undha nA bardha na/nyer sems

ting 'dzin sgo brgyar ldang zhing 'jug /bha wa ma tu sya sdyi ti a ha U na me/srid pa nyam nga'i gnas 'dir dman bdag la/ /a twaM sha ra a nya U na na asti/khyod min skyabs
gzhan cung zad ma mchis so/ /e ba e ba a sha nir sarba thA/de lta nyid na deng nas rnam kun tu/ /2 ku ru Na sya a ba lo ki ni na A la pa pra pa dantu/thugs rje'i gzigs pa
g.yel med bka' drin mdzod/ /3 khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang dbang mus pa rje/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin khyod kyi/ /mtshan gyi yi ge rna bar lhung tsam gyis/
/rab dga'i sa thob pas kyang mi 'gran pa'i/ 4 /dga' spro ting 'dzin brtan pos bdag rgyud gtams/ /mthong ba med kyang rnam pa blo yul du/ /wal wal dran pa nyin mo'i cha
kun dang / /mtshan dus rmi lam du yang brjed ma gyur/ 5 /e ma dus gsum sgrib med gzigs pa yis/ /'jigs rung srid mtsho sgrol ba'i ded dpon de'i/ /zhal mthong gsung gi bdud
rtsi thob pa zhig /nam zhig 'byung snyam sems pa kho na las/ 6 /yid la bya ba'i skabs gzhan 'phrogs gyur te/ /mgo la me shor bzlog lta'i brtson 'grus kyis/ /de don bsgrub
pa'i thabs la rab brtson pas/ /shugs ring lam gyi ngal ba ji snyed pa/ 7 /ji mi snyam pa'i dga' spro'i ngang du gnas/ /de nyid tshe na rten 'brel gzhan dbang 'gas/ /lus
ni dpal ldan sa skyar gnas mod kyang / /sems ni rigs kyi bdag po mus pa rje'i/ 8 /phyogs su yang yang rgyug la ngal ba med/ /de nas yun ring ma lon mgon khyod kyi/ /thugs
rjes mngon sum zhal mthong gsung thos pa'i/ /skal pa thob tshe 'di 'dra'i ngo

mtshar gnas/ 9 /bden nam brdzun snyam yid gnyis khyogs la 'phyang / /dus der thog mar sdom gsum bka' drin stsal/ /der rjes zab rgyas chos kyi gter kha phye/ /tha na 'di phyir
phan pa'i bslab bya dang / 10 /zang zing bskyangs pa'i drin kyang pha mtha' yas/ /khyad par dus gsum rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs che/ /'brel tshad don ldan khyod dang slob bu
bdag /byang chub bar du 'bral ba med do zhes/ 11 /zhal bzhes bdud rtsis bdag blo'i bum pa bkang / /de phyir dal ba don ldan 'bras bur bcas/ /mdzad pa'i bka' drin mnyam
med mgon khyod la/ /bdag gzhan lus srog longs spyod dus gsum gyi/ 12 /dge tshogs mchod sprin rgya mtshor sprul nas 'bul/ /de la brten nas bdag dang 'gro ba yis/ /bcas dang
rang bzhin gyis bsdus sdig sgrib kun/ /ma lus byang nas 'di dang phyi ma'i don/ /yid la re ba ji bzhin kun 'grub ste/ /spyi dang bye brag bstan pa rin chen 'di/ /srid mtha'i
bar du 'phel zhing rgyas byed cing / /'gro kun dag pa'i zhing du 'dren par shog 14 /sangs rgyas kun las lhag pa'i bka' drin can/ /rgyal ba'i 'phrin las gcig bsdus mtshan
ldan gyi/ /'dren mchog khyod kyis bdag cag gdul byar bcas/ /byang chub bar du 'bral med thugs rjes skyobs/ 15 /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i
chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po bka' drin gzhal du med pa'i rgyal ba
mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang

sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi zhal snga nas rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te gsum pa'o/ /sarba mangga laM/ gcig zhus// // ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus
zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART IV: Teachings from Nam mkha' dpal bzang (1535-1602); vol. kha, text no. 2, pp. 247-258

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las rje thar rtse
nas nam mkha' dpal bzang pos rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs so//

rgya gar skad du/ pra dznyA de shwa ra ga ga na shrI bha dra ya na mo/ bod skad du/ mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug nam mkha' dpal bzang la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir
kun mkhyen gnyis pa ltar/ /rab grags rgyal bas lung bstan e wa~M pa/ /mkhas kun dga' ba'i 'dren pa bzang po yis/ /bstan pa'i gsal byed nam mkha' dpal bzang rgyal/ /zhes
pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa shrI e wa~M pa chen po chos kyi rje nam mkha' dpal bzang po'i drung du/ rang lo gzhon nu'i dus dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin cung zad mnos
pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar/ ! tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ dze tA ri/ byang chub
bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya

pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis 'od zer/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla
ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ye/ grags pa dpal/ sru lung pa kun smon/ brag phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ chos rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje thar rtse
nas nam mkha' dpal bzang ba/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ mus chen/ grub chen dkon mchog blo/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo
'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub

man 'dra/ yang na/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rkyang 'dur rab 'byams pa dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan
man 'dra'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs/ dkyil chog 'chi bslu/ bstod pa rnams dze tA ris mdzad pa/ dga' ba'i dpal gyis 'gyur mdzad pa thos so/ /yang ngan song sbyong ba kun rig rtsa
ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa sa lugs ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ kun dga' snying po/ shes rab bskyangs/
zhi ba snying po/ dge mtshan bshes gnyen/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin bzang / brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che/
sa paNDi ta/ tshogs bsgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ ti shrI kun dga' blo gros/ bla ma dam

pa/ blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rje
sangs rgyas rin chen/ dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i gzhan phan skor gsum dang / rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i
bsnyen rgyas/ rdul tshon kha skong / gzhan phan mtha' yas/ cha gsum gyi yig cha dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ ! /yang sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi
nang nas sta gon dang 'brel ba'i dkyil 'khor lnga tsam gyi

dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ bram ze dzi na mi tra/ swa sti phA la/ sgra gcan zin/ pra dznyA pA li ta/shes rab bskyangs/
ye shes rdo rje/ pra hi ta/rab tu phan pa/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ kha che dharma phA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gnyal pa nyi shes/ snur
nyi ma/ 'od zer/ gshen rdo rje seng ge rgya gsar pa/ 'bro dzi ti pa/ snye mdo pa bsod nams dpal/ gnyal pa chos grags/ bya rin chen 'od/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bag
ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ chos rje mgon po dbang phyug gnyan
lo grags pa blo gros/ rje pra dznyA dhwa dza/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ rje dpal rdor pa/ ra chen yon tan dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan pa man 'dra/ dkyil 'khor phyi
ma bcu gcig gi bdag mdun sgrub tshul/ dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len/ de'i sta gon gyi zur 'debs dang bcas pa rje sangs rgyas rin chen pas mdzad
pa rnams thos so/ ! /yang dpal kye rdo rje'i chos skor gyi gtso che'i chos su grags pa'i 'phags yul gyi gzhung 'grel rnams thos pa la/ thog mar Dombhi pas mdzad pa'i bdag
med ma'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi 'od/ 1 rdzogs

rim lhan cig skyes grub/ 2 tshogs 'khor 'du ba bsgrags pa dang bcas pa rnams 'brog 'gyur/ 3 de nyid bcu pa mar me mdzad dang dge blo'i 'gyur/ 4 phyag gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs
a la la badzras mdzad pa/ 5 dran pa gcig pa gardha ri pas mdzad pa/ 6 dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs bsod snyom pas mdzad pa/ 7 dkyil chog bzang po yongs bzung / 8 rigs bsdus
kyi sgrub thabs/ 9 sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa/ 10 bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i sgrub thabs/ 11 sgrub thabs de gsum la dgos pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga 12 'grel pa ku mu
ti rnams mi thub zla bas mdzad pa 'brog 'gyur/ 13 dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin chen 'bar ba dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ 14 slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad
pa'i dkyil chog nas gling ma/ 15 sgrub thabs mtsho skyes/ 16 mar me'i rtse mo lta bu'i rdzogs rims/ 17 tshogs 'khor dam tshig lnga pa/ 18 bstod pa nyi shu pa rnams 'brog
mi'i 'gyur/ 19 'grel pa padma can khu dngos grub kyi 'gyur rnams thos/ 20 yang skabs kyi 'grel chung brgyad du grags pa la/ nag po pas mdzad pa'i gleng gzhi'i 'grel pa/
21 sgrol ma can gyis mdzad pa'i klu'i 'grel pa/ 22 padma'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i glu'i kho na nyid gsal ba/ 23 mngon par rtogs pa'i rim pa/ 24 kyai rdo rje de kho na
nyid kyi rim pa/ 25 dur khrod kyi 'grel pa che chung gnyis/ 26/27 brda'i 'grel pa rnam par nges pa rnams dang / 28 slob dpon

nag po pas mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gzhung 'grel/ 29 sgrub thabs de nyid gsal ba/ 30 phyag bcu drug pa dpa' gcig 31 bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs/ 32 tshogs 'khor gyi
cho ga rnams 'gos 'gyur/ 33 phyag gnyis pa dpa' gcig 34 ta ra kla shu dang / tshul khrims grags kyi 'gyur/ rab gnas kyi cho ga dang / 35 sbyin sreg cho ga ga ya dha ra dang
'gos 'gyur/ 36 gshin gyi cho ga nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 37 ro sreg cho ga dang mchod rten gyi cho ga ste gzhung de rnams dam tshig rdo rje'i slob ma nag po shanta
bha dras mdzad pa dang / 38/39 de dag gi rgyab rten du dka' 'grel rnal 'byor rin po che sbyor phreng dang / yang rdzogs rim theg chen zhes bya ba 'gos kyi 'gyur dang /
phyag rgya bzhi pa zhes bya ba'i lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs dgra las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ ga ya dha ra dang / gyi jo'i 'gyur rnams kyang thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po yan chad ni gzhan du btsal dgos/ de nas rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon rgyal/ rgyal tshab kun dbang pa/ mkhas grub dpal rdor
ba gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ chos rje dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang lce bsgom kha skyong brag pas mdzad pa sogs rin spungs skor gsum las/ thog mar dpe chos rin spungs dang / de'i 'grel
pa gnyis kyi lung thob pa'i

brgyud pa ni/ lce bsgom 'dul ba rdo rje/ smon lam mgon/ rin chen ye shes/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ rgya ma pa yon tan 'od/ hor ka bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor gyi
dbang phyug dpal ldan bzang po/ byang sems sbyin pa/ bla ma nam mkha'i mtshan can/ ra ston yon tan dpal bzang / mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje
shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rgyal sras pa/ 'gro mgon dpal ldan ye shes/
hor ka bzhi pa man chad 'dra'o/ /gtam rgyud rin spungs dang man ngag rin spungs gnyis kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'gro mgon dpal ldan ye shes/ hor ka bzhi pa man chad
gong bzhin no/ /yang brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang gi rjes su/ rje dpal ldan don grub/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor ku
sa li pa/ ma ho pa dhya ya/ de las a nandas thos so/ ! /yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom
ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ rgyal ba byams pa mgon po/ 'phags pa thogs med/ mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa rnam grol sde/ mkhas mchog mchog
gi sde/ mkhas mchog 'dul ba'i sde/ mkhan po rnam snang mdzad bzang po/ slob dpon seng ge bzang po/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ paNDi ta gu

na mi tra/ paNDi ta rin chen bzang po/ shar phyogs pa zla ba bzang po/ bstan skyong 'bum phrag gsum pa/ rngog lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab/ 'dre chen shes rab 'bar/ ar byang
chub ye shes/ 'dul 'dzin dkar mo/ dkar chung ring mo/ zhang ye pa/ gnyal zhig 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ zad ring dar ma tshul khrims/ bo dong ba brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu/
sems dpa' chen po bsod nams seng ge lho pa grub pa seng ge khro phu tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ de la thugs sras lo tsA
ba sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal dang / mkhas pa lung mang pa dang / dharmA shrI gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka la mi pham g.yag gi mtshan can sangs rgyas dpal gyis gsan/
de nas rong ston chen po shAkya rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ byams mgon gnyis pa don yod dpal bzang po/ yongs rdzogs gnas lnga mkhyen pa'i paNDi ta shAkya mchog ldan
dri med legs pa'i blo gros/ las chen ye shes lhun grub/ 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog chos rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal
bzang / des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rje thar rtse ba'i rjes su/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ ku sa li pa paNDai pa/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'dir smras pa/ dzi na sya bi ha ra ba lo ki ta dznyA ni ka ru Na dheM/rgyal ba'i gtsug lag kun gzigs mkhyen brtse'i gter/ /bi shuddha
shi la kA Sha ya maM laM ka ra sho dha na/rnam dag tshul khrims ngur smrig rgyan

gyis mdzes/ /a bhatta a tstshinta karma wa ti/rmad byung rgyun mi chad pa'i 'phrin las can/ /badzra dha ra tsu Da laM ka ra na ma/rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gtsug rgyan de la 'dud/
/'dren mchog bzang po'i zhabs la byis pa'i dus/ /dbang sogs dam chos sgo skal cung zad mnos/ /mang po'i gsung gi bdud rtsi ma thob pa'i/ /skal dman bdag la thugs rjes bskyab
tu gsol/ /nam mkha' lta bu'i gsan pa mtha' yas kyi/ /dpal ldan bla ma rnams kyi 'phrin las rgyun/ /bzang por mdzad pa'i skyes chen khyed lta bu'i/ /zab rgyas chos kyi
rgya mtshor bdag gyur cig /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed
ces bya ba las/ 'dren mchog nam mkha' dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te bzhi pa'o// //mangga laM// ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar
gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART V: Teachings from Kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub (1571-1642); vol. kha, text no. 3, pp. 259-272

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las 'khon ston 'jam
pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub kyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI manydzu gho Sha nA tha bhu mi paNDu lo ka shwa ra a nanda pu nya ni ra bho ga ye na mo/ bod skad du/ dpal mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs sa skya pa 'jig rten
dbang phyug kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub la phyag 'tshal lo/ /kun dga'i gzugs sku 'gro ba'i bsod nams su/ /lhun gyis grub pa bkra shis grags pa'i gter/ /bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan 'dzin pa'i mdzad 'phrin can/ /dpal 'byor bzang po sa skya pa de bsngags/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa rigs ldan chos kyi rgyal po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun
dga' bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du/ dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin mnos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar/ ! tshe dpag med dze tA ri lha
dgu'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ snying po'i zhabs/ dze tA

ri/ byang chub bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya
paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ grags pa dpal/ sru lung pa kun dga'
smon lam/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen gangs pa/ sa bzang ma ti/ theg chen pa/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpal chos pa/ mus srad pa
rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i
dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des

bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan yan sngar dang 'dra ba las/ de nas bla ma dam pa/ blo gros brtan pa/ dpal
tshul ba/ chos rje shar pa/ ngor chen kun bzang / sems dpa' chen po/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje sangs rin pa/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje man 'dra'o/ /yang na rdo rje
'chang yan sngar dang 'dra ba las/ ngor chen kun bzang / mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ mi nyag grags rdor ba/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje man gong bzhin no/ ! /yang 'khon sa skya
pa'i yab chos dpal yang dag he ru ka mar me dgu par grags pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje
sems dpa'/ sprul sku dga' rab rdo rje/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ ro langs

bde ba'i dngos grub/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ slob dpon hU~M ka ra/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ bal po shI la manydzu/ sna nam rdo rje bdud
'joms/ gnyal dznyA na ku ma ra/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal po/ gtsug tor shes rab/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / bal po/ shAkya blo gros/ shes
rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin
po che/ kha 'ub pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros dpung rgyan mdzes pa'i tog dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa
rin chen rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma dam

pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ mtshungs med nam
mkha' blo gros/ chag lo tsA ba rin chen chos kyi rgyal po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam
pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na nye brgyud ni/ dpal he ru ka slob dpon hU~M ka ra/ slob dpon
padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po bsrung ba/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen man gong bzhin no/ /yang na sa chen kun dga' snying po nas/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa shes rab blo
gros/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan man gong dang 'dra'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs rim pa gsal ba dang / dkyil chog blo dman dga' ba skyed byed
dang / rdul tshon la brten nas sgrub mchod byed tshul rnams sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa rnams thos/ yang phur pa'i dkyil chog rdo rje las rim slob dpon
padmas mdzad pa dznyA na ku ma ra'i 'gyur/ sgrub thabs chung ngu sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma rje btsun gyis mdzad par grags pa/ 'gro mgon bsod nams
rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas pa bklags pas don grub/ 'bring po don grub snying po/ bsdus pa yang snying lhan skyes dkyil chog rtogs par sla ba/ de'i lhan
thabs rin po che'i do shal dang / sgrub

thabs chung ngu sa los mdzad pa/ yang dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga blo gros kha 'byed dang / dbang gi mtshams sbyar blo gsal dga' bskyed sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa
thos so/ ! /yang rdo rje 'jigs byed sa lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad
bzang po/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ grub chen nA ro pa/ a sdyu la badzra/ bha ro phyag rdum/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ gan
pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal bzang / chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje buddha singha/ rje nam mkha' dpal
bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje
buddha/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i lung thos so/ ! /lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi khrid thob pa las/ thog mar
tog rtse pa'i bsam mi khyab kyi khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rta mchogmda' can/ bI Na ba/ pi wang 'dzin/ rgyal po indra bhu ti/ phun tshogs zhabs/ grub chen
sgeg

pa'i rdo rje/ gundha ri pa/ padma badzra/ chos kyi pa/ bzang po'i zhabs/ tog rtse pa/'jor 'dzin/ bhu Sha Na/ dha ma pa/ kahna/grub thob/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi/ se ston/
zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen/ bsod rtse/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal tshul/
grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ zha lu pa chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje
nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen kun bzang /
mkhas mchog dkon blo/ mkhas btsun dpal ldan rgyal po/ rje nam mkha'i mtshan can/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ ! /bsam mi khyab kyi byin rlabs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ sa skya paN chen/ 'od shAka la ru ba/ ye shes mgon po/ bag ston/ gzhon tshul/ tshul rgyal ba/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa man gong dang 'dra/ !
/phyag rgya chen po yi ge med kyi byin rlabs gdams ngag gi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ de ba a kar tsandra/ de gnyis ka
la jo bo a mo gha badzra gyis gsan/ de la 'brog mis gsan/ bla ma se mkhar chung ba man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /mchod rten drung thob kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje

'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ arYa de wa/ dge slong nag po zhabs/ zla ba grags pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ma he'i dbu can/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog
mi man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /gtum mo lam rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ slob dpon dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs can/ dza landha ra pa/ nag
po spyod pa/ shrI dha ra/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi man 'dra'o/ ! /yon po srong ba'i brgyud pa yang de dang 'dra'o/ ! /indra bo dhi'i lam gyi brgyud pa ni/ /dang po dpal ldan
sde'i zhal snga na/indra bo dhi che ba/ /de bzhin du drang srong gzugs/ yang tshangs pa'i zhabs/ dang / /bram ze mo ni rdo rje grub/rnal 'byor ma/ /de nas shrI badzra bo
dhi bar pargyal/ /de'i slob dpon de'i phyi ma u pa ma'i zhabsdang / /gos bral gcer bu/ zhal snga de bzhin no/ /dpal ldan dznyA na chung babo dhi rgyal/ /de bzhin shrI yo
bo dhi dang / /slob dpon padma badzra dang / /Dombhi he ru ka'i zhal snga de bzhin no/ /yan lag bar pa dpal ldan mo/ /bung ba'i mkha' 'gro ma padma de bzhin no/ /dur khrod
du na kI lar bzhugs/ /lha lcam legs smin de bzhin no/ /bdag kyang dang po grub pa yin/ /zhes pa ltar/ rdo rje 'chang / dpal bde ba chen po/ indra bo dhi/ dpal tshangs
pa'i zhabs/ bram ze mo/ grub pa'i rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bo dhi bar pa/ slob dpon u pa ma'i zhabs/ slob dpon gos bral zhabs/ rgyal po dznyA na bo dhi/ slob dpon padma badzra/
Dombhi he ru ka yan lag bar ma'i zhabs/ lha mo bung ba'i

padma/ lcam legs smin/ rgyal po indra bo dhi chung ba/ de'i slob ma bram ze rin chen rdo rje/ de la kha che shes rab gsang bas gsan/ de la 'brog mi ste de man 'dra'o/ /nye
brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / indra bo dhi che ba/ lcam legs smin/ shes rab gsang ba/ 'brog mi man chad gong bzhin no/ ! /padma badzra'i lam gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang
/ bi la ba badzra/grub thob chos 'chad kyi phyag rgya/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ indra bo dhi/ lcam legs smin/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ rje ga ya dha ra/ 'brog
mi man 'dra'o/ ! /Dombhi pa'i lhan cig skyes grub kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ Dombhi ba/ a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/
bsod snyoms pa/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /khrid yig rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung la lung rigs smra ba mgon po rin chen gyis
zin bris mdzad pa'i steng nas gnang / lam skor brgyad kyi khrid yig sa skya pa gong mas mdzad pa rnams dang / bsam mi khyab kyi rgya gzhung / rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i
mchan bu sa bcad dang bcas pa/ mar me'i rtse mo'i rgya gzhung / lhan cig skyes grub kyi rgya gzhung / bsam mi khyab kyi byin rlabs bya tshul 'khon dkon mchog rgyal pos mdzad
pa de'i lo rgyus/ lam skor dgu'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa rnams thos so/ ! /yang mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can dmar mo'i
rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can/ bla ma

rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rwa pa chos grags/ bla ma don yod rdo rje/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen/ lo tsA ba manydzu shrI/ bsam grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun a nanda
dhwa dza/ rdo rje 'chang nor bu phun tshogs/ mkhas grub lha dbang blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod
nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /dus 'khor nas bshad pa'i lha mo sna tshogs yum gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ shrI kA la
tsakra/ mahA paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen/ lo tsA ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde/ 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal/ chag lo gsum pa/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug drin chen byams pa rab
brtan/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i lung yang thos/ ! /yang
gnyos mgon trakshad lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ bram
ze mchog sred/ rnal 'byor pa ro zan de wa/ rnal 'byor ma bde ster ma/ bla ma ba liM ta a tsArYa/ kha rag gi gnyos lo tsA ba/ sras rdo rje bla ma/ dpal 'byung / dpal seng
/ yab grags pa dpal/ sangs rgyas ras chen/ bla ma rin chen rgyal po/ bla ma byang dar/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun ye shes rin chen/ kun

spangs chos kyi rin chen/ dbu ma pa dpal ldan rin chen/ byang sems bsod nams rin chen/ brag dkar ba sems dpa' chen po bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho/ chos
rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na mnyam med sangs rgyas ras chen/
rgyal sras stag tshangs pa/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas phyar chen/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen 'byung gnas/ drin chen mkhas btsun sangs rgyas/ kun mkhyen saM ga bha dra/ rgyud 'dzin
sangs rgyas bzang po/ dbu ma pa man gong dang 'dra/ chos skyong chen po trakshad dang / mgon po stag bzhon gyi gtor chog rjes gnang gi yi ge rje thar rtse pa nam mkha'
dpal bzang bas mdzad pa'i lung yang thos/ ! /yang chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i chos dang chos ma yin pa rnam par 'byed pa'i
bstan bcos sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba/ kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa'i spyi don rta bdun gyi rgyal po sdom gsum nyams len gsal ba zhes bya ba dang / Tikka rgyal ba'i
gsung rab kyi dgongs gsal gnyis kyi steng nas bshad lung zhib tu thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bro lung
pa/ mkhas pa dkon mchog grags/ g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ chos rje gzhon nu seng ge mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gung ru shes rab bzang
po/ kun mkhyen bsod

nams seng ge 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge chos rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ 'dren mchog nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs
kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub kyi rjes su/ rje dharma pa/ rje ma
ho pa dhya ya/ des bdag la'o/ /brgyud rim 'di ni chos rje sa paN nas da lta'i bar gyi sdom gsum rab dbye'i bshad rgyun bar ma chad pa'i brgyud pa yin te/ 'di'i tshul/ mkhas
mchog klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i sdom gsum rab dbye'i bshad rgyun gyi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa'i lam rim dang smon lam bcas pa dngos grub kyi pho nya
zhes bya ba las 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin pas/ sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin dpyod ldan gzur gnas rnams kyis snying la bcang bar gces so/ /'dir smras pa/ A nanda sya pu Nya
dznyA sambho ga de/kun dga'i bsod nams ye shes lhun grub sku/ /su ru tsi ra ha su bhA Sha sastA ka ra/rab mdzes ngur smrig rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i dpal/ /bha ba shAnta
shre ya gu Na ratna ni dhe/srid zhi'i dge legs yon tan rin chen gter/ /manydzu gho Sha gu dya pA da sya padme na maH'jam dbyangs bla ma'i zhabs kyi padmar 'dud/ /gang sku
ngur smrig rgyal mtshan gyis mdzes shing / /gang gsung gzhan skyon brjod pa'i dri mas dben/ /gang thugs zhe sdang khong khros ma gos pa'i/ /gang gi yon tan dran pas lhag
par dad/ /bdag kyang dam pa khyed bzhin sku tshe bdun bcu rtsa gnyis bzhugs pa dang / /mdzad

pa'i 'phrin las ma lus mthar phyin te/ /bstan dang 'gro ba'i don rnams re ba bzhin/ /'grub ste skye dgu bde bas 'tsho gyur cig /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las
dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ rigs ldan 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub
kyi zhal snga nas rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te lnga pa'o// //sarba mangga laM// ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART VI: Teachings
from Lu phu ba 'Bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor; vol. kha, text no. 4, pp. 273-290

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las rje lu phu ba
'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor gyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ swA mI ananda nA mi ka pA da ya na ma/ swa sti shrI rastu ka lyA Na mi traM pra Na ba/ bod skad du/ chos kyi rje kun dga'i mtshan can zhabs la 'dud do/ /dpal
dge legs su gyur cig dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rab tu bsngags so/ /kun nas dga' ba'i mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyas/ /dpal ldan 'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i bsil zer gyis/ /skal
bzang thar pa'i dpal 'byor la 'god pa'i/ /bshes gnyen mtshan mo'i mgon de spyi bos mchod/ /ces pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug 'bum chen kun
dga' dpal 'byor ba'i drung du dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin mnos pa la/ thog mar/ slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas kyi drung du/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang pos dngos su
gsan pa'i tshe dpag med lha bcu bdun gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur

ba mda' 'phen mar grags pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas/ rje ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ rngog ston byang chub dpal grub/ rje
btsun shi la rasmi/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs dbang gi rgyal po/ mkhas grub shAkya kun dga'/ mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/
des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /ku ru kulle thun mong ma yin pa gsang sgrub lha lnga'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i byin rlabs 'jigs
med grags pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ bskal ba bzang po/ Dombhi ba/ tsa dya ba/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje
gdan pa chen po/ rdo rje gdan pa chung ba/

rje btsun ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ bla ma khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa kun
dga' bsod nams/ mnyam med chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang gzungs kyi dpal bzang po/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug dge legs bzang po/ A nanda ma ti bzang po/
mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub shes rin/ rje rdo ring pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs byin rlabs dang bcas pa yi ge rnying ma'i lung yang thos so/ /tshogs bdag dmar chen gyi rjes gnang 'phags pa rin po
che'i mngon rtogs tshigs bcad ma'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ sa ra ha

pa/ klu sgrub/ ri khrod pa mgon po/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/
rong pa shes bzang / bla ma gzhon tshul/ bla ma ngag dbang / byang seng pa/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab
dam pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rdo ring kun spangs pa/ rje kun dga' grol mchog rje ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa
ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /kag chol 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gdan pa/ tha bi ra/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ lcags thang
pa/ sa chen/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje

sa paN/ khang bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ bla ma ngag dbang grags pa/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rdzogs rim rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ mtshan mo rgyu ba/ mtshan ma gyen bsgrengs rnams kyi khrid thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ la li ta badzra/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ grub chen a mo gha badzra/ don yod rdo rje/ skyo ston 'od 'byung / skyo ston sku mched/
jo sras khams pa/ gnyan ston rin chen brtan pa/ de sras 'od srung / gnyan ston chos rgyal/ 'dzin pa rin she 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa/ bla ma
cha rgyan dbang rgyal/ klog kya/ bla ma grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen gang pa/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam mgon kun dga' grol mchog rje lha dbang grags pa/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ /brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rje A nandas mdzad pa/ khrid kyi yi ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa thos so/ ! /yang rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rnal 'byor bzhi'i
khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la li ta/ a mo gha/ ye shes 'byung gnas/ padma badzra/ di paM ka ra/ rwa rdo rje grags/ rwa chos
rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng ge rwa

shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen dang ma ba/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ nyang stod arYa/ grub chen kun dga' blo gros/ rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/
chos rje rin rnam/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /khrid yig lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrIs mdzad pa thos so/ ! /rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi man ngag zab mo yang gsang mthu bzlog nag
por grags pa zhal shes dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung
gnas sbas pa'i dpal/ padma badzra/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ bla ma rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa sga lo/ bla
ma shes rab seng ge mnyam med grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ chos rje dge legs dpal bzang / sngags 'chang a nanda ma ti bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang
byams pa chos rin chen/ rje dbon brtson 'grus rgya mtsho/ bla ma blo gros dpal ldan/ 'dren mchog sangs rgyas mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ sbas pa'i rnal
'byor nam mkha' rgya mtsho/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sbas pa'i rnal 'byor nam

mkha' rgya mtshos/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan pa dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa sangs rgyas 'od zer gnyis las kyang gsan gsungs/ yang brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rwa ye shes seng
ge nas/ rwa dharmA seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa dbon shes rab rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ bla ma brtson 'grus
byang chub/ sems dpa' chen po bsod nams yon tan/ chos rje dge legs bzang po man gong dang 'dra/ ! /rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi chos skor sna tshogs kyi lung thob pa la/ rgyud
rtog pa bdun pa rwa lo'i 'gyur/ rwa los mdzad pa'i dka' 'grel/man ngag gnad kyang zer/ nag 'grel/tshig don rnam par bshad pa'ang zer/ man ngag bcud thigs/gnad kyi man ngag
kyang zer/ zhal dgu pa'i sgrub thabs/ phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i dbang chog
zhi rgyas dbang drag gi sbyin sreg bzhi/ shog ril gsum pa/ nyi ma bzhi pa/ de'i 'grel pa 'bum seng gis mdzad pa/ cu tshun dha ri'i rtog pa rwa lo'i 'gyur/ te'u lo pa'i rtogs
pa'i 'grel pa dharma seng ges mdzad pa/ bzlas pa'i man ngag 'chi kha ma'i man ngag uShNi Sha rwa lugs kyi gdams pa/ lag len khrigs bkod/ dngos grub kyi spyod pa zhi
ba ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal nag po'i rang bzhin zhes bya ba'i bstod pa ldong ston gyis mdzad pa/ rgya ston gyis mdzad pa'i rtog gsum gyi 'grel pa dri med snang ba/
'khrul 'khor gyi man ngag zhal shes la/ shog dril

gsum gyi 'grel pa/ bsrung bzlog bsad gsum gyi man ngag sbyin sreg 'dod pa'i don 'grub/ drug cu pa'i gtor chog rnams dang / zhi ba'i las bdun gyi brjed byang rje rdo rje 'chang
gis mdzad pa/ chos kyi rje lu phu ba chos kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad chen mo rnams kyi lung thob/ ! /dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i
man ngag zab mo bram ze mngags gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal
sde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna kirti/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba chen po/ bla ma gnam kha 'ub pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon
rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang ston/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ gzungs dpal/ dge bzang pa/ rdo ring
kun rgyal/ mkhan chen byams bzang / 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gnyos mgon traka shad nag po gtso 'khor dgu'i
rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ rnal 'byor ma ro san lde pa/ rnal 'byor ma bde ster ma/ ba liM ta a tsarYa/ gnyos lo tsA ba/ rdo
rje bla ma/ dpal byung / dpal ye/ yab grags pa dpal/ sangs rgyas ras chen/ bla ma rin chen dpal rgyal/ bla ma khyad par ba/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal po/ grub chen blo gros
snyan

pa/ bla ma yon tan rgyal mtshan/ byang sems bsod nams rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /grwa pa mngon shes nas brgyud pa'i dzambha la dmar po'i las tshogs kyi yi ge rnying ma yongs rdzogs kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon padma/ grwa
pa mngon shes can/ grwa pa thugs rje 'bum/ shu la tsaNDa/ slob dpon tshul rgyal/ mkhan po nyi ma/ slob dpon don bzang / dbus pa grub brtson/ ka bcu pa 'phrin las bzang
po/ blo gros bzang po/ rin po che seng ge dpal/ chos rje brag thog pa/ rje kun dga' rnam rgyal/ rje mus pa rnam rgyal dpal bzang / kun bzang nyi zla'i mtshan can/ des nam
mkha' dpal 'byor bsam 'grub/ ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /zhing skyong dur khrod
bdag po'i chos skor thob pa la/ de'i brgyud gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo le'u brgyad pa/ bla ma bai ro tsa na las brgyud pa/ 'jim pa lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ de'i sgrub thabs
las phyung ba bai ros mdzad pa/ 'jim los bsgyur ba/ de'i rjes gnang gi yi ge bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag 'jim lo'i zhal gdams sogs man ngag tshan pa du ma yod
pa'i yi ge rnying ma'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ padma badzra/ ra hu la/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dpal dam tshig rdo
rje/ 'chi med blo gros bzang

po/ mkhas pa bai ro tsa na/ dpal chen sga lo/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yar bsgom/ rgyal tsha lung
mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla
ma dpal ldan rgyal po/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ chos rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du/ gsang sngags rnying ma'i chos skor 'ga' zhig thob pa la/ spyir yang gsang sngags rnying ma 'di
la bka' gter gnyis las/ bka' ma'i dbang du byas na/ sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur sogs dang tshul 'dra ba'i grub pa brnyes pa'i slob dpon so so nas bzung / da lta'i
bar du brgyud pa bar ma chad du byon pa'i chos skor du ma zhig yod la/ gter ma la sgrub pa chen po bka' brgyad du yod pa las/ de yang bskyed pa mahA yo ga ste bskyed rim
gtso bor ston pa/ gter kha gong mar grags pa chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi rnam 'phrul mnga' bdag nyang ral gyis gter nas spyan drangs pa'i bka' brgyad bde gshegs
'dus pa'i skor dang / lung a nu yo ga ste rdzogs rim gtso bor ston pa'i gter kha 'og mar grags pa/ nyang ral gyi sprul pa gu ru chos dbang gis lho gter nas spyan drangs
pa'i bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs

rdzogs kyi skor dang / bskyed rdzogs zung 'jug ston pa rig 'dzin rgod ldem gyis byang gter nas spyan drangs pa'i bka' brgyad drag po rang byung rang shar gyi skor dang / gzhan
yang sprul sku bde chen gling pas gter nas spyan drangs pa'i bka' brgyad khro 'bar ma dang / padma gling pas gter nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs kyi me long la sogs pa bka'
brgyad kyi skor mtha' yas pa zhig yod pa las/ de lta bu'i bka' brgyad yongs rdzogs kyi dbang bskur ba'i tshe/ dkyil 'khor rnam dag 'di ltar 'byung ste/ dbus su bdud rtsi
yon tan che mchog rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor/ shar du dpal chen badzra he ru ka yang dag thugs kyi dkyil 'khor/ lhor 'jam dpal sku'i dkyil 'khor/ nub tu padma gsung gi dkyil
'khor/ byang du phur pa 'phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor/ shar lhor mngon rdzogs rgyal po bla med he ru ka ma mo rbod stong gi dkyil 'khor/ lho nub tu bla ma rig 'dzin gyi dkyil
'khor/ nub byang du phyag rdor dregs pa kun 'dul 'jig rten mchod bstod kyi dkyil 'khor/ byang shar du drag po stobs ldan nag po dmod pa drag sngags kyi dkyil 'khor te
dkyil 'khor dgu po 'di gzhal yas khang gcig gi nang du chug pa zhig 'byung ba yin la/ 'di rnams la lha grangs mang nyung mi 'dra ba du ma 'byung yang / phyi'i khyams kyi
bka' srung sogs kun dril bas lha grangs bdun brgya dang nyer lngar grags pa nges pa yin la/ 'di kun gyi sgrub thabs dkyil chog dbang bskur sogs dpe steng nas nyams su len
pa rnying ma ba rang gi lugs kyi phyag len gyi mchog yin te/ lugs 'di la mkhas pa'i snga

rabs kyi bla ma rnams kyi gsung las/ rab shog ser gyi steng nas nyams su len/ 'bring shog ser ma zhal bshus ma 'chugs pa'i dpe thog nas nyams su len/ tha ma lce thog nas nyams
su len rung ba tsam yin zhes 'byung ba yin no/ /de lta bu'i bka' brgyad rtsa ba las 'phros pa'i bka' brgyad bye brag ma'i nang tshan 'phrin las phur pa'i chos skor la/
lho gter nas gu ru chos dbang gis spyan drangs pa'i phur pa yang gsang spu gri'i skor dang / ratna gling pas gter nas spyan drangs pa'i phur pa yang gsang bla med kyi skor/
byang gter nas rig 'dzin rgod ldem pas spyan drangs pa'i skor la/ bskyed pa mahA yo ga dang sgo 'brel ba phur pa lha khra'am che mchog gi skor/ lung a nu yo ga gzhir
bzhag pa'i phur pa lha nag gam/ drag sngags kyi skor/ rdzogs pa chen po a ti yo ga dang sgo 'brel ba'i phur pa lha 'dus sam/ dril bsgrub kyi skor rnams su yod cing / de
lta bu'i bka' brgyad rtsa ba dang bye brag gi lung man ngag rnams zhu ba'i sngon du/ rab chos skor de dang 'brel ba'i gter kha so so'i de dang de'i dbang thob pa zhig dgos
pa yin la/ de min na'ang sa lugs kyi yang phur sogs snga 'gyur gyi bka' ma lhad med gang rung zhig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa zhig dgos pa yin zhing / tha na'ang gsang
sngags gsar rnying gang rung gi bla med kyi dkyil 'khor gang rung gcig tu dbang bskur ba thob pa gcig nges pas dgos pa yin zhes rnying ma ba la mkhas pa'i rtsa brgyud
kyi bla ma rnams gsungs pa yin la/ 'dir skabs su babs pa phur ba yang gsang

bla med kyi skor rnams byung tshul ni/ 'dir smras pa/ grub pa'i dbang phyug padma 'byung gnas kyis/ /yang gsang spu gri'i chos skor zab mo 'di/ /lho phyogs gnam skas brag la
gter du sbas/ /dus phyis gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug gis/ /gter nas spyan drangs 'phrin las dar rgyas spel/ /de nas rim bzhin brgyud de rigs sngags 'chang / /tshe yi rig
'dzin dbang po ngag dbang lhas/ /rjes bzung rig pa 'dzin pa kun tu bzang / /snga 'gyur chos kyi nyi ma snyan grags kyi/ /rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i dpal 'byor bzang po can/
/gang de'i bar du legs par byon pa yi/ /zhes pa ltar las/ de lta bu'i rdo rje phur ba yang gsang spu gri'i gter chos rnams thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ bi to ta ma la 'bum
sde'i rgyud las bskal pa dum bu'i rgyud rtsa ba rdo rje khros pa phur pa'i khog dbub/ rdo rje phur pa yang gsang gi thun mong tshom bu'i sgrub pa/ rdo rje phur pa'i dbang
bskur yang gsang man ngag rdo rje phur pa yang gsang spu gri'i yang snying gsang sgrub kyi las byang / u rgyan gyi snying gtam yang gsang phur ba'i spyi sdom mtha' rgyas
ma'am gab pa zhus lan/ rdo rje phur pa'i lha khrid dkar po lam gyi sgron ma chos nyid gsal ba'i nyi ma/ 'khor sla thegs su lam du khyer ba'i khrid yig yang gsang spu gri
'bar ba'i sgrub thabs mngon rtogs rgyas pa/ phur pa glo bur bcog brdungs ral gri phyung brdeg tu bsgrub pa/ rdo rje phur pa yang gsang spu gri 'bar ba las dam can bcu gnyis
ming po dang bcas pa'i bskul/ rdo rje phur pa'i pho nya dang gdab las/ rdo rje phur pa'i srung ma dam can sde drug

gi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje phur pa'i las kha tshar ba/ rdo rje phur pa'i dgra bgegs 'dul ba'i las phran/ dam can spyi sgrub zab mo/ mgar gyi dpe/ zhal gdams/ zhal gdams gud du
gsungs pa/ rdo rje phur pa'i gdon 'dul/ rdo rje phur pa'i rtsa ba spu gri reg chod pa/ 'byung ba rang shar gyi rgyud lung bsgrub pa'i them yig rdo rje phur pa'i chad rkyen
tshe lung khrus lung gi dgongs pa bstan pa/ thugs kyi phur gcig ma phur pa'i snying tig yang gsang spu gri 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje phur pa'i rgyun gtor/ phur pa
dbang dang gzi brjid bskyed pa/ phur pa srog gi spu gri/ phur pa'i bstod pa khrag 'thung ma sogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ rdo rje gzhon nu/ gsang
ba'i bdag po/ rig 'dzin rdo rje chos/ mkha' 'gro las kyi dbang mo che/ pra bha ha ti/ padma saM bha wa/ mkha' 'gro mtsho rgyal/ chos dbang rin po che/ de'i sras padma dbang
chen/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ pra dznyA dhwa dza/ phag ston shAkya mgon po/ sprug ston dpal ldan mgon po/ mkhas grub chos rgyal mtshan/ chos rgyal bsod nams/ de'i sras
bsod nams bkra shis/ rin po che gzhon nu stobs ldan pa/ bo dong tshe ring dbang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
! /yang na sngags 'chang tshe ring dbang po/ srid gsum bla ma mahA maNDa dha ra/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /brgyud pa de las 'ongs pa'i
gshin rje tshe bdag gi las

tshogs/ yang bzlog nag po drag sngags spu gri'i 'khor lo/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi yang bzlog rdo rje pha lam sogs ratna gling pas gter nas spyan drangs pa'i man ngag gi yig
sna 'ga' zhig dang / gshin rje'i las tshogs lnga'i Da ki'i za yig rnam dgu 'khon sbyong an dar rdo lung ma spa gro skyer chu'i lha khang nas mnga' bdag nyang gis spyan
drangs pa/ byang zang zang lha brag nas rig 'dzin rgod ldem pas spyan drangs pa'i gu ru thugs sgrub kyi dpe tshan nyer gcig pa/ slob bu'i 'dod pa brtag thabs kyi man ngag
phyag rdor dregs pa kun 'dul la brten pa'i man ngag char 'bebs/ sprul sku padma gling pa'i gter chos/ gsol kha mtshon cha can gyi lag len nag po 'gro shes/ mngon spyod
dgra bo sgrol ba'i las kun la gces pa'i lag len yig chung zab rgya can/ gu ru 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ slob dpon padma/ gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes kyis phyi rabs bstan pa bsrung
ba'i mtshon char phung po ri bo cher sbas pa zhang khrom gyis gter nas bton pa rnams thos so/ /yang bzlog de rnams ni chos rje srid gsum pas bla ma dpal sding pa la
yang gsan gsungs/ 'dir smras pa/ pu Nya sA ga ra pra dzA ti shrI kSho tre/bsod nams rgya mtshos bskrun pa'i dpal zhing du/ /ra bI u da ya sya maNDa le ba pra kA shashtsa/nyi
ma 'char ka'i dkyil 'khor ltar gsal zhing / /karma sa hasta kandha mahA bhA sa/'phrin las 'od stong phung po cher 'bar ba/ /gu ru A nanda pA da sya padme nA ma/bla ma
kun dga'i zhabs kyi padmar 'dud/ /shes bya kun la mkhyen pa'i spyan mnga' zhing / /bde stong dga' bzhi ye shes thugs mnga' ba/ /srid zhi'i dpal 'byor

kun la mnga' brnyes pa'i/ /yongs 'dzin bla ma'i rnam thar bsam bzhin dad/ /thub dbang rgyal tshab dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis shing rta'i srol/
/ma lus chos kyi mdzod la dbang bsgyur ba'i/ /dam pa khyed 'drar bdag kyang 'gyur bar shog /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob
pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ chos kyi rje 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor gyi zhal snga nas rjes su bzung ba'i skabs
te drug pa'o// //sarba mangga laM// ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART VII: Teachings from Nags dgon sdom brtson dam pa sByin
pa grags pa; vol. kha, text no. 5, pp. 291-316

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las chos kyi rje
sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pas rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs so//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI tsakra sya nA tha dA na kirti nA ma ti shikShya shI le na sya ru tsi ra ma ma na ma/ bod skad du/ dpal 'khor lo'i mgon po sbyin pa grags pa zhes bya
ba'i bslab gsum khrims kyis mdzes pa de la bdag 'dud do/ /sha chang spangs sogs tshul khrims rnam dag cing / /bdag pas gzhan gces 'byongs pa'i sems dpa' che/ /sbyin pa la
sogs tshogs gnyis mthar phyin pa'i/ /snyan pa'i grags pa gsal der phyag bgyi 'o/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa chos kyi rje sdom brtson rigs sngags 'chang ba sbyin
pa grags pa'i drung du/ dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin mnos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar/ ! chos rgyal ma'i 'don thabs su grags pa'i 'jam dbyangs sa paN sbrags sgrub kyi bla ma'i
rnal 'byor thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ mkhan chen g.yag phrug

sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shes bya kun rig kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel/ chos rje kun dga' chos bzang / rje nor bu phun tshogs/ rje lha dbang blo gros/ chos rje blo gros
rab yangs/ chos rje sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /chos rje sangs rgyas rgya mtshos
mdzad pa'i 'jam dbyangs sa paN sbrags sgrub kyi yig cha'i lung yang thob/ ! /ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dbang byin rlabs zab mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe
dpag med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti phu ba/ ras chung ba/ mi la ras pa/ dwags po lha rje/ mtha' tsa ba/ 'bri khung pa/ spyan snga ba/ yang dgon pa/ spyan snga rin chen
dpal/ rje zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal/ chos rje

bde legs rin chen/ kun dga' dpal bzang / dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang po/ drin can dpal ldan mgon po/ chos rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog
lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rje
sangs rin/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ shrI ba blo gros rgyal mtshan/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na
sa lo/ paN chen lha dbang blo gros/ nub dgon pa sangs rgyas grags pa/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /kyai
rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang

bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'og min chen por sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / /zag med sgyu mar rdo rje bdag med ma/ /so wa na thar rnal 'byor dbang phyug che/ /u tsa ya nar
brtul zhugs nag po pa/ /kan pa gling du grub chen Da ma ru/ /mkha' 'gro rdzong du a wa dhu ti pa/ /kha rag thod bur ga ya dha ra'i zhabs/ /mu gu lung du sgra bsgyur 'brog
mi rje/ /mkhar chu chu khar se ston kun rig zhabs/ /sag thang ding du zhang ston dgon pa ba/ /kha gdang gnas su bla chen sa skya pa/ /chu mig rdzing khar bla chen bsod
nams rtse/ /sgo rum gnas su rje btsun grags pa'i zhabs/ /byang ngos sprul sder sa skya paNDi ta/ /lha khang lho ru 'phags pa rin po che/ /skyed 'phrang gnas su zhang ston
dkon mchog dpal/ /na bza' brag phug dgon par bsod nams dpal/ /bsam yas dkar por 'gro

mgon bsod nams mtshan/ /byang chub rdzong du mtshungs med blo gros brtan/ /shar stod gnas su dpal ldan tshul khrims zhabs/ /zhe dgon gong mar grub chen buddha shrI/ /e wa~M
dgon par kun mkhyen kun dga'i mtshan/ /bsam gtan phug tu mus chen sems dpa' che/ /byang chub gling du rje btsun kun dbang pa/ /e wa~M thar rtser rje btsun dkon mchog 'phel/
/bde ba can du sangs rgyas rin chen zhabs/ /dpal ldan sa skyar 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rje/ /e wa~M gnas su dkon mchog lhun grub mtshan/ /thar pa rtse ru sangs rgyas seng
ge'i zhabs/ /yol dgon gnas su blo gros chos 'phags pa/ /mnga' ris dgon par kun dga' lung rigs zhabs/ /dben gnas nags dgon yang rtser sbyin pa grags/ /de yis rjes bzung
ngag dbang kun bsod do/ /yang na chos rje sa skya paN chen nas/ /spyi mo lung du tshogs bsgom kun dga' dpal/ /nyan po gong mar nyan chen bsod nams brtan/ /dkar po brag tu
rin chen seng ge'i zhabs/ /bla ma dpal ldan pa man gong dang 'dra/ /yang na/ mus chen/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ gsum kas rjes su
bzung ba dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha mchog seng ge ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje
btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na mus chen/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen

man 'dra/ yang na/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na/ sems dpa'
chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun spangs chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mkhas pa'i dbang po klu sgrub rgya mtsho/
sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang / glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje
kun dga' grol mchog mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ blo gros rgyal mtshan/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /dpal kyai rdo rje'i rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa/ rje btsun gyi dag ldan/ shar chen gyi dag ldan go sla dang bcas pa'i
steng nas tshul bzhi sngon du 'gro ba'i bshad bka' rgyas par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ Dombhi he ru ka a la
badzra/ dpal ldan nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa dza ya shrI/ slob dpon sbyangs dka' zla ba/ de la slob ma'i mchog dpa' bo rdo rje/ seng ge rdo rje/ sgra gcan
'dzin dang gsum las/ 'dir dge slong dpa' bo rdo rje/ des lo tsA ba chen po shAkya ye shes la gnang / de la 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/
se mkhar chung ba kun rig 'khyin lo

tsA ba 'od kyi snang ba dang bzhi las/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa chen/ yang na bla ma mnga' ris pa/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ dgra lha 'bar/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ yang na
se 'khar chung ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa chen/ 'khyin lo tsA ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa skya pa chen po'o/ /de ltar brgyud pa'i bka' bab bzhi dang
ldan pa'i bla ma sa skya pa chen pos/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ tshul khrims grags/ gtsug tor rgyal po gsum la gnang / de gsum kas rje btsun grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ des chos rje sa skya pa paNDi ta chen po la/ des 'phags pa rin po che la/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ chos rje brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma blo gros brtan
pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug chos rje grags pa mtha' yas/ mus chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sdom brtson dam
pa sbyin pa grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan
man 'dra/ yang na/ ngor chen/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po gnyis ka la/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug pa dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge de gnyis ka la 'dren
mchog ratna

wardha/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen/ sa paNDi ta/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ rje ratna ni ra bho
Sha man 'dra/ rgyud sde spyi rnam rje btsun rtse mos mdzad pa/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi mdzad pa'i ljon shing / stong thun sa bcad/ rgyud sde'i dum bu/ yab yum
gyi bstod pa gnyis/ bdag med bstod pa'i 'grel pa sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ kye rdor rgyud kyi byung tshul ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun bzang gis mdzad pa/ tshul bzhi'i rnam
gzhag glo bo mkhan chen pas mdzad pa/ 'grel pa dag ldan/ dag ldan kha skong / dag ljon lung 'grel shar pas mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs tshul gsum mdzes rgyan/ ljon shing mdzes
rgyan rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi mdzad pa rnams kyi lung thos so/ ! /gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i rjes gnang mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ dpal bde/ dri med sbas pa/ ratna badzra/ ratna kirti/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo tsA
ba/ bla ma gnam kha 'ub pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sa chen/ rje btsun/ byang chub dpal/ bde ba dpal/ grags pa gzhon nu/ bsod nams grags pa/ grags pa tshul khrims/ shes rab
rdo rje/ rgyal bzang pa/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge shar pa ye rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha
mchog seng

ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa
rje btsun gyis mdzad pa thos/ ! /yang bla ma chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du/ phyag na rdo rje gtum po khyung chen thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i
bdag po/ klu sgrub zhabs/ paNDi ta 'bar ba'i gtso/ grub chen zhing gi rdo rje/ rngog lo chen po shes rab grags/ sras slob dpon bha wa/ gtsang ston smra ba'i seng ge rnal
'byor dbang phyug mdo sde seng ge grub ston shAkya gzhon nu/ lce blo ldan seng ge lce btsun bsod nams dpal/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje/ de'i sras rdo rje seng ge de'i
sras rin chen seng ge de'i sras shAkya seng ge lce btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug sangs rgyas seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom
brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/'di ni phyag rdor gtum chen lha nyer gcig gi dbang gi brgyud pa bzhin bris pa yin la/ rjes gnang rkyang pa'i brgyud pa zhig da dung btsal
bar bya'o/ /'di'i gong gi brgyud pa 'ga' zhig brtag des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /mi g.yo ba sngon po'i rjes gnang chu srung dang bcas pa
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa mched/ ba ri ba/ sa chen/ rje btsun bsod rtse/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags
pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor

chen kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags
pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /mi g.yo ba dkar po'i sgrub thabs yon tan khris mdzad pa'i gsal byed yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis
mdzad pa la sems dpa' gsum brtsegs kyi sgom tshul bogs 'don sdigs mdzub kyi sbyor ba/ leb rgan dar gyi sbyor ba/ bsnyen sgrub kyi bar chad bsal ba/ grib sel/ rtsod pa
las rgyal thabs kyi las tshogs rnams kyi yi ge'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mi g.yo ba/ 'od byed 'byung gnas dpal/ kha che paN chen dA la shi la/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/
'dul 'dzin byang sems pa/ rgyal tsha chos dbang ba/ rgyal tsha gzhon nu grags/ mkhan chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ g.yag ston sangs rgyas dpal ba/ rong ston shes bya kun rig
paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shrI ba blo gros rgyal mtshan/ sdom brtson dam
pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /dA na shI las mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / sgrub thabs bstod pa sogs mkhas pa yon tan khris
mdzad pa rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ ! /ri khrod ma lo ma gyon ma'i sgrub thabs bum chog dang bcas pa chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa/ de la brten nas

grong khyer du rims nad gcod pa'i man ngag dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che
ba/ chung ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ brag phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ shar pa sku mched/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ bla ma ri khrod pa/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje
sangs rgyas seng ge rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'jam dbyangs smra seng
gi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ dam pa rgya gar ba/ kha che gu hya pa/ rlan bsgom yab sras/ slob dpon 'od shAka pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ skyi ston/

rin chen grags/ rgya

dmar dbang phyug grags pa chos kyi sengge / gtsang nag brtson 'grus sengge / dan bag dar seng / gnyal zhig 'jam rdor/ zad pa dar tshul/ dge bshes gra thang pa/ bla ma dam pa

mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas sengge/ rje blo gros chos grags/ rje kun dga' lung
rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /rje btsun sa skya pa gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum phal cher gyi lung thos

rnam grangs la/ rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams la bstod pa/ shar chen la bstod pa lnga/ grub chen buddha shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ mkhan chen bkra shis rin chen/ lo chen rin chen

/ lam

'bras/ bsam mi khyab/ lhan cig skyes grub/ mchod rten drung thob/ yi ge med pa/ padma badzra'i lam/ gtum mo lam rdzogs/ yon po bsrang ba/ indra bhu ti'i lam/ bde mchog rim
lnga/ rtsa dbu ma'i ring brgyud/ bde mchog dkar po/ mahA ma ya'i spros med/ gsang 'dus rim lnga 'gos lugs/ ra rtse sems 'dzin/ shin tu spros med/ spyod 'jug zhen pa bzhi
bral rnams kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ shes phyin dkar mo/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil chog 'dod rgyal/ tshogs bdag 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil
chog gtsug tor/ nor rgyun ma'i dkyil chog gi cho ga sa skya pa'i bka' srung rnams la bstod pa/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga sa skya paNDi ta/ grub chen buddha shrI/ sa bzang
'phags pa rnams kyi rnam thar/ gsan yig chen mo/ lam 'bras chos 'byung rtsom 'phro/ bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ zhus lan gsang ba'i sa bcad/ dbang bzhi'i rtogs bskyed/
mngon rtogs tshul bzhi'i sdom tshig phyi nang gi bskyed rim dbang dang bcas pa'i sdom tshig nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bir bsrung bar chad kun sel/ sku'i rnam 'gyur
drug gi zin bris/ bir bsrung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ de'i nyams len/ de dang lam 'bras mtshan mtshon sbyar ba/ bir bsrung gsar ma/ lus dkyil rtsod spong
che chung / rgyud gsum gnod 'joms rtsa 'grel/ zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi sa mtshams bshad pa/ kyai rdo rje'i rgyud kyi byung tshul dang / bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam

thar/ brtag gnyis kyi 'gyur chad bsabs pa shlau ka gnyis/ brtag gnyis 'grel pa'i dkar chag kyai rdor Dombhi lugs kyi sgrub thabs/ 'phrin yig dbang po'i rdo rje/ gzhal yas khang
gi tshad rnam par bzhag pa/ 'phar ma gnyis kyi don bshad pa/ mtsho skyes dang Dombhi lugs kyi tho yig sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi bsdus don/ bstod pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel
pa/ mtsho skyes lugs kyi maNDal mchod chog bskyed rim gnad kyi zla zer/ gtor chog gi 'grel pa/ 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ shes phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ gur rigs
bsdus kyi sbyin sreg gar gyi shan 'byed/ sangs rgyas kyi gar/ phyogs bzhi gtor ma'i btang thabs/ chos skyong gi man ngag rnams kyi dkar chag mgon rkyang gi sgrub thabs rgyud
'grel las phyung ba/ lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / gtor chog dgra las rnam rgyal/ gtor sgrub kyi man ngag thugs dam bskangs pa'i cho ga kyai rdor bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/
sambhu Ta rdo rje dbyings kyi sgrub thabs/ gtor chog mchod phreng / dkyil chog sbyin sreg bkra shis/ tshogs 'khor gsang ba kun rgyan/ tshogs 'khor kun bzang rnam rol/
bde mchog bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga bde mchog pho brang gi rnam gzhag ril bu la brten nas mkha' spyod bsgrub pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs dang / bde mchog dkar
po'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs cho ga dang bcas pa/ rdo rje lha mo'i tshe sgrub/ la wa pa bcu gsum ma'i mngon rtogs kyi tho/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs kyi tho/ za byed
rdo rje mkha'

'gro'i sbyin sreg mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs/ gtso bo yab yum gyi sgrub thabs/ sngags phreng mchan ma/ dkyil chog mchod phreng / gsang
'dus mi bskyod pa'i sgrub thabs/ shin tu rnal 'byor gyi khyad par/ gtor chog mchod phreng / rdo rje sems dpa'i mchod chog dkyil chog sbyin sreg rab gnas/ bkra shis/ rdo
rje phreng ba'i sa bzung gi cho ga dgra nag gi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i char 'bebs/ 'jigs byed kyi gtor chog 'jigs byed kyi rdzogs rim/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/ de'i
dag pa/ sgrub thabs kyi lung sbyor/ dkyil mchog spros med mdzes rgyan/ kun rig dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs/ gzhan phan mtha' yas rdul tshon kha skong / cha
gsum gtor ma/ dkyil 'khor sgo sbrags kyi bshad pa/ spyod rgyud spyi rnam/ bya rgyud spyi rnam/ mi 'khrugs pa'i sgo nas gshin po rjes 'dzin/ 'od zer dri med kyi dkyil chog
dri med lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang / 'od dpag med kyi tshe sgrub/ seng ge sgra/ sna tshogs yum/ rma bya chen mo/ so sor 'brang ma/
'byung po 'dul byed/ rta mgrin rnams kyi sgrub thabs/ sman bla'i mchod chog sems bskyed rang gis blang pa'i cho ga mchod sbyin chen po'i zin bris/ gtor chen gyi lhan thabs/
