dkar chag mdor

bsdus shig rdo rje theg pa'i bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chag mtshan nyid bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chag rje btsun gong ma gsum gyi bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag rang gi grwa sa spyi la gdams
pa/ sa bzang pa bsod nams dpal/ lo tsA ba rdo rje dpal/ dge 'dun mgon/ a mo gha/ bla chen chos rin pa/ gling 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsam 'grub rgyal mtshan/ slob
dpon sa bzang / dbu ma pa shes rab rgya mtsho/ mdo stod pa dge bzang rnams kyi dris lan/ sde snod 'dzin pa ratna shrI la gdams pa/ gsang sngags pa kun dga' gzhon nu la gdams
pa/ bla ma sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gdams pa gnyis/ byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa shlau ka gcig rgya rong pa bkra shis dpal la gdams pa/ sgrub
pa po blo bzang la gdams pa gnyis/ nyag re sangs grags la gdams pa/ paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen la springs pa/ bal yul ye rang gi paNDi ta shrI ma no bo dhi yab sras la
springs pa/ dpon po rgyal mtshan dpal yab yum sras bcas la gdams pa/ ya tshe rgyal po hasti rA dza yab yum sras bcas la gdams pa/ de'i blon po la gdams pa'i shlau ka gcig
a ya dbang phyug bkra shis la gdams pa/ dpon rgan thar pa ye shes la gdams pa/ slob dpon bzod chen la bstod pa/ phyi nang gi yas gtam/ theg pa chen po'i smon lam/ gser 'od
dam pa las btus pa'i smon lam/ der ma thus pa chos rje shar pa'i rnam thar/ mngon byang gi bshad pa/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i rnam bshad/ rnal

'byor rgyud kyi spyi rnam rtsom 'phro/ kyai rdo rje'i mngon rtogs bsdus pa/ bka' shog thor bu ba kha yar rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal

grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags

pa gnyis/ phan mdzad ma/ 'phags pa'i bstod pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang la bstod pa/ rgyal tshab dam pa la bstod pa tshan pa gsum/ kun mkhyen la bstod pa/ 'dren mchog la bstod

chos rje dpal ldan pa la

la bstod pa/ bla ma kun brtson pa la bstod pa/ chos rje gang ba bzang po la bstod pa/ mkhan chen dkon mchog chos skyabs la bstod pa/ bla ma tshul khrims dpal la bstod pa/

yin thang la zhib tu gzigs pa'i bris yig rgyal

tshab dam pa'i rnam thar/ mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng ge'i rnam thar/ chos rje tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar/ rje nyid kyi rnam thar zhus lan ma/ chos rje
shar pa'i gdung brgyud kyi byon tshul/ spyi rnam gsal byed/ ljon shing gsal byed/ 'og ma'i stug po bkod pa'i rgyan/ gnod sbyin kha pa ra'i lo rgyus/ mngon par rtogs pa'i
tho yig chos sna so dgu'i grangs 'dren tshul/ rgyu dus kyi dbang gi sngon du gsungs pa'i gsung rgyun/ rnal 'byor ma kun spyod kyi 'chad thabs/ dpal mngon par rtogs pa'i sa
bcad/ mahA ma ya'i bsdus don/ rtog pa bdun pa'i bsdus don/ rnam rgyal gyi rtog pa che ba'i bsdus don/ rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi dkar chag rnal 'byor ma yi bkra shis/
lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi ngag 'don/ kyai rdor mngon rtogs bsdus pa/ phur pa'i sgrub thabs/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs/ de'i dkyil chog mngon rtogs yan lag drug
pa'i dka' gnas bsdus pa/ 'jigs byed bcu bdun ma/ la wa pa/ bong zhal can/ drag po sgrol dbang / dgra gdong / 'khor chen/ gdong drug rnams kyi dbang gi tho re re/ spros med
rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ spros med kyi khrid yig gdugs dkar can gyi mngon rtogs/ phyir bzlog so 'brang gi mngon rtogs/ gdugs dkar can/ tshe dpag med/ gza' yum/ kyai rdor
nag po pa rnams kyi dbang gi tho re re/ gdugs dkar can gyi gtor chog bsrung ba lnga yi dbang tho/ 'od zer can gyi dbang tho/ bcu gcig zhal gyi sgrub thabs/ spyan

ras gzigs kyi sgom thabs chung ba/ don zhags dpa' gcig gi rjes gnang / chab gtor gyi tho/ so 'brang gi rjes gnang gi tho/ seng ge sgra'i gdon 'grol/ mchod rten bsgrub pa'i
tho/ gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i mngon rtogs nyin zhi mtshan khro'i 'don thabs/ sgrol ma gser mdog can gyi sgrub thabs/ dug sel ma yi sgrub thabs/ rnam rgyal gyi rjes gnang

'bring po/ rnam sras kyi rjes gnang / rnam 'joms/ ma Ni badzra gyi gtor 'bum/ phyag rdor gtum po'i sgom bzlas/ 'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes gnang / mi g.yo ba'i rjes
gnang / sgrub thabs/ sha wa ri'i rjes gnang / 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang / 'jam dbyangs smra seng gi rjes gnang / gang blo ma'i rjes gnang / sangs rgyas klu dbang

gsung rgyun/ sems bskyed kyi cho ga nA ro pa nas brgyud pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga yas gtam rin chen rnam spel/ rig gter gyi nyer mkho mtha' gnyis gsal

shis mgon la

phul ba/ a seng rdo rje brtan pa la phul ba snga phyi bdun/ mnga' bdag grags pa rgyal mtshan la phul ba/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyi gdung rgyud gu ge thar po la phul ba gnyis/

bzhi/ yid 'byung ba'i tshigs bcad/ rdo rje 'dzin dbyangs las btus pa/ a seng la phul ba gnyis/ rje'i mdzad 'phrin gyi mchod brjod/ bla ma bzang po ba la gdams pa/ yang dgongs

dpon po tshe bzang gi shes

zhus lan/ kun rig gi bsnyen pa byed tshul/ der ma thus pa la brgal lan tshig don mun sel/ bstan bcos sdom gsum rab dbye'i dris lan lung gi tshad ma/ mkhas pa rnams 'jug
pa'i sgo'i rnam par bshad pa rig gnas gsal byed/ bla ma dmar chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar/ grub ston yon tan dpal dang / la ru ba bsod nams seng ge'i rnam thar sogs bka'
'bum dkar chag nang bzhin thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ chos rje blo gros bzang po/ rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags
pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na chos rje blo gros bzang po/ rje thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun
grub/ rje

nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dharmA ba/ ma ho padhya ya/ des bdag la'o/ ! /bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i bstan pa spyi'i chos 'byung chen mo/ rang gi slob ma la gdams pa'i bu
ston snying thur/ rgyud sde spyi rnam chen mo rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ bla ma chos dpal/ mkhas pa tsandra pa/ rje tshul khrims
rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang mkhyen rab rje/ chos rje rin chen rgyal po/ bla ma don grub rgyal mtshan/ rje byang gling pa/ rje kun dga' lung rigs/ sdom brtson dam pa sbyin
pa grags pa/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rje byang gling pa'i rjes su/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
bikShu paNDai pa dharmA swa mi las kyang zhib tu mnos so/ /'dir smras pa/ sardha shwa ra dA na kirti ya na ma/grub pa'i dbang phyug sbyin pa grags la 'dud/ /a haM te
pra pA do da dha/bdag kyang khyed kyi bka' drin chu gter las/ /rYu ba nArdza sa dA dza ra/lang tsho'i 'dam skyes nam yang ma rgud cing / /sha gandhasatra sha bha Sha tu/legs
bshad dri bsung pad tshal khyab pa lags/ /slar yang sbyin sogs thun mong nyams len dang / /rmad byung sngags kyi lam gyis rang gi rgyud/ /grol nas grags pa gsal ldan
sa skya pa'i/ /bstan 'dzin gsung gi 'phrin las spel bar shog /sbyin bya dbang bzhi rgyud pa rnam dag las/ /legs 'ongs smin grol nyams len mthar phyin cing / /snyan par rab
grags skyes bu dam pa yi/ /rnam thar 'dzin pa khyed 'drar bdag gyur cig /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las

dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ rje nags dgon pa sdom brtson dam pa sbyin pa grags pa'i zhal
snga nas rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te bdun pa'o// //mangga laM// ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART VIII: Teachings from dBang
phyug rab brtan (1559-1636); vol. kha, text no. 6, pp. 317-376

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las chos kyi rje
nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun dbang phyug rab brtan gyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ pra Na mya Na shrI wa ra dI buddha shtsa dA ya sya badzra tsarYe shwa ra pra tiddha sya banda naM kA ro mi/ bod skad du/ dpal mchog dang po'i sangs rgyas
dang gnyis su med pa'i rdo rje slob dpon dbang phyug rab brtan la gus pas phyag bgyi'o/ /mtshungs med sa skya'i rje btsun mchog rnams kyi/ /snyan brgyud gdams pa rgya mtsho'i
mnga' bdag mchog /nyams dang rtogs pa'i gter chen grub dbang che/ /skal bzang yongs kyi mgon khyod phyag gi gnas/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa sa skya pa'i man
ngag gser chos su grags pa'i gdams pa snyan brgyud zab mo kun gyi chos kyi gter chen po grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan gyi drung du dam pa'i chos thos pa la/ thog mar/
! /rig 'dzin rgod kyi ldem 'phru can nas brgyud pa'i tshe dbang lcags gdong ma thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos

sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rgyal ba rigs lnga/ sprul sku phyag na rdo rje/ smug nag dbang gi mkha' 'gro/ tshangs pa'i rgyal po gdong gsum pa/ rig 'dzin lha dbang brgya
byin/ rig 'dzin klu rgyal 'jog po/ skal ldan rgyal po dza/ mkhas pa shAkya pra bha/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ bal po shi la manydzu/ mkha' 'gro
ye shes mtsho rgyal/ sprul sku rig 'dzin chen po/ sras mchog rnam rgyal mgon po/ sngags 'chang rdo rje dpal/ mtshan ldan byams pa bshes gnyen/ bla ma sangs rgyas dpal
bzang / sngags 'chang chos rgyal bsod nams/ sngags 'chang chos skyong bsod nams/ drin can tshar pa chos rje/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag
dbang phyug rab brtan/'di la gu ru mtshan brgyad kyi gsol 'debs la gsung

gdangs mdzad cing tshe mda' la dar dmar po btags pas g.yob pa sogs mdzad kyin 'dug des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi
drung du/ gzungs grwa lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang ngam rigs gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri ba/ gnyan ston
grags/ gnyan rin chen grags/ lha sa'i gnas brtan dkon rgyal/ de'i sras rdog ston bya'u rgyal/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ rong pa sher seng / kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston
thams cad mkhyen pa/ lce nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje ka bzhi pa chen po/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje rdo ring pa/ tshar pa chos rje/ mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhan chen
bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ yab sras de gsum la/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab

brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'khon sa skya pa'i yab chos dpal yang dag he ru ka mar me dgu par grags pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku dga' rab rdo rje/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ ro langs bde ba'i
dngos grub/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ slob dpon hU~M ka ra/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ bal po shI la manydzu/ sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms/
gnyal dznyA na ku ma ra/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal po/ gtsug tor shes rab/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / bal po shAkya blo gros/ shes rab
tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal

po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun
dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros dpung rgyan mdzes pa'i tog dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/
mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ mtshungs med nam
mkha' blo gros/ chag lo tsA ba rin chen chos kyi rgyal po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga'
bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na nye brgyud ni/ dpal he ru ka slob dpon hU~M ka ra/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/
'khon klu'i dbang po bsrung ba/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen man gong bzhin/ yang na sa chen kun dga' snying po nas/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa shes rab blo gros/ gan pa chos
rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang rje btsun de nyid kyi drung du/ sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur thun mong gi rdzogs rim
gyi man ngag zab mo rdzogs pa chen po a ti yo ga'i khrid nyams khrid du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ mkha' 'gro las kyi dbang mo che/ grub chen hU~M
ka ra/ slob dpon padma 'byung

gnas/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ bal po shI la manydzu/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ jo mo mkhar chen mtsho rgyal/ mkhar chen dpal gyi dbang phyug sna nam rdo rje bdud
'joms/ chim ston shAkya pra bha/ shud bu dpal gyi seng ge nyang ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rba sgom blo gros dbang phyug ldang ma lhun gyi rgyal mtshan/ lce btsun seng ge
dbang phyug grub thob gcer sgom chen po/ slob dpon gnyer sgom chen po/ go rub rin chen chos kyi dbang phyug mtshungs med shes rab rin chen/ 'bri phyug pa rin chen 'bum/ yar
klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog mnyam med sangs rgyas gling pa nam mkha' bsod nams/ zhal bu ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rin po che nam mkha'
rdo rje/ rje bla ma grub pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang chos rgyal/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag grub pa mchog gi ded dpon dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa
ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba'o/ /yang na chos rgyal 'phags pa yan chad sa skya pa'i zab chos rdo rje phur pa'i stod las byang chub bsgrub pa'i
dbang dang 'dra la/ de nas brgyud lugs gzhan 'ga' zhig las brgyud de 'ongs pa/ theg chen chos rjes ched gnyer du ma mdzad de gsan pa las/ de nyid kyi drung du yar klung
pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis gsan te mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog la gnang zhing / de nas bsam gtan gling pa man chad gong dang 'dra'o/ /'di'i yig skor gyi lung thob
pa'i chos kyi

rnam grangs la/ rdzogs chen gyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs spyi gtsug nyi zla ma/ de'i brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ chos 'byung bdud rtsi'i khungs 'byin/ rje btsun bsam gtan gling
pa'i bstod pa/ de'i rnam thar mnal lam ma rje rang gis mdzad pa/ yang dag rtsa ba'i gzhung / ru lu ser phreng thugs kyi lde mig khrid kyi zin bris sa bcad 'gro kun dga'
bskyed/ khrid yig chen mo'i lam rim thar pa'i sgo 'byed/ rje bsam gtan gling pa'i gsung rgyun zin bris su btab pa/ rin po che rlung gi phra thig bsam gtan gol sa gcod
pa/ rim pa gnyis la 'jug pa'i sgo/ phur pa rtsa dum/ phur pa rtsa dum gyi rgyud bshad kyi zin bris/ rje bsam gtan gling pa'i gsung rgyun lung bsdus/ zab mo lung gi phreng
ba/ bsam gtan mig gi sgron ma/ sngon gyi mkhas pas mdzad pa'i rdzogs chen rtsod spong nas bsdus pa'i yi ge ste rdzogs chen a ti yo ga'i glegs bam yongs su rdzogs pa nos/
! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdams pa dmar mo skor gsum du grags pa las/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen nA ro pa/ pham thing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa/ chos rje
bla ma dam pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye

rgyal/ ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rdo ring rin po che/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs
pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /sa skya pa'i gser chos mkha' spyod bsgrub pa'i man ngag zab mo thun mong
ma yin pa'i bsam mi khyab/ rnal 'byor ma'i lus dkyil bsgom tshul gyi yig chung zab mo/ rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig rje mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i steng nas nyams khrid
lung dang bcas pa nos so/ ! /indra mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/
grub chen lwa ba pa/ indra bhu ti/ lcam legs smin ka ra/ bram ze bi ru ba/ sha wa ri/ mai tri pa/ rgya gar phyag na/ bal po bha ran ru rtse/ bal po ye shes rdo rje/ bla ma
sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog
dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ theg chen chos rgyal/ gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ nyi lde ba ngag dbang grags pa/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang

rdo rje rnal 'byor ma rig pa can ma'am/ mai tri mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs spru lung pa'i yi ge'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dpa' bo
spyan ras gzigs/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ ri khrod blo gros/ mai tri pa/ rgya gar phyag na/ ka ma la badzra/ dza ya se na/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun
grags pa/ chos rje paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos rgyal/ gu shrI nam
mkha' bzang po/ nyi lde ba ngag dbang grags pa/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen
brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung
du/ dpyal lugs kyi phag mo skor gsum du grags pa/ zhal gnyis ma/ don grub ma/ dbu bcad ma gsum gyi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor
ma/ lakShiM ka ra/legs smin zer/ bram ze birWa pa/ slob dpon a wa dhu ti/ grub chen ldong ngar ba ting 'dzin rdo rje/ bsod snyoms pa chung ba ting 'dzin bzang po/ bal po
bha rantra ru tsi/ ha ngu dkar po yang zer/ dpyal lo kun dga' rdo rje/ zar ston A tsarYa/ gtsang yang dag rdo rje/ dbus pa shes rab rdo rje/ lce thams cad mkhyen pa mdo
sde seng ge gru shAkya 'bum/ lce blo ldan seng ge lce btsun

bsod nams dpal/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje/ spos khang pa 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen dga' gdong pa chos rgyal dpal bzang / 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal
mtshan/ zhwa lu sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs
pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /de ltar phag mo zhal gnyis ma sogs la phag zhal dngos su yod pas rdo rje
phag mor 'jog pa 'thad mod/ gzhan nA ro mkha' spyod sogs la phag zhal med pas phag mor 'jog pa ji ltar rigs snyam pa'i dogs pa dpyod ldan la 'byung la/ rang gi bsam tshod
ni zhal gnyis ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma thams cad kyi rtsa ba'i lha dang / gzhan 'dir bshad pa'i sangs rgyas mkha' 'gro ma dang / mai tri mkha' spyod/ nA ro mkha' spyod
la sogs pa la phag zhal dngos su med kyang zhal gnyis pa rtsa bar byas nas de las gyes pa lta bu'i lha yin pas phag mor bzhag pa yin te/ sgrub thabs rnams kyi nang nas kyang
zhal gnyis ma 'di thog mar 'byung zhing / rnal 'byor ma gzhan gyi sgrub thabs 'di'i rjes su 'byung ba yin no/ /de skad du rje btsun rin po che grags pa'i rnal 'byor byang
seng gi dris las las/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma thams cad kyi rtsa ba lta bur rgyal po indra bhu tis mdzad pa'i phag mo zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs las zhes gsungs pas kyang
shes nus so/ /mdor na phag mo gzhan rnams ni phag mo'i

rigs las byung ba la phag mor bzhag pa yin no/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du/ sa skya pa'i khyad par gyi gdams pa dmar po skor gsum du grags pa'i chos skor thob
pa la/ thog mar rje btsun ma ku ru kulle thun mong ba'i rjes gnang dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun rig byed ma/
rgyal po lhan skyes rol pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba/ rdo rje gdan pa a mo gha badzra/ lo chen rin chen grags/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun
rin po che/ rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ 'u yug pa kun bsod/ nyi thog pa kun smon/ bla ma yon tan dpal/ bu lung pa kun rdor/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ brag phug pa
chen po/ ri khrod pa blo brtan/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa/ de gnyis la tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i
mnga' bdag rje btsun dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ bdag med ma/ bi ru pa/ nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ gnyis spangs
zhabs/ ga ya dha ra/ bla chen 'brog se ston/ zhang ston/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ glo bo shes rab rin chen/
'phags pa rin po che/ rgyal tshab chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa

yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang man
'dra/ ! /yang ku ru kulle thun mong ma yin pa gsang sgrub lha lnga'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i byin rlabs so 'jigs med grags pa sogs kyi yig cha'i steng nas thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje snying po/ Da ki ni su bha gi Dombhi he ru ka tsa na wa/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri lo tsA ba/
bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla
ma mnyam med chen po/ gzungs kyi dpal ba/ yar klung pa khu dbon/ pha brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ bla ma blo gros rnam rgyal/ phyogs las rnam par rgyal
ba'i lha/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhas pa gzhon nu stobs ldan/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i gsal byed dbang bzhi'i dmigs
pa sbyar ba dang / de gnyis ka'i gsal byed rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang dpal tshogs kyi bdag
po'i thun mong ba'i rjes gnang rje rdo rje

'chang gi yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ grub chen sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ grub chen sha wa ri/ bal po hU~M ka ra/ mal
lo blo gros grags/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ rje skyobs pa dpal/ rong pa shes rab sengge
/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ nyi lde pa ngag
dbang grags pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ de gnyis char la tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug
nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /khams gsum dbang bsdud tshogs kyi bdag po'i rjes
gnang thun mong ma yin pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha wa ri pa/ hang ngu ka ra/ mal lo tsa ba/ bla ma sa skya
pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ yang na/ bi ru pa/ nag po
pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a wa dhu ti pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla chen sa skya pa/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa
paN/ khams sgom byang chub dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod la bla chen kun

blo dang / brag phug pas gsan/ de gnyis la chos rje bla mas gsan/ de la yar klung pa/ yang na rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar
klung pa khu dbon/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhas pa
gzhon nu stobs ldan/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang nor lha'i gtso bo dbang bsdud
'dod pa'i rgyal po'i thun mong ba 'dod pa lha'i rjes gnang dang / thun mong ma yin pa gsang sngags sgra'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal mchog rdo rje chos/ yum
bde ba rgyas byed ma/ grub chen dze tA ri/ la li ta badzra/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ rdo rje gdan pa/ tha bi ra/ ba ri ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/
rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa khu dbon/
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo ring pa/ rje sgo rum pa/ de gnyis la tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen brtse
dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang jo bo rje nas brgyud pa tshogs bdag
dkar po gtso 'khor bzhi pa'i rjes

gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ indra bhu ti/ rgyal po grags pa/ byang chub 'byung gnas/ rin po che 'od zer/ yang dag sbyin pa/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ jo bo rje/ rgya brtson
seng / grub thob shol po ba/ sangs rgyas dbon ston pa/ sangs rgyas ston tshul/ khyung tshangs pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon grags tshul/ snar thang mkhan
po nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ dbu ma grub pa brtson 'grus/ bla ma ka bcu pa/ gung pa bkra shis bzang po/ gnyag phug pa bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog
pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen
brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /de ltar rje btsun sa skya pa
yab sras rnams la bka' babs pa'i dmar po skor gsum gyi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang rnams sngon du song nas/ nor lha so so'i man ngag gi chos skor yongs
rdzogs thob pa las/ thog mar rje btsun ma ku ru kulle'i chos skor la/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus rjes gnang dang bcas pa dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa/ yang lo rgyus kyi
yi ge lugs gcig thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i zur 'debs gzungs kyi dpal ba'i gsung las buddha shrIs zin bris su bkod pa/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs las sbyor
sngags btu rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis las phyung

ba/ sgrub thabs kyi rgya gzhung rgyal po lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ lhan skyes sgeg pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ sgrub thabs ku ma ra bo dhis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs ma taM kis mdzad pa/ man ngag chen po lnga zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa dA na shi las bsgyur pa/ shAkya
mtshos mdzad pa'i man ngag chen po lnga dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi gdams pa rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ mngon
rtogs 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ las sbyor gyi yi ge paNDi ta don yod rdo rjes ba ri lo tsA ba la gnang ba/ nus pa ma nyams pa khams gsum dbang du byed pa sogs dang
/ rdzas sbyor gyi yi ge ba ri ba'i gsung / gtor ma'i cho ga tshigs bcad ma nyung ngu / sbyin sreg gi yi ge tshigs bcad ma/ sngags kyi zhal shes/ bris sku'i man ngag gsung
rdo rje ma'i lag 'gul/ ku ru kulle gzhon nu ma'i man ngag bka' sdod pho nya mo'i yi ge ku ru kulle sngon mo char 'bebs kyi yi ge sgrub thabs nag po 'gro shes/ khams gsum
dbang du bsdu ba'i gnad yig ganggI chu rgyun/ 'khor lo'i yig chung / nang sgrub kyi skor ba/ khams gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub
kyis mdzad pa bai ro tsa nas bsgyur pa/ de'i lag len gyi yig sna ko sa lar 'khrungs pa'i brtul zhugs spyod pa rnam par snang mdzad rdo rje'i gdams ngag 'khor wa ru Na'i
char chog char chog yig sna/ de'i zhal shes/ char 'bebs dang

rgyal po dbang du bsdu ba sogs kyi yi ge sgrub thabs kyi sa bcad/ mngon rtogs ngag 'don chung ngu / grub chen Dombhi he ru ka nas brgyud pa'i gsang sgrub kyi chos skor la/
sindhu ra'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga tshigs bcad ma/ byin rlabs kyi lag len shin tu gsal ba bla ma mnyam med chen pos mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs/ bstod pa Dombhi he ru kas mdzad
pa/ bsnyen pa'i yi ge sgrub pa dang las sbyor gyi yi ge bsnyen sgrub las gsum chig dril gyi gdams pa shin tu zab pa/ de rnams kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i zhal shes/ zhal shes
kyi yig chung / yig chung gi yang yig rje btsun ma ku ru kulle'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub las sbyor dang bcas pa'i yi ge shin tu rgyas pa dngos grub 'byung
gnas zhes bya ba shar dwags po'i paNDi ta bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ gnyan lo tsA bas paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dbang du bsdus pa'i rje btsun ma ku ru kulle
dpal mo snying gi gser thag can du grags pa'i chos skor/ lo rgyus/ bsnyen pa srog gi 'khor lo/ longs spyod rdzas kyi 'khor lo/ dbang bsdud yid bzhin gyi 'khor lo/ rjes gnang
gi yi ge rnams/ zhar las byung ba/ gnyan lo tsA ba'i dbang gi lha gsum gyi nang tshan/ nor rgyun dmar mo'i sgrub thabs/ de'i gsal byed A tsarYa'i zhal las byung ba/ dpal
lha mo ti nu ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i lung blangs pa/ rjes gnang gi yi ge rnams thos so/ ! /khams gsum dbang bsdud tshogs bdag bgegs kyi rgyal po dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis
pa'i chos skor thob pa las/ dang po rtsa ba'i yi ge la/ tshogs bdag gi

lo rgyus/ mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos las byung ba'i gtam rgyud cung zad/ rjes gnang gi yi ge rnying pa mal lo'i gsung / thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi lag len yar klung
pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi zin bris/ khyad par gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa/ thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi gsal byed bdag chen rdo
rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/ thun mong gi rjes gnang gi yi ge chos rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gi rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro le'u bcu dgu pa las phyung ba/
tshogs bdag gi snying po'i gzungs lo tsA ba bsod nams dpal bzang gis dpal ldan sa skyar bsgyur pa/ grub chen nag po spyod pas mdzad pa'i rgya gzhung gi skor la/ rdo rje
mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgom bzlas kyi yi ge tshogs bdag gi sgrub thabs/ bstod pa/ bris sku cho ga gtor ma'i cho ga sbyin sreg gi cho
ga rnams paNTi ta ga ya dha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur pa/ shin tu myur ba'i lha bgegs chen po'i sgrub thabs dI paM ka ras mdzad pa/ tshogs
bdag las bzhi'i 'khor lo'i yi ge grub chen Dombhi he ru kas mdzad pa/ nag po pa'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa rje btsun rin po ches mdzad par grags pa/ bsnyen sgrub las sbyor
sbyin sreg dang bcas pa'i yi ge rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ gsang sgrub lha dgu'i sgrub yig rnying pa/ de'i lag len chos rje sa paN gyis
mdzad pa cung zad mi 'dra ba gnyis/ tshogs bdag gi mngon

rtogs/ gtor 'bul/ sgrub rtags/ las phra mo'i yi ge zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum spog chog dang bcas pa gsal bar ston pa'i sgrub thabs
chen mo gzhan las ches mchog khyad par 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub khrid kyi sdom tshig shin tu gsal ba/
gtor chog yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa gsal byed dam lhan thabs kyi yi ge la/ bris sku bri zhing bsgrub pa'i yi ge bris sku bri tshul
dang rab gnas kyi yi ge bse gdong can mnan pa'i yig rnying tshigs bcad/ de'i lag len rje bla ma dam pa'i gsung las yar klung pas zin bris su btab pa/ sku rten bri ba/
dngos grub kyi rten gtor bca' ba/ gsang rten lus la bcang ba/ rgyun gtor gter du sba ba/ thun mong ma yin pa'i gnad dbab rnams kyi yi ge bka' rgya can/ bsgrub pa'i 'gab
'dre mnan pa/ gsang rten bca' ba/ bla rdo 'chang ba/ dngos grub blang ba'i thabs rnams ston pa'i gsang ba'i yi ge bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/ gsang ba snying
gi 'khor los las bzhi bsgrub tshul/ spogs chog gsang ba thugs kyi man ngag nor bu bsam gtan/ tshogs bdag dang tsa rtsi ka zhal sbyor gyi thab gter dang / bang mdzod kyi
cho ga rnams ston pa'i zab gnad kyi yi ge sbyin sreg gi lag len/ bi na ya ka'i rgyud nas gsungs pa'i phyag mtshan bcu gnyis kyi las tshogs/ 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad
pa'i bstod pa/ spyan 'dren mchod phreng

dang / bstod pa dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad pa/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i bstod pa rnams thos so/ /tshogs bdag gsang sgrub dmar po zhal gcig phyag drug pa'i
sgrub thabs dpal nA ro pas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur pa/ de'i lag len gyi yi ge Dombhi he ru ka nas brgyud pa'i tshogs bdag dmar chung
gsang sgrub zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa yum nor rgyun ma dang lhan cig bsgrub pa'i yi ge de'i dbang bsdud kyi yi ge rten gyi yi ge rnams thos so/ /'di ni zhal gzigs kyi
brgyud pa kho nar 'dod do/ /zhar las 'ongs pa jo bo a ti sha nas brgyud pa'i tshogs bdag dkar po'i sgrub skor la/ spyir tshogs bdag rigs lnga ston pa'i rgyud rin po che'i
gter mdzod dI paM ka ra dang nag tshos bsgyur pa/ tshogs bdag dkar po chags pa'i rdo rje zhal gsum phyag drug pa yab yum gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon indra bhu tis mdzad pa/
dI paM ka ra dang rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ de'i lag len sgrub thabs/ bstod pa jo bos mdzad pa/ rten 'brel gyi rab gnas/ gnad dbab rgya brtson seng gi gdams pa/
gnad la bor ba bzlas pa'i zhal gdams/ sbyin sreg dang bsad pa'i las sbyor/ spog chog lha chen chags pa rdo rje'i rjes gnang lo rgyus dang bcas pa/ tshogs bdag dkar po glang
gdong phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag dkar po sha ba'i gdong can gyi sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag spre'u'i gdong can phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs a mo gha badzras
mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gsang sgrub phyag bzhi

pa'i sgrub thabs kyi yig rnying / de'i rten bca' ba sogs kyi zhal shes dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid bstod cing gsol ba btab pa 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/
tshogs bdag yang gsang drag po btsan thabs su bsgrub pa phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ sbyin sreg spog chog dang bcas pa rje sa skya pas mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag glang po'i
gzugs sgrub kyi sgo nas nor sbyin pa'i zhal gdams/ thab 'khor/ mdzod 'khor/ dge 'dun 'du ba'i 'khor lo sogs kyi gnad yig dang bcas pa rnams so/ ! /dbang bsdud 'dod pa'i
rgyal po'i man ngag gi chos skor thob pa la/ thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis las/ dang po la bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus mdor bsdus pa/ dbang bsdud las kyi 'khor
lo/ yang bsdud thugs kyi 'khor lo byung tshul sogs lo rgyus cung zad rgyas par phye ba bla ma chos kyi rje'i gsung / dbang bsdud kag chol ma'i lung gi rjes gnang gi cho
ga dpal ldan sa skya paNDi tas mdzad pa/ byin rlabs kyi lung bla ma'i zhal shes sa skya paNDi ta'i man ngag nam mkha' mdzod kyi rjes gnang bla ma sa skya pa'i gdams pa/
gro ge ma'i rjes gnang bla ma'i phyag bzhes sngags 'chang rgyal po dpal gyi mdzad pa/ sngags kyi rgyal po'i dam tshig gi dngos grub mchog bsgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba 'dod
rgyal gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rgya gar mkhan po de bzhin gshegs pa bsrung ba'i dpal gyi zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ba ri rin
chen grags kyis bsgyur pa/ gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor los snod bcud dbang du bya ba

paNDi ta rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paNDi ta tha bI ri'i zhal snga nas dang / ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur pa/ dpal mkha' 'gro ma'i sgrub thabs/ dbang bsdud las kyi
'khor lo'i man ngag ba ri lo tsa bas bsgyur pa/ khams gsum dbang du bsdu ba'i man ngag khyad par can bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ 'phrin las bzhi'i sgrub thabs kyi
don yang dag par bsdu ba rgya sgom tshul khrims grags kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon rin chen rdo rje'i sgrub thabs gsal bar byed pa'i 'grel pa rin po che'i myu gu rje sa skya
pa chen pos mdzad pa/ 'phrin las bzhi'i dbye ba'i man ngag las bzhi 'khor lo'i rab gnas/ spyi'i man ngag mdor bstan zhes bya ba dbang gi 'phrin las kyi lag len man ngag mngon
rtogs dmar khrid du bkod pa rgya sgom tshul khrims grags kyis mdzad pa/ dbang bsdud kag chol gyi sgrub thabs rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge
rje sa skya pa chen po'i zhal gdams thun mong ma yin pa/ bzlas pa'i zhal gdams bla ma sa skya pa'i gsung / dbang gi gtor ma'i man ngag sa skya paNDi ta'i phyag bzhes/ dbang
gi 'khor lo'i rab gnas ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams pa/ mchod pa 'bul ba'i man ngag bstod pa sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi rim pa dang / 'khor lo'i nang tshang
bstan pa ba ri ba'i gdams pa/ bsgom pa'i dus kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi zhal gdams bla ma sa skya pa'i gdams ngag shin tu zab pa/ sngags kyi yi ge'i byin 'jug dang bzlas thabs
zhal shes/ gnad kyi sgrub thabs snying 'dra ba/ sngags

dang 'khor lo'i gdan lung 'bog pa ra dza la sogs pa dbang du byed pa'i yig chung / man ngag gi bsdus don nyung ngu mchan dang bcas pa/ ka kha 'khor lo brtsegs rin chen phreng
ba zhes bya ba las phran tshegs bstan pa'i skor/ dbang gi sbyin sreg bla ma sa skya pa chen po'i phyag bzhes/ sku gsung thugs kyi rab gnas kyi zhal gdams zin bris/ 'khor
lo'i rab gnas bya thabs ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams ngag bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge bsdus pa/ DA ki ma'i 'gro ba dbang bsdud kyi gdams pa zhes bya ba dbang drag gi man
ngag 'khor los bsgrub bya dgug pa sogs ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams pa/ bla ma sa skya pa'i zhal gdams/ gtor ma'i zhal gdams rje sa skya pa'i phyag gzhes/ gnod sbyin rin chen
bsgrub pa'i u pa de sha 'khor lo'i man ngag gsung tshad ma/ 'khor lo'i bri ltab sba ba'i man ngag dbang gi tsakra'i zhal gdams/ nam mkha' mdzod kyi gdams pa/ bsnyen sgrub
las gsum gyi gnad bod du 'gyur ba'i gdams ngag la zab pa/ zhal gdams zin bris ma/ DA ki ma'i gdams pa/ DA ki ma'i srog snying khong nas phyung ba ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams
pa chig brgyud/ DA ki ma bsgrub pa'i lag len/ rtags kyi yi ge ba ri lo tsA ba bod du 'byon khar bla ma rdo rje gdan pas gnang ba/ gzhan dbang du byed pa'i gdams pa rin
po che pa'i zhal gdams mthar thug tshe bsring ba'i thabs/ de'i zhal shes/ rgyas pa'i gtor ma'i phyag bzhes sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ drag po'i 'phrin las bsgrub pa'i man ngag
lung 'bogs pa'i yi ge nyin bsrung mtshan

bsrung gi man ngag de'i yi ge mchan bu dang bcas pa rnams thos so/ ! /gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge'i skor la/ khams gsum 'gro ba dbang byed kag chol ba'i bla ma brgyud
pa'i lo rgyus mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa/ dbang bsdud kag chol ma'i A l-i kA l-i'i sngags ring bri bzlas kyi man ngag sa skya paNDi tas dag cing gsal bar mdzad pa/
kag chol chen mo rtsa ba'i tho yig brjed byang rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel Tika sbas pa mig 'byed gser gyi thur ma rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ 'khor lo'i rab
gnas bya ba'i man ngag zhal gdams dang bcas pa sa skya paNDi tas rgyas par bkod pa/ bde ba rgyas byed ma'i sku la brten pa'i dbang gi nang sgrub zab mo rje sa paN gyis mdzad
pa/ gsang sgrub tha chen tsakra'i yi ge dang / gnad 'bebs nyi zla'i 'khor lo'i gdams pa rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i spogs chog gi gnad la dbab pa'i
gdams pa dang / sbyin sreg gi yi ge rgyas pa rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ yul bdag dbang du bya ba ba ri ba'i man ngag rje sa skya pa'i gsung / bzlas pa'i sngags kyi 'byin
'jug gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor lo'i bsdus don/ ma grub spogs pa'i cho ga 'khor lo'i lteb tshigs kyi zhal gdams/ ma grub gnad 'bebs kyi 'khor lo'i yi ge pho mo gnad kyi 'khor
lo/ gnad 'bebs nyi zla'i gdams pa/ pho mo gnad kyi 'khor lo'i zhal gdams rnams rje sa skya pa chen po'i zhal gyi gdams pa/ tha chen 'khor lo'i yi ge gsang ba'i sgrub
thabs/ de'i zhal gdams/ bla ma sa skya

ba'i gdams ngag nor bu rin chen phag mo grub pa la gnang ba/ tha chen 'khor lo'i yi ge dbang bsdud dam pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i rdzas sgrub gshen bde ba'i rdo rjes bla ma skya pa
chen po la zhus pa/ de'i gsal byed zhang btsun sag thang pa'i zhal gdams/ dbang gi rlung 'khor zab mo/ rlung lha las la bzhugs pa sogs gab pa'i man ngag sa skya pa'i zhal
gdams/ A l-i'i gnad kyi man ngag yid bzhin nor bu/ de'i zhal shes/ A l-i'i sbyin bsreg rje sa chen dang 'gro mgon phag mo grub pa gnyis kyi zhu ba zhu lan A l-i kA l-i
las sna tshogs la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i gdams pa/ 'dod rgyal yab yum sbrags te bsgrub pa'i man ngag lag len du dril ba'i nag po 'gro shes sngags 'chang rgyal po dpal gyis
mdzad pa/ de'i zhal shes sa skya pa'i gdams pa khyad par can 'dzam gling gser gyis bkang ba las che cher dga' ba de nyid kyis mdzad pa thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang
gi zur 'debs 'jam dbyangs mgon pos mdzad pa/ dbang bsdud las kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel pa/ khyad par can gyi sgrub thabs nor bu gsal 'bar snying gi thig le'i dwangs ma rnams so/
/de lta bu'i dbang bsdud nor lha'i man ngag gi glegs bam yongs rdzogs kyi dkar chag rje tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos mdzad pa yang thos so/ /chos skor de dag gi brgyud
pa gzhan rnams ni gong gi rjes gnang so so'i brgyud pa dang 'dra la/ ! /ku ru kulle'i nang sgrub slob dpon klu sgrub nas brgyud pa'i lha lnga'i chos skor rnams kyi brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ klu'i byang chub/ dga' rab rdo rje/ rdo rje

gdan pa/ arYa pa la/ bai ro tsa na/ rje btsun gnas nang pa dus gsum mkhyen pa/ nas brgyud de/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ tshar chen man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang ku ru kulle'i
phyi nang gsang gsum gyi sgrub yig rgyas pa zhal shes dang bcas dwags po bkras rnam pas mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dwags po bkras rnam pa/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang
/ rje karma 'phrin las pa/ tshar chen man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang dmar mo skor gsum gyi chos skor gyi dkar chag dang / 'dod rgyal gyi thun mong ma yin pa'i bla ma brgyud
pa'i gsol 'debs tshar chen gyis mdzad pa gnyis/ de'i rjes gnang gi lag len zin bris gsal byed rje rin rnam pas mdzad pa/ 'dod rgyal gyi 'khor lo bri ba'i zin bris kyi yi
ge de'i sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa nyams su len tshul/ rje bsam gtan gling pas mdzad pa'i nyi zla 'khor lo'i yi ge rnams kyang thos/ ! /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi
drung du/ gur mgon lha brgyad sbrags te sgrub pa thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang dang / lha mgon bcu gnyis ma'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang
/ rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin bzang / brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod
nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun
nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma

dam pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ de gnyis la mkhan chen
thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang
lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i brgyud pa rdzong lugs ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ zhang pa/ na bza' pa/ bla ma dam pa/ gzungs pa/ dge bzang ba/ bla ma rin chen/ zur
shAkya dpal ba/ rje mus srad pa/ sgyi chu ba shes rab rin chen/ tshar chen man 'dra/ yang na brag phug pa nas/ brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ sa skya bu ston dbang
phyug dar/ theg chen chos rgyal/ rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / mus srad pa man 'dra/ ! /'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang pu tra'i zur bkar
grags pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paNDi ta dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon
tan tshul khrims/ bla ma mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/
chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal

mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo
ring pa/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang
na 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal
mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang man gong dang 'dra/ ! /yang gnyan mgon chen po gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor thob pa la/ thog mar bsnyen
dus kyi mgon por grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ ba liM ta/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba/
bi ma la gupta/ ratna kirti/ ratna badzra/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ gnam kha 'ub pa/ rje sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa
paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen seng ge rgyal mtshan/ yar klung pa khu dbon/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa

skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /bsgrub dus thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kha che rin chen rdo rje yan sngar bzhin/ de nas ta thA ga
ta rakShi ta/ gnyan lo/ kha 'ub pa man sngar bzhin/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ bzhi thog pa kun rin/ bzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs
med shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug grub mchog bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /bram ze sngags gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa yan sngar ltar/ de nas bzhi thog
pa kun rin/ bzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ ! /dpal mgon gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen
yan khrid kyi brgyud pa bzhin/ de nas rje bon dkar ba/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ ! /dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i man ngag gi chos skor yongs rdzogs thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs ni/ rje tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i dkar chag gi yi ge
las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ de la spyir kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir gsang sngags rnying ma ba dang / gsar ma ba dang / ches gsar ma ba dag las brgyud pa'i zhing skyong nag
po chen po gdong bzhi pa'i man ngag gi rigs mang po dag snang ba las/ gtso

bor ni mgon po 'di nyid kyi chos skor 'phags yul nas spyan 'dren par byed pa po ni gnyan lo tsA ba chen po dar ma grags nyid yin la/ de nyid nas brgyud de byang gi phyogs 'dir
man ngag gi bshad srol che cher rgyas par mdzad pa ni/ rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras brgyud par bcas pa dag yin pas lugs 'di ni snying por gyur pa'i man ngag tu bzung
ngo / /de nyid kyi man ngag rnams gab 'khrugs 'thor ba'i skyon spangs pa'i phyir dkar chag tu 'god par bya ste/ tshul 'di la'ang brgyud pa rnam par dag pa gsum las 'ongs
pa'i gdams ngag gi srol gsum mnga' ste/ ma hA paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa dang / shrI paNDi ta ta thA ga ta rakShi ta las brgyud pa dang / kharsa pa Ni ri
sul gyi rnal 'byor ma ku sa li chen mo nas brgyud pa'o/ /dang po ni/ mgon po gdong brnyan can nam/ las sbyor gyi mgon por grags pa nyid yin pa la de'i sgrub thabs kyi rtsa
ba'i rgya gzhung slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang gnyan los bsgyur pa/ rgya gzhung gi 'grel pa dri med don gsal 'jam dbyangs
rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ mngon rtogs/ gtor chog 'khor mang gi mngon rtogs rnams bla ma gong mas mdzad pa/ las sbyor gyi gsal byed las kyi gsham bu brgyad pa'i yi ge gnyan
gyis mdzad pa/ zhar la dpal mgon khyung zhal can gyi sgrub thabs gser gyi spu gri'i lag len gyi yi ge 'di la bla ma kha cig gdong brnyan can zer ba'i chos skyong zur
pa zhig yin gyi/ zhal bzhi pa'i rigs ma yin zhes gsungs

par grags na'ang / de ni rigs pa ma yin pa'i tshul gzhan du shes par bya'o/ /gnyis pa ni/ bdag mdun mgon po zhal khra can nam/ bsgrub dus kyi mgon por grags pa la byed cing
/ las bzhi'i bye brag tu bsgrub tshul shin tu zab pa zhig snang ngo / /'di la rtsa ba'i sgrub thabs ta thA ga ta rakShi ta rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i dam tshig
gi dngos grub bsgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba'i rgya gzhung dang / de la brten nas gnyan los mdzad pa'i lo rgyus dang / sgrub thabs kyi rim pa dang bcas pa yod cing /
phal cher ni snyan brgyud kyi zhal shes la rag las par gsal lo/ /gsum pa la zab cing rgya che ba phyi'i sgrub skor/ rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun pa gsang ba'am nang gi
man ngag snying nang gi khrag lta bu khyad par gyi man ngag go /dang po la yid ches shing khungs btsun pa'i phyir du brgyud pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge nus ldan du bya ba rjes
gnang gi yi ge rtsa bar gyur pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge gsal byed du gyur pa lhan thabs yan lag gi yi ge 'phral du nye bar mkho ba gtor chog dang bskang ba/ bstod
bskul gyi skor rnams so/ /dang po la lo rgyus kyi yi ge rgyas pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa rin po che'i gsung las byung ba'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge'o/ /gnyis pa rjes
gnang gi skor la/ bla ma gnyan los mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rjes gnang kha 'ub pas mdzad pa/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rjes gnang gsal ba rje btsun
rin po ches mdzad pa/ rjes gnang shin tu rgyas pa'i nag po 'gro shes yar klung pa ldong ston seng ge rgyal

mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ de nyid las brgyud pa'i gri snying bla rdo srog 'khor phyag mtshan rnams kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge gsum pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge'i skor la/ rtsa
bar gyur pa ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs mchan bshad du grags pa'i yi ge gzhung de la brten nas bsnyen sgrub kyi man ngag gnyan lo'i u pa de sha zhes
bya ba dang / bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi gnad kyi yi ge gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub dus kyi las khrigs bla ma kha 'ub pa chen pos mdzad pa/ tsa turmu kha'i u pa de sha zhes
bya ba rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ gong gi kha 'ub pas mdzad pa'i las khrigs kyi gsal byed chos rje gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi sgrub
thabs nag po 'gro shes dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa/ rnam gsum lag len gsal byed chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi gsung rgyun bsod nams grags pas
zin bris su bkod pa/ bsnyen pa'i go rim gyi yi ge bzlas pa dang gegs sel gyi man ngag gser chos bsnyen sgrub las gsum spog chog shi sa bstan pa dang bcas pa'i mngon rtogs
gsal byed gnad kyi zhal gdams mthar thug gtor ma'i zhal gdams snyan brgyud/ las rab 'byams dang bsad bskrad kyi 'khor lo'i zhal gdams snying nang gi ga lta bu/ bye brag
tu bsad las kyi 'khor lo man ngag mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs can du grags pa/ 'khrul 'khor ltab cing sba ba sogs mnan pa'i man ngag snyan brgyud sbas don gsal ba rnams yar
klung pa mkhas grub seng ge

rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge sgrub thabs rta bdun rgyal po 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ de skor gyi yig chung bzhi rnams
yod/ bzhi pa lhan thabs kyi skor la/ spyi'i lhan thabs dang / bye brag gi lhan thabs/ las phran bu'i man ngag go /dang po la zhal gdams don lnga ma shAkya'i dge slong gnyan
gyi u pa de sha zhes bya ba/ zab pa'i gnad drug gi yi ge mchan bu dang bcas pa ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma'i gsung / de'i gsal byed bla ma gnyan gyis nye gnas dar ma seng
ge la gnang ba/ mgon po pha ltar bskul zhing lha mo sring ltar gdung ba'i man ngag gi yi ge 'di'i khyad par gyi dam tshig gi yi ge 'khon nag zas su bza' ba'i gdams pa
slob dpon padmas mdzad pa/ nyams chag bskang ba'i yi ge rgyas bsdus gnyis gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ dam tshig gso ba'i padma kha sbyor gyi yi ge rgyas bsdus kha 'ub pas mdzad
pa/ gnyis pa la/ sngon 'gro rten gyi skabs su phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid dang bcas pa'i rten bca' ba'i yi ge bla ma gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ nang rten bla rdo bca' ba'i
yi ge rgyas bsdus gnyis gnyan lo'i gsung / gsang rten gyi skabs su gtum po rang bsrung 'khor lo'i bri tshul/ de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag de'i bri yig de'i sngags
byang / rten gyi 'khor lo'i bri tshul rgyas pa/ 'khor lo'i rab gnas/ rgyal tsha lung mang pos mdzad pa'i rten gyi yi ge rang bsrung che ba ling tshe nyi shu pa'i bri yig
'phags pa rin po ches zhang ston chos rje la gnang ba rnams so/ /mchod pa'i skabs su me tog

bzhi sbyor gyi yi ge de'i gsal byed ba liM gi me tog rnying pa'i u pa de sha mgon po'i spos sbyor gyi man ngag rnams la gnyan gyis mdzad pa'i yig chung re re yod do/ /gtor
ma'i skabs su gtor ma bca' thabs dang / gtong thabs kyi yi ge gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ brtag gtor gyi man ngag tshigs bcad ma rnams thos so/ /dngos gzhi bsnyen pa'i skabs su
sngags byang / sngags kyi them yig zhib mo/ them yig gsal byed bdag chen rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad pa/ sngags kyi gnad them yig spel tshig thor
bu ba 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge rnams yod do/ /bsgrub pa'i skabs su sgrub pa'i gnad rje btsun gyi gsung /
sgrub pa'i rtags kyi yi ge gtor len bya rog gi brtag pa/ 'khu ldog mi 'byung zhing las myur du bsgrub pa'i yi ge rtsa ba dang gnas 'bebs dang las tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i zhal
gdams/ 'khor lo dang ling tshe dang ling ga'i zhal shes/ 'khor lo bri thabs/ 'khor lo'i sngags byang / 'khor lo'i sngags bkod tshul/ las tshogs 'ga' zung gi 'khor lo'i
man ngag rnams thos/ las sbyor gyi skabs su bsad sngags ring thung gnyis/ kha sbyor dbye ba bzhi'i man ngag las sbyor yig chung / mngon spyod bsad las kyi yig chung / dgong
zor gyi yi ge rgyas bsdus gnyis/ ra zor gyi yi ge las mthar sbyin sreg gi yi ge rgyas pa gong mas mdzad pa/ bsdus pa sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad

pa/ kha sbyor dbye ba dmod bskul rnams so/ /spog chog gi skabs su ma 'chun na rang nyid zhal bzhi par bskyed pa'i man ngag rtsa dbu ma chos 'byung dang bcas pa'i gnad dbab
yi ge shi sa bstan pa'i man ngag gi yi ge gsum pa phran bu'i skor la/ mgon po la gtsug lag khang gtad pa'i cho ga de'i gsal byed/ rang dang slob ma gtad pa'i yi ge rdzas
dang yo byad bsrung ba'i yi ge nor gyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i man ngag sre'u gso ba'i 'khor lo'i man ngag yang de'i man ngag bram ze kha spu can gyi gdams pa/ nor sgrub yid
bzhin nor bu'i man ngag dbang sdud gri lag g.yob pa dar thogs kyi gdams pa/ bsgrub bya dbang du bya ba/ spyod lam dbang du bya ba/ shwa bzlog gi man ngag dgra la ltas ngan
gtong ba'i man ngag chig brgyud ma/ cho 'phrul dbab pa'i man ngag dgra bo cham la 'bebs pa'i rdzas sbyor/ bskrad pa'i las sbyor/ de'i zhal shes/ ngag mnan pa'i man ngag
bka' sdod ma hA ba la la brten nas 'dre btsan thabs su mnan pa'i man ngag rnams so/ /lnga pa nyer mkho'i skor la gsum ste/ gtor chog bskang ba/ bstod bskul lo/ /dang po
la gnyan los nye gnas dar ma seng ge la gnang ba'i gdong bzhi pa mchod pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ de'i kha skong gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ bla ma kha 'ub pas mdzad pa'i gtor chog
rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i gtor chog gtor chog 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ dmar chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i gtor chog drag po'i gtor bzlog gi man ngag yar klung
pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad

pa/ de'i phyag len rje btsun chos rjes mdzad pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa la dam rdzas kyi bskang ba spyan 'dren dang bcas pa gnyan los mdzad pa/ phyag mtshan 'bul ba'i tshigs bcad
gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ gtor bskang kha 'ub pas mdzad/ mdos bskang mgon po nyid kyis bla ma kha 'ub pa la dngos su gnang ba rnams so/ /gsum pa la/ bstod pa srin gzugs ma
slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ zhal bzhi pa'i bstod pa sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ bstod pa mi rtog ma ri
sul gyi rnal 'byor mas mdzad pa/ bla ma gnyan gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa paM pad ma/ kha 'ub pas mgon po zhal gzigs pa'i bstod pa/ mal lo tsA bas rmi lam du mgon po zhal gzigs
nas bstod pa/ rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i bstod bskul/ sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i bstod pa/ 'phags pa rin po che'i bstod pa/ bstod pa dam pa kun grags kyis mdzad pa/
chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa stong nyid ma dang / srid gsum dbang bsgyur ma gnyis/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i mtshan can gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ dmar chos kyi
rgyal pos mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ bstod pa 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston gyis mdzad pa/ bkra shis grub kyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ dharmA shrI bha dras bstod pa/ mkhan chen gnas
drug pas bstod pa/ rtsa sngags kyi don bstod bha wan yon tan blo gros kyis mdzad pa/ sku gsum ma dang thun gsum ma gnyis chos rje gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa/ ha ha rgod
pa ma chos

rje bzang po rgyal mtshan pas mdzad pa/ rtsa sngags dang mthun par shrI man bha dras bstod pa/ bzang po'i mtha' can gyi bstod pa/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor zur shAkya dpal gyis
mdzad pa'i bstod bskul/ gnyan gyis mdzad pa'i rtsa sngags kyi drag bskul/ bstod bskul mngon spyod rol pa/ bstod bskul las kyi rgyal po/ dmod bskul las kyi rgyal po rnams
gnyan los mdzad pa/ kha 'ub pas mdzad pa'i dmod bskul rnams so/ /de dag gis ni phyi'i sgrub skor rnams brjod zin nas/ gnyis pa nang gsang ba'i man ngag ni/ rtsa gsum 'khor
lnga'i bsgrub gzhi la/ bsgrub bya las bzhi'i mgon po bkod pa'i sgrub byed bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag gis tshe 'dir zung 'jug gi go 'phang bsgrub pa'i thabs dang
/ de'i cha rkyen las bzhi bye brag tu bsgrub pa'i thabs ches zab pa zhig yin no/ /'di la rtsa ba'i yi ge tshigs bcad ma dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa/ gsang sgrub
kyi khrid gzhung mtshungs med skyes mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ khrid yig zhib mo zung 'jug rnam par rol pa bdud sde 'joms pa'i bshan pa chen po zhes bya ba brgyud
pa'i gsol 'debs dang bcas pa rnams so/ /gsum pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu'i man ngag la gnyis te/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas bla ma gnyan la gdams pa'i thun mong ma yin
pa'i shog ril nyer gcig dang / de las zab pa'i yig chung ngo / /dang po la gtso bor gyur pa bsrung bzlog bsad mnan tshe sgrub dang bcas pa'i shog ril/ sbas te 'dzam gling
du ma grags pa'i snying nang gi khrag lta bu'i shog

ril/ chos skyong zhi ba nor du bsgrub pa'i shog ril/ nang tsitta la brten nas zhal dngos su blta ba zhing skyong gi shog ril/ phyi'i 'gab 'dre bdud mo shanti ro zan mnan pa
'brug mgo can gyi shog ril/ nang gi mal 'og bsrung ba/ byad ma'i ngag mnan pa'i shog ril/ gsang ba rang srog rten gyi 'khor lo kha sbyar gyi shog dril/ 'khor bsrung zhing
mi 'khu mi ldog pa'i shog dril/ yum chen khros ma'i shog dril chig brgyud/ 'chi med tshe bsgrub pa'i shog dril/ dgos 'dod nor bu bsgrub pa'i shog dril/ rdzas dang / srog
'khor la brten nas sku dngos su blta ba'i shog dril snying rgya can/ ltas ngan cho 'phrul dbab pa'i shog dril/ dgra srog myur du gcod pa nag po srog rtsa rnon po'i shog
dril/ dgra mkhar rmang nas sgyel ba nag mo mkhar sgyel gyi shog dril mkhar bshig pa'i spu gri nag po zhes bya ba/ ser ba dbab pa gdong bzhi pa'i spu gri ngar ma'i shog dril/
zhing sel 'jug pa spu gri so 'debs kyi shog dril/ tsa turmu kha gcun thabs nyi zla can gyi shog dril/ gnad la dbab pa lha mo nag mo'i shog dril bka' rgya can/ ma 'chun
'khu ldog byed na mnan pa'i shog dril/ las byed du ma 'dod na ar gtad kyi shog dril shin tu sbas pa rnams so/ /shog dril dang po'i gsal byed rje btsun chos rjes mdzad
pa dang / rgyun gyi nyams kho bos mdzad pa rnams thos so/ /gnyis pa la tsa turmu kha dkar po tshe 'phel gyi sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang gi yig chung / ser po rgyas pa'i yi ge
nag po dgra bgegs sgrol ba'i yi ge dmar po

dbang bsdud kyi yi ge las bzhi'i mgon po'i mngon rtogs kyi gsal byed/ mgon po ser po'i rjes gnang gi yig chung / las bzhi'i mgon po'i sgrub thabs theg chen chos rgyal gyis
mdzad pa/ mgon dkar gyi tshe sgrub zla ba'i chu rgyun brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dang bcas pa/ gnyan lo bod du 'byon khar ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas gnang ba'i bram ze dmod pa'i
srog mthu dgra bo'i srog gi shan pa dmar po/ lam bar gyi chom rkun brtag pa'i phyir du gdong bzhi'i bka' sdod drang srong nag po pra se na'i man ngag de'i zhal shes tsa
turmu kha'i than 'gyed gnyan gyi mgul khug ma/ yum chen bzhi'i than 'gyed/ gnyan mgon gyi par bu'i man ngag gnyan mgon lha dgu'i nor sgrub thun mong ma yin pa/ rdzas kyi
sgo nas dgra bsad pa'i las sbyor/ rdo nag yig dmar gyi sgrub mthu/ khang sel nag po/ dgra bo zla ba gcig la bsad pa mdze po nag po'i man ngag dgra bo klu la gtad pa gnyan
gyi na ga stobs 'phrog mon pa nag po nor sher gyi man ngag dar lung gi brag spre'u dmar 'dzings 'dra'i rmang nas gnam kha 'ub pas bton pa'i zangs khab dmar po'i bsad las/
sreg byed me'i sbyor ba/ gcun pa'i mthar thug sdig pa nag po'i 'khrul 'khor gyi las tshogs rnams thos so/ /gzhan yang gdong bzhi pa'i sgo nas sre'u gso ba'i rgyud kyi
gdams pa/ bu 'tshol ba'i man ngag mngal bsrung ba'i gdams pa/ sre'u gso ba'i yi ge srid med pa btsal ba/ lte ba bsgyur ba/ yod pa gso ba rnams kyi yi ge bla ma gnyan gyis
mdzad pa/ zhal gdams snying gi dum bur

grags pa'i skor la/ spu gri so 'debs kyi zhal gdams/ rang bsrung khra mo yid bzhin 'khor lo'i zhal gdams/ rten gyi zhal gdams/ gtor ma'i zhal gdams/ sngags kyi zhal gdams/
'khor lo'i zhal gdams rnams thos/ 'di dag ni cha shas sam rkang grangs tsam yi ger bkod pa yin gyi/ thun mong ma yin pa'i gnad phal cher brgyud pa'i man ngag dang ldan pa'i
bla ma'i snyan brgyud ltos pa kho nar snang bas man ngag dang bral ba dang lung med kyang dpe tsam la brten nas gzu lum du spyod pa rnams ni mun khung na mda' 'phen pa
dang / byis pa gri khar rtse ba dang mtshungs pas shes ldan dag bag yod pa byos shig tshul de dag rnams gang las brgyud pa yin zhe na/ smras pa/ rdo rje 'chang dang klu
sgrub mgon/ /ba liM ta pa ye shes zhabs/ /mar me mdzad dang dpal bde ba/ /sbas pa'i zhabs dang rin chen gnyis/ /rnal 'byor dbang mo lo chen gnyan/ /kha 'ub pa dang sa skya
pa/ /rje btsun sku mched paNDi ta/ /blo gros rgyal mtshan dkon mchog dpal/ /brag phug pa dang bla ma rje/ /bla chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'i mtshan/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang
dbang zhabs/ /mthu stobs dbang phyug kun spangs rje/ /gang des bka' 'bangs bdag la 'o/ /phyi yi man ngag phal cher ni/ /bla ma dam pa yar klung pa/ /bsod nams rgyal
mchog 'jam dbyangs che/ /de nas gong bzhin brgyud kyang chog /phyi yi sgrub skor 'ga' zhig ni/ /chos rje bla ma dpal ldan pa/ /shar chen pa dang rdo rje 'chang / /bdag chen
kun dga' dbang phyug

la/ /'khon ston mkhas grub ma tis gsan/ /yig chung 'ga' yi lung dag ni/ /bla chen bdag po zha lu ba/ /paN chen shAkya mchog ldan la/ /rje btsun chos rjes gsan pa 'o/ /bdag
ni snyigs dus kha ba'i ljongs/ /ma rung rgyu ba'i khrod du lhung / /'on kyang sngon gyi las dbang gis/ /yongs 'dzin dam pa 'ga' dang mjal/ /khyad par zhing skyong nag po'i
skor/ /mkhas grub dam pa bdun las thos/ /yang sgos drin can rdo rje 'chang / /kun spangs chen po'i zhabs pad bsten/ /dad gus gser gyi lde mig gis/ /zab don thugs kyi sgo
phye nas/ /snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i bum bzang gnang / /rnam dpyod snyim pas rab bzung ste/ /nan tan ro 'dzin gyis myang pas/ /nges shes snying gi dkyil du shar/ /phyogs
gzhan smon pa'i re ba bral/ /e ma kho bo skal ba bzang / /zhes so/ /de ltar dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag gi chos sna'i rnam grangs rnams dang / de dag brgyud pa gang
las 'ongs kyi tshigs su bcad pa de dag ni rje tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag gi dkar chag las ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ de nas rje blo
gsal rgya mtsho'i rjes su/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang
chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du/ tsa turmu kha'i man ngag gi chos skor gzhan yang thob pa la/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs rdo 'bid srog gi spu gri dmar len
zhes bya ba paNDi ta bho ta ris mdzad pa/ rje tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i

zhal bzhi pa'i bla rdo'i man ngag khyad par can gyi yi ge yang des mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi cho ga rgyas pa dngos grub kyi rgya mtsho/ bram ze mngags gtad kyi yig chung / dpal
mgon gdong bzhi pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge bka' rgya can/ gsang sgrub rjes gnang gi yig chung / dpal mgon khyung zhal can gyi rjes gnang / ta thA
ga ta rakShi tas rgya gzhung gi 'grel pa/ gsang khrid kyi sngon 'gro'i yi ge gsang sgrub kyi las sbyor gyi yig chung / gdong bzhi pa'i shwa zlog gi man ngag rnams tshar chen
gyis mdzad pa/ zhal bzhi pa'i theb zlog rtsi tshul gnyan gyi u pa de sha zhal bzhi pa'i tsi ta'i sgrub mthu zab mo/ gdong bzhi pa'i sgo nas cho 'phrul dbab pa/ yum singga
li nag mo'i than 'gyed/ rgyal 'bud/ 'khar ba nag po brdab pa'i man ngag rnams kyi yig rnying / gnyan lo dang gnam kha 'ub pas mdzad pa'i gdong bzhi pa'i sgo nas dpal
'bar gyi me bkra brtag pa'i man ngag gi yi ge rnams kyang thos/ ! /yang rje mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal mgon zhing skyong nag po chen po dgra bo'i
stobs 'phrog gdong bzhi pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i sgrub thabs snying thig ha la nag po'i be'u bum yongs rdzogs thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ de nyid kyi man ngag
gi ma yig rje tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ bu yig la 'khor lo'i man ngag 'khor lo bri ba'i man ngag srung ba'i 'khor lo'i man ngag bsnyen pa'i sngon 'gro rnam gsum gyi man
ngag zhal gdams snying gi dum bu spu gri so 'debs kyi man

ngag gnad la dbab pa rnam bzhi'i man ngag sngags dag par bya ba'i man ngag rigs sngags go ldog pa'i man ngag shi sa bstan pa'i gnad lnga'i man ngag spog chog gi mtshams sbyor
gyi man ngag ste ma yig bu yig yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ dpal bde
ba/ paN chen dri med sbas pa/ mkhas pa rin chen rnam gnyis/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ bla ma paNDe ba/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ gnam kha 'ub
pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag
phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kun spangs chos kyi
nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'brog nub ri shar pa rdo rje 'dzin pa byams pa don grub/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin rdzong lugs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams las brgyud pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag rje
mus srad pa'i dkar chag nang bzhin thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs rnams dkar chag de nyid las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ rje btsun dpal ldan sa skya pa la dpal rdo rje nag po
chen po zhal bzhi pa brgyud pa'i srol

mi 'dra ba gnyis las/ brgyud de 'ongs pa'i man ngag mnga' ste/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta nas brgyud pa dang / ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma nas brgyud pa'o/ /dang po la ta thA ga ta
rakShi ta nyid kyis mdzad pa'i rgya gzhung gi yi ge dang / de'i lag len bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge bla ma gnyan gyis mdzad pa yod do/ /gnyis pa ri sul gyi rnal 'byor
ma las brgyud pa la/ rtsa ba'i gzhung dang / de la brten pa'i man ngag gnyis las/ dang po ni/ sgrub thabs mchan bshad ces bya ba sngags dang bcas pa'o/ /'di la gsal byed
kyi yi ge mchan dang / mahA kA la'i sngags kyi gnad ces bya ba sa gcod kyi yi ge dang / sngags them bstan pa dang / mchod pa'i de nyid bstan pa dang / sngags kyi kha skong
sngags chad 'jug rnams yod do/ /gnyis pa de la brten pa'i man ngag la lnga/ lo rgyus kyi yi ge dang / mchod chog dang / rjes gnang dang / bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man
ngag dang / man ngag phran tshegs rnams so/ /dang po la bla ma gnyan gyis chos skyong btsal ba'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge yod la/ gnyis pa mchod chog la/ rgyun du mchod pa gtor
ma'i cho ga dang / khyad par du mchod pa kha skong gi cho ga'o/ /dang po la dpal gdong bzhi pa'i mgon po mchod pa'i cho ga gnyan gyis nye gnas dar ma seng ge la gnang
ba/ de'i kha skong rdo rang byung gru gsum sogs 'god tshul/ gtso 'khor gsum ma'i sgrub thabs gnyan gyi man ngag gnam kha 'ub pas mdzad pa'i sgrub pa'i las khrigs/ sa chen
gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ bstod

'bum/ bskul rnams so/ /gnyis pa khyad par du mchod pa la/ ma hA kA la'i rten gzugs bsgrub pa'i man ngag gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ mdos chog gnam kha 'ub pas mdzad pa/ mdos gshom
rgyas pa chos rje a nanda ma tis mdzad pa rnams so/ /gsum pa rjes gnang la/ bla ma gnyan gyi yi ge gcig rje btsun chen po'i yi ge gcig chos rje a nandas mdzad pa'i yi ge
gcig rnams yod do/ /bzhi pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag la/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi man ngag dngos dang / de'i gsal byed kyi yi ge phra mo'o/ /dang po la gnyis/
yab yum sbrags pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum dang / yum gyi bsnyen sgrub las gsum mo/ dang po la gtso 'khor gsum pa la brten pa'i bsnyen sgrub mnan gsum gyi man ngag gnyan
gyis mdzad pa/ gtso 'khor gsum lnga gnyis ka'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum/ de'i gsal byed kyi yi ge rnying pa/ mgon po bsgrub dus kyi las khrigs/ de gnyis ka'i gsal byed bsnyen
sgrub las gsum gyi las khrigs chen mo/ yang bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi las khrigs nag po 'gro shes su grags pa chos rje gzungs pas mdzad pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa yum gyi bsnyen
sgrub las gsum la/ yum srin mo las mkhan sgrub thabs gnyan chig brgyud ma'o/ /gnyis pa gsal byed kyi yi ge phra mo la gnyis/ thun mong du gsal byed dang / so sor gsal
byed do/ /dang po ni/ gnyan gyi gdams pa drug pa dang / zhal gdams don lnga ma dang / 'di'i khyad par gyi dam tshig dang / chos skyong bsten thabs dang / gtor ma bca'
thabs

dang / gtor ma gtong thabs rnams so/ /gnyis pa la so sor gsal byed la/ rten gyi man ngag ces bya ba phyi rten nang rten gsang rten de kho na nyid kyi rten 'cha' tshul gnyan
gyis mdzad pa/ ma hA kA la'i rten bca' ba zhes pa nang rten gyi gsal byed chung ngu zhig gsang rten gyi gsal byed gtum po rang bsrung gi 'khor lo dang / rten bca' thabs
zhes pa'i yi ge re re/ rten bca' thabs kyi gnad gsal byed kyi yi ge gcig srung 'khor la sngags 'bri lugs/ srung 'khor gyi sngags byang / bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi zhal phyag
gi khyad par/ rten gyi mdun du 'bul ba'i rdzas/ me tog bzhi sbyor gyi yi ge gnyis/ mchod pa'i spos sbyor/ thun mong gi bsnyen sgrub/ thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa 'phags
pa rin po che'i yi ge sngags kyi gnad/ sgrub pa'i man ngag rje btsun gyi gsung / glo bur du las 'chol ba'i man ngag bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi rtags mtshan/ gtor ma'i
bkra rtags brtag pa/ 'khor lo'i zhal gdams/ 'khor lo bri thabs/ 'khor lo'i sngags/ 'khor lo'i man ngag thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams pa zhes bya ba/ 'khor lo dang / ling
ga'i zhal gdams gnad kyi yig chung re re/ yang gsang thugs kyi nying khu/ kha sbyor dbye ba'i man ngag dmod pa las sbyor/ mngon spyod bsad las/ sgong zor/ 'phang pa khyu
mchog zor gyi las/ las mtha' sbyin sreg las mi byed na shi sa bstan pa/ bdag bskyed/ rtsa dbu ma'i man ngag lha mo nag mo'i zhal gdams rnams so/ /lnga pa man ngag phran

tshegs la/ sre'u gso ba'i yi ge che chung gnyis/ las rgyas pa yid bzhin nor bu/ gri lag gi dbang gi las/ bsgrub bya dbang du bya ba/ 'khon nag zas su bza' ba/ ltas ngan btang
ba/ cho 'phrul btang ba/ bskrad pa'i las/ yang bskrad pa'i las zhal shes dang bcas pa/ mnan pa'i las/ ma hA bA la la brten te 'dre mnan pa/ shwa zlog mgon po la rang dang
slob ma rdzas dang yo byad la sogs pa gtod pa/ gtsug lag khang gtod pa/ de'i lag len gsal byed/ gnas dang mal cha nor rdzas bsrung ba/ mgon po'i gsang ba/ dam tshig gso
ba/ nyams chag bskangs bshags/ spyod lam dang dbang gi bya ba rnams so/ /de ltar dpal rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i man ngag dang yi ge'i tho 'di ni/ dpal ldan
sa skya pa'i lugs tshang la ma nor bar bkod pa yin la/ gzhan dag gi mgon po gdong brnyan can gyi man ngag bsres te/ dkyil 'khor dang / sku gsung thugs yon tan dang 'phrin
las kyi mgon po sogs su phye ba/ blun po mgu bar byed pa'i yi ge du ma snang ba/ mkhas pa dag gis mchil ma'i thal ba ltar ring du dor bar bya/ zhes pa de dag ni mus sras
pa'i dkar chag nas ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ man ngag gi yig skor de rnams yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa yan chad zhal bzhi pa'i man
ngag gzhan dang 'dra la/ des sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje A nanda ma ti/ zur ston shAkya shrI bha dra/ rje mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgyud gsum smra ba shes
rab rin chen/ rje tshar chen blo gsal rgya

mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang rje bla
mas mus srad pa'i dkar chag nang gi man ngag 'di rnams bla ma gzhan dang gzhan dag las kyang gsan gsungs so/ ! /yang zhing skyong dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi rgyud dang
/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang / las tshogs kyi yig sna mang po dang bcas pa/ bai ro tsa na dang / rje sa chen dang / yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan sogs kyis mdzad pa'i
lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ padma badzra/ ra hu la/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dpal dam tshig gi rdo rje/ 'chi med blo
gros bzang po/ mkhas pa bai rAo tsa na/ dpal chen sga lo/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yar bsgom/
rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal
mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun spangs chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje
'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'khon sa skya pa'i bka' srung dkar bdud lcam dral gyi sgrub skor/ 'khon rog shes
rab tshul khrims la/ bzhi thog bla brang

gi ltag gi nyi zla phug par chos skyong rang gis dngos su gnang ba'i yig skor cha tshang dang bcas pa/ bdud rgyal thod phreng can gyi rgyud/ man ngag zhar byung dang bcas pa
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab
yon tan/ 'khon tshul khrims rgyal po/ 'khon rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims/
'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon
po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ kha 'ub pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kun bzang chos
kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rje btsun de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal ldan lha mo 'dod pa khams kyi dbang phyug ma 'jigs byed dud pa'i sol ba can gyi chos skor thob pa la/ phyi
sgrub gtso rkyang gi rjes gnang rngog bsod nams don grub kyis mdzad

pa/ dang / gsang sgrub nan chags ma lha nyi shu'i rjes gnang rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyi yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/
'phags pa klu sgrub/ lus med ye shes mkha' 'gro grub chen ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog thogs med grags pa/ rgyal
tsha ra mo/ kun dga' rdo rje/ gzi brjid grags pa/ rin chen bzang po/ chos rgyal ba/ don grub dpal/ rngog byang chub dpal/ rngog bsod nams don grub/ rngog bsod nams lhun
po/ rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ drin can tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rgyal tsha ra mo/ slob dpon lcam me/ slob dpon nam mkha' dbang phyug kun dga' dbang phyug rin dpal/ grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ kun dga' bzang po/ rngog bsod nams don grub/ shAkya don 'grub/ bsod nams lhun po man 'dra/ yang na rin chen bzang po nas/ rin chen dpal/ dpal gyi rdo rje/ slob
dpon bzang dpal/ byang chub dpal man 'dra/ yang na rin chen bzang po/ sangs rgyas seng ge dpal gyi rdo rje man 'dra/ ! /dpal ldan lha mo dud sol ma'i man ngag zab mo'i chos
skor yongs rdzogs kyi glegs bam thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar glegs bam dkar chag rje tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang rngog zhe sdang
rdo

rjes mdzad pa/ de'i lag len gyi yi ge rngog bsod nams don grub kyis mdzad pa/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa/ de'i gsal byed mar rngog gi phyag len
gyi yi ge gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge rgyas pa rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ rgyud kyi skor la/ mkha' 'gro ma me lce 'bar ba'i rgyud le'u nyi shu rtsa
gnyis pa/ dud sol ma'i sgos rgyud dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud/ phyi sgrub kyi skor la lha mo'i sgrub thabs bram zes mdzad pa/ de'i bsdus don shog gcig ma/ de'i 'grel pa
lag len gyi zhal gdams shin tu zab pa/ gsang sgrub ma mo nyer gcig gi rjes gnang / lha mo'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge sgrub pa dang las sbyor gyi zhal gdams/ yang na dud sol ma'i
zhal gdams zab mo/ zhal gdams rmis ltas ma/ gsang sgrub kyi rgya gzhung birWa pas mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa lag len ma/ drag mo rkang thang rno ba'i mde'u kha la reg chod/
drag mo rkang thang gi sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa/ drag mo rkang thang yang snying bkol ba'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo yang gsang rkang thang du bsgrub pa/ tshe dang bsod
nams rgyas pa sogs kyi yi ge rten dang ltas ngan dbab pa'i yi ge mngon shes dang pra dbab pa'i yi ge zhal shes dang bcas pa/ dud sol ma'i gtor chog rgyas pa/ dud sol ma'i
spyan 'dren/ mchod 'bul/ gtor bskangs/ gtor bshags/ bstan skyong sogs kyi yi ge bstod pa 'phrin las rnam bzhi ma/ lha dbang po brgya byin gyi dge bcu'i sgo nas bstod
pa/ phyogs bcu'i lha mo'i bstod bskul/ gtor zor

'phangs pa'i yi ge gtor mnan gyi yi ge lha mo'i 'phrin las kyi las byang rgyas pa/ rnga brdung thabs kyi yi ge sgrub thabs mkhan chen gnas drug pas mdzad pa'i yi ge ste dkar
chag nang bzhin tshang bar thob/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin pas mdzad pa'i phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge yang thos/ ! /yang rje de nyid kyi drung du/ rdo rje 'jigs byed
kyi man ngag gi yig skor dbus stod pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ rgyud rtog pa gsum pa'i man ngag gi zhal shes/ rtog gsum 'phrul 'khor gyi yi ge
gshin rje gshed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi lung sbyor rin chen 'od kyi sgron ma/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bsnyen sgrub kyi yi ge snying gtam lag len/ de nyid grub pa'i rtags rmi
lam gyi brtag tshul/ drag shul spyod pa'i cho ga'i yi ge 'jigs byed la brten pa'i zhi ba dang / tshe bsring ba dang / 'byor pa dang / rig brgyud rgyas par byed pa'i sbyin
sreg gi cho ga 'jigs byed la brten nas yams nad dang / gdon dang / dgra bgegs zhi bar byed pa'i man ngag rgyal srid dang grags pa dang 'byor pa chen po thob par 'jigs
byed la brten nas bsgrub pa'i gdams ngag rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dbang gi sbyin sreg de'i 'gugs pa'i man ngag zab mo/ rgyal po dang btsun mo la sogs pa dbang du bya ba'i man
ngag rnal 'byor pa pho mo gang yin kyang pha rol po dbang bsdud kyi man ngag bu mo rengs pa'i sbyor ba/ 'jigs byed kyi las ma grub na spogs pa'i cho ga dpal gshin rje
gshed kyi rtsa ba'i sngags bzlas pa'i tshul

nges pa seng ge'i nga ro/ 'jigs byed la brten nas pha rol po dbye ba'i man ngag gtan dgra yul nas bskrad pa'i man ngag rgyal blon btsun mo dmag dpung dang bcas pa rengs pa'i
man ngag yang pha rol po rengs par byed pa'i gdams ngag gcig gdug pa can gyi dbang po rnams nyams par byed pa'i man ngag dgra bo srin por 'dzin pa'i man ngag dgra bo la
rims nad btang ba'i man ngag dgra bo smyo ru 'jug pa'i man ngag 'jig rten gsum gyi bdud sde phung bar byed pa'i man ngag 'jigs byed la brten pa'i sa gsum 'joms pa'i 'khrul
'khor/ las sbyor bdud sde'i mtshon cha 'bar ba'i phreng ba/ mngon spyod kyi yi ge bshan pa chen po rnam par rol pa spog chog gi man ngag 'jigs byed kyi drag po'i sbyin
sreg dus kyi me lce 'bar ba/ gtor ma drug cu rtsa bzhi'i man ngag gi yi ge bzlas pa'i man ngag thugs kyi 'khor lo'i gdams pa/ rtog pa bdun pa'i 'phrul 'khor gyi yi ge gshin
rje rgyal po bsad pa'i cho ga btsun mo dang bcas pa bsad pa'i man ngag rtsa sngags kyi 'khrul 'khor dngos grub kyi gzi brjid rab snang zhes bya ba/ rdo rje 'jigs byed
las thams cad kyi sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'khor lo rin po che'i mdzod ces bya ba/ rtog bdun 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga gshin rje dmar nag gdong drug sogs la brten nas sems can
gyi don du 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga rtsom tshul/ rgyud rtog gsum gyi sa bcad/ rtog gsum gyi rgyas 'grel rin po che'i snye ma rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dbus stod pa dpal
'dzin nyi ma bzang po/ bla ma stag lung

pa/ zha lu ba chen po stag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje/ mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ 'gos ston rdo rje seng ge tshar chen blo gsal rgya
