mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'jigs byed kyi rgyud rtog pa bdun pa'i rnam bshad rgyal ston gyis mdzad pa'i steng nas lung bshad shin tu smin pa dang / uShNi Sha rwa
lugs kyi yig sna la/ de'i mngon rtogs/ srung zlog gnyis kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag lhan thabs kyi yi ge zhal gdams gnad kyi lde mig drag po'i las sbyor gyi yig sna/ srung
zlog zab gnad/ gzhan yang zhal shes kyi yig chung 'ga' re dang bcas pa dang / las gshin lha bcu gsum gyi mchod chog thar pa gling pa arYa de bas mdzad pa rnams thos pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ro langs ma/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas
pa/ padma badzra/ dI pa~M ka ra rakShi ta/ bla ma rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa shes rab rgyal
mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhas grub brtson 'grus byang chub/ gnyen po ba slob dpon kun dga' rgya mtsho/ dbus stod pa
yon tan chos

rin/ yer pa ba brtson 'grus rgya mtsho/ mal gro ba grub chen chos skyong rgya mtsho/ mdo khams pa bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin mkhyen
brtse dbang phyug mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos kyi rgya mtsho/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o// ! //yang sa skya pa'i man ngag 'jam dpal nag po'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa chung ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/
slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paN/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa ye shes dpal/ blo bzang dkar mo/ dkon mchog thugs
rje/ gling smad paNDi ta/ shes rab dpal ldan/ khams gsum thams cad mkhyen pa/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po/ slob dpon chen po rin chen chos mchog
mdo khams pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ rje tshe dbang bkra shis/ mthu stobs dbang phyug rnam rgyal bkra shis/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'di'i man ngag yongs rdzogs kyi yi ge rje sa chen gyi gsung rab dang / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa gnyis ka'i
lung yang thos so/ ! /mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i sgrub skor las tshogs mang po dang lhag par rjes gnang / bris sku bya thabs/ rab gnas sogs kyi yig chung zhal shes mang
po rdo rje 'dzin pa nam mkha'i

mtshan can gyis phyogs gcig tu bris pa'i man ngag gi yi ge gsar rnying rnams kyi lung yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ye shes kyi mgon po/ ra hu la gupta badzra/ khyung
po rnal 'byor/ rmog cog pa/ skyer sgang pa/ gnyan ston rin po che/ sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub tsang ma shang ston/ rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag pa byams pa dpal/ blo gros
dpal bzang / kun dga' dpal bzang / chos rgyal dpal bzang / 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rje/ rje rdo ring pa/ rje tshar chen/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang
phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang gnod sbyin chen po zangs kyi bag tse can gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ma hA de wa/ A tsarYa nyi 'od grags pa/ sras zla ba nag po/ paNDi ta dha ra tra shu/ mgar lo tsA ba/ gnam kha 'ub pa/ rje sa chen/ shu bu bkra
shis 'od zer/ grub thob mdar char/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje/ jo sras sangs rgyas rin chen/ shes rab mtsho/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug lcang spe ba seng ge 'bum/ kun
mkhyen dpal ldan pa/ seng ge bzang po/ rnam grol ba rin chen bkra shis/ rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po/ bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu dpal/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ sgyi
chu ba shes rab rin chen/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug grub mchog bsod nams chos 'phel/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang phyug rab
brtan/ des bdag

sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang mthu stobs thogs med dpal mgon stag zhon nag po gtso 'khor gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag
na rdo rje/ slob dpon shinta garbha/ khrag 'thung nag po/ slob dpon padma/ bal po bha su dha ra/ snub ye shes/ gter ston rgya zhang khroM/ gter ston grwa pa kun dga'
grags/ so ban 'bum grags/ skyo ban mthu chen/ lce mdo sde seng ge rje btsun sga lo/ lce blo ldan seng ge lce btsun bsod nams dpal/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs
rin chen rgyal mtshan/ dga' gdong pa chos rgyal dpal bzang / dpal ri ba chos rgyal dpal bzang / rje btsun yab chos rgyal rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen
thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis la nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje dbang
phyug rab brtan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na rje btsun sga lo/ sras shes rab seng ge bla ma a ka ra siddhi/ bla ma rin chen dpal
bzang po/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na lce mdo sde seng ge gru shAkya 'bum/ lce blo ldan seng ge man 'dra/ gtor chog bskang gso rnams tshar chen gyis mdzad
pa'i lung yang thos so/ /'dir smras pa/ bhaTTa ra ka shwa ra Ta tri dha syA a dhiShTha na/rje btsun dbang phyug rab brtan byin rlabs kyis/ /shrI manta a mr-i ta A yuHtsa
bho ga tsa/dpal ldan 'chi med tshe dang longs spyod dang / /A shwa raHba ra

tsA nanda puNya tsa/dbang phyug mchog dang mtha' yas bsod nams dang / /ya sha aya da ya puShTiM shre yantu/snyan grags dar zhing rgyas pa'i dge legs mdzod/ /bdag kyang sa skya'i
rje btsun snyan brgyud kyi/ /gter chen nyams rtogs mnga' bdag khyed lta bur/ /gyur nas bstan 'gro'i don mang mthar phyin te/ /skal bzang mang po'i re ba skong bar shog
/dbang bcu mnga' ba'i skyabs mchog thugs rje yis/ /nyams rtogs yon tan kun gyis rgyud phyug cing / /'chi med rab brtan dbang po kun gsal ba'i/ /ngang nas 'di phyi'i don
kun 'grub gyur cig /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/
chos kyi rje nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dbang phyug rab brtan gyis rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te brgyad pa'o// //mangga laM// // ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs
bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART IX: Teachings from Ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa (1572-1641); vol. kha, text no. 7, pp. 377-780

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las mkhan chen 'jam
pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang chos kyi grags pas rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ sarba bi dznyA na lo ka tsakShu bhaTTa ra ka ma ho pA dhya ratna wa ge shwa ra dharma kirti pA de padmo mu laM pra Na mya/ bod skad du/ thams cad rnam par
mkhyen pa'i 'jig rten gyi mig rje btsun mkhan chen rin po che ngag dbang chos grags zhabs kyi padmo'i drung du rab tu 'dud do/ /mdo rgyud man ngag rig gnas kyis bsdus pa'i/
/shes bya ma lus gzigs pa'i thams cad mkhyen/ /phyi rabs bstan 'dzin kun gyi rgyan gcig po/ /ngag dbang chos grags dran no brtse bas skyongs/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam
par gyur pa mi 'phrog pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje tshad med pa'i mnga' bdag mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi rnam thar sngon gyi skyes chen rnams dang dbyer med nges pa'i 'gran
bral gyi yongs 'dzin dam pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyi drung du dam pa'i chos kyi

bka' drin nos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar/ ! /tshe dpag med grub chen dze tA ri lugs kyi dbang bskur ba lan grangs mang du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ slob dpon
dgra las rnam rgyal/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po/ ting 'dzin bzang po/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal
ba/ brag phug pa blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs

'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje btsun dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na
sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang nas/ gu ge paNDi ta/ glo
bo mkhan chen/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ ! /

yang rje de nyid kyi drung du/ rje btsun bcom ldan 'das ma sgrol dkar spyan bdun ma yid bzhin gyi 'khor lo'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro bas de'i tshe khrid nyams khrid du bstsal
nas/ rgyab rten gyi lung la/ khrid yig zla ba'i chu rgyun gyi nyams len gyi yi ge rjes gnang brgyud 'debs dang bcas pa rje tshar pas mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg mkhyen brtse
bas mdzad pa/ bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs dang / sbyin sreg gi yi ge sogs 'di skor gyi chos sna mang po'i yig lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma
dkar mo/ paN grub ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa/ rje btsun ba ri lo tsA ba/ grub chen sle nag pa/ bshes gnyen sbre pa/ mnyam med sgam po ba/ dwags
sgom tshul khrims snying po/ sgom byung shes rab byang chub/ 'dul 'dzin pa/ rje 'bri khung

pa/ rje dam chos gling pa/ bla ma chos kyi tshul khrims/ mnyam med lha lung pa/ theg gnas pa chen po/ bla ma chos kyi dbang phyug 'dren mchog byang chub bzang po/ kun mkhyen
bkra shis rnam rgyal/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / spangs gshong ha ri kha pa dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun karma 'phrin las pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam
pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo nas brgyud pa'i byin rlabs sam dbang skur zab mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med mgon/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/
ti pu pa/ ras chung rdo rje grags/ mi la bzhad pa'i rdo rje/ dwags po lha rje/ khams pa rdo rgyal/ 'bri khung 'jig rten mgon po/ spyan snga ba/ yang dgon pa/ spyan snga
rin chen ldan/ zur phug pa/ chos rje rgyal mtshan dpal/ bde legs rin chen/ kun dga' dpal bzang po/ dpal ldan bzang po/ chos rje dpal mgon pa/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis/ de gnyis kyis 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rig 'dzin rgod ldem pa nas brgyud pa'i tshe
dbang

lcags sdong ma thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rgyal ba rigs lnga/ sprul sku phyag na rdo rje/ smug nag dbang gi mkha' 'gro/ tshangs pa'i rgyal
po gdong gsum pa/ rig 'dzin lha dbang brgya byin/ rig 'dzin klu rgyal 'jog po/ skal ldan rgyal po dza/ mkhas pa shAkya pra bha/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ paN chen bi ma
la mi tra/ bal po shi la manydzu/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ sprul sku rig 'dzin chen po/ sras mchog rnam rgyal mgon po/ sngags 'chang rdo rje dpal/ mtshan ldan byams
pa bshes gnyen/ bla ma sangs rgyas dpal bzang / sngags 'chang chos rgyal bsod nams/ drin can tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rig 'dzin rtsa ba'i
bla ma/bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rgyud sde spyi'i dgongs
pa 'grel pa slob dpon chen po a bhya ka ras mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa la/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i
gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs lha bcu dgu/ 'phags lugs lha so gnyis/ rnam snang sgyu dra lha zhe gsum/ dgra nag lha bcu gsum ste pha rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi/ brtag
gnyis nas gsungs pa'i kyai rdor lha dgu ma'i bzhi/ gur rigs bsdus lha nga gsum/ sambu Ti'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i bdag med ma lha mo nyer gsum/ brtag gnyis nas gsungs pa'i
bdag med lha mo

bco lnga/ brtag gnyis nas gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle lha mo bco lnga/ gur nas gsungs pa'i rdo rje sgrol ma lha bcu gcig samba Ti nas bshad pa'i he ru ka lha bcu bdun te dkyil
'khor bcu gsum po 'di kyai rdo rje'i phyogs su gtogs so/ /samba Ti nas bshad pa'i rdor sems zhi ba dkar po lha so bdun/ bde mchog rtsa bshad kyi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i 'khor
lo bde mchog zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa/ sngon po zhal gcig phyag gnyis ma/ gser mdog can zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa ste de gsum gtso bor gyur pa'i lha re gnyis re yod
pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum/ phag mo dmar mo/ sngon mo/ ser mo gsum gtso bor byas pa'i phag mo lha so bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor gsum/ a bhi dha na nas gsungs pa'i hU~M mdzad lha bcu
gcig a bhi dha na las gsungs pa'i 'khor los bsgyur drug lha bdun cu rtsa gnyis/ rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i rdo rje bdud rtsi lha nyer gcig bdud rtsi hU~M
mdzad lha nyer dgu/ bdud rtsi khro bo lha nyer gcig bdud rtsi 'khyil ba lha bcu gsum/ sangs rgyas thod pa lha nyer lnga/ sangs rgyas thod pa shes rab ma dang bral ba lha
dgu/ ma hA ma ya'i rgyud chung las gsungs pa'i ma hA ma ya lha lnga/ gdan bzhi'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i rnal 'byor nam mkha' lha nga brgyad/ ye shes mkha' 'gro lha bcu gsum/
drang srong nyi ma'i shing rta sogs 'dul ba'i ched du gsungs pa dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo lha drug brgya so bzhi/ de nyid 'dus pa'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i rdor dbyings
lha nga gsum/ sbyong rgyud dang brtag pa phyogs

gcig pa las gsungs pa'i gtsug dgu lha so bdun/ sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i rgyud dang / 'jam dpal grags pa'i mtshan brjod 'grel chen las gsungs pa'i chos dbyings gsung dbang lha
nyis brgya nyer gcig 'byung 'dul lha so gsum mam so bzhi/ 'od zer can gyi rtogs pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer can lha nyer lnga/ gzungs grwa lnga'i rtog pa las gsungs pa'i gzungs
grwa lnga lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor te pha rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi/ kyai rdor bcu gsum/ bde mchog bco brgyad/ dus 'khor/ yo ga'i gsum/ bya spyod kyi gsum ste
phreng rkyang gi dbang du byas pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis kyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ a bha ya ka ra/ a nu pa ma
rakShi ta/ bIkSha ta de ba/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ bhu mi shrI/de'i dbon po/ bi ma la shrI/ de'i sras/ bo dhi singha/ skyi ston 'jam dbyangs/ kun mkhyen chen po/ ma ti paN
chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge ngor chen dkon mchog lhun
grub/ 'dren mchog nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na a bha ya ka ra/ nA ya ka pa/ dha sha bha la shrI/ bIkSha ta de ba man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na paN chen shAkya shrI/ glang baM po ba/
gnyag rdo rje 'dzin

pa/ khams pa dkon mchog rin chen/lho tshad pa yang zer/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ de la kun mkhyen chen pos ye shes zhabs lugs kyi gtso byas phal che ba zhus/ de la ma ti paN chen/
sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o/ /yang dkyil 'khor bsrung ba lnga/ mkha' 'gro lnga/ 'khor los bsgyur ba drug rnams so sor phye nas/ lnga
bcu rtsa lngar phye ba'i brgyud pa ni/ a bha ya/ shAkya rakShi ta/ gho dra gu ru/ bi bhu ta tsandra/ go de ba shrI/ kShanti shrI/ paNDi ta buddha shrI/ paNDi ta nA tha/
skyi ston 'jam dbyangs/ kun mkhyen chen po/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o/ /yang na a bha ya/ legs spyod 'byung
gnas sbas pa/ bde ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pa/ ratna rakShi ta/ zhang lo tsA ba grub pa dpal/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ bla ma dgus pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ skyi ston man
'dra'o/ ! /yang dkyil 'khor nyer brgyad du bsdus kyai rdor lha dgu ma bzhi/ bcu bdun ma bzhi/ bdag med ma gnyis/ bde mchog gsum/ phag mo gsum/ bdud bzhi rnams re re bsdus
nas/ pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kha che paN chen yan sngar dang 'dra/ de nas lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ lha khang dkar ru ma/ yar lung pa slob dpon ral gri'i gcung po sher smon/
bla ma byang seng / skyi ston pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na a bha ya/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ bIkSha ta de ba/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ dbon po bhu mi shrI/ de'i sras bi ma la shrI
bha dra/ lo tsA ba blo ldan/ byang seng pa/ mkhas mchog pa/skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen chen po/ sa bzang ma ti paN

chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ ! /yang slob dpon chen po darpan A tsarYa zhes bya ba tshems lan nyi shu brjes sku tshe lo stong dang nyis
brgya bzhes pa des mdzad pa'i/ kr-i ya sa mutstsha zhes bya ba rdo rje slob dpon rnams la nye bar mkho ba'i cho ga mtha' yas pa phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa'i bstan bcos chen
po nas 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam grangs la/ sngar rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis po ji lta ba bzhugs pa la/ de'i steng du gza' yum
gyi dkyil 'khor/ nor rgyun ma'i dkyil 'khor/ rnam rgyal gyi dkyil 'khor te dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bstan pas dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang bskur ba'i cho
ga rgyas par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ a bha ya ka ra/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ dar paN a tsarYa/ 'gro ba'i me long / sa manda bha
dra/kun tu bzang po/ dznyA na dzyo ti/ye shes kyi glog shrI ha nu manta/dpal yid kyi 'gram pa/ shrI bhunydza bha dra/'jam dpal bzang po/ shrI bha dra/dpal bzang po/ dharmA
dzyo ti bha dra/chos kyi thog bzang po/ man dzi ba bha dra/yid rgyal bzang po/ sho taM shrI bha dra/wa tru ma'i yi ge la sho dang go nor ba yod pas go tam shrI yin nam/
shrI bi dza ya bha dra/dpal rnam rgyal bzang po'i zhabs/ shrI mA da na bha dra pa da/dpal myos bzang po'i zhabs/ shrI lakShmi bha dra bA da/dpal phun tshogs bzang po'i
zhabs/ ga ga na bha dra/nam mkha' bzang po/ A tA ya dzi ba bha dra/chu'i 'tsho ba bzang po/ shrI ha ra Sha bha dra pA dra/dpal 'phrog byed bzang po'i zhabs/ a bha ga bha
dra/skal ldan bzang po 'di bal po ye rang paNDi ta yin no/ /bal

yul ye rang gi paNDi ta dza ba ta a nanda bi dza bha dra/skye dgu kun dga' 'tsho ba bzang po/ de'i sras/ paNDi ta mahA bo dhi/byang chub chen po/ des sa bzang 'phags pa ku
ma ra ma ti/ bikShi a nanda bha dra rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ man gong bzhin no/ /'di'i paNDi ta mahA bo dhi'i lo rgyus ni/ dza ba paNDi ta la sras yun ring du ma
byung ba la/ rdo rje gdan du byang chub chen po la/ gsol ba 'debs su byon pas/ yum mngal dang ldan par gyur nas sras gcig bltams pas mtshan mahA bo dhir btags so/ /kr-i
ya'i dbang rgyun 'di bod du ma 'gyur ba la/ dus phyis dpal ldan sa skyar 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan pa'i phyag tu sa mutstsha'i rgya dpe zhig bal yul gyi tshong pa'i
lag nas byung ba de kun spangs chos grags pa'i phyag tu byung / de nyid kyi bka'i mnyan pas bskul zhing mthun rkyen sbyar ba la brten nas/ br-i ka ma la shi la'i paNDi
ta chen po manydzu shrI dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba sa bzang gzhon nu blo gros kyis bsgyur nas/ dbang lung gsan sa ma rnyed par yod pa'i tshe mnga' ris pa rdo rje dpal gyis
ye rang du sa mu tstsha'i dbang zhus zer ba'i gtam gsan nas/ sa bzang 'phags pa dpon g.yog bdun gyis ye rang du byon nas paNDi ta ma hA bo dhi la dbang lung yongs su rdzogs
par thob nas dar rgyas su mdzad pa'o/ ! /yang rje thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid kyi drung du/ gnyis med kyi rgyud las gsungs pa rje btsun sa skya pa la kyai rdo rje la
bka' srol bzhi bzhugs pa'i thog mar kyai rdo rje Dombhi lugs kyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi he ru ka a la la

badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ dza ya shrI dznyA na/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi lA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/
sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ rong pa sga lo/ rong pa shes rab seng ge zhang grags 'byor/ bla ma bsod nams lhun grub/ bla ma ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ bla chen
kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ ra ston yon tan dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun
dga' bsod nams/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos
grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs rdo rje 'chang kun bzang bas mdzad pa dang / dkyil chog rje btsun bsod nams rtse mos mdzad
pa'i lung dang bcas pa thos so/ ! /kyai rdo rje grub chen mtsho skyes lugs kyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bi la sya badzra/ yan lag med pa'i rdo
rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ indra bhu ti/ lcam legs smin/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi/ se 'khar chung ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen/ rta stag
so ba khu dbon/ rgyal mtshan grags/ dpal chu bo ri pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje

'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar
rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog 'dor len byed tshul kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i mtsho skyes phra mig maNDal mchod chog ngor chen kun bzang
gis mdzad pa/ dkyil chog rje btsun bsod nams rtse mos mdzad pa/ nas gling ma'i dbang gong ma'i cho ga mus chen gyis mdzad pa yang thos/ ! /kyai rdo rje grub chen nag
po lugs kyi sku gsung thugs snying po kyai rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ nag po zhi ba bzang
po/ 'gos khug pa lhas btsas/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon skyi chu ba shAkya 'bar/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun
rin po che/ dkar shAkya grags/ ba de lung pa kun bzang dpal/ bla ma dar ma ye shes/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ bla ma dpal ldan don grub/ sa bzang 'phags
pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ rje lha mchog seng ge buddha singha / thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod
nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen

thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng
ge man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ kun dbang / kun mkhyen/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje gnyan chen grags pa blo gros/ rje buddha singha man 'dra'o/ ! /yang mkhan chen
'jam pa'i dbyangs de nyid kyi drung du/ grub chen ma Ni ka badzra gyi lung rnam 'joms lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang
/ phyag na rdo rje/ rje btsun byams pa/ skal ldan ga ga dha ra/ slob dpon ma Ni badzra/ paNDi ta dza ya warma/ paNDi ta dznyA na shrI/ lo tsA ba cog grub rab zhi/ bla ma
yon tan legs pa/ rje bsam gtan dbang phyug bla ma don grub ye shes/ chos kyi blo gros/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rje dkon mchog rdo rje/ bla ma shes rab 'bum/ rong pa
chos kyi dbang phyug bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/ bya sder ba byang chub gzhon nu/ bya sder ba byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang / gu ge paNDi
ta/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ 'khon dkon mchog tshul khrims/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen
thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang gtsug tor gdugs dkar can gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
sangs rgyas gdugs dkar mo

can/ slob dpon tsandra go mi/ gi ra wa ta/ badzra rakShi/ shu raM ga bha dra/ kha che paNDi ta dkar po/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun
rin po che/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ bla ma ye shes rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rin po che/ zhang ye shes/ bla ma dkon mchog tshul khrims/ bag ston
gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang / mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang / mkhas grub dpal ldan
rdo rje/ mkhan chen ratna shi la/ rje sgo rum pa/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ mkha' 'gro ma de wa sbyin/ kha che ratna badzra/ bram ze saddza na/ sras ma na dznyA nA pA la/
dmyal pa ye shes dbang phyug dge bsrung / god sngon pa/ spu ston 'bar thog pho rog dar ma mdo/ thog pa 'bur/ jo gdan dbang rin/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ ston pa dar ma shAkya/
spu bos dbang / lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bag ston man 'dra'o/ ! /yang gzungs grwa lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i rigs gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/
phyag rdor/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri ba/ gnyan ston grags/ gnyan rin chen grags/ lha sa'i gnas brtan dkon rgyal/ de'i sras rdog ston bya'u rgyal/ rgyal
tsha lung mang po/ rong pa sher

seng / kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ lce nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje ka bzhi pa chen po/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi
rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ yab sras de gsum la rje dbang phyug rab brtan pas gsan/ de la mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag
dbang chos grags kyis gsan/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na mkhyen rab chos rje/ sgog 'brog gnyis las/ byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs/
rje dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ ! /yang 'od zer can ma lha lnga'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ jo bo ta ti a shwa ka shrI/ la li ta badzra/
a mo gha badzra/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ sga lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/
sras shes rab seng ge 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen bu/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ rje rdo rje 'chang / paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ nam brtan pa/
ratna shi la/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa/ rje mkhyen brtse dbang phyug bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang bcom ldan 'das sgyu 'phrul chen po snying rje'i rnam par rol pa yid bde'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las gsungs pa'i sgyu ma chen
po lha lnga'i

rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen ku ku ri pa/ mtsho skyes rdo
rje/ Dombhi ba/ ti lo pa/ na ro pa/ mar lo chos kyi blo gros/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog tsha chos sku/ rngog tsha dkon mchog dpal/ klo kya
dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ khro phu ba sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu
ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ rje rdo rje 'chang / paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun
grub/ rje kun dga' grol mchog 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na rje kun dga' grol mchog mkhan chen karma bzang po/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na
rdo rje/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ku ri pa/ nA ro pa/ shanti pa/ jo bo rje/ rong pa mgar dge klo kya stod pa/ steng pa thugs gsal/ 'phar lung pa rgyal sras/ rkyang po
nyi she zla tsha dar rgyas/ zla tsha grags rgyal/ spen phug pa bsod nams mdzes/ don ri grags chen/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras rin chen
rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog

grub/ ka bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ chu mig kha pa dkon mchog dpal bzang / 'brog sgang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling pa 'jam dbyangs chen po/
thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ gsang
phu ba rngog legs pa'i shes rab/ mnga' ris pa byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal mtshan/ phu chung pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ka ma ba 'brom rin chen rgyal mtshan/ zhang
ston dar ma rgyal mtshan/ stabs ka ba 'brom byang chub bzang po/ ston pa nam mkha' rin chen/ snar thang mkhan po nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rin chen gling pa rin chen byang chub/
sga lung pa rigs kyi bdag po'i dpal/ sga lung pa byang chub dpal/ smyug pa'i slob dpon bsod nams 'od zer/ gos sngon chu ser ba sangs rgyas bzang po/ bya bral ba bsod
nams bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ stag tshang chos 'khor ba mkhan chen nam mkha' 'od zer/ pa tshab dga' ba gdong pa gnas brtan ye shes tshul khrims/ nub chos lung pa ratna
a ka ra shanti pa/ smyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lcags thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams dpal ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad
mkhyen pa

ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i ras bris
kyi dkyil 'khor la brten nas byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/ mchog dbang gong ma bzhi dang bcas pa rgyas par thob nas/ de dang 'brel ba'i lung gi skor la/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i
dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs bdag 'jug dang bcas pa rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags pas mdzad pa/ rje 'gyur med bde chen gyis mdzad pa'i dus 'khor gyi dbang gi
bshad pa chen po'i lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa 'bro lugs ni/ ston pa shAkya thub pa/ rgyal po zla ba bzang po/ lha'i dbang po/ gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i
dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan te chos rgyal bdun/ rigs ldan grags pa/ padma dkar po/ bzang po rnam rgyal/ shin bzang ba/ phyag na rin chen/ khyab 'jug
sbas pa/ nyi ma grags pa/ shin tu bzang po/ rgya mtsho rnam rgyal/ rgyal dka'/ nyi ma la sogs pa la rigs ldan nyer lnga'i nang nas rigs ldan bcu gcig pa rgyal dka' 'das pa
nas/ rigs ldan bcu gnyis pa nyi ma byon pa'i dus na/ slob dpon chen po tsi lu paNDi dus zhabs pa chen po byon nas dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang / rgyud 'grel man ngag mtha'
dag thob par 'dod cing / yang lugs gcig la tsi lu paNDi tas shambha lar byon pa'i tshe spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa dge slong zhig la yang dbang rgyud 'grel man ngag dang
bcas pa thob par bzhed

la/ yang lugs gcig la dus zhabs pa chen pos rigs ldan bcu bdun pa dpal skyong la zhus par yang bzhed de brtag par bya dgos/ de nas dus zhabs pa chung ba/ kha che zla ba mgon
po/rgyal sras na lendra pa/ bla ma lha rje/'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/ gra sgom dkon mchog bsrung / sgro ston gnam la brtsegs/ grub chen yu mo dad pa rgyal po/ sras
dharmA shwa ra/ bla ma nam mkha' 'od zer/ se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam gsar shes rab 'od zer/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/
byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ chos rje yon tan rgya mtsho/ jo nang kun mkhyen chen po/ chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ dbon rgyal ba jo bzang / rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags
pa/ shang ston kun dga' dpal ldan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / paN chen shes rab bkra shis/ rje btsun byams pa shAka 'od/ thugs sras chos dar grags 'phel/ lo chen 'gyur
med bde chen/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang dus 'khor rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/lugs
'di la tsi lu paNDi ta dang / dus zhabs pa chen po so sor bzhed par snang / tsi lu paNDi tas shambha lar byon nas spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa dge slong zhig la zhus/
des bo to a tsarYa/ dus zhabs pa chung ba manydzu kirti/ sa manta shrI/ rwa lo tsA ba chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun sga lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/
bla ma shes rab seng ge skyi ston

grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun mkhyen chen po man 'dra/ yang na/ sga lo/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ skyi ston man 'dra/ yang na/ sga lo/ bla ma tshul khrims dar/ dus 'khor
ba ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs zhabs/ skyi ston man 'dra/ ! /bu lugs kyi brgyud pa la yang gnyis las/ rwa lugs ni/ rong pa dus 'khor ba shes rab seng ge yan 'dra/ de nas
bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ 'bro lugs ni/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer yan 'dra/ de nas 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen
pa/ yang na se mo che ba/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ stag sde ba seng ge rgyal mtshan/ gshong lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gshong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ mang mkhar
lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ yang na/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ 'dzin pa rin chen shes rab/ shar pa dus 'khor ba
ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ dbon rgyal ba jo bzang /
rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags pa/ shang ston kun dga' dpal ldan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / paN chen shes rab bkra shis/ rje btsun byams pa shAkya 'od/ thugs sras chos
dar grags 'phel/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang dpal gsang
ba

'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba kun mkhyen rin po che'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa sa lugs ni/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sangs
rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ dpal sde ba/ dri med sbas pa/ ratna badzra/ ratna kirti/ bla ma paNDi ba/ gnyan lo/ kha'u pa/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/
'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bkras dpal ba/ dga' ldan pa/ khams pa rdor dpal/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ gangs pa grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rje
rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / kun mkhyen/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang
chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ kha che paN chen/ kha che ga ga dha ra/ paNDi ta bi na shrI/ khams pa
rdor rgyal man 'dra/ kha rag gnyos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam rdor/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ dpal bde ba/ dri med sbas pa/ yi ge'i
rnal 'byor pa/ kA hNa pa/ dznyA shrI/ ba liM a tsarYa/ gnyos ston rdo rje bla ma/ gnyos ston grags pa dpal/ lha nang pa/ rin chen do pa/ rdo rje tshul khrims/ rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ don ri grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs pa man 'dra/ yang na/ gnyos ston rdo rje bla ma/ gnyos ston dpal le/ gnyos ston grags pa

gong bzhin las/ rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags/ kun tu bzang po/ ye shes dpal bshes gnyen/ ratna kirti/ pu Nya shrI/ rwa rdo rje grags/ rdo rje sra brtan/ la stod dkon

rdo rje/ gnyis spangs zhabs/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ kun dga' snying po/ tha ga na/ shanti pa/ shaddha ka ra/ padma ka ra/ lo chen rin bzang / rkyang pa
chos blo/ dge bshes skyabs seng / rdo rje sra brtan man chad 'dra/ ! /yang dpal gsang ba 'dus pa spyan ras gzigs lha bcu dgu'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ spyan ras gzigs/ jo bo rje/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ rgya lcags ri ba/ rgya ston lcags ri ba/ shAkya grags/ spen phug pa/ dar shAkya pa/ zhang
g.ye ba/ gze ba don grub/ bar thang pa yab sras/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu
bsod nams/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ rje rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun bzang ba/ kun mkhyen/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog rin chen

pa/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /yang rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po de nyid kyi drung du kha 'ub brag rdzong pa'i nyams len gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa slob
bshad zab mo lung gi skor dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar snang ba gsum gyi khrid legs par thob nas/ de'i skabs su lung gi skor nos pa la/
bla ma rgya bod kyi rnam thar rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i glegs bam nang bzhugs pa/ sa skya pa chen po'i rnam thar rje btsun gyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon rin po che'i rnam thar
tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa/ rje btsun gyi rnam thar sa paN gyis mdzad pa dang / rnam thar mnal lam ma bandhe bshes gnyen grags kyis mdzad pa/ sa paN gyi rnam
thar lho pa rin chen dpal gyis mdzad pa dang / ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa rin po che'i rnam thar shar pa ye shes ye chen mo yin/ rgyal mtshan gyis
mdzad pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba'i rnam thar chos rje dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ tshogs sgom rin po che'i rnam thar gnyag snying po rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ nyan chen pa
bsod nams brtan pa'i rnam thar dkar po brag pas mdzad pa/ rgyal ba brag phug pa'i rnam thar ri khrod pas mdzad pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas
mdzad pa/ bla ma dam pa'i rnam thar dpal ldan pas

mdzad pa/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge'i rnam thar rang nyid kyis mdzad pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa'i rnam thar mus chen gyis mdzad pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal
mtshan gyi nam thar dang / grub chen buddha'i rnam thar ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa mus chen gyis mdzad pa/ mus
chen gyi rnam thar bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar yid 'phrog utpa la'i phreng ba/ rdo ring rin po che'i rnam thar/ tshar
chen gyi lam yig rnams tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa/ mus chen sems dpa' chen pos mdzad pa'i dpal kyai rdo rje'i mngon rtogs/ lus dkyil/ dbang chu gsum dang / de
dag gi gsal byed tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i lhan thabs rnams kyang thos/ snang gsum khrid kyi skabs su zin thun la brgyud pa'i lo rgyus dang / tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi'i
sgo nas chos kyi khog phug pa'i chos sna drug cu bgrangs tshul dang bcas pa dang / de nas snang ba gsum gyi khrid rnams rdzogs pa'i rjes su maNDal tshom bu lnga pa la
brten pa'i byang chub kyi mchog tu sems bskyed pa brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi phyag len phyogs gcig tu byas pa thob cing / de nas bla med rdo rje theg pa'i lam thun mong ma
yin pa la smin grol gnyis las/ thog mar rje btsun yab dpal dgyes pa rdo rje lha dgu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad tshang ba'i sgo
nas dbang btegs kyi dkyil 'khor sogs dbang chu chen mo las ji skad bshad pa'i tshul gyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub pa rgyas par thob

cing / de nas 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi khrid tshugs pa'i skabs der bla ma don yod grub pa'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs gnang ba thob nas lta khrid kyi nyams
blangs gnad gsum gyi sngon du rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi mtha' rten dang bcas pa legs par nos shing / lta
khrid kyi skabs su zin thun la dbang bzhi'i dam tshig spyi dang / khyad par rtsa ba dang yan lag gi ltung ba'i rnam gzhag rtsa ltung 'khrul spong gi steng nas gnang ba
thob/ de nas bum dbang gi phyi bskyed rim gyi khrid tshugs nas lam 'bras glegs bam gyi lung gnang ste/ de la yang thog mar glegs bam dkar chag rdo rje'i tshig rkang / gzhung
snyag ma/ kun gzhi'i yig chung / gdan rtsog lus dkyil/ 'chi bslu/ bum dbang gi mda' kha ma/ thig le'i rnal 'byor/ phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid/ dbang bzhi pa'i mda' kha
ma/ bar do'i gdams pa/ lam dbang / tshad ma bzhi/ gdams ngag drug rten 'brel lnga/ grib sel gyi sbyin sreg grib ma khrus dang tsha tshas sel ba/ thig le bsrung ba/ yig brgya'i
'don thabs/ rlung sbyor bdun gyi khrid/ bha ga'i yi ge bcu'i yig sna 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ dbang phyug gi don brgyad/ bcu gsum gyi phyed 'og ma'i mngon rtogs te gsal byed

mdor bsdus pa/ bdud rtsi ril

bu'i sgrub thabs/ gegs sel la byung rgyal du mi gtong pa'i gnad bzhi/ 'byung ba lus 'khrugs dang spyod lam gyi gsal ba/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba/ man ngag gi gnad drug
gi bkri ba/ gang zag dbang po rab 'bring tha gsum gyi sgo nas bkri ba/ gnad bcu gcig gi dkri ba/ lam 'jug ldog phyag rgya 'jug ldog lam bsre ba 'gros bzhi dang bcas pa/
phyi nang gi mdzad pa bcu gnyis/ lam zab bla ma'i yig chung ste glegs bam yongs su rdzogs pa thob/ de nas po ti dmar chung gi lugs kyi skor thos pa la/ thog mar bla ma tshad
ma'i skabs su brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ de'i kha skong / sa chen dang birWa pa mjal pa'i lo rgyus/ sga thang la bskur ba/ nyams myong tshad ma'i skabs gzhung ji lta ba

zhal shes/ dbang bzhi

/ lung tshad ma la/ lung 'di nyid dang zhib tu sbyar ba/ yang rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis rje sa chen la gnang ba'i zab chos bzhi ni/ lam zab khrid yig bla ma rin 'byung

sbyar

ba/ bir bsrung gsar ma rnams thos so/ /yang chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i gzhung bshad man ngag gter mdzod/ rje mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i bir bsrung thun
mong pa'i rgyun gyi nyams len gyi yi ge slob bshad brgyud pa gsum 'dus kyi gsol 'debs lam gyi rim pa'i smon lam dang bcas pa'i lung yang thos/ de'i skabs su nang bskyed
rim gyi khrid kyi gong du lam dus kyi dbang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi yig cha'i steng nas gnang ba mdzad nas/ nang bskyed rim dang ma 'brel ba'i lam zab phyi mar grags
pa dang / de las 'phros pa'i lam zab bla ma rin 'byung / nang bskyed rim dang 'brel ba'i lam zab nang ma ste lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs kyi bka' gsum/
bir bsrung thun mong ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs kyi bka' gnyis/ gsang dbang gi lam gtum mo'i khrid kyi sngon du rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i
byin rlabs kyi bka'/ 'di yum gyi lam dus kyi dbang yin gsungs nas thugs rtsis kyang che bar mdzad/ gzhan yang rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs bdag chen rdo rje 'chang

mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang rje klu sgrub rgya mtshos/ rje btsun dam pa kun dga' grol mchog la yang lam 'bras
yongs su rdzogs pa gsan gsungs/ ! /yang rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po de nyid kyi drung du/ gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i chos skor thos pa la/ thog mar lha lnga'i
dkyil 'khor ras bris la brten pa dbang bzhi mtha' rten dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa chag lugs ni/ 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub
chen bi ru pa/ Dombhi he ru ka bi ra ma ti/ gambhi ra ma ti/ niShka langga de wa/ ra wentra bha dra/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal/ gshong lo tsA
ba blo gros brtan pa/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug bya ster ba byang chub rin chen/ ra ga brag pa shAkya seng ge chos rje phyogs
las rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po/ rje btsun rdo ring ba
chen po/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la'o/ ! /dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ niska langka de wa yan gong bzhin/ de nas dpyal lo tsA ba chos bzang /dpyal pas sga lo la
bum dbang man chad las ma gnang ba la/ khong gis dha na shI la dang / 'jam gsar la

brgyud nas dbang gong ma gsum yang mdzad do/ /rje btsun sga lo/ rong pa sher bzang / skyi ston grags rgyal/ chos rje jo nang kun mkhyen/ chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ chos
rje ye shes rgyal mtshan pa man 'dra/ ! /dha na shI la'i lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bi ru pa/ nag po pa/ sa li pa/ shI la tsaNDa/ dha na shI la/ 'jam gsar/
rje btsun sga lo man sngar dang 'dra/ ! /rdzogs rim zab mo shin tu spros pa med pa'i de kho na nyid kyi man ngag nyams khrid du nos nas/ de dang 'brel bar spros med rgyun
gyi rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs/ 'od gsal 'char ba'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi byin rlabs/ lung gi skor la bi ru pas mdzad pa'i spros med rdo rje'i tshig rkang / gzhan yang birWa
pas mdzad pa'i bskyed rim gyi gzhung gsum dang / rdzogs rim gyi gzhung gsum/ las rdzogs kyi gzhung gnyis te brgyad/ ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi bum
pa/ dkyil chog bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun/ khrid yig spros med mdzes rgyan/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung la mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos zin bris mdzad pa'i khog
phub/ bskyed rim rnam bshad/ khrid kyi zur 'debs dang / yang rje klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gsol 'debs lam rim dang bcas pa/ rgyun gyi nyams len gyi yi ge rnams thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gshin rje gshed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ bi ru pa/ Dombhi pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ blo bzang snying po/ dar paN a tsarYa/ glo bo lo tsA ba/ bla ma
sa blo gros dpal pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng

ge bu ston rin po che/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ theg chen chos rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po/ rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na bla
ma dam pa nas/ chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ bdud
rtsi byin rlabs dang / rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ gshin rje gshed/ bi ru pa/ ma taM gi pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ la li ta badzra/ shanti rakShi ta/ dharmA
badzra/ dar paN a tsarYa/ glo bo lo tsA ba man 'dra/ ! /yang rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po de nyid kyi drung du/ gur rigs bsdus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ bi ru pa/ Dombhi he ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa dza ya shrI/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa'
bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ ne tse sbal ston/ rta stag so ba rin chen don 'grub/ gan pa
ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ kha char ba bsod nams rgyal

mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /sambhu Ti rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ bi ru pa/ Dombhi he ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa/ rgyal ba dpal/ mi thub zla
ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa
paN/ tshogs bsgom pa/ gnyag snying po rgyal mtshan/ zhang bkra shis dpal/ spangs sgang pa grags pa dpal/ paN chen ma ti/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid kyi drung du/
dgyes pa rdo rje rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' thob pa la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa/ thun mong ma yin pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje gur/ rgyud sde gzhan dang thun mong gi

bshad rgyud dpal sambu Ti rnams paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi lo tsA ba chen pos bsgyur pa/ rdo rje 'chang gnyis pa dpal sa skya pa'i bla ma gong ma rnams kyi mdzad
pa'i rgyud sde de rnams kyi rnam bshad la/ rje btsun sku mched kyis mdzad pa'i stong thun/ rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag dang / mngon par rtogs pa ljon shing gi steng nas
tshul bzhi sngon du 'gro ba can gyi rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa dag ldan/ gur gyi 'grel pa gur rgyan/ sambu Ti'i 'grel pa gnad kyi gsal byed dang bcas pa bsdus don so so'i steng
nas bshad bka' legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi he ru ka a la la badzra/ rdo rje nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms
pa/ rgyal ba dpal gyi ye shes/ slob dpon mi thub zla ba/ de la slob ma'i mchog dpa' bo rdo rje/ seng ge rdo rje/ sgra gcan 'dzin dang gsum las/ 'dir dpa' bo rdo rje/ des
lo tsA ba chen po shAkya ye shes la gnang / de la slob ma'i mchog 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ se mkhar chung pa/'di man ngag lugs kyi
rgyud 'dzin yin/ khyin lo tsA ba 'od kyi snang ba dang bzhi las/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ yang na/ bla ma mnga' ris pa/ sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ sa chen/ yang na se mkhar
chung pa/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa chen/ yang na khyin lo tsA ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa skya pa chen po ste/ de ltar brgyud pa'i bka' bab bzhi dang
ldan pa'i bla ma sa skya pa chen pos/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ tshul khrims

grags/ gtsug tor rgyal po dang gsum la gnang / de gsum kas rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan la gnang / des chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po la/ de nas 'phags
pa rin po che/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ de la dpal ldan bla ma dam pa dang / chos rje blo gros brtan pa/ de gnyis ka la bla ma dpal ldan
tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/
ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ kun mkhyen yongs 'dzin man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang nas/ gu ge paNDi ta/ glo bo mkhan/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo
rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ ! /yang rgyud sde'i dum bu che chung gnyis/ stong thun gnyis kyi don bsdus/ yab kyi bstod pa daNDa ka yum gyi bstod pa dri ma
med pa'i phreng ba/ de'i 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / dag ldan kha skong / dag ljon lung 'grel gnyis shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa dang / kyai
rdo rje'i rgyud kyi byung tshul dang bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar/ brtag gnyis kyi 'gyur bsabs pa shlau ka gnyis/ brtag gnyis kyi 'grel pa'i dkar chag rnams rje kun dga'
bzang gis mdzad pa

rnams thos so/ /rtsa rgyud rkyang pa 'phags mchan 'phags pa'i sa bcad dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal bzang po/ bla ma dpal
ldan seng ge chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ /rgyud gsum man ngag lugs kyi bshad srol gyi ring brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ nag po
pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a wa dhu ti pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi/ de la slob ma'i mchog bzhi las/ 'dir se mkhar chung ba/ de nas zhang dgon pa ba/ rje sa chen man sngar dang 'dra'o/
/nye brgyud ni/ bla med phyogs ni ris bsgyur mig bcas pa/ /rig byed kyis gsal lag pas me la bgos/ /de 'od kun gsal chu gter 'byung bar babs/ /blo ldan don 'di shes na
smra bar gyis/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang kun bzang / gu ge paNDi ta/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/
rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /tshe
dpag tu med pa'i mdo paNDi ta pu Nya sambha wa dang / pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur pa/ bla ma legs rin pa'i Tika chung gi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas shAkya thub pa/ phyag na rdo rje/ dzai ta ri/ don yod rdo rje mched/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po
che/ chos rje sa paN/ rgyal tshab chos

dbang / rong pa shes seng / bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ mgon po 'bum/ nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang / kun dbang pa/ 'dren
mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des
bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang chos kyi rje de nyid kyi drung du/ paN chen shAkya shrI nas brgyud pa'i bde mchog lhan skyes dkar po'i byin rlabs
sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas khrid zab mo nyams khrid du stsal nas/ de'i rgyab chos kyi lung gi skor la dpyal a mo ghas mdzad pa'i khrid yig rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs dang byin rlabs kyi yi ge gzhan khrid kyi yig rnying chung chung gnyis/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyis mdzad pa'i bde mchog dkar po'i tshe khrid/ sa los mdzad
pa'i bde mchog dkar po'i khrid kyi nyams len gyi yi ge rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'khor lo bde mchog paN chen shAkya shrI/ sa skya paN chen/
g.yag sde lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris sangs rgyas ye shes/ rin po che bsod nams grags/brgyud yig gzhan mar mi snang yang / 'dir bla ma dam pa dang mkhan chen shes rdor ba gang rung
zhig dgos par snang / rin chen grags tshul ba/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ rje kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ de
gnyis ka las 'dren mchog sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo

rje/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa
ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na kha che paN chen/ dpyal chos bzang / mkhan chen rdor dpal ba/ g.yag sde bsod nams seng ge mnga' ris pa gsang ye man 'dra/ !
yang dam pa de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gser chos nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs zab mo sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ de'i bskyed rim rnal 'byor bcu gcig
gi khrid dang / rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma'i dmigs khrid/ de dag gi skabs su zhal shes la/ maNDal gyi dus su bla ma bskyed bstim/ 'gro ba dag pa'i rjes su lus dkyil gsal gdab
lugs/ 'pho ba'i skabs su yab bde mchog lhan skyes dang mnyam sbyor du bskyed pa'i 'pho ba/ yum rkyang la brten pa'i 'pho ba gnyis/ bsam mi khyab kyi skabs su thun mong
ma yin pa'i zhal shes gser chos ma rnams kyi dmigs khrid zhib par stsal nas/ de'i rgyab chos kyi lung gi skor la rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig gi
lung / phag mo zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang pas mdzad pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul gyi yi ge tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i sgrub mchod
kyi cho ga mngon rtogs/ brgyud 'debs/ mkha' spyod zhal bzang blta ba'i smon lam/ ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs/ rnal 'byor ma'i bstod pa rnams thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor

ma/ grub chen na ro pa/ phaM thing pa sku mched/ klo kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ shar chen pa/ rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rdo ring rin po che/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ rje bsod nams
chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na bla ma dam pa'i rjes su/ yar klung pa
seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan man gong dang 'dra'o/ ! /rje
btsun nus pa'i gter chen de nyid kyi drung du/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi chos skor thob pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar rdo rje 'jigs byed lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor
du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ro langs ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ a mo
gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa'i dpal/ padma badzra/ di paM ka ra rakShi ta/ rwa lo tsA ba chen po rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng
/ rje btsun sga lo/ rong pa shes rab seng ge bag

ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring
pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje btsun mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ chos rje grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod
pa/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang chen po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje btsun
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/
'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ shar gling pa rgyal mtshan bzang po/ sgo rum pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ sngags 'chang 'jigs med dpa' bo/ bla ma bsod nams mchog ldan/ drin can tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /las gshin lha bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ brtse chen pa kun blo/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang
po/ rdo rje gdan pa man

'dra/ ! /'jigs byed sngags btu'i byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rwa shar pa ltar na/ rwa chos rab yan dbang gi brgyud pa bzhin/ de nas dharmA seng ge rwa shes rab rgyal
mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ khams pa yon tan 'bum/ bsam yas mchod rten dkar po sangs rgyas skyabs/ lha rin po che bsod nams
rin chen/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa man 'dra/ ! /shin tu zab pa gzhan las khyad par 'phags pa sku gsum gsal
byed rdo rje'i tshig rkang la brten pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi gdams pa rwa khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud myong khrid du legs par thob nas/ de'i rgyab chos lung gi skor la/
shis brjod sprin gyi rnga dbyangs/ brgyud pa gsum 'dus kyi rwa lugs kyi dbang gi brgyud 'debs/ lam gyi rim pa dang sbyar ba'i smon lam/ lam bzang grub pa'i dga' ston/
sgrub thabs bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i bzhad sgra/ mngon dkyil gyi lhan thabs/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs rnams tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa/ 'jam
pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i khrid kyi brgyud 'debs lam rim pa dang bcas pa/ de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i shis brjod/ rje bsod nams chos 'phel gyis mdzad
pa'i dbang bshad mthong ba don ldan/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg mi mthun kun sel/ drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog gi cho ga rnams dang / rwa pod nas lung thos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs

la/ rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i dgra gdong 'jigs gsum gyi chos skor gyi dkar chag rgya ston gyis mdzad pa'i bla ma rgya bal gyi lo rgyus/ rgyud rtog pa bdun pa/
gtam rgyud rtog pa gcig pa/ 'khor lo'i rgyud rtog pa gsum pa/ las mkhan te'u lo pa'i rtog pa/ te'u lo pa'i chu bya'i rtog pa/ dngos grub kyi rgyud rtog pa bzhi pa/ te'u
lo pa'i sgrub thabs rgyud 'bum pa nas phyung ba/ de'i gsal byed rA dharmA seng ges mdzad pa/ yang de'i gsal byed rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/ 'jigs byed dpa' gcig gi sgrub
thabs rgya gzhung 'jam dbyangs grags pas mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs a mo gha badzra gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs shrI bha dras mdzad pa/ yang a mo gha badzra kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub
thabs rgyas pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'jigs byed kyi dkyil chog sbyin sreg ratna a ka ra shanti pas mdzad pa'i tshogs 'khor/ bla ma bha ros mdzad pa'i 'jigs byed zhal gcig phyag
gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ bla ma rwa lo chen pos mdzad pa'i rtog bdun gyi nag 'grel dang / dka' 'grel bcud kyi thigs pa/ rtog pa bdun pa'i lag len gyi snying po bsnyen
sgrub las/ las gshin sbrel ma dgra srog dbang bsdud/ rtog pa bdun pa'i lag len khrigs chags su bkod pa/ bsad pa mtshon cha lta bu'i man ngag ha la nag po'i shog ril gsum/
sbyin sreg gi yig sna bzhi/ dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i mngon rtogs yid bzhin gyi gter mdzod/ gtso bo'i sgrub thabs dri med snang ba/ zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs khams
gsum za byed/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs dri med chu rgyun/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i mngon

rtogs rin chen don bsdus/ dbang gi chu bo dgongs pa rab gsal te rwa chen gyis mdzad pa'i yig sna bcu drug 'khor lo'i gsal byed phyi ma dang / 'khor lo'i nang tshan las thams
cad gsal bar byed pa gnyis buddha shrI dznyA nas mdzad pa/rgya gzhung yin/ rwa dharmA seng ges mdzad pa'i man ngag bcud thig dbang gong ma dang tshogs 'khor gyi yi ge gnyis
rwa ye shes seng ges mdzad pa/ dkar chag gi yi ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ dkar chag du ma 'dus pa shin tu zab pa'i man ngag gi yi ge'i skor la/ thog
mar rwa chen gyi gsung bgros/ rdzogs rim kyi man ngag la/ sems 'dzin gyi man ngag mtshan ma gyen bsgrengs kyi yi ge rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi man ngag mtshan mo rgyu ba'i
man ngag dang bzhi/ yang mtshan ma gyen bsgrengs kyi yi ge rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi yi ge mtshan mo rgyu ba'i yi ge 'chi kha'i man ngag gi yi ge gtor ma'i lag len dang bcas
pa'i yi ge rnams rwa ye shes seng ges mdzad pa/ dug dbang rma bya rgyas pa zab cing rgya che ba'i yi ge ma tshang ba med pa/ uShNi Sha'i srung 'khor/ phyir bzlog gi yi
ge'i tshogs rwa rgan lo tsA ba'i lugs rwa nub pa nas brgyud pa/ rgya ston gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig zhal shes kyi yi ge dang bcas pa/ rwa chen gyis bla ma bha ro'i drung

'jigs byed zhe

dgu ma'i sgrub thabs/ zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i gsang ba'i sgrub thabs/ 'jigs byed kyi gtor ma'i cho ga dang gsum/ slob dpon ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/

mdzad pa/ las gshin gyi sgrub thabs a mo gha badzra gyis mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge rgyud sde 'dzin pa chen po byang chub grags kyis zin bris su btab pa
las gshin gyi sgrub thabs rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/ las kyi gshin rje'i srid pa'i

bha ros rwa lo la gnang ba/ 'jigs byed man ngag rgyal sen bsrung ba 'khor lo dgu pa zhes bya ba/ 'jigs byed dmar po'i mda' gzhu 'gengs pa'i dbang bsdud/ drag po mda' gzhu

po gtsug

ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang

dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gur gyi mgon po'i phyi srung ba'i 'khor lo la brten pa'i rdo rje'i brag rdzong ma'i khrid kyi rim pa bsnyen pa byed tshul gyi bar rgyas shing
zhib par stsal nas/ de dag gi nang gses kyi man ngag phran tshegs skor la/ sngags pa nang rgyas kyi man ngag don tshan gsum/ mal phur gyi gdams pa/ e ka dza ti la brten
pa'i rims bsrung ba/ rmi ngan bzlog pa'i zhal shes/ mgon po'i tshe sgrub dang bcas pa/ slar de'i rjes su nang gi brag rdzong ma drag po sngags bkod kyi gdams pa/ gsang
ba'i brag rdzong ma sems nyid ye shes kyi rtsal 'don/ rnam rtog bzhi dang bdud bzhi tshar bcad de tshe 'di nyid la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i thabs
khyad par can rnams nyams khrid du nos nas/ yang gur gyi mgon po'i nang khrid thun mong ba yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi khrid yig gi steng nas dmigs khrid lung
dang bcas pa dang / nang khrid thun mong ma yin pa rje tshar chen gyi gsung la mkhyen brtse bas zin bris btab pa'i yi ge dang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi gsung

glegs bam/ kha skong glegs bam/ gyi ljags glegs bam rnams yongs rdzogs thob pa'i/ thog mar snyan brgyud glegs

sbrel ba'i gsang sgrub kyi yig rnying / yum 'jigs byed khrag 'thung ma gaNDe la brten nas bsgrub pa/ pu tra'i rkyal 'bud kyi rtsa ba'i yi ge de'i lag len gyi yi ge rkyal

/ gtor chen gyi yig chung / gtor ma'i sgo nas dgra bgegs kyi srog 'phrog pa/ gtor ma'i sgo nas bsad las kyi yi ge rnying pa/ dpal 'bar brtag pa/ nag po chen po 'khor
