nas bshad pa'i mgon po rigs drug gi mngon rtogs/ rigs drug gi rjes gnang gi yi ge rnams bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ chos skyong spyi'i bskang
bshag gur zhal las mgon dang bcas pa'i bstod pa stag tshang lo tsA bas mdzad pa ste kha skong glegs bam gyi skor 'di dag ched gnyer chen pos legs par thob pa'o/ /yang
mgon pod kyi ljang lugs kyi rnam grangs la/ brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs lam rim dang bcas pa thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ mgon po'i skye rgyud kyi
yig rnying / lha dngos dang brgyud pa'i lo rgyus ston

pa'i yi ge dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ dbang dang rjes gnang gi skor la/ dbang chog gi yi ge bram zes mdzad pa gnyis/ lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang gi zin bris/ dbang chog gi
bsdus don/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i dbang chog dbang gi lag len dharmA gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ gcer bu dang bran bdud kyi rjes gnang gi zur 'debs kyi yig rnying
/ rgyud kyi skor la/ gtso rkyang ston pa'i rgyud gur nas phyung ba/ mgon po khros pa'i rgyud gur nas phyung ba'i nag po chen po'i rgyud bcu bdun ma ston byed dur khrod
nag po'i rgyud le'u bcu gnyis pa/ 'di dkar chag na mi gsal/ rgyud 'di'i sngags btu'i le'u 'gyur khyad tshigs bcad ma/ rgyud kyi don 'grel bzhi sdom bcu pa/ dur khrod
nag po'i byung khungs stong thun gyi khog don bsdus pa dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus don/ des mdzad pa'i dur khrod nag po'i rnam bshad rdo
rje'i tshig don gsal byed/ sgrub thabs kyi skor la/ sgrub thabs bsdus pa dpa' bo gcig pa'i rgya gzhung bram zes mdzad pa/ de'i bsdus don dharmA gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/
sgrub thabs 'bring po nag po phur bu'i sgrub thabs bram zes mdzad pa/ srog phur gyi yi ge bram zes mdzad pa/ phur bu'i sgrub thabs kyi gsal byed sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ srog
gi spu gri'i sgrub thabs gyi ljang gis bsgyur pa/ de'i gsal byed sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs rgyas pa 'phrin las gsang ba'i sgrub thabs bram zes mdzad pa/ des
mdzad pa'i bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i bsdus

don dang / nag po chen po'i gdams pa lag tu blangs pa'i rim pa dharmA gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ bcu bdun ma'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi mi bslu ba'i gsang tshig gru gu ston
pas mdzad pa/ bcu bdun ma'i bod rbad gsad gsum gyi sgrub thabs lag tu blangs pa'i rim pa yid bzhin nor bu rin chen gyi ljang gi slob ma gnyis kyis bka' bgros nas yi ger bkod
pa/ nag po gshin rje ltar bsgrub pa bcu bdun ma'i bsnyen sgrub las tshogs thor bu dang bcas pa dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i gter zhes bya ba dam pas mdzad pa/ nyer mkho lhan
thabs kyi skor la bcu bdun ma'i mngon rtogs/ nag po'i las byang / mchod phreng gtor chog dang bzhi bram zes mdzad pa/ de'i bsdus don dharmA gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ sbyin
sreg gi cho ga bram zes mdzad pa me lha'i bstod pa dang bcas pa/ de'i bsdus don dharmA gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ bstod pa'i phreng ba bram zes mdzad pa/ yang bstod pa sngon
tshe ma bram zes mdzad pa/ dregs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i bsnyen sgrub rbad bsad kyi man ngag bkra shis kyi cho ga bram zes mdzad pa/ las mgon gyi skor la/ gcer bu zangs
gri can gyi sgrub thabs bram zes mdzad pa/ de'i sgrub thabs gong ma'i yi ge bran bdud kyi sgrub thabs bram zes mdzad pa/ sa chen gyis do ba ston tshul la gnang ba bran
bdud kyi lung sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i yi ge bran bdud kyi sgrub thabs la nye bar mkho ba ru mtshon bca' thabs yar klung pas mdzad pa/ las sbyor thor bu'i skor la/ ser ba 'bebs
pa'i yi ge de'i gsal byed kyi yi ge rbod stong

bzlog pa'i yi ge rdo rje'i tshig tu sbas te gsungs pa'i man ngag brgyad ni/ dregs byed rnon po'i man ngag bgegs 'joms pa/ char dbab pa/ char bcad pa/ yi dwags bskrad pa/ phyag
rgya 'gugs pa/ rgyal po la sogs pa dbang du bya ba/ rigs sngags dang rbod gtong bzlog pa'i man ngag ste brgyad do/ /paN chen byams pa gling pas mdzad pa'i mgon po'i las
byang 'phrin las phun tshogs ma'i lung dang bcas thob pa'i/ de ltar gong du bkod pa'i mgon po'i khrid rnams dang / snyan brgyud dang kha skong glegs bam gyi man ngag rnams
kyi brgyud pa ni/ gong gi lha brgyad sogs kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa rnams dang 'dra la/ mgon pod gyi ljang lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon bram ze
mchog sred/ slob dpon la li ta badzra/ grub chen nag po ro 'dzin/ lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ tshar dgu ston pa/ gru ston/ dge bshes dbugs/ sa skya dge slong dharmA
gzi brjid/ nyi thog pa sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba/ mdar mkhan po blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos rje brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams
cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa drin can tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse dbang phyug grub mchog bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga'

bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ badzra pa Ni/ ku ku ri pa/ la li ta badzra/ gyi ljang dbu dkar/ khams pa gru gu ston pa/
mon mig dmar ston pa/ ra lam mar ston/ mgon po jo zhang / lang gro byang chub dar/ lce ston mdo sde seng ge dkar gshong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris bla chen chos
dpal bzang po/ stag tshang lo tsA ba madznyu shrI/ gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mus chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po man 'dra/ yang gru ston
la bdag po bsod yon pas gsan/ de la mnga' ris bla chen pas gsan no/ /yang brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ shaddha ka ra warma/shaddha
dad pa/ a ka ra 'byung gnas te/ dad pa'i 'byung gnas go char bsgyur pa dag par 'dug dad byed go cha ma dag ces lo chen bsod nams rnam rgyal gsungs par grags/
di paM ka ra/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul purNa/ rgya lcags ri gong kha ba/ rdzing bu kha pa shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma shAkya/ zhang ston ye shes/ gze ba
don grub/ bar thang pa yab sras/ slob dpon dar shAka pa/ spur ston bsod nams dbang phyug bla ma mchog ldan pa/ skyi ston grags rgyal/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen
nam mkha' ye shes/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge phyi ma gsum char la theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos gsan/ de la chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun
bzang pa/ gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /yang na skyi

ston/ kun mkhyen dol bu shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang seng ba/ theg chen pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na nam mkha' lhun bzang pa la/ brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang pos gsan/
de la thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pas gsan no/ /yang na/ ra lam pa/ zhang chung pa/ la lung pa/ skye med jo gdan/ gru ston man sngar dang 'dra'o/ ! /yang na brgyud
pa lugs gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ grub chen nag po ro 'dzin/ lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa
chen po/ bla chen yar bsgom se bo/ rgyal tshab lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa/ chos rje tshul khrims pa/ tshar chen blo
gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug grub mchog bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/
des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang dam pa de nyid kyi drung du dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa nas brgyud pa'i dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin
nos pa la/ thog mar bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ gsang phu

ba rngog legs pa'i shes rab/ mnga' ris pa byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal mtshan/ phul chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ka ma ba 'brom rin chen rgyal mtshan/ zhang ston
dar ma rgyal mtshan/ stabs ka ba 'brom byang chub bzang po/ ston pa nam mkha' rin chen/ snar thang mkhan po nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rin chen gling pa rin chen byang chub/ sga
lung pa rigs kyi bdag po'i dpal/ sga lung pa byang chub dpal/ nyug pa'i slob dpon bsod nams 'od zer/ gos sngon chu ser ba sangs rgyas bzang po/ bya bral ba bsod nams bzang
po/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ stag tshang chos 'khor ba mkhan chen nam mkha' 'od zer/ pa tshab dga' ba gdong pa gnas brtan ye shes tshul khrims/ nub chos lung pa ratna a ka
ra shanti pa/ snyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lcags thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams dpal ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo bo rje/ nag tsho tshul
rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba/ bya 'dul 'dzin/ mkhan po chos kyi byang chub/ mkhan po zol phu ba/ slob dpon dkon mchog seng ge de gnyis la mkhas btsun tshul khrims rin
chen/ bla ma dar ma bzang po/ chos rje gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rgyal mtshan don grub/ chos rje gtsang pa rin rgyal/ bya btang buddhi satwa/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen
grags pa/ spyan snga bsod nams lha'i

dbang po/ smyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lcags thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams dpal ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag
dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang spyan snga rin chen ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan
gyi yig cha'i steng nas sbyor dngos rjes gsum cho ga cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa dang / de nas bka' gdams glegs bam yongs rdzogs kyi lung thob pa'i chos sna'i rnam grangs
la/ bstan pa rin po che'i lha chos phun sum tshogs pa'i lo rgyus ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i dpal 'byor zhes bya ba glegs bam gyi lo rgyus chen po dang / thugs dam
rgyal ba yab sras kyi bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa'i gter zhes bya ba dang / lha chos nyams len gyi man ngag thig le chen po'i dbyings su byang chub sems gnyis spel ba zung
'jug nyi zla'i thig le zhes bya ba/ thig le bcu drug gi dbang chog dang khrid yig zung du 'jug pa ste chos tshan gsum po 'di dge ba'i bshes gnyen ston pa nam mkha' rin
chen dang / snar thang mkhan po rin chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan pa gnyis kyis mdzad pa dang / glegs bam rang gi ngo bo la dang po sprul pa'i glegs bam gyi bzhugs tshul bzhin
la 'brom chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyis logs su nan gyis bstan pa'i bka' rgya chen mo/ yang 'brom gyis mdzad pa'i rang rgyud la bskul ma 'debs pa dad pa'i ljon shing zhes bya
ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i gsol 'debs yan

lag bdun ldan gnyis dang / pha chos nor bu'i phreng ba'i rtsa ba byang sems nor bu'i phreng ba dang / pha chos nyi shu rtsa drug las zhus lan gyi dngos gzhi nor bu'i phreng
ba la le'u tshan nyer gsum dang / ka ba shAkya dbang phyug gis dbu mdzad pa'i mkhas btsun mang po dang / yon bdag shAka mgon la sogs pa'i skye bo'i tshogs dang bcas pa'i
dbus su lha chos bdun ldan gyi 'khor lo bskor ba la 'phros nas chos 'di nan gyis bka' rgyas btab pa la le'u tshan gcig ma 'ongs lung bstan chen mo'i le'u gcig shing pho
rta'i lo la bla ma dga' ldan du byon pa'i tshul rnams mgur du bzhengs pa'i 'chi med rdo rje'i glu zhes bya ba le'u gcig ste yongs dril pha chos nyi shu rtsa drug bu chos
skor la 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi skye rabs bstan pa las rngog gis zhus pa'i rngog chos nyi shu dang / khu ston gyis zhus pa'i khu chos gnyis te yongs dril bu chos
la le'u tshan nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ de ltar le'u bzhi bcu zhe brgyad la mi the ba'i ngo mtshar ba'i gtam thor bu ba rnams lo tsA ba la sogs pa rje'i sras dam pa rnams kyis
zur du gleng ba'i kha bskangs pa'i le'u dang bcas pas glegs bam yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung thob pa las/ de dag gi dbang lung sogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgya chen spyod pa'i brgyud
pa/ zab mo lta ba'i brgyud pa/ nyams len byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa gsum ni yongs su grags pa ltar yin la/ de rnams nas jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha dI paM ka ra shrI
dznyA na/ 'brom chos kyi rgyal po rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ gsang phu ba rngog legs pa'i shes rab/ mnga' ris pa byang chub sems dpa'

shes rab rgyal mtshan/ phul byung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ka ma ba 'brom rin chen rgyal mtshan/ zhang ston dar ma rgyal mtshan/ stabs ka ba 'brom byang chub bzang po/ ston
pa nam mkha' rin chen/ snar thang mkhan po nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rin chen gling pa rin chen byang chub/ sga lung pa rigs kyi bdag po'i dpal/ sga lung pa byang chub dpal/
nyug pa'i bla ma bsod nams 'od zer/ gos sngon chu ser ba sangs rgyas bzang po/ bya bral ba bsod nams bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ stag tshangs chos 'khor ba mkhan chen
nam mkha' 'od zer/ pa tshab dga' ba gdong pa gnas brtan ye shes tshul khrims pa/ nub chos lung pa mkhan chen ratna a ka ra shanti pa/ paN chen ngag dbang grags pa dpal bzang
po/ lcags thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams dpal ldan pa/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa dgos 'dod 'byung gnas de nyid kyi drung du/ thub pa'i bstan pa rdzogs par skyong ba'i srung
ma'i dbang po rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi gsar rnying bka' gter dang rjes su 'brel ba'i gdams pa zab mo thob pa la/ gos sngon can gyi rjes su gnang ba thob nas/ de'i
rgyab chos kyi lung gi skor la/ phyag na rdo rje'i rgyud pa 'og le'u le'u bcu gsum pa zangs dkar gyis bsgyur pa/ phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ gtor chog sbyin sreg
'khrul 'khor bcings pa/ bskrad

pa'i 'khor lo/ bsnun pa'i 'khor lo/ bum pa'i cho ga rnams slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa zangs dkar gyis bsgyur pa/ gos sngon can gyi sgrub thabs kyi spyi don/ sgrub
thabs/ bum chog 'khrul 'khor/ gtor chog mthu zlog sbyin sreg gi yi ge lung dang bcas pa rnams dge slong chos dbang phyug gis mngon rtogs su sbyar ba/ thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che dgon pa ba/ zangs
dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ g.yer po jo ston/ gcung bsod nams rin chen/ 'chims phu ba padma bkra shis/ brtag pa lha rje jo bzang / khro phu lo tsA ba/ bla chen
bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu sems dpa' chen po/ spangs brtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog
grub/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje
dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /zangs dkar lo tsA bas stod kyi phyogs
su gnang ba gtum ston blo gros grags nas brgyud pa'i rnam sras stod lugs sam/ bya her lugs su grags pa'i gser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ zangs
dkar lo tsA ba yan gong bzhin las/ gtum ston blo gros grags/ gtum ston

yon tan khu bsgom pa/ mkhan po lung ston/ slob dpon legs pa'i shes rab/ bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/ bya sder ba byang chub gzhon nu/ mang mkhar ba blo bzang dkar mo/ mang
mkhar blo bzang grags pa/ bzang ldan mkhan po shAkya blo gros/ 'bul dpon rdo rje rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /smad kyi char
g.yor po jo ston la gnang bas smad lugs su grags pa/ rgyal po chen po ngal gsos po bde byed 'khor dang bcas pa dang / dregs byed klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes su gnang
ba/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i yi ge'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ phyag rdor gyi brgyud pa bzhin nam/ yang na phyag na rdo rje/ ka ma ru pa/ ka ha na pa/ 'gro
bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che sardza na/ kha che te dza/ de wa/ zangs mkhar lo tsA ba/ zhu sa skya pa/ jo btsun grags pa seng ge rgya ston sgrub pa
po/ rgya ston grub mchog bla ma rdo rje dpal/ khro phu ba sems dpa' chen po/ spangs rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa man 'dra/ yang na bu ston yab sras/
slob dpon rin chen bsod nams 'phel/ stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ rje btsun yab/ chos rgyal rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ tshar chen thams cad mkhyen
pa man

'dra/ yang na khro phu lo tsA ba/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen ka bzhi pa/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ mkhan chen rin chen rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros/ rje rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ yang na skyor mo lung pa'i phyag len ltar thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon 'gro bzang / grub chen bheM ka ra wa ti/ kha che dgon pa/ zangs mkhar lo tsA ba/ g.yor po jo ston rtse mo/ sbal ting dgra bcom pa sems dpa' rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab seng ge bsam yas pa tshul khrims dbang phyug se ba can pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen ka bzhi pa/ dga' ldan
phug pa blo bzang grags pa/ de gnyis las mkhan chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dmar ba kun dga' tshe 'phel/ spyan snga shAkya rgyal mtshan/ tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /'phags pa klu sgrub kyis sprang po nyi ma'i dngos grub bsgral ba'i chos skyong ba'i rgyal po chen po rta sngon bdud mo bzhi bskor
dang / nang ma mo ltar bsgrub pa lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/
dpal kun tu bzang po/ 'gro bzang snying po/ bhreM ke ra wa ti/ kha che dgon pa ba/ zangs mkhar lo tsA ba/ bhal ti sems dpa' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen brtson 'grus dbang phyug
mkhan chen zhig po shes rab seng ge bsam yas pa tshul khrims

dbang phyug se ba can pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma blo gros bzang po/ bla ma chos skyong bzang po/ dga' ldan phug pa blo bzang grags pa/ mkhan
chen chos rgyal mtshan pa man 'dra/ ! /yang gsang srin po bzhi bskor thob pa'i brgyud pa ni sngar bzhin no/ /yang na/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mai tri pa/ spyan
snga chos rgya mtsho/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /shu raM
ga warma'i lugs kyi rnam sras mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha bco lnga'i rjes gnang / las mkhan dang bcas pa'i mdung dmar can gtso 'khor gnyis kyi rjes gnang /
gar mkhan mchog ljang khu zhal gcig phyag bco brgyad 'brug zhon gyi rjes gnang / gar mkhan mchog dmar smug zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad kyi rjes gnang / dregs byed srin po

no/ /yang na tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mai tri pa/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/

sa skya pa ngag dbang

'bar ba'i sgrub thabs 'gro bzang gis mdzad pa/ de'i Tikka /sre thod kyi zhal gdams/ bai shrA ma Na'i rtog pa gsum pa dang / ltas ngan gtong ba dang / sngags pa 'khon rgyas/

pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud le'u nyi shu rtsa bdun pa/ rnam sras kyi rgyud le'u bcu dgu pa/ sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs lo tsA ba manydzu shrIs bsgyur pa/ nor
gnas kyi sgrub thabs/ yang sgrub thabs chung ngu gcig gsang sgrub sre thod ma rnam sras kyis zangs mkhar ba la gnang ba/ gtor chog bstod pa dang bcas pa/ gtor chog chen
mo/ man ngag thun mong ma yin pa phyi nang gi bsgrub lugs/ tshe bsgrub pa/ bse rag kha 'ching rnams 'gro bzang gis mdzad pa/ sre thod la brten nas bsgrub lugs/ byis pa

'grel pa'am lag len gyi gsal byed zangs mkhar gyi 'gyur/ gar mkhan mchog gi bstod pa/ spyan 'dren/ bskul/ gsang sgrub rnams shu raM ga warmas mdzad pa zangs mkhar ba'i

'gyur/ gar mkhan mchog gi sgrub thabs mgul khug ma khro los mdzad pa/ mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa yab yum 'khor 'brog gnas mched lnga dang bcas pa'i bstod pa/ bskul/
zhal gcig phyag drug pa/ lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i sgrub thabs dza wa ri pas mdzad pa/ nang sgrub drag po ljang nag las mkhan dang bcas pa'i sgrub thabs/ nang sgrub
thugs dam gnad du dril ba'i gdams pa zab mo/ gsang ba ltar bsgrub pa'i yig chung / rnam sras ljang khu klu chen brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rgya gzhung dza wa ri pas mdzad pa/
sgrub thabs 'gro bzang gis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa ma ti kirtis mdzad pa/ zab tig gi man ngag zangs mkhar ba'i mgul khug sro ma can du grags pa'i skor la/ ljang ser be con ma'i
sgrub thabs rgya gzhung / bsnyen pa'i yi ge shin tu rdzogs pa'i dbang du bya ba zhes pa/ ljang ser mgul khug ma'i gsang sgrub kyi lag len gyi yi ge mgul khug ma de'i

sgrub las gsum gyi zhal

gdams gsang chog ces pa/ 'di ni bsnyen pa'i zhes pa'i yig skor/ mgul khug ma'i rten gsum gyi zhal gdams bsdus pa/ zab tig sro ma can gyi gdams pa las/ byi ba la brten nas nor

chen po'i rnam thar/ brda don gsal ba'i khrid yig lam sbas bshad kyi khrid yig bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub thabs phyag len/ 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi zin bris/ mngon byang
gi bshad pa rgyas pa/ rdo rje dril bu'i bshad pa/ rnam

'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs bya tshul gyi yi ge mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang gi yi ge rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa
chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa
ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kun bzang
mar grags pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung la 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug gis zin bris gnang ba'i skor thob pa la/ lam 'bras kyi chos 'byung rgyas pa/
snang gsum gyi khrid yig 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta khrid rgyas pa/ bum dbang gi lam gyi khrid/ gshed dmar spros med kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ bskyed rim gyi bshad
pa/ spros med kyi khrid yig rgyas pa/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid yig sum pa lo tsa'i blo sbyong gi khrid yig spyan ras gzigs kharsa pa Ni la brten pa'i snying po don
gsum gyi yi ge sems nyid ngal gso'i khrid yig rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug mthu stobs dbang

mkhan chen thams

cad mkhyen pa de nyid kyi drung du/ gsung ngag rin po che'i snying po rgyu dbang lam du byed pa/ slob dpon gyi zab mo rdo rje lus kyi dkyil 'khor du lam dbang zab mo lan mang
du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'chi med rdo rje'i sku brnyes rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /ma skyes ma 'gag rdo rje bdag med ma/ /skal ldan snang ngor rtag bzhugs birWa pa/ /tshe yi
rig 'dzin brnyes pa'i nag po pa/ /skye 'chi med pa'i don rtogs DA ma ru/ /gzung 'dzin kun spangs a wa dhu ti pa/ /gangs can dpal du byon pa klu 'dzin zhabs/ /sgra bsgyur
chos kyi rgyal po 'brog mi rje/ /rgyud dang man ngag kun rig mkhar chung ba/ /mngon shes rdzu 'phrul mnga' bdag dgon pa ba/ /sa stag re bdun bar bzhugs sa skya pa/ /chu
stag zhe gcig bar bzhugs bsod nams rtse/ /me byi bdun bcu'i bar bzhugs grags pa'i zhabs/ /chu stag bdun bcu'i bar bzhugs paNDi ta/ /lcags 'brug zhe drug bar bzhugs 'phags
pa'i mchog /me lug re brgyad bar bzhugs dkon mchog dpal/ /lcags stag don bzhi'i bar bzhugs brag phug pa/ /shing yos re bzhi'i bar bzhugs 'gro mgon rje/'di gnyis gang rung
gcig gis chog /sa khyi zhe gsum bar bzhugs ri khrod pa/ /sa yos re bdun bar bzhugs dpal ldan pa/ /lcags byi gya gnyis bar bzhugs buddha shrI/ /me byi don lnga'i bar bzhugs
e wa~M pa/ /lcags stag gya gsum bar bzhugs mus pa che/ /sa khyi nga lnga'i bar bzhugs kun dpang pa/ /chu stag don gnyis bar bzhugs mkhas grub che/dpal rdor/ /sa bya
re gcig bar bzhugs kun mkhyen rje/ /shing khyi

bdun bcu'i bar bzhugs dkon mchog 'phel/phyi ma de lnga char la gsan/ /shing sprel don gnyis bar bzhugs buddha'i mtshan/mus chen dang kun mkhyen la gsan pa/ /shing lug re brgyad
bar bzhugs seng ge'i mtshan/phyi ma de gsum char la gsan pa/ /me sbrul re gcig la gshegs dkon lhun rje/ /me khyi don bdun bar bzhugs spyan snga ba/ /sa rta don bdun
la gshegs buddha'i mtshan/ /lcags sbrul bdun bcu'i bar bzhugs mkhan chen rje/ /mgon des rjes bzung sngags 'chang a nanda'o/ /yang na ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan
snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ yangs can mkhan po dbang phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ ! /yang na mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /dpal mgon bram nag bshan pa drug bskor nag po dom mchong du grags
pa'i rjes gnang / de'i man ngag gi yi ge rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ dzo ki ka ma ru pa/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam
skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/ brang mo che pa/ rje btsun re mda' ba/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ rgya
ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ rje btsun

kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ rje btsun dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri
ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa che chung / bla ma
dpal ldan pa/ shar chen pa/ ngor chen pa/ mus chen pa/ kun mkhyen pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen dbang
phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /bstod pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ sgrub
skor chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i stong mchod kyi lag len/ rnam rgyal gyi gzungs rtog pa gnyis dang bcas pa ba ri bas bsgyur pa/
rtog pa'i 'grel pa dang / sa bcad rje btsun rtse mos mdzad pa dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa gnyis/

po 'bum/ bram chen nam

mkha'/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen
dkon mchog lhun grub/ mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ !
/'byung 'dul me dbang ma'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ma/ a bhya dang / shu bhaM ka ra/ pU dza gupta/ ratna rakShi ta/
go taM shrI/ kirti paNDi ta/ yar klung grags rgyal/ rgyal mtshan rin chen/ gar thig bsod rgyal/ gzhon seng ka bcu pa/ bla ma mgon po 'bum/ chos rje dpal tshul ba/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / rje yongs 'dzin/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ mkhan chen dbang
phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa mtshan
don dang ldan pa de nyid kyi drung du/ snyan ngag la sogs pa thun mong gi rig gnas kyi skor dang / mdo phyogs kyi pod chen drug gi bshad lung sogs thob pa'i tshul ni/

sbyar ba'i steng / rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sa bcad mkhas pa'i rna rgyan/ rnam bshad blo gsal mgrin pa'i dpal yon/ spyi don legs bshad nor bu'i phreng mdzes rnams kyis gsal
byed kyi rgyan du mdzad nas gsung bshad rgyas shing dka' gnas kyi mtha' chod pa dang / de las 'phros nas snyan ngag gi bstan bcos me long gi gzhung la mkhas pa snga ma rnams
kyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa so so las brtsams te dogs slong gi dri ba dang / de'i rang lan rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bstan bcos khyad par can snyan ngag me long las brtsams
pa'i dri ba dbyangs can mgrin pa'i nga ro'i rang lan dbyangs gsum rnam gzhag skal bzang bcud thigs zhes bya ba'i steng nas bshad pa zhib tu thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa

lhun grub/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / brtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya
pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel la spyi don/ Tikka kun mkhyen rin po che'i rjes 'brangs dang bcas pas mdzad pa'i yig
cha so so dang / khyad par chos rje sa

paN gyi rigs gter rtsa 'grel/ rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i tshad ma rigs pa'i gter gyi dgongs don gsal bar byed pa'i legs bshad ngag gi dpal ster zhes bya ba'i rab byed dgu pa
yan gyi spyi don rnams kyi steng nas bshad pa rgyas pa dang / rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i pod chen drug gi 'brel gtam gyi tshad ma'i skabs de rang nyid kyi zin thun bskyar chos
su byas nas zhib tu gnang ba nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa tshad ma'i skyes bu/ 'jam dbyangs/ dgra bcom pa chos skyabs/ paN chen mi wang 'ga'/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/

pa rgyal

mtshan/ de gnyis la mkhas pa'i dbang po dpal ldan bzang po/ mkhan chen rin po che dbang phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa

dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi dka' 'grel kun mkhyen gyis mdzad
pa/ zur bkol dge 'dun nyi shu'i skyes bu mchog gi gsal byed sogs gtso bor gyur pa/ gzhan yang rjes 'brangs mkhas pa so so'i spyi TIka rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dka' 'grel

rnam chung ngu /'di slob dpon rin po che bsod rtse'i spyi rnam chen mo'i nang na tshang bar yod/ brtag gnyis kyi sa bcad/ brtag

gnyis kyi tshig 'grel mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying pos mdzad pa/ brtag gnyis dka' 'grel 'khon sgyi chu bas mdzad pa 'di gnyis rang lugs la rgyud kyi yig cha khungs thub yin
pas gces spras su byas te lung rgyun mi nyams par bya ba'i phyir 'dir bzhugs pa yin/ sa chen rang gis mdzad pa'i brtag gnyis kyi dka' 'grel man ngag don gsal bya ba shog
grangs nyer bdun/ rdo rje gur gyi tho yig 'di las 'bum lnga dang rtsa bshad sbyor tshul dang / le'u gang las brjod bya gang bstan yod/ gur gyi bshad pa'i chings/ rdo rje'i
glu bshad pa/ rtsa'i mngon rtogs kyi 'grel pa/'di lhag pas mi dgos bya'ang bshad/ rdo rje snying 'grel snga 'gyur gyi yig sna/'di 'phro can zhig yod/ mtsho skyes kyi
lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi bsdus don/dbu phyogs la sa gzhung sbyar ba'i steng du bshad pa thor re ba gcig 'dug yang mchod brjod dang brtsam par dam bca' sngon
du 'gro ba'i bskyed rdzogs dang bcas pa tshan pa gnyis 'dug smon lam dbang bzhi ma'i bshad pa yang bsdus don gyi mjug na yod/ de'i 'grel tshig gi bum pa/ rdo rje gur gyi
zin bris sgo rum dpe khang nas byung ba mchan yang tho re yod pa/ sambu Ta'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel/ sambu Ta'i rgyud phyi ma'i TIkka tshan pa gnyis/rje btsun rtse mos rgyud
phyi ma la rnam bshad mi mdzad pa'i rgyu mtshan yang sa chen gyi gnyis po 'di yod pas yin/ kye rdo rje'i gdan gyi rnam dag sngon byung cho 'phrul dang sbyar ba/ de nyid
bcu'i gsal byed/ rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa rnams ka pa la bzhugs/ kha pa la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi le 'grel tshigs bcad ma/
bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi zin bris/ bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang gi tho yigthe tshom can yin zer/ bde mchog gi rgyud kyi

dka' gnas kyi zin bris/ nag po pa'i lo rgyus/ gzhung drug spyi'i rnam gzhag gzhung drug so so'i bsdus don/ dbang chog ras bris la brten pa/ sgrub thabs sbyin sreg rdzogs rim
gsang ba'i de kho na nyid/ o la pa ti'i rnam gzhag 'khor lo sdom pa'i rim bzhi'i lam slong / o la pa ti dang / dpyid kyi thig le'i sngags rim bsgom tshul/ nag 'bum 'di
la chos sna bco lnga bzhugs pa dang / bcu bdun du bzhugs pa gnyis su yod 'dug 'jigs byed rtog bdun gyi rnam bshad/ 'jam dpal/ mi g.yo ba/ sgrol ma rnams la bstod pa re re/
sgrol ma lha bcu bdun gyi dbang gi tho yig man ngag gces bsdus rin chen phreng ba/'di'i nang na grub pa'i slob dpon so so las brgyud pa'i man ngag rnam grangs du ma yod
cing / 'di sa chen rang rkyang pas mdzad pa min pa 'dra ste/ sked bar na rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i phyag chen gces bsdus kyi nang tshan 'dra dang / mjug na sa paN gyis mdzad
pa'i lam sbas bshad kyi man ngag 'ga' re yang 'dug sa skya pa rang gi man ngag snga phyi slob rgyun zhig gis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i lung rgyun mkhan chen shes rdor
bas gsan pa 'dir bcug pa yin pa 'dra/ 'di la 'gal ba med do/ /uShNa'i srung 'khor/ mahA ma ya'i rgyud stong phrag brgyad cu pa nas gsungs pa'i bha ya na'i srung 'khor/
skyu ra a skyabs la zhu yig bum gter bya thabs/ rdo rje phur pa'i mngon rtogs/ phur pa'i las byang / khyung khra'i man ngag bla ma mal nas brgyud pa/ dur khrod bdag po'i
sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi Tikka mu tig phreng ba gnyan phul byung bas mdzad pa/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i 'bru 'bum gnyan gyis mdzad pa rnams
legs

par thos so/ /gnyan gyis mdzad pa 'dir yong ba yang sngar gyi rgyu mtshan dang mtshungs/ rje mus srad pa'i gsung las/ mu tig phreng ba 'di gnyan gyis mdzad zer yang brtag dgos
gsungs shing / khong rang sa chen gyis mdzad par bzhed/ de ltar na 'di'i dbu phyogs na brgyud pa smos skabs/ rdo rje 'chang nas bla ma mal lo tsA ba la brgyud tshul gyi
bar gsungs pa'i rjes su/ des bdag nyid kyi bla ma rtsod pa'i dus su rdo rje theg pa ston pa rnams kyi nang nas gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa las stod 'bro yi yul du
sku 'khrungs pa/ mtshan brjod par dka' ba'i bdag nyid chen po la bshad do zhes gsungs pa 'di bla ma sa skya pa chen po yin nam min/ yin na 'di sa skya chen gyis ma mdzad
pa gzhir bzhag la/ min na sa chen gyi bla ma gang la ngos 'dzin/ pu hrang lo chung dang / su ma ti kirti ni 'khrungs yul gyi stabs kyis min pas/ sngar smos pa de ni sa chen
nyid yin par shes par bya'o/ /bka' bum nang gi chos sna'i grangs lnga bcu nga bzhi yod/ 'ga' zhig gis sum cu rtsa lnga zhes pa'ang bshad/ ! /gzhan sde'i mun pa 'joms mdzad
mi thub zla/ /dge legs bsod nams shar ri'i rtser 'phags pa/ /mkhyen rab dpal mo'i bdud rtsi 'od dkar can/ /dpal ldan rtse mo'i zhabs kyis bdag cag skyongs/ /zhes pa'i
bstod yul dam par gyur pa slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo'i gsung rab rnams thos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po la bstod pa tshangs dbang
ma shlau ka bco lnga yod pa/ yang brgyud pa dang bcas pa'i bstod pa gang thugs ma/ phya pa

chos kyi seng ge la bstod pa shlau ka sum cu rtsa gsum yod pa/ rgya bsgom tshul khrims grags la springs pa/'di'i nang na sa chen la bstod pa che chung gnyis dang / phyis mdzad
pa'i nyung shas gcig dang gsum yod par bshad/ tshul dang po gsum gyi rnam gzhag ston pa rgyud sde spyi rnam/ 'jam dbyangs dang sa chen gyi bstod pa tshig lhug ma/ brtag
gnyis kyi rnam bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer/ sambu Ti'i sa bcad/ TIkka gnad kyi gsal byed/ brtag pa gnyis pa'i rab byed gnyis pa las brtsams te kha sbyor thig le'i bshad don/de
nas las bzhi'i sbyin sreg bya ba po ti'i tho yig dang gsan yig la 'dug kyang / glegs bam gyi spyi grangs la mi 'dug pas lung ma byung / 'di yi nang na tshe sgrub zab
mo zhig kyang 'dug sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi 'grel pa nga pa la/ kyai rdo rje'i las dang po pa'i bya ba/ Dombhi lugs kyi dkyil chog mtsho skyes lugs kyi dkyil chog nas
gling ma/ mngon rtogs yan lag bzhi pa/ man ngag lugs kyi dbang chu chen mo/ kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas bzang drug kye rdor zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bdag med ma'i dbang gi
tho yig khams pa ne tso sbal ston la gnang ba/'di'i nang na steng gi tshom bu bai ta li g.yas dang / 'og gi tshom bu gau rI g.yon du bya bar bshad/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i
mngon rtogs/ de'i dbang chog bde mchog gi mchod phreng rgyas pa/rje btsun rin po ches lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs chen mo mchod phreng bla mas mdzad pa blta bar kha 'phangs
pa de 'di yin/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rtog pa'i TIkka'di slob dpon rin po ches gsang phur mdzad pa phyis bka' gnang nas rje btsun gyis kyang gsal bar mdzad pa yin pas sku
mched gnyis ka'i thun mong ba yin/ rnam rgyal gyi rtog pa'i sa

bcad/ rje btsun gyi seng ge sgra'i sgrub skor/ don zhags kyi sa bcad/ lha lnga'i bstod pa/ don zhags kyi lo rgyus/don zhags kyi lo rgyus gzhan zhig 'dug pa 'di slob dpon rin
po ches mdzad pa yin min brtag dgos/ sngon du 'gro ba'i cho ga nyams su blang tshul/ don zhags rgyud chung gi TIkka /rdo rje gdan pa'i chos drug mi g.yo ba'i chos skor
rgya gzhung bstod pa dang bcas pa/ kha 'bar ma'i gtor chen/ spyod 'jug gi TIkka chen mo/'di'i mjug la dge slong chos kyi seng ges mdzad pa las zer ba 'di phya pa ni min las
che su yin brtag dgos/ 'di las dang po pa rnams kyis go bde ba legs po rang gnang / chos la 'jug pa'i sgo/'di'i nang na lnga sde bzang pos sngon la ston pa'i drung du
tshur shog gi bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas bden bzhi'i chos 'khor bskor bar gsungs 'dug yi ge'i rnam gzhag dang 'brel ba byis pa bde blag tu 'jug pa'i sgo rnams thos so/ /yongs
dril chos sna sum cu rtsa gnyis snang / zhwa lu mkhyen rab rin po ches nyi shu rtsa lnga zhes pa'ang bshad/ ! grags pa'i zer gyis srid gsum gsal bar byas/ /'jam pa'i
rdo rje dge bsnyen zol 'chang ba/ /thar pa'i rgyal mtshan dpe bral srid 'dir gsal/ /'khon ston 'jam dbyangs dpa' bos bdag cag skyongs/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa
rje btsun rin po che'i gsung 'bum thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ slob dpon rin po che la bstod pa/'di bstod pa gdung dbyangs ma bya ba bzhugs kyang gsan yig na med
pas lung rgyun mi snang / lam 'bras brgyud 'debs bla ma rdor 'dzin ma/ yang brgyud 'debs chung ba gcig sa chen gyi rnam thar/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i

rnam thar/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i TIkka tshar gsum khug pa'i man ngag gra ston zhus lan/ 'grel pa dag ldan/ mngon rtogs ljon shing / stong thun sa bcad/ rgyud sde'i dum bu brgya
bcu gsum pa/ rdo rje gur gyi sa bcad/ 'grel pa gur rgyan/ gur gyi thig chog yab kyi mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa/ kye rdor dpa' gcig gi mngon rtogs/ bdag med ma'i mngon
rtogs/ bdag med ma'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams par bskur ba'i tho yig tshogs 'khor 'bring po/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg rnams ca pa la bzhugs/ cha pa la he ru ka'i
chas drug rdo rje dril bu bgrang phreng gsum gyi de kho na nyid/ dga' ston spring yig rgyud 'bum gyi dkar chag bla ma gong ma'i chos skor gyi dkar chag kyai rdo rje'i chos
skor gyi dkar chag ste yig sna gcig la chos tshan gsum/ skyabs su 'gro ba la sems bskyed pa'i cho ga rin chen 'bar ba'i bsdus don/ dus mtha'i cho ga gzhan phan bdud rtsi/
yab yum gyi bstod pa gnyis/ kyai rdo rje'i bkra shis shlau ka bdun pa ste 'di yan gyi kye rdor gyi phyogs gtso bor gyur pa la chos sna sum cu rtsa gnyis/ bde mchog brgyud
pa'i lo rgyus/ bstod pa nyung ngu zhig he ru ka byung tshul/ lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs chen mo/ nag po dkyil chog gi sa bcad 'khrugs can 'khrugs med gnyis/ sgrub thabs dang
sbyin sreg gi sa bcad/ nag po bshad sbyar/ nag po dkyil chog dril bu pa'i lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs kyi don 'grel/ rim lnga'i don 'grel/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ zhal gnyis
ma'i sgrub thabs/ sngags kyi de kho

na nyid kyi man ngag las bcu'i gsal byed/ mai tri mkha' spyod kyi rgyud chung / sgrub thabs gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi cho ga rgyal ba'i sdes mdzad pa dang
gsum la/ rje btsun gyis mchan btab pa/ na ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs bskyed rim dang bcas pa'i bzlas sgom la brten pa'i mkha' spyod bsgrub pa/ sa chen gyis mdzad/ byin
rlabs kyi yi ge tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ sbyin sreg mar me'i sbyin sreg skra sen dbab pa/ gnod sbyin mo'i sgrub thabs/ tshangs pa'i bu mo'i sgrub thabs/ padma sa ta'i man
ngag khol po sa ta'i man ngag sman chen po'i bcud len te 'di rnams sa chen gyis mdzad pa yin yang phag mo skor gsum gyi man ngag rnams phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir bla ma
gong mas 'dir bris par gnang gsungs/ rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig nges brjod bla ma'i 'khrul 'khor bri bsgom gyi man ngag rnal 'byor ma kun spyod kyi sa bcad/ de'i Tikka ste
bde mchog gi phyogs la chos sna sum cu so gnyis/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag gi sgrub thabs/ dgra nag lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor/ mngon rtogs/ 'jigs byed kyi
bstod pa slob dpon rin po ches mdzad pa la kha skong gnang ba/ bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i sgrub thabs te chos sna thor bu ba lnga/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma'i skor la/ sgrol ma
nyin zhi mtshan khro'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa 'don thabs las kha tshar ba dang bcas pa/ sgrol ma spyi sgrub so so'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa/ 'don thabs kyi brjed byang / sgrol
ma nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs/ TIkka dang sa bcad/ sgrol ma lus

dkyil gyi sgrub thabs/ phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs/nyi ma sbas pa'i las tshogs kyi 'grel pa yin/ de'i bsdus don/ mchan dkyus su bcug pa gsal ba'i 'od zer/ gnyan sgrol
gyi sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa/ maNDal bzhi pa'i gsol 'debs rnams te chos sna bcu gsum sgrol ma'i dkyil chog gi bsdus don dang / 'chim chos bzang la springs pa dang
bcas pas chos sna bco lnga yod/ chos sna dgu pa phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs zer ba de la las tshogs kyi rim pa le'u nyi shu rtsa drug yod/ rje btsun gyi rnam thar
mnal lam ma khams pa sbas ston gyis bris pa/ nang gi lhung bzed brtag pa rje btsun gyi gsung bzhin sna ro'i bandes bris pa/ ga ring rgyal po la brtsis bsdur gyi yi ge
rtsa ltung 'khrul spong / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i TIkka rnams so/'di'i mjug na lha'i gdan dang sa bon gang las bskyed pa yang bshad/ /ja pa la ngan song sbyong rgyud kyi
spyi don gzhan phan spyi chings su grags pa/ sbyong rgyud sa bcad/ yo ga'i dkyil chog rdo rje 'byung ba'i TIkka /kun rig gi cho ga gzhan phan 'od zer/ gzhan phan nyer mkho/
argha'i cho ga rab gnas don gsal/ rigs gsum spyi'i dkyil chog 'jam dbyangs dpa' bo gcig sgrub kyi TIkka /mi g.yo ba'i bstod pa 'thad ldan ma/ 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod
pa rgyud gsum 'khor lo/ sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma/ mtshan brjod 'don thabs dmigs tsho gsum yod pa/ a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/'di rje btsun gyis mdzad pa yin
min the tshom yod zer/ de'i dkyil chog don yod zhags pa'i cho

ga de'i maNDal gyi cho ga lha lnga'i bstod pa srung 'khor bri tshul/ phyag rdor gos sngon can gyi gzungs chog rnam 'joms kyi rgyud kyi TIkka dang /'di yang the tshom can du
grags/ sa bcad dpung bzang gi mdo 'grel/ mi g.yo ba gsang chen gyi 'grel pa/'di las mi g.yo ba sngon po lha dgu bstan/ gtor chen don lnga the tshom can/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/
shAkya'i rgyal rabs/ bod kyi rgyal rabs/ bod kyi dge 'dun gyi 'dul grwa gyes tho/ dus tshod bzung ba'i rtsis yig gza' skar gyi 'phrod brtag pa/ zhe sa dgu 'khrugs kyi
yi ge phyag chen gces bsdus kyi man ngag 'di la tshad ldan gyi grub chen so so nas brgyud pa'i sems kyi gnas lugs gtan la 'bebs pa gtso bor gyur pa'i man ngag gi rim pa
du ma yod/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras kyi skabs kyi rmi lam bzung sbyangs sogs kyang 'dir bzhugs/ chos spyod rin chen phreng ba/ sdom pa nyi shu pa'i
TIkka /spyod 'jug gi sa bcad de gtor ma brgya rtsa nas 'di'i bar la chos sna bcu gcig nyams mgur gyi skor la ye shes rdo rje la gnang ba/ zhen pa bzhi bral/ khams bde
dris pa/ sa skya'i gnas bstod/ rmi lam nyams len/ gnyen po bsten tshul/ sems 'dul tshul/ sgrub pa nyams su len tshul/ gsang sngags nang gi nyams len/ rang la rang gi bskul
ma/ nyams dbyangs chen mo ste bcu gcig nyams dbyangs chen po 'di la shar chen pas 'di gling ras kyi zur za chen mo la gzhan zhig gis bcos bsnan byas pa yin gsungs par
grags/ sman spyad rgyal po'i dkor mdzod bya ba bka' 'bum gyi zhabs na bzhugs/ 'di la le'u'i rim pa du ma yod/ le'u'i mjug na gso spyad bdud rtsi thigs pa las zer

ba yang 'dug skabs 'gar bla ma rje btsun pa'i gdams pa'o zer ba yang 'dug pas rje btsun gyi gsung rgyun la bu chen zhig gis zin bris byas pa yang 'dra/ des na rje btsun gyis
mdzad pa de gzhan zhig yod par sems/ gang ltar glegs bam gsum na bzhugs pa'i chos sna'i grangs la brgya dang sum cu so bdun yod/ mkhyen rab rin po che'i rnam thar na brgya
dang drug cu yod par bshad/ lam 'bras skor la po ti gcig logs su bzhugs pa dang bcas pas rje btsun gyi gsung 'bum po ti bzhi'o/ /de ltar dkar po rnam gsum gyi bka' 'bum
dang / lung rgyun phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa dang po nas med kyang dus phyis bla ma dpal ldan seng ge ba'i thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir du chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa'i bkas bskul te 'khon shes rab rdo rjes lung rgyun su yod la zhus te dar rgyas su mdzad cing / de dag gi brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen shes rdor bas bla ma so so la gsan pa
las/ mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun dbang ba/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel
ba/ sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa
ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shar khang pa man

'dra/ ! /rgyud sde spyi'i stong thun/ dag ldan/ mngon rtogs ljon shing / gur gyi sa bcad/ gur rgyan rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ dkar po rnam gsum/ sa paN/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam
skya/ dpal ldan seng ge bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba man 'dra/ ! /nag po dkyil chog de'i TIkka/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ mai tri mkha' spyod kyi sgrub
thabs/ rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ pra phab pa/ gnod sbyin mo sgrub thabs/ tshangs pa'i bu mo'i sgrub thabs/ padma pa ti'i man ngag sman chen po'i bcud len/ mai tri mkha'
spyod kyi rjes gnang rnams ni/ brag phug pa/ bla ma bsod nams pa/ shes rdor ba man 'dra/ sgrol ma spyi sgrub/ so so'i sgrub thabs/ khol po pa ti'i man ngag bstod pa 'don
thabs/ nyi sbas kyis mdzad pa'i phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa'i TIkka/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog rnams ni rin po che bsod grags
pa/ chos rje bsod nams pa/ shes rdor ba man 'dra/ sgrol ma'i bstod sgrub gnyis ni/ nyi sbas/ te lo/ nA ro/ nag po pa/ gu rub lo tsA ba/ rong pa/ brang ti dar ma snying po/
sa chen/ 'chim khu dbon/ bla ma 'jam gsar/ lce mdo sde seng ge sga lo/ rong pa shes bzang / rin po che bsod grags pa man 'dra/ sa chen gyi rgyud sde spyi rnam/ brtag gnyis
kyi sa bcad/ TIkka/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi le 'grel/ sa bcad mal lo'i gsung la zin bris byas pa'i TIkka che ba/ 'jigs byed rtog bdun gyi TIkka che ba rnams ni/ sa
chen/ gan pa ston

dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma ye shes dpal/ shes rdor ba man 'dra/ rje btsun rtse mo'i sambu Ti'i TIkka/ rje btsun gyi rab gnas don gsal/
he ru ka'i chas drug gtor ma brgya rtsa rnams ni/ rje btsun sku mched/ sa paN/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya/ dpal ldan pa/ shes rdor ro/ /sgrol ma zhi khro'i thugs sgrub
ni/ chos rje khu dbon/ shar pa shes 'byung / ye shes 'byung gnas/ dkon mchog 'byung gnas/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ seng ge ba/ shes rdor ro/ /mi g.yo ba'i chu bsrung
ni/ rje btsun sku mched/ sa paN/ mdo sde dpal/ lo mchog bag ston/ shes rdor ro/ /ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje pa/ 'u yug pa bsod seng / spru
lung pa kun smon/ la ru ba yon tan dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bag ston/ shes rdor ro/ /gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa ni/ chos rje khu dbon/ shar pa sku mched/ 'jam dbyangs
chen po/ bag ston/ shes rdor ro/ /rdo rje 'byung ba'i TIkka ni/ chos rje khu dbon/ spru lung pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ slob dpon rin chen dpal/ bla ma rgyal ba dpal/
bla ma thogs med pa/ shes rdor ro/ /don zhags kyi lo rgyus/ sa bcad/ rgyud chung gi TIkka lag tu blang pa'i rim pa rnams ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ gtsang
po zho ra ba/ la ru ba/ grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen bu/ mkhan chen dar ma ba/ shes rdor ro/ /dril bu pa'i dbang chu/ sgrub

thabs gnyis/ sa skya paN chen pa yan 'dra ba las/ bo dong rin po che/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge kun mkhyen bu/ rin po che bsod grags pa man sngar bzhin no/ /sdom pa nyi
shu pa'i TIkka/ mtshan brjod 'don thabs rnams ni/ ka bzhi pa grags gzhon/ rin po che bsod grags pa/ mkhan chen gzhon nu mgon/ shes rdor ro/ /kyai rdo rje'i dbang chu chen
mo/ dbang chog nas gling ma/ chos la 'jug pa'i sgo/ byis pa bde blag tu 'jug pa/ mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa/ bdag med ma'i mngon rtogs/ lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs gsum/ phag
mo zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs/ sngags kyi byin rlabs/ las bcu/ 'chim chos seng la springs pa/ gzhan phan nyer mkho/ arga'i cho ga kha 'bar ma'i gtor chen rnams ni/ sa
paN/ 'phags pa/ 'jam skya/ a mo gha/ shes rdor ro/ /dril bu pa'i lo rgyus/ rim lnga/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ nges brjod/ bla ma'i 'phrul 'khor bri thabs rnams ni/ stod lo/
a mo gha/ shes rdor ro/ /sgrol ma nyer gcig ma'i sa bcad dang TIkka/ nyi sbas kyi nyer gcig ma'i las tshogs dang bcas pa'i sa bcad rnams ni/ bla ma thub mgon/ a mo gha/
shes rdor ro/ /rigs gsum spyi'i rigs gtad/ a ra pa tsa na'i mngon rtogs/ dkyil chog rnams kyang gong dang 'dra/ dpa' bo drug pa'i rgyud kyi TIkka ni/ chos rje pa/ shang pa
bsod rin/ slob dpon bzung lus/ rin po che bsod nams 'byung ba/ sher rdor ro/ /brtag gnyis kyi TIkka rnam bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer ni/ chos rje khu dbon/ de

gnyis ka la shangs pa bsod rin/ srad pa kun rin/ shes rdor ro/ /rab gnas bzang drug dus mtha'i cho ga bstod pa DaNDa ka kyai rdor gyi bkra shis rnams ni/ 'phags pa/ cog ro
ston gzhon/ chos brtson/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ shes rdor ro/ /'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje myu gus mdzad pa'i TIkka ni/ sa chen/ rje btsun/ paN chen/ khams pa dbon/
sga lo/ a ka ra/ sangs rin/ shes rdor ro/ /tshogs bdag gi sgrub thabs che chung / rje btsun/ paN chen/ skyobs pa dpal/ gzhon nu bkra shis/ rdo rje dpal/ go ru she rin/

rgyal/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ka bcu pa gzhon seng / shes rdor ro/ /gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i brgyud pa ni/ klu sgrub/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang
po/ dpal sde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags pa/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo/ kha 'ub pa/ rje sa chen/ rje btsun/ chos rje pa/ byang chub dpal/
bde ba dpal/ ka bzhi pa grags gzhon/ rin chen bsod grags pa/ rin po che grags tshul ba/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba man gong bzhin no// //rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen brtse chu
shel khams/ /gdul bya dag pa'i snod du shar ba las/ /deng 'dir rje btsun bla ma sa skya pa/ /kun

dga' rgyal mtshan zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i gsung 'bum thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thub pa
dgongs gsal/ sdom gsum rab dbye/ mkhas 'jug legs bshad/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen blo gsal ba rnams la dri ba'i tshul 'phro can/ rol mo'i bstan bcos/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas
byang sems rnams la 'phrin du gsol ba/ skyes bu dam pa'i 'phrin yig yi ge'i sbyor ba/ sgra la 'jug pa'i rnam bshad/ lung rigs rnam dag dang mthun par dpyad dgos tshul/ smra
sgo'i bsdus don/sgra'i gnad bsdus pa yang zer/ byis pa bde 'jug gi rnam bshad/ sgra nyer bar bsdu ba/ bde bar gshegs pa'i thugs rje la bskul ba/ mngon brjod kyi bstan
bcos tshig gi gter/ sdeb sbyor sna tshogs mu tig gi chun po/ nga brgyad ma rtsa 'grel/ tshad ma rigs pa'i gter/ de'i rang 'grel/ chag lo'i dris lan/ zhang lo la gdams pa/
glo bo lo tsA ba la springs pa/ 'chad kha nam mkha' 'bum gyi dris lan/ bka' gdams do skor gyi dris lan tshigs bcad ma/ snye mo sgom chen gyi dris lan/ rtogs ldan zhig gi
dris lan/ lta ba ston pa'i tshigs bcad kyi tshogs/ chos spyod kyi le'u/ sgrub pa'i le'u/ 'bras bu'i le'u ste le'u gsum tshigs bcad du yod pa/ bstan pa la dga' ba'i lha rnams
la springs pa/ mi nyag gi yul na bzhugs pa'i mkhan slob rnams la chab shog nyi ma 'bum la springs pa/ zhen pa bzhi bral/ lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ thub pa'i bstod
pa tshigs

bcad bco lnga pa/ thub pa'i bstod pa tshigs bcad dgu pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa tshigs bcad bcu gcig lha sa'i bde bar gshegs pa rnams la bsngags pa/ bod yul la bsngags
pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi phyag mtshan gyi ri mo'i skabs kyi tshigs bcad kyi tshogs/ gur ston gyi zhus lan/ gangs ri'i khrod kyi sgom chen rnams la springs pa/ mu
stegs btul ba'i tshigs bcad/ ba gor zhes bya ba'i sgra las drangs te yon tan sgrogs pa'i tshal la bstod pa/ ri khud kyi rnga bo che la bstod pa/ gdong bzhi pa la bstod
pa/ theg chen lam gyi rnam gzhag mdor bsdus pa'i tshigs bcad/ snang ba mtha' yas kyi bsgom don/ 'chi kha'i gdams ngag sems kyi gnas lugs mtshon par byed pa'i tshigs bcad
brgyad pa/ rten 'brel lnga'i yi ge bsngo ba yon bshad dang bcas pa/ dam tshig gi bshad pa/ maNDal 'bul ba'i cho ga sgrub pa lung sbyin/ aShTa'i gzhi bshad/ tshogs 'khor rtsod
spong / rnam 'joms kyi rnam bshad bdud rtsi spel ba/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs bstod pa dang bcas pa/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ gza' yum mchod pa'i cho ga brtag gnyis
kyi bsdus don rje btsun gyis mdzad pa las cung zad spros te sna bsrings pa/ zung 'jug gsal ba/ bdag med bstod 'grel/ rigs kyi rab dbye'i bshad sbyar/ brtag gnyis la mkho
ba'i sgra sgrub tshan pa dgu pa/ rigs dang ye shes bsre ba'i bshad pa/ gsol 'debs gang drin ma chen mo/ bstod pa sku'i spyod pa ma/ birWa pa'i bstod pa

dad chu ma/ 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa rgyud gsum 'khor lo'i rnam bshad/ rje btsun gyi bstod pa yon tan rgya mtsho ma/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed chen mo/ de'i lung sbyor rnams
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon 'dul 'dzin/
byang seng pa/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan pa/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma don rgyal ba/ slob dpon
'dul 'dzin/ byang seng pa/ shar chen pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / yongs 'dzin/ sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shar khang pa/ rje thar brtse
ba nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rje shar khang pa man 'dra/ chos rje pa'i gsung rab 'di rnams kyi lung gnang dus mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi
gsung las/ sgra la 'jug pa'i rnam bshad kyi gsham na kho bos sbyar ba'i sgra'i bstan bcos las shes par bya'o/ /zhes gsungs mod/ de ni deng sang grags tshod mi snang zhing
bka' 'bum na yang mi bzhugs pas btsal bar bya'o/ /po ti ta pa'i mjug tu yan lag brgyad pa'i snying po/ dug gcod zab mo/ gzhung lugs legs bshad dang gsum 'dug kyang gsan
yig la mi

snang bas lung rgyun yang mi mdzad/ po ti ta pa'i mjug na lam sbas bshad kyi khrid yig mdzad byang med pa/ skyes bu'i rnam 'byed gzhon nu'i mgul rgyan/ rlung ltas brtag pa/
thod pa brtag pa/ sgra'i bstan bcos mkhas pa'i kha rgyan/ rme brtsegs kyi sgrub thabs las tshogs/ cho ga'i sdom tshig mdzad byang med pa/ lam zab gu shrI jo 'bum ma/ 'dod
rgyal gyi rjes gnang rnams kyang gsan yig na med pas lung mi mdzad/ 'di rnams dang sngar smos pa'i gsum po e wa~M gyi bka' 'bum rnying pa gnyis na'ang mi bzhugs zer/ 'bri
khung pa la zhu yig de yang gsan yig na med/ e wa~M gyi bka' 'bum rnying pa na bzhugs pa'i rnal 'byor pa phru ma pa la gdams pa/ phung po gsum pa 'don thabs/ mdo sdud
pa 'don thabs rnams kyang gsan yig na med cing lung mi mdzad/ dbus gtsang mnga' ris dang bcas pa'i bu slob la bka' shog gnang ba de bka' 'bum rnying pa na med kyang gsan
yig na snang zhing lung rgyun yod/ 'di rgya nag nas bod spyi la gnang ba yin/ 'don thabs gnyis dang / gzhon nu'i mgul rgyan ni sa paN la kha 'phangs pa yin/ gzhung lugs legs
bshad dang grub mtha' rnam 'byed mi gcig ste/ grub mtha' rnam 'byed ni rigs gter rang 'grel dang mkhas 'jug sogs kyi gong du brtsams tshar bar gzhung de dang de'i tshig
las shes/ cig shos ni ling chu rtser khab tu sbyar gsungs pa yod pas grub mtha' rnam 'byed min pa de kas shes shing de dang mi mthun pa yang mang du yod do/ /'on kyang
bdag cag gi bla ma

thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid 'di la thugs rtsis cher mdzad cing / sa paN gyi gsung yin pa gzhir bzhag gnang / sman yan lag brgyad pa'i snying po 'di sa paN gyi gsung rigs 'dra
bar snang / gzhung tshogs nyung la don rgya che ba go bde ba zhig 'dug nga brgyad ma'i 'grel par kho bos byas pa'i sman yan lag brgyad pa'i don bsdus pa bya ba yod pas
der blta bar bya gsungs pa de dang gcig pa yin shas che/ sgra'i bstan bcos mkhas pa'i kha rgyan 'di tshig gi phrad dang byed tshig drug sgra sogs skad gsar bcad dang mthun
pa'i dngos gtsang zhing shin tu mkho ba zhig 'dug pas/ sa paN gyi gsung rigs 'dra bar snang / snyan ngag nga nyid ces pa'i 'grel par kho bos byas pa'i snyan ngag mkhas
pa'i kha rgyan du blta bar bya gsungs pa ni snyan ngag rang gi dbang du byas pa'i kha rgyan yin pas sgra'i 'di dang mi gcig par sems/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gu shrI jo 'bum
gyi don du gnang ba 'di sa paN gyis ma mdzad pa 'dra ste 'di'i dbu phyogs la bltas pas shes so/ /nga brgyad ma'i 'grel par sa paN rang gis mdzad pa'i sgra'i bstan bcos shes
rab 'phro ba dang / sku gzugs kyi phyag tshad bstan pa dang / sa brtag pa la sogs pa'i bstan bcos yod par gsungs kyang dpe rgyun ma mched pa'am/ deng sang grags tshod
chung bar snang / deng sang lung rgyun bzhugs pa'i chos sna'i grangs la bdun cu rtsa lnga yod ces mkhyen rab rin po che'i rnam thar nas bshad/ tha pa la bzhugs pa'i bka'
'bum gyi tho yig na a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs kyi rjes su/ 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa zhig yod par

bshad 'dug kyang / bka' 'bum nang na sngar byung ba'i bstod pa dpal ldan blo gros ma las gzhan mi 'dug pa ci yin/ sa paN gyis ri bo rtse lngar 'jam dbyangs gtso 'khor lnga
zhal gzigs dus spros bral stong nyid nam mkha'i khams su/ sing las seng ge sngon po'i steng du zhes sogs kyi bstod pa 'di la lung rgyun yod med kyi rtsad gcod dgos shing
/ phyi nang kun rig ces pa'i nang rig pa'i thad kyi 'grel par/ 'dul ba dang mngon pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rnams la yang kho bos byas pa'i bstan
bcos yod gsungs pa 'dug pas de dag gang yin snyam pa'i rtog dpyod dang / rgyal sras lam bzang 'di pha rol tu phyin pa'i bstan bcos chen por 'dug mod/ 'on kyang phyis rgya
nag nas yar gnang ba yin pas nga brgyad ma'i 'grel par gsungs pa'i bstan bcos kyi nang tshan du mi 'gro ba 'dra/ kha cig sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras kyi khrid kyi

/ bsnyen pa'i

grangs tshad kyi zhus lan/ dam tshig gsum gyi glu'i rjes la bya ba'i smon lam/ bdag 'jug dpal 'byung ma/ jim gir ma/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas pa len pa'i lag len/ dbang gong
ma gsum gyi lag len tshigs bcad ma/ lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs/ tshogs 'khor bdud rtsi bum pa/ de'i lung sbyor/ yang tshogs 'khor bsdus pa/ bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub thabs
bdud rtsi 'byung ba/ bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa rnam dag phreng ba ma/ dag pa gsum gyi khrid yig dbang gsum pa'i lam/ tshogs sbyor mngon rtogs/ 'pho ba'i rnal 'byor/

la gdams pa/ lo pa'i zhu lan/ dbon nag la gdams pa/ des chos bzhengs pa'i tshigs bcad/ dus mchod bzhi'i ngos 'dzin/ springs yig gcig dga' ba'i gtam/ dbus gtsang gi bu slob
rnams la springs pa/ dus 'khor thugs dkyil gyi mngon rtogs/ lnga bsdus sgra gcan gza' lnga dang bcas pa'i rtsis gzhi/ rtsis bsdus gsal ba'i sgron me/ nyi khyim 'pho ba'i
nges pa/ rtsis kyi gtsug lag dang mthun par nges pa/ dhu ba gnyis pa zhes pa'i rtsis/ lo bdag gi rtsis nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa/ rten cing 'brel 'byung gi gtsug lag gi rtsis

po/ mchod phreng kun bzang mchod sprin/ nag po pa'i sbyin sreg gi sdom tshig sbyin sreg gi cho ga dril bu lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs/ na pa la bde mchog lU hi pa'i sgrub thabs

kha skong mdzad pa 'jim gir dang / go bo can la gnang ba'i bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad gnyis/ phag mo lha so bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi mngon rtogs/ de'i

thabs/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog sgrol ma lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs/ 'jigs pa brgyad skyob kyi sgrub thabs/
u rgyan sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ phyag drug sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs

te sgrol ma'i chos sna dgu/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i dkyil chog'di klu byang dang sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gnyis kyi dkyil chog dang mthun pa kha che paN chen
nas sa paN la brgyud pa yin/ ye shes zhabs kyi lo rgyus/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs/ dgra nag gtso rkyang gi sgrub thabs bsdus pa/ rdo rje 'jigs byed zhal

pa'i sgrub thabs/ spyan ras gzigs phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ yang

phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs tshan pa gnyis/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs/ rta mgrin khyung gshog can gyi sgrub thabs/ byams pa'i sgrub thabs/ byams pa la sogs pa 'dod pa'i lha
rnams la bstod pa/ mi g.yo ba phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ mi g.yo ba'i bstod pa/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal lha dgu'i sgrub thabs/ gdugs dkar gyi
sgrub thabs/ lo ma gyon ma'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ de'i bstod pa/ lha mo tsunda'i sgrub thabs/ mya ngan med pa'i 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ yang 'od zer can

phreng tshan pa gnyis/ srung ba lnga'i sngon 'gro gtor ma/ srung ba lnga'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ lha lnga'i bstod pa/ dkyil 'khor lha tshogs kyi bstod pa/ phyogs

thugs dam gtor ma'i rims pa/ klu gtor/ chu gtor/ gtor ma'i de nyid brgyad pa/ bstod dbyangs rgya mtsho snyan ngag gi rgyan gyis rnam par bkra ba/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa
la bstod pa/ 'jam dpal la mtshan don gyi sgo nas bstod pa/ 'jam dpal la bstod pa tshan pa drug spyan ras gzigs/ byams pa/ gnas brtan bcu drug rnams kyi bstod pa tshan pa
re/ chos spyod yan lag bcu pa/ yan lag bdun pa/ phyag mchod sdig bshags bsngo ba dang bcas pa'i tshigs bcad/ sems bskyed pa'i cho ga sa paN gyis bsam yas su chos 'khor bskor
ba'i tshigs bcad las spel ba/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed bsngo ba bya tshul 'bring du bstan pa/ de rnams kyi tshul cung zad bsdus pa/ skyabs 'gro'i rnam gzhag bo lod kyi
don du mdzad pa/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed a rog gi don du mdzad pa/ dbang bskur gyi bslab bya/ rgyal po la gdams pa/ de'i sa bcad/ theg pa chen po la gsal ba yi ge'i ma
mo la spel ba/ de'i bsdus don/ shes bya rab gsal/ las 'bras gsal ba'i me long / rgyal bu jim big thi mo la gtam du bya ba nor bu'i phreng ba/ rgyal bu mangga laM la gtam
du bya ba bkra shis kyi phreng ba/ rgyal bu ne mo gan la springs pa'i rab byed/ rgyal bu hong ko'i don du sangs rgyas kyi gsung las byung ba'i chos kyi tshul brjod pa/ rgyal
bu de gus bo ga la nye bar gdams pa bdud rtsi 'byung gnas/ rgyal bu de mur bo ga la gdams pa zla ba'i 'od zer/ dpon mo tshe sunda ri zhes bya ba'i sems la phan pa'i

chos/ rgyal bu jim gyim la springs pa/ yang de la springs pa/ bden gnyis rnam nges la/ zab mo snang ba'i rab byed/ phyag rgya chen po nyams su blang ba'i gnad/ phyag chen nyams
su blang ba'i man ngag yan lag bdun gyi gtam/ dam chos pad dkar gyi chos kyi rnam grangs kyi dogs dpyod/ theg pa chen po'i man ngag yang dag par bsdus pa snying po'i
sdom/ thabs la mkhas pa'i sdom/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sdom/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom/ sangs rgyas kyi sdom/ rgyud bla'i bsdus don/ skyo ba'i gtam/ snyigs ma'i dus kyi ngan
pa'i tshul/ theg pa'i rnam dbye/ rnam thar sgo gsum du bsdus te nyams len/ yi ge'i ma mo la spel ba'i tshigs bcad/ yang tshigs bcad thor bu ba gcig ston brtson gyi dris
lan/ theg chen lam gyi snying po/ gzhan tshigs bcad thor bu gcig dbus gtsang du chos 'khor gnang ba'i bka' yig sdom brtson gcig la springs pa/ zab don nyams su len tshul/
yan lag bdun gyi gtam/ ji big de mur la springs pa/ phi gyang hus glegs bam bsgrubs pa la bsngags pa/ rgyal bu byang chub sems dpa' la gnang ba'i bka' yig rgyal bu a kho
la springs pa/ rin po che dpag shi la springs pa/ paNDi ta lakShmi ka ra la springs pa/ gshong ston la gnang ba/ rwa dbon la bskur ba/ snar thang / ral gri la springs pa/
spyi bo lhas pa la bskur ba/ khro lo la springs pa/ chag lo la bskur ba/ dbus kyi bka' gdams pa spyi la bskur ba/ dbus kyi mtshan nyid pa spyi la bskur ba/ stag lung pa
la bskur ba/ dbus kyi sgom chen

pa rnams la springs pa/ rgyal bu ji big de mur la gnang ba/ du gal dur mig la bskur ba/ jim gyim ho go la gnang ba/ grags bzang dang ston gzhon la gnang ba/ gos dar stong dang
dgu brgya bzhi bcu tham pa phul ba'i mchod brjod dang bsngo ba/ tshe dpag med la bstod pa/ yang tshigs bcad thor bu gnyis/ mgon g.yag la bsngags pa/ chang la bsngags
pa bdud rtsi bum pa/ jim gyim gyis bka' 'gyur bzhengs pa'i gsal byed/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bzhengs pa la bsngags pa/ shin tu rgyas pa'i sde snod bzhengs pa la bsngags
pa/ manggalaM yab yum gyis rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang / phal po che bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed/ ji big de mur gyis phal po che sogs bzhengs pa'i gsal byed/ a rog chos 'bum
bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed/ go pe las rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed/ dge 'dun bzang po sogs kyis rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bzhengs pa'i mtshonbyed/ rin chen
dpal gyis 'bum bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed/ zin shing gi ston pa btul ba'i tshigs bcad/ theg pa chen po'i slob dpon slob ma sogs kyi rnam dbye/ 'dul ba'i las chog bsdus
pa/ las chog rgyas pa/ bsnyen gnas kyi cho ga rgyal po yab sras kyis mchod rten bzhengs pa la bsngags pa'i DaNDa ka bsngags 'os bsngags pa'i rab byed/ rgyal rabs la bsngags
pa'i tshigs bcad/ dus phyis thos pa'i chos kyi gsan yig de'i 'phro lung dang brgyud pa sna tshogs byas pa/ rgyal po go pe la sras dang btsun

mor bcas pa la shing mo yos la gnang ba'i bkra shis/ me pho 'brug la gnang ba'i bkra shis/ me mo sbrul/ sa pho rta/ de nas lo gnyis la mi snang / lcags mo bya/ chu pho khyi/
chu mo phag shing pho byi ba/ shing mo glang / stag gi de ma tshud/ me mo yos/ sa pho 'brug sa mo sbrul/ lcags pho rta/ lcags mo lug chu pho sprel/ chu mo bya/ shing pho
khyi/ shing mo phag me pho byi/ me mo glang / sa pho stag sa mo yos/ lcags pho 'brug rnams la lo gsar shar rim gyis gnang ba'i bkra shis kyi phreng ba tshigs su bcad pa
dgu dang bcu gsum la sogs pa ci rigs pa yod/ yang mangga laM yab yum la gnang ba/ ji big yab yum la gnang ba/ dpon mo che la gnang ba/ yang bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad
pa gcig rnams bzhugs pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon
'dul 'dzin/ mkhan chen byang seng ba/ shar chen pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / yongs 'dzin/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje thar rtse ba nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na yongs
'dzin/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng
ge bla ma

don yod rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ ! /chos kyi rje mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i zab mo sngags kyi phyogs gtso bor gyur pa'i gsung 'bum gyi lung thob
pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ bla ma rin chen 'byung ldan la gsol ba 'debs pa/ rdo rje 'chang la bstod pa gnyis/ sems dpa' chen po'i rnam thar bstod pa kha skong dang bcas
pa/ yang de nyid la bstod pa/ bdag chen chu mig pa/ rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug pa/ go bo rab 'byams pa shes rab dpal rnams la bstod pa re re/ kun mkhyen/ sangs rgyas
'phel la bstod pa gnyis/ chos rje gung ru la bstod pa/ kye rdor 'grel pa lugs dang / bde mchog brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong / phar tshad brgyud 'debs/ byams pa dang / sgrol
ma'i bstod pa/ chos skyong gi bstod pa/ lam 'bras kyi smon lam/ smon lam dbang bzhi la sbyar ba/ sems dpa' chen po'i rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa/ lam 'bras bla
ma brgyud pa la yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga brda grol nges pa'i dpal ster/ zab don bdud rtsi nying khu rtsa 'grel/ a seng ma'i 'grel pa/ lam 'bras chos 'byung kha bskangs pa/
snang gsum gyi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i gsal byed/ gzhung ji lta bar bkri ba'i lam spyi'i rnam gzhag bdag med ma'i mngon dkyil gyi tho/ lam dus kyi dbang bskur gso thabs/
bir srung gi phyag len/ mngon rtogs tshul bcu bzhi'i ngag 'don/ mchod gtor gyi rnal 'byor/ blos bslangs sogs kyi sgo rkyang sbrags sogs kyi khyad

par/ zla zer gyi rtsod spong / rgyud kyi tshig don 'ga' zhig la dogs dpyod/ rab gnas dge legs rgya mtsho/ kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi rnam bshad/ lus dkyil gyi rnam bshad/ dbang
chu'i sa chog gi gsal byed/ dbang chu'i rnam bshad/ gur gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i dkyil chog sambu Ti'i cho ga'i gsal byed/ rgyud kyi bsdus don tshigs bcad ma/ rnam 'joms
bir lugs kyi byin rlabs bya tshul/ bde mchog chos 'byung / lU nag gi mngon rtogs/ bde mchog lU hi pa rnam bshad/ rim bzhi'i khrid yig mkha' spyod sgo 'byed/ rdo rje theg
pa la log smra tshar gcod rigs pa'i mtshon cha/ 'jam rdor gyi sgrub dkyil/ 'jam rdor dang spyan gzigs kyi sgrub dkyil mi 'dra ba'i khyad par/ 'jam rdor gyi gtor chog mchod
phreng / 'jam rdor rnam bshad/ 'jigs byed sa lugs kyi mngon dkyil/ spros med rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ mngon par byang chub pa'i tshul la grangs nges phye ba/ kun rig rtsod
spong / kun rig gyi sbyin sreg sbyong rgyud kyi TIkka/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gzhung bzhi nyams su len tshul/ arga'i cho ga sdom gsum kha skong / de'i sa bcad/ dris
lan padmo bzhad pa/ nyi zla seng ge dang / dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ rin chen dpal gyi dris lan/ mus srad pa/ tshul khrims bzang po/ shes rab seng ge rin chen
byang chub/ tshe rgyal skyabs rnams kyi dris lan/ rtags 'jug gi TIkka/ smon lam chen po bcu pa/ yang smon lam chen po bcu pa/ bsngo ba mdor bsdus dang bcas pa/ sog po

bka' bcu pa/ drung chen kun spangs pa/ go bo sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan rnams la gdams pa re re/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ gling smad paNDi ta/ karma mi pham mgon/ chu
'dus mkhas btsun pa/ slob dpon sbyin bzang pa/ chum bde chen gyi mkhan po rnams la bstod pa re re/ gsung ngag brgyud pa'i bris sku'i dkar chag sa chen gyi bris sku chen
mo'i dkar chag bde ba can gyi smon lam/ mdo khams su 'bul bsdud kyi phyag rtags/ gyad gnyer sger gsum la dge bskul btang ba'i yi ge sdom gsum 'khrul spong rnams thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen chen po/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen
thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang chos kyi rje mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi gsung rab
khyad par can rnams kho bos phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa la shog grangs lnga brgya re la po ti rer byas pa glegs bam bdun tsam byung ba'i nang nas bdag nyid kyis lung nos
pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs bya tshul/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed cho ga theg chen sgo 'byed rgyal sras
lam gyi rtsa ba/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i dbang gi cho ga bklags chog tu bkod pa/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa lha lnga'i rjes gnang go bde bklags chog dpal

mgon zhal gyi rjes gnang gi tho yig mun sel sgron me/ tshe dbang lcags sdong ma'i phyag len 'chi med bdud rtsi'i bum bzang / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang
/ dpal mgon gdong gnyan can gyi rjes gnang go bde bklags chog dpal mgon brtsegs zhal can gyi rjes gnang gi phyag bzhes gsal ba'i sgron me/ gshed dmar spros med kyi 'od
gsal 'char ba'i byin rlabs kyi lag len khrigs chags su bkod pa/ dpyal lugs kyi phag mo skor gsum sogs kyi byin rlabs dang rjes gnang 'ga' yar gyi zin tho/ rje btsun ma ku
ru kulle'i gsang sgrub lha lnga'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga gsal ba'i sgron me/ dpal 'dod pa'i rgyal po gsang sngags sgra'i rjes gnang rgyas pa bklags chog tu bkod pa/ dpal
tshogs kyi bdag po dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis pa'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag len khrigs chags 'dod dgu'i dpag bsam/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos dpal tshogs
kyi bdag po'i khyad par gyi rjes gnang ma nor don tshang gsal ba'i sgron me/ gnyan lo tsA ba'i dbang gi lha gsum gyi rjes gnang bklags chog gsal ba'i sgron me/ rje btsun
dzam lha dmar po brgyud pa lugs gnyis kyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i phyag bzhes gsal ba'i sgron me/ gsang khrid 'chad dus kyi mgon po lha dgu'i rjes gnang
bya tshul/ rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor gyi khog phub kyi snyan brgyud mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ phyi srung ba'i 'khor lo la brten nas sgrub pa phyi'i
brag rdzong ma'i khrid kyi yi ge 'dod dgu'i dpal ster/ nag po chen

po'i gsang khrid kyi yi ge bla ma'i gsung 'gros yid bzhin gyi nor bu/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po rwa lugs kyi dbang gi cho ga las brtsams te dri ba rtog dpyod sprin gyi
rnga gsang gi rang lan dpyid kyi rgyal po'i dga' ston legs bshad khu byug gi sgra dbyangs gsar pa/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dbang gi cho ga'i dka' gnas las brtsams te
dris pa'i rang lan snying po 'dzugs tshugs/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed pa'i rim pa'i rnam bshad bdud rtsi'i bum bzang bla ma dgyes pa'i mchod sprin/ rje btsun bla
ma sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la brtan bzhugs rdo rje tshig mchog byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i zil dngar kun tu rgyas par byed pa/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la bstod pa
rdo rje'i brtan bzhugs lha'i rnga dbyangs 'chi med dpal ster/ lhag pa'i lha gtsug tor rnam rgyal ma la bstod cing gsol ba gdab pa 'chi med 'dod dgu'i dpag bsam tshe rig
bdud rtsi dpal sbyin/ lhag pa'i lha gtsug tor rnam rgyal ma la bstod cing gsol ba gdab pa 'chi med 'dod dgu'i dpal sbyin/ rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po byams pa thugs rje
dpal bzang po'i rnam thar ngo mtshar rin po che'i phreng ba/ bka' drin gzhal du ma mchis pa mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang phyug dpal bzang po'i rnam thar rtogs pa brjod
pa ngo mtshar yid bzhin gyi phreng ba dad pa'i dpal rgyun/ nai gu chos drug gi nyams len bsdus pa'i yi ge rgyud kyi spyi don tshul dang po gsum gyi rnam gzhag ston pa
rgyud gsum la 'jug pa'i sgo/ rgyud kyi spyi don tshul bzhi pa mngon rtogs kyi rnam gzhag

ston pa brgyud gsum snying po'i legs bshad/ dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i rgyud gsum dngos gzhi'i bshad pa khog phub gnad kyi lde mig 'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyal
po'i rnam bshad theg pa chen po'i nyams len gnad kyi sgron me/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan la bstod pa yon tan rgya mtsho ma'i tshig don rnam bshad legs
bshad nor bu'i phreng mdzes/ mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam gsum las brtsams te bstan bcos chen po mkhas pa 'jug sgo'i dgongs pa spyi'i ngag gis ston pa legs bshad nor bu'i phreng
mdzes/ sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba'i rnam bshad zla 'od nor bu/ bod kyi mkhas pa snga phyi dag gi grub mtha'i shan 'byed mtha' dpyod dang bcas pa'i 'brel pa'i gtam
bskyel dpyod ldan mkhas pa'i lus rgyan rin chen mdzes pa'i phra tshom/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i dbang gi skabs las brtsams te dri ba'i rang lan mkhas pa'i rna rgyan/ mchog
gi rnam 'dren 'gyur med bde chen zhabs kyis lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gzhung shing las brtsams te dris lan gnang ba'i zhus lan dpyod ldan rna ba'i rgyan/ gsung ngag rin
po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i dka' ba'i gnas rnams las brtsams te dris pa'i rang lan gzur gnas drang ba'i gtam bskyel bdud rtsi'i thigs phreng / dpal kyai rdo rje'i
mngon rtogs lam dus bsdus 'bring rgyas gsum gyi rnam dbye bdud rtsi gtam bzang slob ma la phan pa/ gsung ngag sngon 'gro'i khrid rim snang gsum snying po'i legs bshad/ gsung
ngag dngos gzhi'i khrid rim rgyud gsum snying po'i legs bshad/ gsung ngag rin po

che'i skabs kyi slob ma rjes 'dzin mdzad tshul nyams su blang bde ba/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul gsang chen chos kyi rnga chen/ rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i
byin rlabs bya tshul legs byas gtam gyi bdud rtsi/ bla ma rin 'byung gi nyams len byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i yi ge 'dod dgu'i dpal 'byor ma lus pa'i 'byung gnas legs byas
kyi rnga bo che/ brda don gsal ba dang lam sbas bshad/ brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ lam zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi nang rnams kyi byin
rlabs bya tshul/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog nag po spyod pa'i lugs kyi mngon rtogs nyams su len tshul rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi rim pa gsal ba/ bde mchog dkar po'i khrid
sngon 'gro'i byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i zin bris pad dkar bzhad pa'i phreng ba/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor las brtsams te dris pa'i rang lan legs bshad ku mu da'i
tshal rab tu rgyas byed/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog dril bu pa'i rim pa lnga'i khrid rim sngon 'gro'i byin rlabs dang bcas pa/ shrI sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams kyis 'khor lo bde mchog gi skor la dri ba zhus pa'i lan mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags nyid kyis mdzad pa/ dpal kyai rdo rje man ngag
lugs kyi dbang gi cho ga'i dka' gnas la dogs slong dpyod ldan yid kyi dga' ston/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i khrid rim bla ma'i gsung 'gros dngos grub myur mgyogs
kyi pho nya/ rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i lam

srol lU nag dril gsum gyi sngon du 'gro ba'i spyi don gyi bshad pa'i zin bris bde chen zhal gyi thigs phreng / dpal 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi bskyed pa'i rim pa'i
rnam par bshad pa'i zin bris bde chen zhal gyi thigs phreng / phyag rgya chen po bsam mi khyab dang / ngag dbang grags pa'i lugs kyi byin rlabs kyi yi ge bklags chog tu bkod
pa/ lam 'bras rdo rje'i tshig gi 'grel pa gnyag ma'i dgongs don gsal bar byed pa gsung ngag bstan pa'i nyin byed/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi bskyed pa'i
rim pa'i bshad khrid rje bla ma mus pa chen po'i gsung rgyun/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang bka' gsar rnying gi dogs dpyod blo gsal nyer mkho'i legs bshad ya
rabs mkhas pa'i gtam bskyel/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos kyi byung tshul mdo tsam dang bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams len 'gos lugs gtsang ma yid 'phrog lha'i rol mo/ gzhan yang
lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rje btsun rin po che dang / grub chen thang stong rgyal po sogs la gsol 'debs kyi yi ge rje rang nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams kyi
sku bstod mang po/ dris lan chab shog zhal gdams kyi skor sogs mdor na gsung 'bum phal cher gyi lung rnams smin rgyas su nos pa'i bka' drin gzhal du med pa thob pa lags so/
/'dir smras pa/ sarba dznyA lo ka pa ri tsakShu me kakun mkhyen 'jig rten yongs kyi mig gcig pu/ /tsitta sya tsi to ma Ni tu le mi traM/thugs ni yid bzhin nor dang mtshungs
pa'i bshes/ /sarba dznyA na ma ho sA ddha manydzu gho Sha/thams cad mkhyen pa mkhan chen 'jam pa'i

dbyangs/ /a bi yo ga hrI da yA sa tsa ma kri ta/ 'bral med snying gi dkyil nas gsol ba 'debs/ /chos kun gzigs khyod mkhyen pa'i me long ngos/ /ma shar shes bya'i gzugs brnyan
de ci zhig /kun mkhyen khyod 'dra sngon kyang gangs ljongs 'dir/ /ma byon pa tsam phyin chad lta ga la/ /des na khyod thugs chos kyi rgya mtsho che/ /gting mtha' mi mngon
las 'ongs legs bshad kyi/ /chu klung stong gis bdag blo mi shes pa'i/ /tsha gdung sel mdzad bka' drin bgrang yas rnams/ /dran pa'i mod la spu ldang mchi ma g.yo/ /da
dung gsung rab rgya mtsho'i dka' gnas la/ /gzhan gyis ma rtogs the tshom sel ba'i phyir/ /mjal 'dod sems kyi lhag ma lus pa'i yid/ /rte'u ma dang bral 'dra'i sdug bsngal
gyi/ /khur gyis mnar ba'i mgon med bdag 'dra la/ /mi mngon dbyings nas brtse ldan bshes khyod kyis/ /gzigs la rnam dpyod blo gros snang ba stsol/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan
bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes
gnyen mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa'i zhal snga nas kyis rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te dgu pa'o// //mangga laM// //gcig zhus// ! mkhan chen a
pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART X: Teachings from Grub mchog mThu stobs dbang phyug and his brother; vol. ga, text no. 3, pp. 657-688

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las rigs ldan 'jam
pa'i dbyangs grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug mched kyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI bhu mi paNDu sdyA ma ba le shwa ra siddhi tsU DA laM ka re na maH bod skad du/ dpal ldan sa skya pa mthu stobs dbang phyug grub pa'i gtsug rgyan de la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /bstan pa'i rtsa lag sngags 'chang chos rje yi/ /thugs kyi sras mchog grags pa'i zla dbang de'i/ /phrin las yar ngo'i cha shas ltar gsal ba'i/ /skyes mchog
dam pa 'jam dbyangs sku mched rgyal/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa dpal sa skya pa rigs ldan 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched zhal rnam pa gnyis kyi drung du/ dam
pa'i chos kyi bka' drin nos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug las/ bcom ldan rdo rje gzhon nu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por stod las byang
chub sgrub pa'i dbang bskur ba rnam par dag pa lan mang du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal chos sku kun tu

bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu yi dbang po bsrung ba/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal po/ rdo rje
gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/
