dpal bzang po/ kha 'ub pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun rdor/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo

rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ dpal ldan sa skya pa sngags 'chang chen po grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po/ grub pa'i skyes chen dam pa sa skya pa mthu stobs dbang phyug des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na bla ma dam pa'i rjes su/ bla ma chen
po kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'khor lo'i mgon po shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun/ gan

pa ston dar/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa dbang rin/ gan pa rin rgyal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa man gong dang 'dra/ yang na rje btsun/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa
chos rin/ gan pa rin rgyal man gong dang 'dra/ yang na 'khon ston dkon mchog rgyal po/ glo bo rdo rje srin po/ glo bo rdo rje 'dzin/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/
bla chen 'phags pa man chad 'dra'o/ ! /yang dpal sa skya pa rgyal sras sems dpa' chen po sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal las/ rdo rje phur pa sa lugs kyi rdul
tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang
po bsrung ba/ rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal

po/ rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying
po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ kha 'ub pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun rdor/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ dpal sa skya pa sngags
'chang chen po grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ grub pa'i skyes chen dam pa sa skya pa mthu stobs dbang phyug sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal/
des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'jam dbyangs sku mched gnyis ka'i drung du/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dpag med kyi dbang bzhi
byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti phu ba/ ras chung ba/ mi la ras pa/ dwags po lha rje/ tha tsa ba/
'bri khung pa/ spyan snga ba/ yang

dgon pa/ spyan snga rin chen ldan/ rje zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal/ chos rje bde legs rin chen/ kun dga' dpal bzang / dbu ma dpal ldan bzang po/ drin can dpal
ldan mgon po/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags
pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ grub mchog mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams la'o/ /kho bo cag gis rje btsun sa skya pa gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rnams phal cher rje btsun mus pa chen po dang / rje nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa/ mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa sogs la nos mod kyang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras nas brgyud pa zhig gus zhen gyis thob 'dod che
bar yod pa bzhin/ dus phyis brgyud pa de las 'ongs pa'i sa skya pa gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rnams grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug gi drung du don gnyer chen pos
nos pa la/ thog mar rje btsun sa skya pa chen po'i bka' 'bum gyi chos kyi rnam grangs la/ljags lung gnang skabs rdo rje sems dpa' he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes sogs
dpon slob thams cad kyis yig brgya gang mang bzlas rjes chos gtor gnang / de skabs maNDal 'bul/ de nas 'o nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i sems can thams cad sogs spyi 'gro ltar
mdzad/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang sa bcad/ gzhung bshad a seng ma/ snyag ma/ gzhung bshad

sras don ma/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyung ngu / mnga' ris pa'i brtag gnyis kyi tshig 'grel/ sgyi chu ba'i brtag gnyis dka' 'grel/ gnyan phul chung ba'i bde mchog nyung ngu'i 'grel
pa mu tig phreng ba/ dge slong phul chung ba bsod nams rdo rjes puNya badzra gyi/ mdzad pa'i lU hi pa'i 'bru 'bum/ lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bir bstod a la la
ste ma/ zhang ston la bstod pa yon tan mchog mnga' ma/ rgyud sde spyi rnam chung ngu / brtag gnyis bsdus don/ brtag gnyis dka' 'grel/ man ngag don gsal/ gur gyi tho yig
yang gur gyi bshad pa'i chings/ rdo rje'i glu'i rnam bshad/ rtsa'i mngon rtogs rnam bshad/ rdo rje snying 'grel gyi snga 'gyur yig sna/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi bsdus
don/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi don 'grel tshigs bcad ma/ rdo rje gur gyi zin bris/ sambu Ti'i dka' 'grel/ yang dag sbyor ba'i rgyud
phyi ma'i rnam bshad/ yang dag sbyor ba'i rgyud phyi ma gsal bar bshad pa/ sambu Ti'i dbang gi don bsdus sam/ mtshan gzhan sambu Ti'i rdo rje'i dbyings kyi dkyil chog
ces pa'ang snang / kyai rdo rje'i gdan gyi rnam gzhag slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam bshad rin chen myu gu/ bde mchog rtsa
rgyud nyung ngu'i le 'grel tshigs bcad ma/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud nyung ngu'i don bsdus/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi zin bris/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' gnas kyi zin bris
dpe sna drug nag 'bum du grags pa la/ nag po pa'i lo rgyus/ nag po gzhung drug gi

don bsdus sam/ bsdus don du'ang grags/ nag po dkyil chog gi bsdus don nam/ sa bcad/ nag po chen po sgrub thabs kyi don bsdus/ nag po dkyil chog ras bris la brten pa/ rdo rje
slob dpon gyi dbang bskur tshul gsal byed dang bcas pa/ nag po sgrub thabs sam/ mngon rtogs rnam bshad/ TIka chung ste mtshan gsum ldan/ nag po sbyin sreg gi rnam bshad/
nag po sbyin sreg lag len/ nag po sbyin sreg dang 'brel ba'i ro sreg gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi rnam bshad/ gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi 'grel pa/ TIkka'ang zer/ gsang
ba'i de kho na nyid kyi don/ bla ma'i gsung dang gzhung na gnang ba gsal bar bshad pa/ o la pa ti'i rnam bshad/ o la pa ti'i man ngag chung ngu / o la pa ti'i man ngag
gam don bsdus/ o la pa ti'i dang dpyid thig gi sngags rim gyi man ngag dpyid thig gi rnam 'grel/ nag po rim bzhi lam slong / de'i lag len/ yang de'i lag len zhes pa rim
lnga'ang ston pa nyung ngu / 'jam dbyangs la bstod pa/ mi g.yo ba la bstod pa/ sgrol ma la bstod pa/ skyu ra a skyabs la zhu yig 'jigs byed rtog bdun gyi rnam bshad/ sgrol
ma lha bcu bdun gyi dkyil chog dpal sa skya pa'i man ngag gces bsdus rin chen phreng ba/ khro bcu'i srung 'khor man ngag bha ya na'i srung 'khor man ngag bum gter gzhug

zer/ dpal dur khrod bdag po'i sgrub thabs/ las tshogs dang bcas pa rnams so/ ! /slob dpon rin po che'i bka' 'bum gyi chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar rje sa chen la bstod
pa tshangs dbang ma/ lam 'bras brgyud pa dang / khyad par sa chen la bstod pa gcig slob dpon cha pa chos kyi seng ge la bstod pa/ rgya sgom tshul khrims grags pa la springs
pa/ rgyud sde spyi rnam chen mo/mchan ma/ brtag gnyis kyi bsdus don bshad sbyar nyi 'od snang ba/ brtag gnyis kyi rnam bshad chen mo/TIka chen yang zer/ yang de nyid mjug
tu dpal kyai rdo rje'i bshad sbyar nyi 'od snang ba zhes pa'ang bzhugs/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi 'grel pa/ chos la 'jug pa'i sgo/ sambu Ti'i bsdus don/ sambu Ti'i
'grel pa gnad kyi gsal byed/ sambu Ti'i brtag pa gnyis pa'i 'grel pa/rab byed rkyang pa ka yin/ 'di la kha sbyor thig le'i bshad sbyar ram TIkka'ang zer/ byis pa bde 'jug
rje btsun gyis mchan gnang ba sna ro'i phyag bris las 'phel ba'i khungs btsun/ kyai rdo rje'i dkyil chog gi nas gling ma/'di bde mchog dang cha mthun/ kyai rdo rje'i las
dang po pa'i bya ba/ kyai rdo rje'i Dombhi lugs kyi dkyil chog kyai rdo rje mngon rtogs rgyas pa yan lag bzhi pa/ kyai rdo rje'i dbang gi chu bo chen mo/ kyai rdo rje'i
rab gnas bzang po drug kyai rdo rje zhi ba'i sbyin sreg'di na me bkra brtag pa gsal/ kyai rdo rje'i las bzhi'i sbyin sregmchan sna ro'i mchan las 'phel ba/ bdag med ma'i
dbang gi tho yig'di khams pa dge bshes sbas don seng ge rgyal mtshan la springs yig kyang zer/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i mngon rtogs/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i dbang gi

bya ba'i TIkka/ dpal bde mchog gi mchod pa'i cho ga gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rtogs pa'i TIkka bsdus don dang bcas pa/ rje btsun seng ge sgra'i gdon sgrol gyi cho ga don zhags
lo rgyus/dge bsnyen zhi ba'i go chas/ don zhags rgyud kyi sa bcad/ don zhags rgyud kyi TIkka rin chen phreng ba/'di nang ri dwags e nya ye dang kr-iShNa sa ra gcig par
gsungs/ don zhags lha lnga'i bstod pa/ rdo rje gdan pa'i chos drug 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs sbyin sreg las tshogs dang bcas pa/ mi g.yo ba'i 'khor lo

! /rje btsun rin po che'i bka' 'bum gyi chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rgyas pa bla ma rdor 'dzin mara grags pa/ lam 'bras brgyud 'debs
chung ngu / slob dpon rin po che sku gshegs dus smre bsngags su bstod pa/ yang slob dpon rin po che la bstod pa khyod nyid dam pa ma/ tshangs spyod ma/ rje sa chen gyi
rnam thar gsan yig mara grags pa/ bla ma bsten pa'i thabs lnga bcu pa'i gsal byed/bla ma lnga bcu pa'i TIkka'ang zer/ tshar gsum khug pa/ bras ston zhus lan/ 'grel pa
dag ldan/ rgyud gsum gyi mngon par rtogs pa rin po che'i ljon shing / stong thun sa bcad tshul bzhi'i bsdus don/ rgyud sde'i dum bu/ 'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi
bsdus don/ 'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur

gyi rnam 'grel gur rgyan/rnam bshad gur rgyan nam TIkka gur rgyan yang zer/ gur rigs bsdus kyi thig chog rab tu gsal ba/ gur la brten pa'i dus tha ma'i cho ga gzhan phan bdud
rtsi/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ he ru ka'i byung tshul/ he ru ka'i chas drug dpal lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs/don 'grel yang zer/ nag po dkyil chog
gi sa bcad 'khrugs can 'khrugs med/ sgrub thabs/ sbyin sreg de kho na nyid gsal ba/ o la pa ti rnams la sa bcad re re/ slob dpon nag po pa'i lo rgyus gzhung drug spyi chings
dang bcas pa/ nag po dkyil chog rdo rje dril bu pa'i lo rgyus/ dril bu pa'i mngon rtogs don 'grel/ dril bu rim lnga'i TIkka /tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ phag mo zhal gnyis
ma'i sgrub thabs/ sngags kyi de kho na nyid gsal ba/byin rlabs kyang zer/ phag mo las bcu/ste mi dbang chos gsum/ mai tri mkha' spyod ma'i rgyud chung / rig byed ma rtse
ma'i sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang ngam/ byin rlabs bya tshul gyi cho ga nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub thabs dang byin rlabs sogs dpe sna bdun/ lam gyi yan lag pra sen dbab
pa/ gnod sbyin mo dgug pa/ sman chen po'i bcud len/ padma pa ti'i sgrub thabs/ khol mo pa ti'i sgrub thabs te dpe sna lnga/ rtsa dbu ma'i man ngag bshad thabs kyi man ngag
kun tu spyod pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus don/gsal byed TIkka yang zer/ nges brjod bla ma'i 'phrul 'khor bri thabs/'di la bris bsgom gyi man ngag kyang zer/ rin chen 'bar ba'i
bsdus don/sa bcad/ rje btsun grags pa'i rnam thar mnal lam ma sna ros bris pa/ gsang sngags nang

gi lhung bzed brtag pa sna ros bris pa/ dga' ston rdo rje grags la springs yig ga ri rgyal po la brtsis bsdur gnang ba'i yi ge rdo rje dril bu bgrang phreng gi de kho na nyid
kyi man ngag rgyud 'bum gyi dkar chag bla ma gong ma rnams kyi brgyud pa'i dkar chag kyai rdo rje'i chos skor gyi dkar chag dang / mal lo dang ba ri ba'i chos skor gyi
dkar chag gshin rje dgra nag gi mngon rtogs/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bstod pa/ yang 'jigs byed kyi bstod pa/ bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa/ sgrol
ma nyin zhi mtshan khro'i sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i man ngag las kha tshar dang bcas pa/ sgrol ma spyi'i sgrub thabs/ lus dkyil dang maNDal/ 'chim chos rje
la springs pa/ so so'i mngon rtogs/ bstod pa 'don thabs kyi brjed byang / sgrol ma nyi shu rtsa gcig gi mngon rtogs yan lag dang bcas pa nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa'i gsal
byed/ sgrol ma lus dkyil gyi sgrub thabs/ 'chim chos seng la springs pa/ de'i bsdus don/ sa bcad/ sgrol ma'i rnam bshad gsal ba'i 'od zer/mchan dkyus su bcug pa/ gnyan
lugs kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa/ sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ gsol 'debs/ sgrol ma ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag dmar po'i sgrub thabs/
brgyud pa gnyis kyi lugs su byas pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed/ kyai rdo rje'i mngon rtogs 'bring po yan lag drug pa/ yab kyi bstod pa DaNDa ka mchan ma/ yum gyi
bstod pa rin po che'i phreng ba dri ma

med pa/ kyai rdo rje'i bkra shis/ kye rdor dpa' gcig gi mngon rtogs ba ri lugs/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i sgrub thabs/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams par bskur ba'i bdag
med ma'i dbang gi tho yig kyai rdo rje'i tshogs 'khor 'bring po/ kyai rdo rje'i las bzhi'i sbyin sreg rtsa ba dang yan lag gi ltung ba'i rnam bshad 'khrul spong chen mo/
ngan song sbyong rgyud kyi spyi don/gzhan phan spyi chings/ gzhan phan 'od zer/ gzhan phan nyer mkho/ sbyong rgyud kyi bsdus don/sa bcad kyang zer/ arga'i cho ga rab gnas
don gsal/ rigs gsum rigs gtad/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo grub pa'i rgyud kyi TIkka/ rgya gar rgyal po'i rgyal rabs/ bod kyi rgyal po'i rgyal rabs/ 'khon gyi gdung rabs/ sde pa'i
gyes mdo/ mi g.yo ba'i bstod pa rigs gsum 'thad ldan/ 'jam dpal la bstod pa rgyud gsum 'khor lo/ rdo rje phur pa'i tho yig kha 'bar ma'i rgyud kyi dgongs pa don lnga pa/
gtor ma brgya rtsa/ dus tshod nges par bzung ba'i yi ge gza' skar 'phrod mi 'phrod kyi yi ge phyag rgya chen po gces bsdus/ phyag yig dgu 'phrul/ las dang po'i bya ba
rin chen phreng ba/ rdo rje 'byung ba'i dkyil chog gi lo rgyus dang TIkka/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan brjod 'don thabs/ don
yod zhags pa'i cho ga lag tu blangs pa'i rim pa/ maNDal bya tshul yang zer/ thabs/ srung 'khor bya thabs/ srung 'khor bri thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs ye shes snang
ba'i sgron ma/ rnam 'joms rgyud kyi gsal byed 'od zer

can dang / de'i bsdus don/ lag na rdo rje'i gzungs kyi lag tu blangs pa'i rim pa/bstod pa rgya gar ma dang bcas pa/ mi g.yo gsang chen gyi rnam 'grel/ 'di la mi g.yo ba'i gsung
rgyud le'u bzhi pa'i man ngag kyang zer/ dpung bzang mdo 'grel/ sdom pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa'i TIkka/ spyod 'jug gi bsdus don/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i TIkka lo rgyus
spyi'i rnam gzhag bsdus don dang bcas pa/ ye shes rdo rje la gnang ba'i mgur/ zhen pa bzhi bral gyi nyams dbyangs/ ye shes rdo rjes snyan gsol ba'i lan gyi mgur/ chog
pa drug gi mgur/ gnas bskor ba la gdams pa/gnas bstod kyang zer/ rmi lam nyams len brgyad kyi mgur/ phyag rgya chen po ngang drug gi mgur/ 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs kyi mgur/
'tshal ba brgyad kyi mgur/ 'tshal pa bcu'i mgur/ rang la rang gis bskul ma'i mgur/ nyams dbyangs chen mo/ gso spyad bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/thor spyad rgyal po'i dkor mdzod
ces pa yang snang / 'di rnams kyang mchan yod mchan bcas legs par thos so/ /'di rnams kyi lung dang glegs bam phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa dang po nas med kyang / dus phyis
bla ma dam pa dpal ldan seng ge'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i phyir du 'gro ba'i mgon po bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bkas bskul te mkhan po shes rab rdo rjes lung
su yod la zhus shing / des mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal
tshab kun dga'

dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ bstan pa'i gsal byed sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga'
rin chen/ grub pa'i gtsug rgyan padma'i rnam 'phrul bsod nams dbang po/ mkhan chen chos kyi rje ratna dhwa dza/ dpal sa skya pa chen mo grub chen mthu stobs dbang phyug des

phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ bstan pa'i gsal byed sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin
chen/ grub pa'i gtsug rgyan padma'i rnam 'phrul bsod nams dbang po/ mkhan chen chos kyi rje ratna dhwa dza/ dpal sa skya pa chen po grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug des
bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /chos rje khu dbon gnyis ka'i bka' 'bum gyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/
dga' ldan pa

kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma don yod pa man 'dra'o/ ! /yang grub mchog dam pa de nyid kyi drung du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i skye rabs sum cu rtsa bzhi pa slob dpon
dpa' bos mdzad pa madznyu shrIs bsgyur pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs/ klu sgrub/ sangs rgyas bskyangs/ legs ldan 'byed/ zla ba grags pa/ rig
pa'i khu byug gzhon nu 'bum/ dha pu ri dza ya a nanda/ khu lo tsA ba/ legs ldan byed/ gtsang nag pa/ gshin chu skor ba/ gtsang po jo nag 'od zer mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs
shAka gzhon/ rang byung rdo rje/ bla ma g.yung ston pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ lho pa rin po che grags pa yon tan/ chos rje grags pa 'byung gnas/ mi pham gnyis pa tshul khrims
dar/ rin po che bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ byams pa kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa chen po
grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /'phags pa rdo rje gcod pa'i mdo dang / yon tan rin po che sdud pa tshigs su
bcad pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa/ byams pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ 'phags grol/ btsun grol/ rnam snang mdzad/ seng bzang / ye shes zhabs/ dpal sbas/ shinti
pa/ wa la tsaNDa/ 'bum phrag gsum pa/ rngog lo/ 'dre shes 'bar/ ar byang ye/ 'dul dkar/ 'dre shes rab

grags/ dbyar nyi dpal/ 'chim nam mkha' grags pa/ jo sras/ gro ston chos rgyal/ rgyal rin/ ngag dbang grags/ yon bzang / sangs rgyas bzang po/ stag ston shes rgyal/ byang bzang
/ bsod blo/ rgya ston tsandra de wa/ ri khrod bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ slob dpon don shes/ rje lha mchog seng ge thar rtse nas sangs rgyas
ye shes/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug des bdag sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i gsung rab ma Ni bka' 'bum du grags pa'i stod cha smad cha'i chos tshan yongs rdzogs po ti
spar ma'i nang bzhin lung nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khri srong lde btsan/ grub thob dngos grub/ mnga' bdag nyang ral/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ shAkya bzang po/ lha rje dge ba 'bum/
lcam ye shes mchog chu sgom pa mtha' bzhi bya bral ba/ tshul chen bsod nams seng ba/ bla ma bkra shis rgyal/ chu rag pa blo rgyam/ 'phags mchog nor bu bzang po/ chos
rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dpal ldan sangs rgyas/ stas dga' ba ngag dbang grags pa/ yig drug pa shes rab dpal 'byor/ rje kun dga' grol mchog bla ma chos skyong
rgyal po/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' rdo rje/ rje rnam rgyal dpal bzang / bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ spyan snga kun dga' don 'grub/ dpal sa skya pa chen po grub mchog mthu stobs
dbang

phyug des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na 'phags mchog nor bu bzang po la hor ka bzhi pa/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan legs pa/ ka
bcu pa/ byang chub dpal/ 'phags pa blo gros rin chen/ yig drug pa man 'dra/ ! /yang grub mchog dam pa de nyid kyi drung du/ rje mkhyen brtse ba'i rnam thar rang nyid kyis
mdzad pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun mkhas pa chen po mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin po che ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan
snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa grub mchog mthu stobs dbang phyug des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'dir smras pa/ yo dznyA kri pA maNDa la
krisatra bilbo bi/gang gi mkhyen brtse dri med dkyil 'khor la/ /pashya dharmA bi pa shyaM bi ma la sphu Ta sya/mtha' yas chos kyi gzugs brnyan gsal bar snang / /bandhu
pra dzA naM sa ha de ba me kalhar bcas 'gro ba'i rtsa lag gcig pu ba/ /shAkya sya de sho dha ra te dza ya ghaH shAkya'i bstan 'dzin mchog khyod rgyal gyur cig /sa 'dzin dkar
po'i ngos kyi skya ba'i 'od/ /gangs ri'i spo la nyi zer 'phro ba ltar/ /che cher gsal las ngo mtshar yul gyi mtshan/ /kun tu grags 'di'i bstan pa yar 'phel shog /'jam
dpal 'jam dbyangs 'jam pa'i rdo rje nyid/ /gzugs gzhan zlos pa'i skyes chen sku mched kyi/ /rigs kyi cod paN gong mar bcas pa yi/ /bstan 'di srid mthar bdag gis 'dzin gyur
cig /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul

legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ dpal sa skya pa rigs ldan 'jam pa'i dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug sku mched kyis rjes su bzung ba'i
skabs te bcu pa'o// // ! mkhan chen a pad rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//PART XI: Teachings from sPyan snga Kun dga' don grub; vol. nga, text
no. 1, pp. 1-142

/ /chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las sprul pa'i sku
spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan gyis rjes su bzung ba'i tshul gyi sarga bzhugs//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI sampatsa ra kAntA ra a gra te ratna nirmma Na kA ya A nanda nA nanda nA mi ka dharmA swa mi tsa ra Na yaM bande/ bod skad du/ dpal lo dgon pa'i spyan
snga rin po che'i sprul sku kun dga'i mtshan can chos rje'i zhabs la 'dud do/ /chos tshul mi 'dra'i chu phran bye ba brgya/ /gang thugs zab yangs rgya mtshor kun 'khyil
ba'i/ /rigs med chos kyi sbyin bdag che ba po/ /'gro kun dga' mdzad don kun grub des skyongs/ /zhes pa'i bstod yul dam par gyur pa sprul pa'i sku spyan snga rin po che chos
kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub kyi drung du dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin nos pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar/ ! /tshe sbyin dpal mo sgrol dkar spyan bdun ma'i thun mong dang
thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ de'i lha khrid rgyas pa rje ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i yig

cha'i steng nas myong khrid du stsal te/ de dang 'brel ba'i yig cha'i lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar lo rgyus/ sgrol dkar gyi rgya gzhung ngag
dbang grags pas mdzad pa/ 'di'i mtshan ma brtag lugs/ sgrub thabs che chung gsum/ paN chen lugs kyi sgrub thabs bum chog che chung rjes gnang gi yi ge rgyas bsdus tshan pa
gsum/ sbyin sreg byed lugs/ zung 'jug gi khrid kyi yi ge rnying pa rgyas bsdus/ 'di'i maNDal gyi cho ga sdig pa zad par byed pa'i cho ga rab gnas kyi cho ga rgyas bsdus/
bsnyen sgrub kyi yig chung / dbang bsdud kyi yig sna/ ngag gi byad bsrung 'grol/ nad gso ba'i cho ga bar chad zhi byed ltas ngan g.yang du len pa'i man ngag sa tsha'i rnal
'byor/ skor ba byed thabs/ 'jigs pa brgyad kyi srung thabs/ mtshon

srung / g.yul las rgyal byed/ lam srung / ce spyang gi srung ba/ jag 'ching / rang la sdang ba 'chings byed/ sgrol ma'i bris sku dang lugs sku bya ba'i thabs/ de'i rab gnas
rgyas bsdus/ yang lam srung che chung / rten 'brel mngon sum du 'char ba'i man ngag srung ba bri sgom gyi man ngag char che ba srung thabs/ gdon gyi cho 'phrul sel thabs/
lha mo'i pra 'bebs/ shes rab blo 'phel/ sgrol ma'i 'pho ba che chung rnams snga rabs kyi yig cha kha 'thor gtsang pa blo bzang pas phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i lung rnams
rdzogs par thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ 'brom ston/ spyan snga ba/ sle nag pa/ dge bshes sgre pa/ sgam
po pa/ bsgom tshul ston pa/ shes rab byang chub/ rje mdo 'dzin pa/ 'bri khung gling

pa/ dam chos gling pa/ chos kyi tshul khrims/ mnyam med lha lung pa/ grub chen thog gnas pa/ chos kyi dbang phyug byang chub bzang po/ rong ston gyi gdan sa pa dwags po bkra
shis rnam rgyal/ spyan snga bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ bla ma bsod nams legs mchog paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa/ rje
dpal ldan chos 'byor/ rgyal ba'i sras po spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun

dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang dwags po bkras rnam pa yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de'i rjes su chos rje karma 'phrin las/ rje tshar chen/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje bsod nams chos
'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rgyal ba'i sras po kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang 'di'i brgyud pa lugs gcig
ni/ rje btsun ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ gnam kha 'ub pa/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal
po sogs nas rim par brgyud pa dang / yang brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ thub dbang / rje btsun sgrol ma/ slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla
ma sle nag pa man gong du bshad pa dang 'dra/ yang brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ lha brag pa byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/
ka bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ grub
mchog bsod nams dbang po/ rgyal ba'i sras po spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /tshe dbang nye brgyud 'chi med dpal
ster du grags pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ snang ba mtha' yas/ tshe dpag med/ rta mgrin/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rje kun dga' grol mchog
bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ rgyal ba'i

sras po spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ 'jam
dbyangs/ klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ zla ba grags pa/ slob pa'i rdo rje/ slob dpon dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / paNDi ta pu Nya shrI/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa
skya pa/ rje btsun sku mched/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ e pa 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ byang sems rin chen mgon/ chos rje rgyal sras pa/ chos rje tshul khrims dpal ba/ sems dpa'
chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog ri pa dpal ldan grags pa/ mkhan chen grags pa rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen grags pa/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ mkhan chen dbang phyug
dpal bzang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa rin po che/ sgro mon can pa rin chen dpal bzang / byang sems rin chen mgon po man 'dra/ yang na sa paN/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu
bsod nams seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ rgyal sras rin po che man 'dra/ ! /tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po zhi ba/ dze ta ri/ gho dhi bha dra/ sa ma ti bho Ta/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ 'chims brtson 'grus seng ge rgya zhang
phug

pa/ byams pa shes rab rin chen/ 'khon ston 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang sems rgyal ye/ bla ma grags dpal/ snur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang brtse ba rin chen
seng ge bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rje/ bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling pa bkra
shis rgyal mtshan/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /'di'i yig cha'i lung yang thob/ ! /spyod pa'i rgyud kyi phyogs su gtogs pa rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ ye shes snying po/ ye shes zhi ba/ sangs rgyas gsang ba/ ku su la che ba/ chung ba/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ go mi sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ snyags
ldem bu ba/ spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bya rin chen 'od/ blo chen/yul glo bo pa mtshan dngos sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa/ bla ma seng ge rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI dznyA na/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun dbang pa/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/
'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ chos kyi spyan ldan
spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa

ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla
ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA wa li ta/ pra dznyA bo dhi/ mu ti ta ko shwa/ dharmA pA la/ dhi paM ka ra/ shrI dznyA na/ go mi spyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal
pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ sras badzra sidhi/ snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ snur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ snur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/
bla ma 'phags pa 'od/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston/ slob dpon rgyal mtshan grags/ bla ma dam pa bkra shis rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rje kun dga' chos grags/ bla ma dam pa
nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs zhal bcu gcig pa
lha so bdun gyi bdag nyid can klu sgrub lugs kyi dbang rigs gtad dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug 'phags pa klu sgrub/ arYa de
wa/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug a wa dhu ti pa/ ku sa li che ba/ ku sa li chung ba/ dpal mar me mdzad ye shes/ 'brom ston pa/ spyan snga rnal 'byor dbang phyug tshul
khrims

'bar/ bya yul ba chen po gzhon nu 'od/ mus smad pa/ phyar chen po/ dpal ldan gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ rgya ston shes rab 'od zer/ dmar ston bsod nams 'phel/ slob dpon grags
'bum/ rong smon ri ba mkhan chen sangs rgyas rin chen pa/ rin chen grags tshul ba/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od zer ba/ dus zhabs pa chen po don grub kun dga'/ bsod nams lha'i
dbang po/ rje btsun ngag dbang chos grags/ bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ rje btsun spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
/yang na dpal ldan blo gros nas/ sangs rgyas bsgom pa/ 'chims nam mkha' grags/ mkhas btsun bsod nams ye shes/ byang sems bsod grags pa/ rin po che grags tshul ba/ kun mkhyen
nam 'od pa/ des chos rje don grub kun dga'/ yang ku sa li yan chad 'dra ba la/ jo bo chen po a ti sha yol chos dbang / dge bshes sgre pa/ rje lung pa/ shar gling pa/
pho ba lung pa/ snye mdo ba thams cad mkhyen pa/ snye mo ba kun dga' don grub/ ra ba grags pa shAkya seng ge mkhan chen grags tshul ba/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od zer/ chos
rje dus zhabs pa don grub kun dga'/ bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ rje btsun ngag dbang chos grags/ bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don
grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang sa skya pa'i yab chos rdo rje phur pa'i smad las drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang rnam par

dag pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon ston klu'i dbang po bsrung ba/ rdo rje rin chen/ shes
rab yon tan/ tshul khrims rgyal po/ rdo rje gtsug tor/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / bal po/ shAkya blo gros/ shes rab tshul khrims/ dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa skya pa chen po/
slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun
bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan po shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan po thugs rje shes rab/ sngags 'chang dharmA kirti/ 'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po/ rgya dkar shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/
spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na chos rgyal 'phags pa yan gong bzhin las de nas/ lo mchog bag ston/ bla ma
tshul rgyal/ bla ma de pa/ dpal tshul ba/ ngor chen kun bzang / paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo man 'dra/ ! /mnga' bdag nyang ral lugs kyi gu ru drag
dmar gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku padma

'byung gnas/ mnga' bdag nyang ral pa/ mnga' bdag ras chung ba/ bla ma bzung ston rin chen/ gu ru dharmA ratna/ rtogs ldan chos nyid rang grol/ drin can sangs rgyas lhun dbang
/ sprul sku kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub rgyal sras chos rje/ bla ma dam pa legs pa dpal bzang / rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga'
bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rje btsun sngags 'chang chen po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga'
bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan ngag dbang kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal po'i rjes su/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ jo gdan mkhan chen shes rab rin chen/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan man 'dra/ ! /'jigs byed rwa lugs ro langs brgyad
skor gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ma/ la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ padma badzra/ di paM
ka ra/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / klog kya dbang grags/ ldong ston shes dpal/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/
na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ byang chub dpal bzang / shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal

mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje lha mchog rje buddha singha/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don
grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na lha mchog seng ge nas/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal/ shar chen/ spyan snga rin po che man
'dra/ yang na lha mchog seng ge buddha singha/ shar chen/ spyan snga rin po che chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ ! /zhe sdang gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed/ ye shes kyi mkha'
'gro ma/ birWa pa/sau ma pu ri/ Dombhi he ru kaha Da kaM ka bi ra Di ba/de bi ko dri/ ma ti garbha/blo bzang snying po/ gambhi ra ma ti/dza gad hi ma/ niska langka de
ba/paN gos dkar/ ra wentra/hi ma ya/ chag lo tsA/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal/ gshong lo tsA ba blo ldan/ bla ma lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug bya sder
ba byang chub rin chen/ rwa ga brag pa shAkya seng ge chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa'
chen po/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug rje dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ spyan snga
chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ yang

na/ sems dpa' chen po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang sgrol ma bla med lha bcu bdun gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun
sgrol ma/ nyi ma sbas pa/ tsandra garbha/ dze ta ri/ ngag dbang grags pa/ shaddha ka ra warma/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ dA na shrI/ manydzu shrI/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros
grags pa/ rje sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ ne tshe sbal ston/ rnal 'byor mngon pa ba/ slob dpon dar ma shes rab/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng
ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / chos rje dpal ldan don
grub/ rje ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /'khor lo bde mchog
dril bu pa brgyud pa bka' bab gnyis dang ldan pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bar 'dzin/
karNa pa/ gu nya pa/ ti

lo pa/ na ro pa/ phaM mthing pa/ klog kya shes rab brtsegs/ mal gyo/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paN/ bo dong rin po che/ khro phu ba/
yang brtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje btsun sangs rgyas seng ge yongs 'dzin nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje kun dga' bkris/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ gu ge paN chen/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ buddha singha/ rje nam
mkha' dpal bzang / rje kun dga' bkra shis/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan/ kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na bo dong
rin po che'i gnas su 'gro mgon 'phags pa'am/ tshogs bsgom rin chen gang rung ngo / kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dril bu pa/ dga' ba'i
rdo rje/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ a bhya ka ra gupta/ de wa purNa/ kha che paN chen/ spyi bo lhas pa seng ge dpal/ zhang 'dre lung pa/ rin po che khro phu ba/ yang rtse
ba/ bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na dril bu pa/ de wa purNa/ kha che

paN chen man 'dra'o/ ! /bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ dpa' bo spyan
ras gzigs/ byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rin chen/ grub chen sha ba ri dbang phyug slob dpon mai tri gupta/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje/ 'grel byed ka ma la badzra/ paNDi
ta dza ya se na/ lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ rgyal tshab chos kyi dbang phyug
lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang / bla ma byang seng / rje btsun dam pa/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po/ gung ru sher bzang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ mus chen
nam mkha' dbang phyug rje stong ra ba kun dga' legs grub/ rje kun dga' chos grags/ bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rtog pa las gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sgrol ma/ kha che
paN chen/ dA na shi la/ sa paN/ 'u yug pa kun bsod/ nyi thog pa kun smon/ yon tan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ brag phug pa/ blo gros brtan pa/
dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ye shes rgyal

mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ gnyan lo/ sangs rgyas seng ge mus chen nam
mkha' dpal bzang / grub mchog rdo rje'i mtshan can/ bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ ! /padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku padma dbang chen/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/
grub thob zla char/ chos rgyal brtson 'grus rdo rje/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ mkhan chen chos rgyal dpal bzang / kun mkhyen dpal ldan seng ge chos rje rin chen
bkra shis/ rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mus chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ sngags 'chang ratna bha dra/ tshar chen blo
gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ mi pham chos rgya mtsho/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gu ru thugs sgrub kyi byin rlabs thugs rje'i dbang lnga thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po he ru ka longs sku rgyal ba rigs
lnga/ sprul sku phyag na rdo rje/ smug nag dbang gi mkha' 'gro tshangs pa'i rgyal po gdong bzhi/ lha dbang brgya byin/ klu rgyal 'jog po/ rgyal po dza/ shAkya pra bha/ o
rgyan rin po che/ bi ma la/ shrI la

manydzu/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ sna snam rdo rje bdud 'joms/ gter ston rig 'dzin chen po rgod ldem/ sras mchog rnam rgyal mgon po/ sngags 'chang rdo rje rnam gnyis/
mtshan ldan ngag dbang grags pa/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / chos rgyal bsod nams/ grub mchog chos skyong bsod nams/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
rtsa ba'i bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gu ru zhi ba zhes
grags pa bla ma gsang 'dus chos dbang lugs kyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs dang / las byang le brgyad ma'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku
thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug rgyal sras padma dbang chen/ drin can sangs rgyas kun grol/ rtogs
ldan dharma'i mtshan can/ sprul sku lha dbang grags ldan/ so ston grags pa seng ge so ston 'dus pa rtsal/ so ston 'jam dbyangs rab 'phel/ so ston kun dga' gzhon nu/ drin
can kun dga' legs ldan tshul khrims/ rje rnam rgyal dpal bzang / bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gur drag nyang lugs kyi gtor ma la brten pa'i dbang bzhi thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku drag po dmar
chen/ sprul sku padma 'byung

gnas/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ mnga' bdag chen po nyang nyi ma 'od zer/ sras nam mkha' dpal/ gzu ston dharmA ratna/ gzu rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rtogs ldan chos nyid rang
grol/ sangs rgyas lhun grub dbang / sprul sku kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub rgyal mtshan chos rje/ brgyud 'dzin legs pa dpal bzang / sprul sku nyang ston chos dbang
/ snub chen rin chen dpal bzang / rje btsun 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan/ padma dbang rgyal rdo rje/ legs ldan bdud 'joms rdo rje/ mthu ldan dbang po'i rdo rje/ rig 'dzin ngag
gi dbang po/ rig 'dzin yul mo ba stobs ldan shul 'gro brtsegs/ bla ma bsod nams rgya mtsho/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ mkha'
'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ nyang nyi ma 'od zer/ sras nam mkha' dpal/ 'di nas bla ma kha cig ma rnyed/ gu ru thugs mchog rdo rje/ gshong chen mkhas btsun bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan/ rig 'dzin bstan pa rnam rgyal/ bla ma bsod nams rgya mtsho/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
! /thugs rje chen po 'gro 'dul gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas/ thugs rje chen po/ srong btsan sgam po/ padma 'byung gnas/ khri

srong lde'u btsan/ grub thob dngos grub/ mnga' bdag nyang ral/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ shAkya bzang po/ lha rje dge ba 'bum/ lcam ye shes mchog chu sgom pa/ mtha' bzhi bya bral
ba/ tshul chen bsod seng / bla ma bkra shis rgyal/ chu rags pa blo rgyam/ 'phags mchog nor bu bzang po/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dpal ldan sangs rgyas/
stas sga ba ngag dbang grags pa/ yig drug pa shes rab dpal 'byor/ rje kun dga' grol mchog bla ma chos skyong rgyal po/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' rdo rje/ rje rnam rgyal dpal bzang
/ bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na 'phags mchog nor
bu bzang po la/ hor ka bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan legs pa/ ka bcu pa/ byang chub dpal/ 'phags pa blo gros rin chen/ yig drug pa man 'dra'o/ ! /gsung
ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i lam gyi snying po rgyu dbang lam du byed pa slob dpon gyis zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo
nas/ thog mar snang ba gsum gyi khrid dang / de nas lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med/ phyi nang gi bskyed rim/ rmi lam 'pho ba bar do sogs zhar byung gi man ngag yongs rdzogs/
dbang gong ma gsum dang bcas pa'i khrid yig rje tshar pa'i gsung la thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtshos zin bris mdzad pa'i yig cha so so'i lung khrid rgyas par
nos nas/ gsung ngag slob bshad

kyi brgyud pa thog mar smras te/ brgyud lugs gzhan rnams rnam grangs kyi tshul du brjod pa ni/ 'og min chen por zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang / /mkha' khyab mkha' yi rdo rje bdag
med ma/ /sau ma pu rir 'khrungs pa'i bi ru pa/ /rgya gar shar phyogs su 'khrungs kA hA pa/ /ma ga dhar 'khrungs DA ma ru pa'i zhabs/ /wa ra NA sir 'khrungs pa'i gnyis spangs
pa/ /'phags yul shar phyogs su 'khrungs ratna shrI/ /bod yul mang mkhar du 'khrungs 'brog mi rje/ /mdog smad phyi 'brum du 'khrungs rje btsun se/ /gtsang gi sag thang
gnas 'khrungs dgon pa ba/ /grom stod kha 'ur 'khrungs pa'i brtse ba che/ /gzims spyil dkar por 'khrungs pa'i bsod nams rtse/ /sgo rum mgon khang mdor 'khrungs grags pa'i
zhabs/ /sgo rum tshogs khang phur 'khrungs paNDi ta/ /stag sde rlung khung du 'khrungs 'phags pa'i mtshan/ngam ring mtsho'i khris na yod/ /ra sa mtshal khung 'khrungs
pa'i dkon mchog dpal/ /de nyid du 'khrungs rgyal ba brag phug pa/ /zha lu khang gsar du 'khrungs 'gro mgon rje/ /'bras khud sgang skyar 'khrungs pa'i dpal ldan pa/ /mdog
gi sgo phur 'khrungs pa'i buddha shrI/ dbu se/ /sa skya'i byi khung sgor 'khrungs kun dga'i mtshan/ /mus stod gling skyar 'khrungs pa'i sems dpa' che/ /lcam mo g.yang grong
du 'khrungs bdag chen rje/ /rdo ring smon mkhar gnas 'khrungs kun spangs pa/ /dmu gshong dga' ba'i tshal 'khrungs tshar chen rje/ /zang zang byang rgyud du 'khrungs klu
sgrub mtshan/ /bar sbug sems 'byor gnas 'khrungs mkhan chen

rje/ /mal gro be'u snar 'khrungs spyan snga ba/ /sa skya'i phun tshogs gling lha chen/ skyes bdag a nanda/ la 'o/ /de ni lam 'bras slob bshad kyi bla ma brgyud pa thun mong
ma yin pa yin la/ brgyud lugs gzhan rnams rnam grangs kyi tshul du brjod pa ni/ yang na chos rje sa paN nas/ gtsang gi sgyer phur 'khrungs pa'i tshogs sgom pa/dbu se/ mdog
stod rje grong du 'khrungs bsod nams brtan/dbu se/ /thang pa ru bzhir 'khrungs pa ratna'i mtshan/dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge /dpal ldan pa man gong dang 'dra/ yang
na nyan chen pa nas/ ra sa mtshal khung 'khrungs pa'i brag phug pa/ /kha snga dgon gsar du 'khrungs ri khrod pa/ /dpal ldan pa man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na rje sems
dpa' chen po'i rjes su/ 'bom gyi la steng du 'khrungs kun mkhyen rje/ /mus stod gling skyar 'khrungs pa'i grub chen pa/ /sa skya'i bde ldan steng 'khrungs dkon mchog 'phel/
/mus kyi gling skyar 'khrungs pa'i sangs rin rje/ /rtse gdong gnas 'khrungs sa skya lo tsA ba/ /sa skyar 'khrungs pa'i dkon mchog lhun grub mtshan/ /rtse gdong phyogs
'khrungs sngags 'chang chos kyi rje/ /lha chen rtser 'khrungs grub mchog bsod nams dbang / /spyan snga chos rje man chad gong dang 'dra/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam
thar dang / rje rdo ring pa'i rnam thar tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ rje tshar pa'i rnam thar lam yig rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang thob/ ! /brda don gsal ba'i khrid
bdag chen blo gros pas mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ bi ru pa/ sa

chen/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas grub pa/ bla ma kun bsod/ brag phug pa man 'dra/ ! /rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi chos bzhi las lam zab bla ma'i rnal
'byor gyi byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan brda don gsal ba dang 'dra/ de nas tshogs bsgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa/ dpal ldan
tshul khrims pa man 'dra'o/ ! /bir srung gi byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ brag phug pa yan gong dang 'dra/ de nas chos rje rnam gnyis/ dpal ldan tshul
khrims pa man 'dra/ ! /lam sbas bshad kyi thugs rdo rje'i khrid bdag chen gyi yig cha'i nang bzhin dang / 'khrul 'khor/ grub chen bcu/ phra mo brgyad dang bcas pa'i brgyud
pa ni bir bsrung dang 'dra'o/ ! /de'i 'khrul 'khor so gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ nyan chen pa/ snyag snying po rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rgyal mtshan 'bum/ bla ma dam pa/ bla
ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa man 'dra'o/ ! /sbas bshad pho brang lnga 'phrul 'khor dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ nyan chen pa/ dkar brag pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims pa man
'dra/ ! /yang lam zab dang bir bsrung gi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ dpal ldan tshul khrims pa yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen/ mus chen/

ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnam 'joms/ birWa pa/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ skyo ston dri
med/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ 'gro mgon bsod rgyal/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen/ rje sangs

dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na skyo ston dar ba ye shes/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul
khrims man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na/ rje btsun/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin rgyal/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal

ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ gzhon nu grub/ zhang byang chub shes rab/ 'gro mgon bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ rje buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab kun

dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen bsod
nams lhun grub/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na 'dren mchog rje sangs rgyas rin chen/
rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ ! /yang rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan bsrung dbang po rdo rje gur gyi mgon po'i snyan brgyud kyi chos skor zab mo thob pa la/ thog
mar mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ paN grub dad byed go
cha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje
btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla
ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/ chos rje skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ grub
dbang bkra shis seng ge tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje byams pa rab brtan/ chos rje snying rje bzang po/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga'
don grub/ des bdag sa

skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /de nas phyi'i srung 'khor la brten pa'i rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i khrid kyi rim pa bsnyen pa byed tshul dang bcas pa/ de'i nang
sel gyi man ngag skor la sngags pa nang rgyas kyi man ngag don tshan gsum/ mal phur gyi gdams pa/ e ka dza ti la brten pa'i rims srung ba/ rmi ngan zlog pa'i zhal shes/
mgon po'i tshe sgrub dang bcas pa/ slar de'i rjes su nang gi brag rdzong ma drag po sngags rgod kyi gdams pa/ gsang ba'i brag rdzong ma sems nyid ye shes kyi rtsal 'don
rnam rtog bzhi dang bdud bzhi tshar bcad de tshe 'di nyid la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i thabs khyad par can rnams nyams khrid du nos nas/ de dag dang
'brel ba'i rgyab chos lung gi skor la/ mgon po me 'bar mar grags pa thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ de nyid kyi dkar chag bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/
nag po chen po'i zhal gdams/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge mal los mdzad pa/ lcam dral gyi rjes gnang 'phags pas mdzad pa/ rjes gnang bla ma dam
pas mdzad pa/ lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang yar klung pas mdzad pa/ rten gzhi'i lung 'brog mi lo tsA bas bsgyur pa'i rdo rje gur gyi rgyud nas phyung ba/ nag po chen po'i sgrub
thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs slob dpon bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa/ bram zes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs ba ri bas bsgyur pa/ gur mgon gter ma'i gzhung
/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs dreg pa zil gnon slob dpon padmas mdzad

pa/ gri gug lha lnga'i dkyil chog bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa lo chen rin bzang gis bsgyur pa/ nag po srog gi spu gri sgrub thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa blo
gros grags kyis bsgyur pa/ pho rkyang gi sgrub thabs bod yig ma sa chen gyi slob ma paNye badzra gyis mdzad pa/ mahA kA la'i man ngag tshan pa gnyis/ las mthar phyin/ mgon
po tshogs bdag ltar bsgrub pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ de'i las sbyor bram zes mdzad pa'i bsad las kyi man ngag bka' bsgo'i tshul du bsgrub pa'i lugs/ drag po'i las sbyor
gsum gyi man ngag mo rkyang gi sgrub thabs gnyan phul chung bas mdzad pa/ mo rkyang gi man ngag mkha' 'gro ma dbang du bya ba/ lha mo'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta lo ka shrIs
bsgyur pa/ lcam dral sbags sgrub kyi sgrub thabs 'phags pas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i lcam dral gyi gtor chog lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa bya thabs mal los
mdzad pa/ bka' sdod kyi yi ge bla ma mal gyi dbon po blo gros seng ges mdzad pa/ lha brgyad kyi sgrub lugs bzhi'i rnam gzhag zhib tu bstan pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ lha brgyad
mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub 'od ldan dpal gyis mdzad pa/ lha brgyad kyi sgrub thabs zla ba phyed kyis rtsal chen rdzogs pa ldan ma kun dga' dpal gyis mdzad pa/ bsad las
dang zor 'phangs kyi man ngag pu tra ming sring gi byin rlabs a gnyan dam pas mdzad pa/ yar klung pas mdzad pa'i rjes gnang rgyas bsdus gnyis zin bris su bkod pa/ pu tra'i
sgrub thabs slob dpon padmas rdo rje gdan gyi ka ba nas

bton pa/ pu tra ming sring gi sgrub thabs bsdus pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ a gnyan dam pas mdzad pa'i pu tra'i sgrub thabs rgyas pa dang / 'bring po lo rgyus dang bcas pa/ yang
pu tra'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa dam pas mdzad pa/ pu tra'i mchod gtor dpal ldan tshul khrims pas mdzad pa/ de'i bstod pa las rnams kun byed ma/ dam pas mdzad pa/ gtor ma
la brten nas dgra bgegs bsad pa sogs shin tu zab pa'i shog ril bdun dam pas mdzad pa/ chos skyong gi lder sku dang bris sku bzhengs thabs 'phags pas mdzad pa/ bsrung bzlog
bsad gsum gyi man ngag tshigs bcad ma dam pas mdzad pa/ rten gtor gyi man ngag sa chen dang dam pas mdzad pa gnyis/ pho rkyang gi sgrub thabs las bzhi'i khyad par brag
steng pas mdzad pa/ zab gtad kyi man ngag mal gyis sa chen la gnang ba/ mahA kA la'i bzlas lung bzhi'i man ngag sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ gsang ba'i man ngag ces bya ba nang
gi sgo nas 'khu ldog spong ba gong mas mdzad pa/ chos skyong lcam dral gyi 'khor lo'i man ngag gsang ba mkha' 'gro go ldog pa'i man ngag nag po chen po'i bod rbad gsad
gsum dril ba'i man ngag 'khor lo'i bca' thabs/ 'khor lo'i rab tu gnas pa'i man ngag dam shing la dbang bskur ba'i man ngag mgon po lcam dral du sgrub pa bram ze mchog sred
kyis mdzad pa/ dgra bo lha dang bral ba'i man ngag mahA kA la'i theb bzlog mkha' 'gro'i 'khu ldog spangs pa'i man ngag las mjug mnan pa bsad pa las kyi 'khor lo mnan pa
dngos gong mas mdzad pa/ nag po

chen po'i phur bu'i sgrub thabs rgya gzhung bram zes mdzad pa mal los bsgyur pa/'di 'od ldan dpal gyi sbags sgrub la dgos pa'i thun sgrub zer ba de yin nam/ mgon po lcam dral
gyi sbyin sreg dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal gyis mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg gi yi ge bram zes mdzad pa/ phur bu'i sgrub pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ phur bu chen po la srin gzugs
kyis bstod pa/ rang srung 'khor lo'i gdams pa rje btsun gyis mdzad pa/ srung 'khor dkar shAkya grags kyis mdzad pa/ ru mtshon 'dzugs thabs yar klung pas mdzad pa/ bran
bdud kyi las tshogs mal gyis sa chen la gnang ba yar klung pas bris pa/ nag po chen po'i sgo nas gzhan gyi ngag mnan pa/ slob dpon padmas mdzad pa'i chos skyong spyi'i dmod
bskul/ mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i drang srong dmod bskul/ pu tra ming sring gsum gyi bod pa'i tshigs sa chen gyi man ngag yar klung pas bris pa/ pu tra'i 'phrin
las 'chol ba yar lung pa nas brgyud pa/ 'khon nag zas su bza' ba'i man ngag slob dpon padmas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i gces bsdus mal los mdzad pa/ mgon po'i gzungs 'dzur/
gtor zor/ dmod bcol rnams bla ma gnyan gyis mdzad pa/ gtor chen padma dbang phyug gis mdzad pa yar klung pa la brgyud pa/ lcam dral gyi gtor chen gyi gsol kha bya tshul
yar klung pas mdzad pa/ mdos bskang rgyas pa bram zes mdzad pa/ mdos bskang spyan chen pos mdzad pa sogs dkar chag nang ltar tshang bar thob nas/ ! /yang gur gyi mgon
po'i nang khrid dam gsang khrid thun

mong ma yin pa rgyas par stsal te/ de'i man ngag gi cha lag lus kyi rtsa 'khor so so la brten nas las bzhi bsgrub pa'i dmigs pa khyad par can zhal shes kyis brgyan pa dang
/ yang srung 'khor brag rdzong ma'i man ngag gi nang tshan rnal 'byor ma'i sgos dgra myur du bsgral ba'i las sbyor zab khyad can dang / nang khrid kyi cha lag snying kha
chos kyi 'khor lo la brten pa'i dmigs yul zhag bdun la med par byed pa'i man ngag zab mo rnams zhib cing mtha' chod pa nos nas/ de dag dang 'brel ba'i lung gi skor la rje
tshar chen gyis bsgrigs pa'i snyan rgyud po ti'i nang nas/ de nyid kyi dkar chag dam pas mdzad pa'i shog ril bcu/ brag rdzong ma'i khrid yig rdo ring pas mdzad pa/ kha skong
po ti'i dkar chag brag rdzong ma'i mngon rtogs/ gtor bsngo rgyas 'bring gnyis/ brgyud 'debs rnam kun ma/ dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ mgon po'i
chog bsgrigs/ ser ba bsrung 'bebs kyi man ngag dug gi rlung chen nag po/ gtor ma gsum gyi rnam bshad/ ru mtshon 'dzugs thabs/ gzungs 'dzugs thabs/ las mgon gyi bskang gso
las bzhi lhun grub/ bstod bskul 'og min bde chen ma rnams tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i nag po chen po'i mdos bskang / rje btsun rdo
ring pas mdzad pa'i ser ba srung ba'i man ngag tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i nag po chen po'i gtor bzlog gi cho ga dgra bgegs kyi stobs 'phrog rol pa/ nag po chen po'i char
dbab pa'i man ngag gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i zab pa'i gnad kyi

man ngag las/ phyi sgrub la brten pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i nang khrid rgyun gyi nyams len gsang ba yang gsang sems kyi gnad lnga
la brten nas 'khu ldog spangs te bran ltar bkol ba'i man ngag gi yi ge las sbyor gyi sngon 'gro'i ling ga bri ba/ dgug gzhug kha sbyor dbye ba'i yi ge bsgrubs kyang rtag
mi 'byung na dpog chog bya ba'i yi ge rigs sngags go ldog pa'i yi ge zab pa'i yang tig snying nang gi man ngag las/ nang rtsa gsum la brten pa'i yi ge gong mas mdzad
pa/ de nyid cung zad rgyas su btang ba'i mgon po mthu med du mi 'gyur ba'i yi ge mgon po dang pu tra lcam sring la brten pa'i shin tu zab pa'i man ngag gi yi ge gsang rten
lus la bcangs pa'i gnad kyi yi ge rnams dam pas mdzad pa/ bla ma'i zhal las byung ba'i man ngag gi tho yig bdag chen gyis mdzad pa/ rdo ring pas mdzad pa'i gsang khrid
thun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i snyan brgyud kyi rin chen lde mig bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsung la yang dgon dpal ldan bkra shis pas zin bris byas
pa'i sgrub yig chen mo/ bdag chen gyis mdzad pa'i lha brgyad kyi sgrub thabs gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu/ brag rdzong ma'i bsdus don/ mal 'og gsang rdzas kyi yi ge tshar
chen gyis mdzad pa rnams thob cing / ! /yang tshar chen gyis bsgrigs pa'i kha skong po ti'i nang nas/ nag po chen po'i lo rgyus/ lha mo'i lo rgyus/ pu tra ming sring gsum
gyi lo rgyus dam pas mdzad pa/ de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i

bskang gso chos nyid ma/ bram zes mdzad pa'i sngon tshe bde gshegs ma/ 'phags pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa gang thugs ma/ las mgon sgo ma dang bcas pa'i bstod pa mal los mdzad pa/
sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i gtum chen ma/ lha mo'i bskang gso bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i bstod pa nag po rngam pa ma/ 'phags
pas mdzad pa'i gur mgon gyi bskul/ yum chen gyi bstod pa kun tu bzang po ma/ lha mo'i bstod pa til dmar ma/ lha mo'i bshags pa 'gro don sku mchog ma/ bstod pa mi pham
ma/ stag tshang lo tsA bas mdzad pa'i chos skyong spyi'i bskang bshags/ 'phags pas mdzad pa'i bdud rtsi lnga mchod/ bdag chen mthu stobs pas mdzad pa'i mnga' gsol gyi
yi ge ratna kirti'i gtor sgrub kyi lag len gsal ba'i sgrol me rnams nos shing / ! /yang tshar chen gyis bsgrigs pa'i mgon pod gyi ljang pu ti'i phyed yan tsam thob pa'i khrid
man ngag de dag phal che ba'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ paNDi ta shraddha ka ra warma/ lo chen
rin chen bzang po/ brag steng / yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ sga a gnyan dam pa/ bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla chen
kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal

mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun spangs chos kyi nyi ma/ rje btsun sgom rung ba kun legs/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje byams
pa rab brtan/ rje snying rje bzang po/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na tshar chen chos
kyi rgyal po/ rje bod mkhar ba/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ des sa skya pa a nandan la'o/ /de ni nang khrid dang brag rdzong ma'i brgyud pa gtso che ba yin lags/ ! /me
'bar ma'i lung sogs kyi phyi sgrub phal che ba'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa nas/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che/ sga a gnyan dam pa/ phing nag rdo rje dpal/ khams pa bkra shis 'od zer/ bar sding ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ 'jam
dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ ! /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po gri gug lha lnga snyan brgyud lugs sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i dbang bzhi
yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ a ni ga badzra/ padma badzra/ intra bhu ti/ phun tshogs bde ba/ nag po spyod pa/
bram ze dpal sbyin/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ se mkhar chung ba/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa
paN/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar

pa rdo rje 'od zer/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun grags/ rong mi ye shes/ tre bo rdo rje grags/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang
pa/ theg chen chos rgyal/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / mnyam med dpal 'dzin bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ thugs sras
kun dga' rgyal po/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don
grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gri gug lha lnga/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma rnams kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por rgya gzhung
lugs kyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ shaddha ka ra/ lo chen/ brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen/
slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ bkras lung pa/ dge sding pa chen po/ sangs rgyas dpal/ rin chen gling pa/ dkar gshog
pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ theg chen chos rgyal/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa/ mkhan chen khrom yon pa/ brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ de la klu dbang
gling pa kun dga' rgyal po dang / lcang lo can pa bsod nams mchog ldan gnyis kyis zhus/ de gnyis la rje tshe bkras pas zhus/ de nas tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/
! /khyad par lha brgyad kyi

dbang thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pas rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal la gnang / de la rje tshe bkras pas gsan/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/
bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol bu/ mkhan chen byang seng / theg chen pa man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa nas/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga'
ldan pa kun bsod/ bag ston/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa man 'dra/ gri gug lha lnga/
lha bcu gnyis ma/ lha bcu bdun ma rnams kyi thun mong gi dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje gdan pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bdag chen ngag pa/ tshar chen man 'dra/ yang
na dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa/ chos rje nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug ye shes bzang po/ rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/ rin chen
chos rgyal/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang tshar pa man 'dra/ yang lha bcu gnyis ma'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ shaddha ka ra nas/ jo bo rje/ lo chen rin bzang
/ dge tshul purNa Na/ rgya lcags ri gong pa/ rdzing bu kha pa shAkya grags/ span phug pa dar ma shAkya/ yang ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ze ba don grub ye shes/ khams pa shAkya
rdo rje/ bar thang pa chos grags/ bla ma dar ma shAkya/ slob dpon bsod nams dbang phyug gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa ta dbon chen mo/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims brtan

pa/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam rgyal/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ yang na bsod nams dbang phyug bla ma mchog ldan/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/
rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge nam mkha' ye shes/ de gsum la theg chen chos rjes gsan/ des 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal man 'dra/ gri gug lha lnga'i dkyil
chog bram zes mdzad pa paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang / 'gos los bsgyur pa'i lung yang thob/ ! /mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs
pa/ mtha' rten sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang bzlas lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ slob dpon la li ta badzra/ nag
po ro 'dzin/ gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ khams pa tshar dgu ston pa/ grub ston bsod nams grags/ bla ma mon mig dmar ston/ bla ma zhang chung ba/ lang 'gro byang chub dar/ de
la lce ston mdo sde seng ge dang / dpal chen skye med jo gdan gyis zhus/ de gnyis la gru ston shAkya 'bum/ dge bshes dbugs/ bla ma dharma gzi brjid/ nyi thog pa kun dga'
zla ba/ mdar mkhan po blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa man 'dra/ yang na grub ston shAkya 'bum/
de la dkar gshong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang / bdag po bsod nams yon tan pas gsan/ de gnyis la bla chen chos dpal bzang pos gsan/ lo tsA ba madznyu shrI dznyA na/
rje mus srad pa/ mus chen rnam rgyal

bzang po/ rje klu dbang gling pa man 'dra'o/ ! /gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad sbags te sgrub pa thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang dang / lha mgon bcu gnyis ma'i rjes su gnang ba
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin bzang / brag steng ba/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa
skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paN chen/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/
bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje
'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ de gnyis la tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag
dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i brgyud
pa rdzong lugs ni/ 'phags pa nas/ zhang pa/ na bza' pa/ bla ma dam pa/ gzungs pa/ dge bzang pa/ bla ma rin chen/ zur shAkya dpal ba/ rje mus srad pa/ sgyi chu ba shes
rab rin chen/ tshar chen man 'dra/ yang na brag phug pa nas/ brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ sa skya bu ston dbang phyug dar/ theg chen chos rgyal/ rdzong pa kun dga'

rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / mus srad pa man 'dra/ ! /gsang khrid kyi sngon 'gro'i gur mgon lha dgu'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang /
mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ paN grub dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/
mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ chos
rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje bzang po rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/ chos rje skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ grub dbang bkra shis seng ge tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse dbang phyug rje byams pa rab brtan/ chos rje snying rje bzang po/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams la'o/ /yang na tshar chen/ rje mkhyen brtse ba/ rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan
man 'dra'o/ ! /phyi'i las mkhan gcer bu zangs gri can dang / nang gi las mkhan ber nag zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa chen yan 'dra/ 'gos ston/
tshar sgang pa/ dge bshes mi g.yo ba/ shes bsgom bla

ma dpal/ slob dpon shes rab bla ma/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa/ yar klung pa khu dbon/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/
rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ gong dkar ba chos rje tshul khrims pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang phyug
rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ !
/yang na sa paN/ mdo khams kyi rta dge bla ma/ slob dpon shes rab bla ma nas/ bdag chen rgya dkar ba/ mkhas pa'i dbang po ratna shi la/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /ru mtshon gyi las mkhan bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i thun mong ba'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan 'dra la/ do pa ston tshul/
rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng bzang / yar klung pa khu dbon/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ gong
dkar tshul khrims pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /bran bdud thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje
gur/ grub chen/ bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ paN grub dad byed go cha/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo
tsA ba blo

gros grags pa/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje sa paN/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas
pa yon tan khri/ drin chen seng ge bzang po/ mkhas grub seng ge rgyal mtshan pa/ mkhan po bsod nams rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya dkar
shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'bum phrag gsum pa byams pa chos kyi don grub/ chos rje tshul khrims pa/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal
mtshan/ mi pham chos rgya mtsho/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang ngor lugs kyi gur mgon
lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/
shaddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob
dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/
bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bzhi thog pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bdag po grags pa rin chen/ bdag po blo gros dbang phyug
sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ rje

btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ chos kyi rje dkon mchog grags pa/ shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / grub mchog rdo rje'i mtshan can/
bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /'di'i gtor ma ni zlum gtor dkar po
rtse rgyan can/ pu tra la yang zlum gtor dkar po chung ngu gcig yin no/ /las mgon pu tra lcam sring gi rjes gnang zur bka' thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags
pa klu sgrub/ padma 'byung gnas/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/
slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid
chen po/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun
