pa ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug stobs
'phrog nag po chen po tsa turmu

kha'i chos skor thob pa'i tshul la/ thog mar sgrub dus kyi mgon po zhal khra can thun mong ba'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ ba ling ta pa/
sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags pa/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ kha
'ub pa/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ yar klung pa/ mkhan
chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ rje bsod
nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /yang na/ bla ma dam pa/ bdag chen kun dga' rin chen/ bzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun kun
spangs chen po man 'dra/ ! /de nas rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun pas zung 'jug gi gdod ma'i mgon po sngon du byed pa'i thabs kyi gtso bo zhal bzhi pa'i gsang khrid zab
mo nyams khrid du bskyangs pa nos nas/ de dang 'brel ba'i yig cha'i lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ rtsa ba'i yi ge tshigs bcad/ brgyud 'debs dang bcas pa tshar chen gyis
mdzad pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje

'chang / klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ kha che'i rin chen grags/ rin chen rdo rje/ ri sul gyi rnal
'byor ma/ gnyan lo/ kha 'ub pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla
ma bdag nyid chen po/ bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs pa/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dge ba rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/ mtshungs med
skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ lcags mo bkra shis seng ge tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ ! /gzhan yang gnyan mgon chen po'i man ngag gi yi ge mang po'i lung thob pa'i
chos kyi rnam grangs la/ gnyan lo chen po'i tshe'i rig 'dzin grub pa'i zab chos bsrung bzlog bsad mnan tshe sgrub dang bcas pa'i shog ril/ sbas te 'dzam gling du ma grags
pa'i shog ril/ zhi ba nor sgrub kyi shog ril/ nang tsitta la brten nas zhal dngos su blta ba'i shog ril/ phyi 'gab 'dre mnan pa'i shog ril/ nang gi mal 'og shog ril/ gsang
ba rang srog rten gyi 'khor lo'i shog ril/ 'khor bsrung zhing mi 'khu mi ldog pa'i shog ril/ yum chen khros ma nag mo'i shog ril/ 'chi med tshe sgrub pa'i shog ril/ dgos
'dod nor sgrub pa'i shog ril/ rdzas dang srog 'khor la brten nas sku dngos su blta ba'i shog ril snying rgya can/ ltas ngan cho 'phrul dbab pa'i shog ril/ dgra srog

myur du gcod pa srog rtsa rnon po'i shog ril/ dgra mkhar rmangs nas bsgyel ba nag po chen po mkhar bsgyel gyi shog ril/ ser ba dbab pa spu gri ngar ma'i shog ril/ zhing sel
'jug pa spu gri so 'debs kyi shog ril/ gcun thabs nyi zla can gyi shog ril/ gnad la dbab pa lha mo nag mo'i shog ril bka' rgya ma/ 'khu ldog byed na mnan pa'i shog ril/
las byed du ma 'dod na ar la gtad pa'i shog ril te shog ril nyer gcig dpal mgon gyi bsnyen sgrub/ rlung 'khor/ gtor chen/ mnan pa rnams kyi zhal shes kyi yig chung / sgrub
pa'i gnad rje btsun gyis gsungs pa/ sgrub pa rkang grangs kyi yi ge gtor len bya rog brtag pa/ 'khu ldog mi 'byung zhing las myur du sgrub pa'i yi ge rtsa ba dang / gnad
'bebs dang / las tshogs kyi 'khor lo yi ge 'khor lo dang ling rtse ling ga'i zhal shes rnams kyi yi ge 'khor lo'i bri thabs kyi yi ge 'khor lo'i sngags bcang gi yi ge 'khor
lo'i sngags bkod tshul gyi yi ge las tshogs 'ga' gsungs pa'i 'khor lo'i man ngag gi yi ge zhal gdams snying gi dum bu/ spu gri so 'debs kyi gdams pa/ zhal gdams snying
gi dum bu las rang srung phra mo yid bzhin gyi 'khor lo'i gdams pa/ zhal gdams snying gi dum bu las rten gyi yi ge zhal gdams snying gi dum bu las gtor ma bzhi'i zhal
gdams/ zhal gdams snying gi dum bu las 'khor lo'i zhal gdams/ bram ze'i dmod pa'i srog mthu/ bka' sdod drang srong nag po'i pra dbab pa/ than 'gyed gnyan gyi mgo spu ma/
yum chen

bzhi'i than 'gyed kyi man ngag spar spu'i man ngag lha dgu'i nor sgrub thun mong ma yin pa/ rdzas kyi sgo nas bsad pa'i sbyor ba/ rdo nag yid dmar gyi sgrub mthu/ khang ser
nag po/ dgra bo zla ba gcig la bsad pa'i bram ze mdze pho nag po'i man ngag dgra bo klu la gtad pa gnyan gyi na ga stobs 'phrog mon pa nag po nor gsher gyi man ngag zangs
khab dmar po'i bsad las/ sreg byed me'i sbyor ba/ gcun pa'i mthar thug sdig pa nag po'i 'khrul 'khor gyi las sbyor/ man ngag gnad brgyad ma sogs yig chung tshan pa bzhi/
gnyan los mdzad pa'i lo rgyus/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi khyad par gyi yi ge rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge bsnyen
sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge nag po 'gro shes dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa'i man ngag
mngon rtogs dmar chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi las khrid nag po 'gro shes gzungs pas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i sgrub khrid bsnyen pa'i go rim
gyi yi ge yar klung pas mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi spog chog shi sa bstan pa dang bcas pa'i mngon rtogs gsal byed kyi zhal gdams mthar thug yar klung pas mdzad pa/
des mdzad pa'i gtor ma'i zhal gdams/ des mdzad pa'i zhal gdams/ des mdzad pa'i bsad las kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs can du grags

pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'khrul 'khor ltab cing sba ba sogs mnan pa'i man ngag sbas don gsal ba/ des mdzad pa'i dpal mgon gyi thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge sgrub thabs
rta bdun rgyal po mdo stod pa 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge bsod nams grags pas mdzad pa/ sri'u gso ba'i gdams pa/ bu 'tshol
ba'i man ngag mngal srung ba'i gdams pa/ yang sri'u gso ba'i gdams pa/ sri'u med pa btsal ba/ lte ba sgyur ba/ yod pa gso ba rnams kyi gdams pa/ gdong bzhi pa'i thugs dam
bskang pa'i man ngag gnyan gyis nye gnas dar ma seng ge la gnang ba/ bstod pa'i skor la klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paM pad ma gnyan
gyis mdzad pa/ gnam kha'u pas dpal mgon dngos su zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa/ mal lo tsA bas rmi lam du zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa/ rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ sa paN gyis mdzad
pa/ 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ dharmA shrI bha dras mdzad pa/ mkhan chen gnas drug pas mdzad pa/ bya ban yon tan
blo gros kyis mdzad pa/ bkra shis grub kyis mdzad pa/ yang des mdzad pa/ bzang po rgyal mtshan pas mdzad pa/ shrI mAn bha dras mdzad pa/ yang bzang po'i mtha' can gyis
mdzad pa'i bstod pa rnams so/ /bskul sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa zur shAkya dpal gyis mdzad pa/ bla rdo'i man ngag tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ tsa turmu kha'i rgya gzhung paNDi
ta ta thA ga ta rakShi

tas mdzad pa/ zhal bzhi pa'i chos skor gyi dkar chag gsang khrid kyi brgyud 'debs/ tshe sgrub srung zlog dang bcas pa'i rgyun gyi nyams len/ de'i rgyud 'debs rnams tshar chen
gyis mdzad pa/ las bzhi'i so so'i yig chung gnyan los mdzad pa/ de'i gsal byed theg chen chos rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi yi ge kha'u pas mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi
yi ge sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs kyi mchan bshad ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge gnyan los u pa de sha sgrub dus kyi las khrigs
kha'u pas mdzad pa/ gnyan los mdzad pa'i stobs chen shugs drag ma/ kha'u pas mdzad pa'i lha mchog ma dang / dur khrod gnas brgyad ma/ yar klung pas mdzad pa'i lo rgyus

kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! dpal mgon brtsegs zhal can gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ ri sul gyi

bzhin no/ ! /dpal mgon dkar po tshe 'phel/ ser po bsod nams sgrub pa/ dmar po dbang sdud/ sngon po bgegs 'joms te las bzhi'i mgon po so so'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa

pa ngag dbang chos

grags/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /gnad dbab kyi mgon po gshin rje gshed ltar sgrub pa'i rjes

dbang rgyal/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ rje btsun bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/

po/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ tsi lu paNDi ta/ dus zhabs che chung / mkhas pa dpe med mtsho/ sA dhu pu tra bi khya ta de wa/dharmA ka ra dang / dharmA mi tra/ paN chen shAkya
shrI/ sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ rgyus pa gzhon seng / dol po ye shes mgon po/ kun spangs kun tu bzang po/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin chen grub/
'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa/ ru pa ka bzhi pa/ slob dpon bsod grags pa/ zhwa lu lo chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ lo chen ratna bha
dra/ rje kun dga' grol mchog mkhan chen shes rab rin chen/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rwa
lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang / zla bzang / lha dbang gzi brjid can/ zla ba'i byin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha yi dbang ldan/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ padma
dkar po/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa tsi lu pa

a tsarYa/ pi to pa dang / dus zhabs pa gnyis/ manydzu kirti/ sa man ta shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / sga lo/ shes seng / dpal ldan seng ge kun mkhyen
bu ston/ gong gsum chos dpal/ dge 'dun bzang po/ dpal ldan legs pa/ nam mkha' tshul khrims/ bsod nams grags pa/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/
rje ratna bha dra/ rje kun dga' grol mchog mkhan chen shes rab rin chen/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
la'o/ /yang na/ dpal legs don grub/ kun dga'/ thar pa bzang po/ lo chen man 'dra/ yang na/ chos kyi dpal ba/ bsod nams 'phel/ paN chen shes rin/ lo chen man 'dra/ yang
na/ rong pa shes seng / kun mkhyen 'phags pa 'od/ kun mkhyen bu ston man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na rong pa sga lo/ dbus pa tshul khrims dar/ shar pa ye shes rin chen/
kun spangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ye/ jo nang yon rgyam pa/ kun mkhyen dol bu/ ma ti paN chen/ phyogs las rnam rgyal/ byang chub seng ge de gsum gyis rjes su bzung ba
theg chen chos rgyal/ dpal legs pa man 'dra/ yang na shes seng / skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol bu man chad gong bzhin no/ /yang na/ jo nang phyogs rgyal/ dbon rgyal
bzang / rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags bzang / zhang ston kun dga' dpal/ nam mkha' dpal

bzang / shes rab bkra shis/ byams pa shAka 'od/ chos dar grags 'phel ba/ lo chen 'gyur med/ rje a wa dhu ti pa/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dus kyi 'khor lo/ zla bzang / lha dbang / gzi brjid can/ zlas byin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs
gzugs/ lha yi dbang ldan/ rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags/ padma dkar po/ bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ bshes gnyen bzang / phyag dmar/ khyab 'jug sbas pa/ nyi ma grags/ shin tu bzang
po/ rgya mtsho rnam rgyal/ rgyal dka'/ nyi ma/ sna tshogs gzugs/ zla 'od/ mtha' yas/ sa skyong / dpal skyong / dus zhabs gnyis/ zla mgon/ 'bro ston lo tsA dkon mchog
bsrung / rnam brtsegs/ grub chen yu mo/ dharme shwa ra/ mkhas pa nam 'od/ grub thob se mo che/ga ga na dhwa dza/ 'jam gsar/ chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs rje/ byang sems rgyal
ye/ jo nang yon rgyam pa/ kun mkhyen dol bu man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na byang sems ye rgyal/ 'phags pa 'od/'dis chos sku 'od dang kun spangs pa gnyis la'ang gsan/
kun mkhyen bu ston man chad gong bzhin no/ /yang na/ 'jam gsar/ rong pa sga lo/ shes seng / 'phags 'od/ bu ston man chad 'dra/ 'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ se
mo che pa/ bo dong rin rtse pa/ stag sde seng rgyal/ gshong ston sku mched/ lo mchog dpal seng / bu ston man chad 'dra/ yang na

lo mchog skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol bu man chad gong bzhin no/ /yang na rin brtse/ 'jim pa rin she ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs la sogs 'dra/ yang na rin she 'jam
dbyangs bzhi thog pa/ byang sems rgyal ye man gong bzhin no/ /de ltar brgyud pa thams cad kyi phyag len phyogs cig tu dril ba'i dbang rgyas par thob nas/ dkyil 'khor yongs
rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs dang / dkyil chog rigs ldan rnam rgyal grags bzang gis mdzad pa dang / dbang chog dang 'grel chen dri med 'od kyi mdor bsdus dang po'i 'grel pa
lo chen 'gyur med kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang thos so/ /mdo rgyud thams cad kyi nges don gyi snying po zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i khrid nges don
gyi dbang dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa rwa lugs ni/ 'og min gnas su chos sku rdo rje 'chang / /chos dbyings chen por longs sku dus 'khor lo/ /dha nye ke Tar sprul
sku shAkya thub/ /shambha la ru chos rgyal rigs ldan rnams/ /orbi pa ru tsi lu paNDi ta/ /bhaM ga la ru pi to A tsarYa/ /wa rentra ru dus zhabs chen po dang / /manydzu de
shar dus 'khor zhabs gnyis pa/ /rgya gar shar du manydzu kirti'i zhabs/ /ye rang grong du manta shrI che/ /me tog ne'u ldan du rwa lo chos rab ra rdo rje grags kyi sras/
dang / /khu lung se khyir ye shes seng ge rwa/de'i sras/ /khu lung chos shing dgon par 'bum seng ra/de'i sras/ /dbon dmar dgon par rje btsun sga lo dang /gtsang rong dkar
phug gi mi nyag rdo rje seng ge de'i sras ye shes rdo rje'i sras te dpal sga lo'i skye ba yin/ /sham

'bar gnas su shes rab seng ge'i zhabs/de'i sras rong pa/ /dben gnas jo mtshor kun mkhyen 'phags pa 'od/ /ri phug dgon par mkhan chen bu ston rje/ /gnas mchog der bzhugs rje
btsun nam mkha'i mtshan/sku zhang / /chos grags zhwa lur mkhas mchog tsandra shrI/ /bsam sding dgon par 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan rje/ ri phug /shar chen gnas
su mkhyen rab chos kyi rje/ /gra thang chos sder lo chen chos skyong bzang / /dpal ldan sa skyar sa lo 'jam dbyangs che/ /sman lding gnas su lo chen ratna'i mtshan/ /chos
lung byang brtser 'jam mgon grol mchog zhabs/ /jo gdan tshogs su mkhan chen rin she ba/ /lo yi dgon par spyan snga kun dga'i mtshan/ /de las thob pa sngags 'chang a nanda
la'o/ /yang na chos rab lha rje dpal rgyal dang / /glo bo lo tsA dol po ye shes mgon/ /kun spangs chen po 'phags 'od man chad 'dra/ /yang na kun spangs byang sems rgyal
ye dang / /mkhas btsun yon rgyam kun mkhyen dol po'i zhabs/ /phyogs las rnam rgyal nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ /grub chen kun blo 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang / /zhwa lu
lo chen man chad sngar dang 'dra/ /yang na sga lo man lung gu ru dang /pu nya shrI /shes seng 'phags 'od bu ston man chad 'dra/ /yang na man lung gu ru lo grags pa/yar lung
lo tsA ba kirti dhwa dza/ /grub pa dpal bzang mkhas btsun yon rgyam pa/ /kun mkhyen dol po man chad gong dang 'dra/ ! /'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rgyal rigs ldan
yan chad rwa lugs dang 'dra/ de nas/ lho phyogs rgya mtsho'i 'gram du dus

'khor zhabs/ /tso ri pa ru dus 'khor zhabs gnyis pa/ /kha che'i grong du paN chen zla ba mgon/ /'phan yul grags su bsgom pa dkon mchog bsrung / /gnam la sgang du sgrom ston
gnam la brtsegs/ /'o yug rgyal khab gnas su yu mo rje/mi bskyod rdo rje mtshan dngos dad pa rgyal po/ /g.yas ru grod chung dgon par de'i sras/ chos dbang zhabs/ /khang gsar
dpal gyi dgon par nam mkha' 'od/ /pho lung pa phug nags su se mo che/chos dbang gi sras ga ga dhwa dza/ /rkyang 'dur chos grwar 'jam gsar shes rab 'od/ /man ngag dge
sding dgon par chos sku 'od/ /skyid phug bde ldan gnas su kun spangs che/akSho bhya mtshan dngos thugs rje brtson 'grus/ /bde chen dgon par byang sems rgyal ye'i zhabs/ /jo
mo nang du mkhas btsun yon rgyam pa/mtshan dngos thugs rje rgyal mtshan/ /sku 'bum chen por kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ /mkhar chung dgon par phyogs las rnam rgyal
che/mtshan dngos chos kyi rgyal po/ /rtse chen chos grwar nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ /sho ma'i ri bor grub chen kun blo'i zhabs/ / brtse chenshar chen gnas su 'jam dbyangs
dkon mchog bzang / /gra thang chos grwar lo chen chos skyong bzang / /dpal ldan sa skyar 'jam dbyangs kun dga'i mtshan/ /ratna bha dra man chad gong dang 'dra/ /yang na/

che ba/ rin rtse ba/ 'dzin pa rin she shar pa dus

'khor ba/ jo nang kun spangs pa sogs sngar dang 'dra/ yang na/ rin she 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyal ye man gong bzhin no/ ! /nye brgyud dpe med 'tsho
nas brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang chen/ grub chen dpe med 'tsho/ grub thob dpal 'dzin/ sA dhu pu tra/ 'od byed lha/ chos 'byung zhi ba/ grub thob nyi ma dpal/ rin chen
'tsho dang / paN chen bi bhu ti/ yang na/ chos 'byung zhi ba/ grags pa'i lha/ paN chen chos kyi 'bangs/ bi bhu ti/ ko brag bsod rgyal/ g.yung phug pa rgyal dge lho pa chos
ldan gsum kas rjes su bzung ba go lung gzhon nu dpal/ thar pa lo tsa/ kun mkhyen bu/ lce btsun nam mkha' man gong dang 'dra/ yang na/ bi bhu ti/ a mo gha/dpyal padmo can
pa'ang zer/ kun mkhyen chos 'od/ kun spangs chen po/ byang sems rgyal ye man ring brgyud bzhin/ yang na/ bi bhu ti/ mar ston g.yang 'bar/ rnal 'byor seng 'bum/ kun spangs
sogs 'dra/ ! /sa skya pa chen pos sga lo la gsan pa'i sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i man ngag gi brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ rigs ldan/ dus zhabs gnyis/ tsa mi/ sga
lo/ bla ma sa chen/ rje btsun bsod rtse/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ rgyus pa gzhon seng / dol po ye shes mgon/ kun spangs chen po man 'dra/ yang na/ rigs ldan/
sprul pa'i dge slong bsod snyoms pa/ phyogs kyi bram ze/ dha ri ka pa/ dus zhabs che ba/ bho dhi bha dra/ tsa mi/ sga lo/ sa chen man 'dra/ ! /nye brgyud paN chen shAkya
shrI nas

brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ rigs gsum mgon po/ dus zhabs gnyis/ nA ro pa/ dpal ldan 'jigs med grags/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ dpyal chos bzang / dpyal a mo gha/ kun spangs pa/
byang sems rgyal ye/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ mkhan chen bu ston man 'dra/ yang na byang sems rgyal ye/ jo nang yon rgyam/ kun mkhyen dol po man sngar bzhin no/ /sa skya paNDi
tas kha che paN chen la gsan pa'i srog rtsol rdo rje'i snyan rgyud kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ rigs gsum mgon po/ dus zhabs gnyis/ dpe med 'tsho/ 'jigs med grags/
'byung gnas sbas/ rnam grags lha/ dad byed/ lha dbang / kha che paN chen/ sa skya paNDi ta/ rgyus pa gzhon seng / dol po ye shes mgon/ kun spangs chen po/ kun mkhyen 'phags
'od/ mkhan chen bu ston man 'dra/ yang na kun spangs/ byang sems rgyal ye/ mkhas btsun pa/ jo nang yon rgyam/ kun mkhyen pa man 'dra/ ! /shin tu nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje
'chang / sha wa ri dbang phyug paN chen/ bi bhu ta/ ko brag pa/ go long gzhon dpal/ thar lo nyi ma/ kun mkhyen bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / sha wa ri/ paN
chen bi bhu ta/ chos sku 'od/ kun spangs zhang / byang sems khams pa/ yon rgyam pa/ kun mkhyen pa sogs sngar dang 'dra/ de ltar dngos su smos pa'i brgyud pa de thams cad
dang / gzhan yang gyi jo/ tsa mi/ sga lo/ sa skya pa/ zhang tshal pa/ jo bo rje nas brgyud pa la sogs pa'i sbyor drug gi man ngag

thams cad gcig tu dril nas ma tshang bar med par bkod pa kun mkhyen gnyis pa bu ston chos rje dang / chos kyi rgyal po phyogs las rnam rgyal bas mdzad pa'i thog mtha' bar dge'i
khrid yig so so dang / jo nang phyogs las pas mdzad pa'i ngo sprod gsang don rab gsal/ zhwa lu mkhyen rab chos rjes mdzad pa'i sbyor drug nyams su len tshul gyi yi ge
lo chen 'gyur med bde chen gyis mdzad pa'i sbyor drug gi khrid yig chen mo dang po'i sangs rgyas 'char ba/ chag lo chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i dus 'khor chos 'byung chen
mo dpag bsam gyi snye ma/ dus 'khor gyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs gsar rnying mang po'i lung sogs thos shing / gong du smos pa'i brgyud pa de rnams kyang thog mar
dge ba bi bhu ti nas brgyud pa dang / bar du dge ba paN chen shAkya shrI nas brgyud pa dang / tha mar dge ba chos rgyal rigs ldan sogs nas rim par brgyud pa gtso che ba
yin gsungs/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel chen po gshong 'gyur la/ lo tsA ba blo gros rnam gnyis kyis bcos pa'i steng nas bshad bka' thob pa'i
brgyud pa'ang gong rwa 'bro gnyis kyi dbang gi rtsa ba'i brgyud pa dang 'dra ba las/ kho bos thob pa 'di ni rigs ldan chen po nas/ shang ston kun dga' dpal ldan/ lo tsA
ba nam mkha' dpal bzang / paN chen shes rab bkra shis/ rje btsun byams pa shAka 'od/ thugs sras chos dar grags 'phel/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen nas brgyud pa de/ gtso che
ba'o/ /yang gong gi yig cha de dag lung gi brgyud pa lugs gzhan ni/ lo chen

'gyur med bde chen yang phal cher sngar dang 'dra ba las/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen gyi rjes su/ rje btsun a wa dhu ti pa/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs/
spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /bu ston dang mkhyen rab chos rje'i yig cha de dag gi brgyud pa'i
lugs gcig ni/ mkhyen rab rje rgyal mtshan rin chen/ don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling rje/ rin chen dbang phyug rin chen rgya mtsho/ bhikShu ku sa li pa/ des bdag sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ bu ston/ bde chen pa chos kyi dpal/ rgyal ba dpal lags/ 'dus bzang
pa/ thar pa'i mtshan can/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ paN chen pra dznyA mangga laM/ 'di'i bar nas bla ma 'ga' zhig ma rnyed/ rje bsod nams rgya mtsho/
spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /dus 'khor sdom chen gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bu ston
nas/ bhu Ta ba yon tan 'byung gnas/ chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang man gong bzhin no/ ! /ye shes khyung khra'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen chen po/
'ga' rong pa lha'i rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa brtson pa/ chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang man sngar dang 'dra/ ! /rdo rje shugs kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo

a wa dhu ti pa/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /grub thob man lung pa nas brgyud pa'i dus 'khor

du thob nas/ de dang 'brel ba'i rgyab chos lung gi chos sna'i rnam grangs la/ u rgyan pa'i gsung 'phros rnam thar ma/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang / bsnyen sgrub kyi sngon 'gro'i
khrid yig bsnyen sgrub kyi dngos gzhi'i khrid zla

seng pas mdzad pa rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ grub thob u rgyan pa/ zla ba seng ge rtogs ldan grags seng pa/ dar ma rgyal mtshan/ mkha'

dbang kun dga' bsod nams

la'o/ ! /ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po nas brgyud pa'i gtum mo zhag bdun ma'i khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro nai gu ma/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang
po/ rnam rgyal mgon po/ gong dkar ba byang chub dbang rgyal/ tshe dbang bkra shis/ dpal ldan grub/ rnam rgyal mtshan can/ kun dga' gzhan phan bzang po/ spyan snga chos kyi
spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /grub chen nA ro pa nas brgyud pa'i ro snyoms skor drug nyams khrid du thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / te lo pa/ nA ro paN chen/ ti phu gsang sngags sdong po/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ rgyal ba lo dang gsum pa/ grub thob gling chen ras pa/

gi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ de wa a kar tsandra/ de gnyis ka la jo bo a mo gha badzra gyis gsan/ de la 'brog mis gsan/

bsrong pa'i brgyud pa yang de dang 'dra'o/ ! /indra bhu dhi'i lam gyi brgyud pa ni/ dang po/ dpal ldan sde yi zhal snga nas/indra bhu dhi che ba/ /de bzhin du yang tshangs
pa'i zhabs/drang srong gzugs/ /bram ze mo rnal 'byor

ma/ ni rdo rje grub/ /de nas shrI badzra ba dhi rgyal/bar pa/ /de yi slob dpon de yi phyi ma utpal ma'i zhabsdang / /gos bral zhabs gcer bu/ dang de bzhin no/ /dpal ldan chung
ba/ dznyA na bo dhi rgyal/ /de bzhin shrI yo bo dhi dang / /slob dpon padma badzra dang / /Dombhi he ru ka'izhal snga de bzhin no/ /yan lag bar pa dpal ldan mo/ /bung
ba'i mkha' 'gro ma/ padma de bzhin no/ /dur khrod du na ki lar bzhugs/ /lha lcam legs smin de bzhin no/ /bdag kyang dang po grub pa yin/ /zhes pa ltar/ rdo rje 'chang /
dpal bde ba chen po/ indra bhu ti/ dpal tshangs pa'i zhabs/ bram ze mo/ grub pa'i rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhu dhi bar pa/ slob dpon u pa ma'i zhabs/ slob dpon gos bral zhabs/
rgyal po dznyA na bo dhi/ slob dpon padma badzra/ Dombhi he ru ka yan lag bar ma'i zhabs/ lha mo bung ba'i padma/ lcam legs smin/ rgyal po indra bhu dhi chung ba/ de'i
slob ma bram ze rin chen rdo rje/ de la kha che shes rab gsang bas gsan/ de la 'brog mi ste de man 'dra'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / indra bhu dhi che ba/ lcam
legs smin/ shes rab gsang ba/ 'brog mi man chad gong bzhin no/ /padma badzra'i lam gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bi la se badzra/grub thob chos 'chad kyi phyag rgya/
yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ indra bho dhi/ lcam legs smin/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ rje ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi man 'dra'o/ ! /Dombhi ba'i
lhan cig skyes grub kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro

ma/ Dombhi pa/ a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /lam skor brgyad kyi khrid yig
sa skya pa gong mas mdzad pa rnams dang / bsam mi khyab kyi rgya gzhung / rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i mchan bu sa bcad dang bcas pa/ mar me'i rtse mo'i rgya gzhung / lhan cig
skyes grub kyi rgya gzhung / bsam mi khyab kyi byin rlabs bya tshul 'khon dkon mchog rgyal pos mdzad pa/ de'i lo rgyus/ lam skor dgu'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bla ma rdo
rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa rnams thos so/ ! /sa skya pa'i yab chos 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud bshad kyi dus su bstan pa'i rgyun mi nyams pa'i phyir/ bla ma gong ma
rnams kyis sbyar nas mdzad pa'i rin chen bzhi'i sngags btu dang / zhal bzhi pa'i sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ go cha'i dpa' bo dang dpa' mo drug gi byin rlabs rnams rje bla ma

pa dpal/ sa bzang paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags

pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ chos rje dpal ldan rgyal po/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug zhe dgon pa chos rgyal mtshan/ sman gur ba rje
bsod nams sangs rgyas/ bhakShu paNDe pa/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ /yang na/ chos rje sa

pa'i gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas de dang 'brel ba'i gter chos kyi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ gu ru drag po'i lo rgyus/ gu ru drag
po'i thugs dam bskang pa'i cho ga drag po gsum dril gyi bka' gtad byed lugs/ gu ru drag po'i them byang / gu ru'i lo rgyus chen mo/ 1 phyi sgrub yon tan kun 'byung / 2
nang sgrub yid bzhin nor bu/ 3 gsang sgrub reg chog spu gri/ 4 yang gsang rkyang sgrub rtsa ba/ 5 tshe dpag med kyi sgos sgrub/ 6 'jam dpal sku'i sgos sgrub/ 7 rta mgrin
gsung gi sgos sgrub/ 8 phyag rdor thugs kyi sgos sgrub/ 9 mkha' 'gro sde lnga yon tan gyi sgos sgrub/ 10 'phrin las dbal gyi sgos sgrub/ 11 khyung gi sgos sgrub/ 12 sdig

pa'i sgos bsgrub/ 13 dpa' bo rigs bzhi'i sgos sgrub/ 14 brda rtags gsal ba'i lde mig 15 dbang chog nor bu'i phreng ba/ 16 las byang me lce'i phreng ba/ 17 zhi ba'i sbyin sreg
chen mo/ 18 rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg chen mo/ 19 dbang gi sbyin sreg chen mo/ 20 drag po'i sbyin sreg 21 me hom rab 'bar/ 22 chom rkun jag pa 'ching ba/ 23 rig ma 'gugs pa/
24 srid pa rigs rgyud spel ba/ 25 phan bya srung ba'i 'khor lo/ 26 rgyal bsran bsrung thabs/ 27 ma thub shi sa bstan pa/ 28 sde brgyad spyi'i bsrung ba/ 29 rbod stong
bzlog pa/ 30 dam sri rgyal bsran gsad pa/ 31 chung sri gso ba/ 32 mdze nad gso ba/ 33 chab gtor/ 34 byad gtong nad pa gso ba/ 35 drag po'i mtha' 'dul bya ba/ 36 chu 'khyags
ser ba bsrung ba/ 37 char 'bebs/ 38 zas nor bsgrub pa/ 39 dgra bo klu la gtad pa/ 40 ser 'bebs thog gi bsad pa/ 41 tshe sgrub sngags kyi kun 'gebs/ 42 dgra grogs mthun
pa'i las mtha'/43'di dpe ma rnyed nas lung ma thob/ zho chang bsrung thabs/ 44 bka' srung drag po gsum dril gyi gsol kha 45ste chos tshan zhe lnga pa 'di them rtsa ba'i
yi ge dang / them med kyi yig chung gi skor la/ tshe dpag med kyi yig chung nas/ zho chang srung thabs yig chung bar dang / bka' srung drag po gsum dril gyi srog gi spu gri'i
sgrub thabs rnams ni yig chung skor dang / yang yig skor la/ gu ru'i phyi sgrub kyi sgrub thabs/ yang yig

/ yar klung pa khu dbon/ pha chos rje brag thog pa bsod bzang / rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal man gong bzhin/ ! /man ngag gces bsdus nas phyung ba'i sgrub thabs/

dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tshab lung gi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ de man tshogs bdag
dang 'dra/ ! /ye shes kyi mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang rgyas bsdus gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi
mgon po/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub/ arYa de wa/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dus zhabs pa/ tsa mi sangs rgyas grags/ dpal chen sga lo/ bde gshegs phag mo grub pa/
'bri khung 'jig rten mgon po/ skyi shod pa bkra shis 'bum/ skyi shod grags pa seng ge slob dpon sangs rgyas gzhon nu/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu
blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta

grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ gnyan lo grags pa blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse
nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/
! /yang na lo chen ma Ni ka shrI/ sprul sku rnam rgyal/ mkhas btsun nam rtse/ bla ma paNDi ta man gong dang 'dra/ mgon po 'khor bcas kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge gtor chog
bskang gso/ mnga' gsol/ gtor ma la brten pa'i las tshogs/ bsrung bzlog gi yi ge rnams bla ma paNDi tas mdzad pa/ rkang pa brgyad pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa lo chen chos
skyong bzang pos bsgyur pa rnams thos so/ ! /chos skyong beg gdong lcam dral gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mahA de wa/ a tsarYa nyi 'od grags pa/

rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po/ bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu dpal/ mus sras pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ sgyi chu ba shes rab rin chen/ pha tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang

gtsang pa rin po che/ pha sangs rgyas bsgom pa/ zom rin po che/ khams pa lung pa/ sangs rgyas jo bo/ sangs rgyas ston pa/ sangs rgyas bsgom pa gsar ma/ rin po che bcu bzhi
pa/ rin po che tshes bcu pa/ spyan snga grags she ba/ lo pa tshul dar/ rin po che bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ rgyal sras ngag dbang chos grags/ rje kun dga' chos grags/

chos grags/ bla ma nam

mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha'i gdams pa dge ba'i
bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa rnams kyi thugs dam rje btsun sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang thob pa'i rim pa ni/ seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma/ sgrol ma myur zhing dpa' ba
la brten nas bgegs dang 'tshe ba zhi ba/ sgrol ma dkar mo la brten nas gdon bgegs zhi ba/ sgrol ma ser mo la brten nas tshe dang longs spyod 'phel ba/ sgrol ma gser mdog

pa'i dkyil chog gtsug

tor rnam rgyal/ nor rgyun ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sa skya pa'i bka' srung rnams la bstod pa/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga sa skya paNDi ta/ grub chen buddha shrI/ sa bzang
'phags pa rnams kyi rnam thar/ gsan yig chen mo/ lam 'bras chos 'byung brtsams 'phro/ bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ zhus lan gsang ba'i sa bcad/ dbang bzhi'i rtogs bskyed/
mngon rtogs tshul bzhi'i sdom tshig phyi nang gi bskyed rim dbang dang bcas pa'i sdom tshig nang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bir srung bar chad kun sel/ sku'i rnam 'gyur
drug gi zin bris/ bir srung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ de'i nyams len/ de dang lam 'bras mtshan mtshon sbyar ba/ bir srung gsar ma/ lus dkyil rtsod spong
che chung / rgyud gsum gnod 'joms rtsa 'grel/ zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi sa mtshams bshad pa/ kyai rdo rje'i rgyud kyi byung tshul dang bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar/

kyi sbyin

sreg gar gyi shan 'byed/ sangs rgyas kyi gar/ phyogs bzhi gtor ma'i gtang thabs/ chos skyong gi man ngag rnams kyi dkar chag mgon rkyang gi sgrub thabs rgyud 'grel las phyung
ba/ lha bdud kyi rjes gnang / gtor chog dgra las rnam rgyal/ gtor sgrub kyi man ngag thugs dam bskang pa'i cho ga kye rdor bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/ sambu Ti rdo rje
dbyings kyi sgrub thabs/ gtor chog mchod phreng / sbyin sreg bkra shis/ tshogs 'khor gsang ba kun rgyan dang tshogs 'khor kun bzang rnam rol/ bde mchog bla ma mchod chog
bde mchog gi pho brang gi rnam gzhag ril bu la brten nas mkha' spyod bsgrub pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs dang / bde mchog dkar po'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs cho ga
dang bcas pa/ rdo rje lha mo'i tshe sgrub/ la wa pa bcu gsum ma'i mngon rtogs kyi tho/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs kyi tho/ za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg
mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs/ gtso bo yab yum gyi sgrub thabs/ sngags phreng mchan ma/ dkyil chog mchod phreng / gsang 'dus mi bskyod
pa'i sgrub thabs/ shin tu rnal 'byor gyi khyad par/ gtor chog mchod phreng / rdo rje sems dpa'i mchod chog dkyil chog sbyin sreg rab gnas/ bkra shis/ rdo rje phreng ba'i
sa bzung gi cho ga dgra nag gi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i char 'bebs/ 'jigs byed kyi gtor chog 'jigs byed kyi rdzogs rim/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/ de'i dag pa/ sgrub
thabs kyi lung

sbyor/ dkyil chog spros med mdzes rgyan/ kun rig dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs/ gzhan phan mtha' yas rdul tshon kha skong / cha gsum gtor ma/ dkyil 'khor sgo sbrags
kyi bshad pa/ sbyong rgyud spyi rnam/ bya rgyud spyi rnam/ mi 'khrugs pa'i sgo nas gshin po rjes 'dzin/ 'od zer dri med kyi dkyil chog dri med lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang / 'od dpag med kyi tshe sgrub/ seng ge sgra/ sna tshogs yum/ rma bya chen mo/ so so 'brang ma/ 'byung po 'dul byed/ rta mgrin rnams
kyi sgrub thabs/ sman bla'i mchod chog sems bskyed rang gis blang ba'i cho ga gso sbyong rang gi blang ba'i cho ga mchod sbyin chen po'i zin bris/ gtor chen gyi lhan
thabs/ gser sku rdo rje 'chang bzhengs tshul/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i sngags la zhus dag mdzad pa/ rags sdom bcu'i 'bru 'grel/ bka' 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag bstan 'gyur gyi
dkar chag mdor bsdus shig rdo rje theg pa'i bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chag mtshan nyid bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chag rje btsun gong ma gsum gyi bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag rang gi grwa
pa spyi la gdams pa/ sa bzang pa bsod nams dpal/ lo tsA ba rdo rje dpal/ dge 'dun mgon/ a mo gha/ bla chen chos rin pa/ gling 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsam 'grub
rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon sa bzang / dbu ma pa shes rab rgya mtsho/ mdo stod pa dge bzang rnams kyi dris lan/ sde snod 'dzin pa ratna shrI la gdams pa/ gsang sngags

pa kun dga' gzhon nu la gdams pa/ bla ma sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gdams pa gnyis/ byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa shlau ka gcig rgya rong pa bkra shis
dpal la gdams pa/ sgrub pa po blo bzang la gdams pa gnyis/ nyag ro sangs grags la gdams pa/ paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen la springs pa/ bal yul ye rang gi paNDi ta shrI ma
no bo dhi yab sras la springs pa/ dpon po rgyal mtshan dpal yab yum sras bcas la gdams pa/ ya tshe rgyal po hasti rA dza yab yum sras bcas la gdams pa/ de'i slob dpon la
gdams pa shlau ka gcig a ya dbang phyug bkra shis la gdams pa/ dpon rgan thar pa ye shes la gdams pa/ slob dpon bzod chen la bstod pa/ phyi nang gi yas gtam/ theg pa chen
po'i smon lam/ gser 'od dam pa las btus pa'i smon lam/ der ma thus pa chos rje shar pa'i rnam thar/ mngon byang gi bshad pa/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i rnam bshad/ rnal 'byor
rgyud kyi spyi rnam rtsom 'phro/ kyai rdo rje'i mngon rtogs bsdus pa/ bka' shog thor bu ba kha yar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab
dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag
chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /yang na/ 'dren mchog dkon
mchog

'phel/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ dharmA swa
mi/ paNDe pa ku sa li/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /rong ston chen po shes bya kun rig gis mdzad pa'i chos tshan brgya dang bzhi bcu zhe
drug gi nang nas/ gnas brtan chen po nags kyi rin chen la bstod pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po la bstod pa/ bla ma bsod nams bzang po la bstod pa/ chos rje blo gros rgya
mtsho la bstod pa/ mus pa nam mkha'i rnal 'byor la bstod pa/ nyi ma dpal bzang po la bstod pa/ mkhan chen blo gros gsal ba la bstod pa/ bla ma dam pa gangs pa la bstod pa/
bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan la bstod pa/ mkhan po 'jam dbyangs kha che la bstod pa/ bla ma dam pa sman gong 'du ba la bstod pa/ dam pa ri khrod pa la bstod pa/ mkhas
pa dpal chen la bstod pa/ bla ma kun 'dus la bstod pa/ lo chen skyabs mchog la bstod pa/ grub thob chen po brgyad cu la bstod pa/ birWa pa la bstod pa/ mkhas pa chen
po shanti pa la bstod pa/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs la bstod pa/ rgyan drug mchog gnyis sa ka'i lha dang bcas pa la bstod pa rin chen spungs pa/ mkhas pa chen po
ka ma la shi la la bstod pa rgya mtsho'i rlabs phreng / rje btsun dam pa rgya gar la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char 'bebs/ grub chen la ba pa la bstod pa byin rlabs kun 'byung
/ dpal nA ro pa la bstod

pa yon tan sgrogs pa'i rnga sgra/ jo bo dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rgya mtsho rnam par rol pa'i bkod pa/ rab sding ma ba la bstod pa/ kha che paN
chen shAkya shrI la bstod pa rin po che'i phreng ba/ bla ma gser gling pa la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi gter mdzod/ paNDi ta dA na shI la la bstod pa mkhas pa dga' byed/ yang
'dzam gling rgyan drug gi bstod pa thar pa'i them skas/ theg pa chen po dbu ma'i bla ma brgyud rim sogs la bstod pa rin po che'i phreng mdzes/ brgyud pa'i bla ma bod du
byon pa rnams kyi bstod pa'i skor la/ lo tsA ba ka cog zhang gsum la bstod pa smra ba'i rgyan/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po la bstod pa rmad byung rgya mtsho'i bkod pa/
lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab la bstod pa mkhas pa dga' ba'i dbyangs/ jo bo rje'i dngos kyi slob ma khu rngog 'brom gsum la bstod pa dad pa'i snang ba rgyas byed/ jo bo'i brgyud
pa'i slob ma po to ba sogs la bstod pa dad pa'i 'od 'phro/ sa chen kun dga' snying po la bstod pa mun pa sel ba'i sgron me/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta la bstod pa mkhas
pa'i mgul rgyan/ jo bos sa skyar 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa bdun phrag lung bstan pa rnams la bstod pa rin chen phreng ba/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal la bstod pa rmad
du byung ba'i 'od phreng / bcom ldan rig ral la bstod pa smra ba'i rgyan/ rgyal sras thogs med pa la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi 'o rgyun/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan la
bstod pa rin po che'i me tog kun mkhyen dol po la bstod pa zab don rin chen phreng ba/ kun mkhyen bu ston la bstod pa rab tu snyan pa'i

gtam/ kun mkhyen shes rab bzang po la bstod pa ngo mtshar rab rgyas/ mkhas pa chen po gro lung pa dang cha gtsang dan gsum la bstod pa rnam rgyal padmo'i phreng ba/ 'gro mgon
phag mo grub pa la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char 'bebs/ thugs dam gyi lha tshogs kyi bstod pa'i skor la rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa spobs pa mi zad pa'i gter/
yum shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma la bstod pa yon tan rin po che'i gter mdzod/ dkon mchog gsum la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rgya mtsho rnam par rol pa'i sprin gyi bkod
pa/ thub pa'i bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char sprin rnam par g.yo ba/ 'phags pa byams pa la bstod pa mkhas pa dga' ba'i dbyangs/ sangs rgyas klu dbang la bstod pa rnam par
rgyal ba'i dbyangs/ phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas rab bdun la bstod pa chos kyi rnga sgra/ de bzhin gshegs pa
'chi med rnga sgra la bstod pa 'chi med mdzod/ thugs rje chen po kharsa pa Ni la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char sprin/ tshe dpag med grub pa'i rgyal mo la bstod pa 'chi med
rnga sgra/ mkha' 'gro ma rme brtsegs la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char 'bebs/ mkha' spyod dkar mo la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rnam rol dang / rin chen rgyan phreng gnyis/ mkha'
spyod dmar mo la bstod pa snyan pa'i sgra dbyangs/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro nai gu la bstod pa byin rlabs myur mgyogs/ rdo rje phag mo la bstod pa byin rlabs char rgyun/
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa la bstod pa byin rlabs rgya mtsho'i

gter/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor 'khor lo la 'khod pa'i khro bo bcu dang bcas pa la bstod pa rngam pa sgra sgrog gsang ba 'dus pa rigs bzhi'i lha mo rdo rje ma lnga la
bstod pa rin chen rgyan gyi phreng ba/ kyai rdo rje la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi char rgyun rnam par g.yo ba/ gshin rje gshed dmar la bstod pa rnam par rol pa'i sgra dbyangs/
rdo rje 'jigs byed la bstod pa 'jigs pa'i sgra sgrog 'khor lo bde mchog la bstod pa byin rlabs myur 'jug bde mchog gi 'khor bzhi'i lha tshogs la bstod pa bdud rtsi'i dga'
ston/ bde mchog gi snying po'i rnal 'byor ma bzhi'i bstod pa snying po'i mchog 'jam dbyangs smra seng la bstod pa shes rab kyi gter mdzod/ mi g.yo ba la bstod pa spobs
pa mi zad pa 'byung ba'i gter/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig la bstod pa ye shes kyi snang ba kun tu rgyas pa/ phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa la bstod pa 'chi med rnga sgra/ de
bzhin gshegs pa kun tu bzang po la bstod pa dga' ba'i me tog kun nas rgyas pa'i phreng ba/ byang sems sgrib pa rnam sel la bstod pa ye shes kyi snang ba kun tu dga' ba'i
dbyangs/ sgrol ma u gra ta ra la bstod pa spobs pa mi zad pa'i gter/ nye ba'i sras brgyad la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi chu char g.yo ba'i sprin/ nye ba'i sras mchog zung gcig
la bstod pa snyan pa'i sgra dbyangs/ bka' bsdu ba po dgra bcom sogs kyi bstod pa'i skor la dam pa'i chos bsdu ba po rnams la bstod pa phul du byung ba'i yon tan gyi bkod
pa/ gnas brtan bcu drug la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rnga sgra/ dgra bcom pa rnams la bstod

pa phul du byung ba'i rnga sgra/ phar phyin drug gi yon tan brjod pa tshogs gnyis la spro ba bskyed pa'i gtam/ bslab pa gsum gyi yon tan brjod pa thar pa'i sa 'dzin dag snang
rgyas pa 'od kyi phreng ba/ rmad du byung ba'i smon lam gyi gtam/ khrid chen dang / sde snod so so'i brgyud pa la bstod pa'i skor la/ nai gu chos drug gi brgyud pa rin
chen sna bdun la bstod pa ganggA'i chu rgyun/ nA ro chos drug gi bla ma brgyud pa la bstod pa byin rlabs gnad kyi zla zer/ zhi byed brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la bstod pa
rmad du byung ba'i phreng ba/ dam chos mngon pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i bstod pa blo gros kyi padmo rgyas par byed pa'i nyi ma/ gnas chen rnams kyi bstod pa'i skor la/ rgya
gar rdo rje gdan la bstod pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan brjod pa/ rgya gar gyi shrI na lendra la bstod pa snyan pa'i rnga sgra/ bya rgod phung po'i ri la bstod pa snyan
pa'i sgra dbyangs/ dga' ldan gyi lha gnas la bstod pa phul du byung ba'i rnga sgra/ rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga la bstod pa phul du byung ba'i sgra dbyangs/ ri bo gru 'dzin
la bstod pa byin rlabs kyi rnga sgra/ bka' srung rnams kyi bstod pa'i skor la/ gur gyi mgon po la bstod pa rngam pa sgra sgrog zhal bzhi pa la bstod pa rmad du byung
ba'i sgra sgrog a go ra la bstod pa byin rlabs char 'bebs/ phyag drug pa la bstod pa dngos grub gter mdzod/ dkar mo nyi zla la bstod pa mi 'jigs pa'i gter/ pu tra lcam sring
la bstod pa snyan pa'i rnga chen/ bdud rgyal thod phreng la bstod pa mthu stobs skyed byed/ phyag bzhi pa la bstod pa rnam par rgyal ba'i bstod

dbyangs/ bsgom rim gyi skor la/ sher phyin nyams su len pa'i man ngag lam lnga gsal sgron/ lam lnga'i khrid yig jo bo'i lugs ting nge 'dzin gyi gol sa'i mtha' dpyad pa'i gdams
ngag bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ blo sbyong spyi dpung don gyi man ngag sku gsung thugs mnyam par gzhag pa'i man ngag rin chen spungs pa dang / sku gsung thugs mnyam par gzhag
pa'i man ngag zab don rgya mtsho/ skyabs 'gro'i man ngag gnad kyi zla zer/ sher phyin stong nyid bzhi sbyor nyams su len pa'i man ngag bdud rtsi'i dga' ston/ dbus mtha'
rnam par 'byed pa'i bsgom rim snying po rab gsal/ mdo sde rgyan gyi bsgom rim legs bshad sgron me/ rgyud bla'i bsgom rim mi pham dgongs don/ rin chen phreng ba'i bsgom
rim rin chen sgron me/ rnal 'byor bzhi'i man ngag gnad kyi snying po/ phar phyin drug nyams su len tshul thar lam bde ba'i 'jug ngogs/ thugs rje chen po'i smar khrid padma
dkar po'i phreng ba/ dbu ma lta khrid zab don gnad kyi zla zer/ lta khrid kyi bsdus don dbu ma 'jug pa'i bsgom rim rin chen sgron me/ spyod 'jug bsgom rim rin chen rgyan
phreng / tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi bsgom rim phul du byung ba'i snying po dang / ngo mtshar snang ba gnyis rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rong ston chen po/ paN
chen rgya rdor ba/ stong chen shAkya'i mtshan can/ stong ra ba kun dga' legs grub/ lum pa ba rje kun dga' chos grags/ rdzong shar ba nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga chos kyi
spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'

bsod nams la'o/ /rong ston gyi rnam thar paN chen shAkya mchog ldan pas mdzad pa'i lung yang thos/ ! /chos kyi rje thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung 'bum gyi
lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po la bstod pa sgra rgyan me tog dkar po'i phreng ba/ yang de la bstod pa dngos grub kun 'byung / de
la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen la bstod pa dad pa'i pho nya/ de la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun
grub la bstod pa ngo mtshar me tog gi phreng ba/ dpal sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa dad pa'i snye ma/ de la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ rtsa ba'i
bla ma ngor mus sa gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa snying gi thig le/ yang de gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i gsal 'debs/

'jo/ phud mchod dgos 'dod kun 'byung / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sku'i rnam 'gyur drug la nang gi rnam dag dang mthun par bstod pa/ rdo rje 'chang la snyan ngag 'khor lo'i
sgo nas bstod pa bdud rtsi'i 'od can/ ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan la bstod pa byin rlabs myur 'jug rje lha mchog seng ge la bstod pa rin po che'i phreng ba/ mkhas
pa lha dbang blo gros la bstod pa rin

po che'i mgul rgyan/ dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs myur du 'jug pa'i pho nya/ de'i kha skong shlau
ka gcig lam zab brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong / 'khor lo bde mchog gi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa byin rlabs char 'bebs/ shin tu spros med kyi brgyud 'debs 'od gsal
snye ma/ tshe dpag med kyi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa/ mgon po'i chos skor gyi brgyud 'debs 'phrin las myur 'grub/ byams pa'i rnam thar bstod pa byams chos kyi
lam rim gyi sgo nas 'debs ba 'debs pa dang bcas mi pham dgongs rgyan/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa yon tan me tog gi phur ma/ dbyangs can ma la bstod pa don rgyan rnam
par bkod pa'i phreng ba/ sgrol ma dkar mo la bstod pa 'chi med rdo rje'i glu dbyangs/ gnyan sgrol dang 'byung 'dul la bstod pa shlau ka re re/ rang la bstod pa che chung
gsum/ dge sbyong gi chos bzhi bsgrub pa'i dam bca' smon lam du byas pa/ rang la bskul ba theg chen lam gyi gsal 'debs/ rang la gdams pa gces pa drug ldan/ sdom gsum 'gal
med du nyams su len tshul ston pa gdams pa sgo drug sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rab kyi kha rgyan/ hor gyi rgyal rabs 'phros cung zad dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i
rtsis nyung ngu rab gsal/ dus 'khor lugs kyi bstan rtsis mkhas pa'i kha rgyan/ 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba'i nyin byed/ sa lo tsA ba
chen po'i rnam thar 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi yon tan

rnam par bkod pa/ dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i yi ge thub bstan rgyas pa'i nyin byed/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len gsang ba'i nye lam tshar gsum khug pa/ gsung ngag
rin po che'i dmigs rim dang mthun pa'i gsol 'debs zab don snying po/ gsung ngag rin po che'i lam khyer gyi smon lam bdud rtsi'i snying po/ man ngag brda 'grel zab don
snang ba/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba'i gzhung shing la 'phros pa'i dri ba tshigs bcad ma/ tshul dang po gsum gyi don nyung ngu'i ngag gis ston pa tshul gsum gsal bar
byed pa'i rgyan/ mngon par rtogs pa'i don nyung ngu'i ngag gis ston pa ljon shing mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ mngon rtogs ljon shing gi gsal byed gong ma'i dgongs rgyan/
bdag med bstod pa'i bsdus don/ rdo rje'i tshigs rkang gi bsdus don tshang bde nyung gsal/ gsung ngag sngon 'gro'i nyams len snang gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ lam gyi
dngos gzhi'i khrid yig rgyud gsum mdzes rgyan/ dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed/ slob ma rjes gzung gi cho ga kyai rdo rje'i dbang bshad lung ngag gi gter mdzod/ kyai rdo
rje'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor lung dang man ngag gi snying po bsdus pa/ sa chog mdor bsdus dbang gi chu bo chen mo mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ rdul tshon chu bor spyan 'dren
pa'i cho ga sgrub thabs bsnyen sgrub yan lag bzhi ldan/ yan lag drug pa/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi ngag 'don/ lus dkyil mdzes rgyan/ sbyin sreg gi
cho ga lag len gsal ba'i me long / de la ltos

pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi tho yig bdag med ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig 'grel pa lugs kyi kyai rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil Dombhi mdzes rgyan/ padma lugs kyi kyai rdo rje'i sgrub
dkyil mtsho skyes mdzes rgyan/ nag po lugs kyi sku gsung thugs snying po kyai rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil nag po mdzes rgyan/ yi dam chos skyong gi gtor chog mdzes rgyan/
mgon po'i bsnyen pa byed tshul/ rdo rje gur gyi sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed rab gsal snang ba/ sambhu Ti rdo rje'i dbyings kyi sgrub dkyil kyi gsal byed nyung ngu rab gsal/
bde mchog lU nag gnyis kyi dkyil chog gi gsal byed khyad par bzhi ldan/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi rnal 'byor bcu gcig nyams su len tshul/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs
gtsug gi nor bu'i rgyan/ de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin chen sgron ma/ bde mchog dpa' bo drug dpa' mo drug gi sgrub thabs byin rlabs kyi cho ga dang bcas pa re re/ rdo

sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed 'chi med bdud rtsi'i snying po/ de'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga bklags pa don grub/ dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis/ 'jigs byed skyo lugs kyi khrid yig gsung
'gros ma/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi sgrub thabs bdud 'joms snang ba/ de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rab gnas snang ba/ de'i sgrub thabs dang gtor chog gi gsal byed bsnyen sgrub
rnam rol/ rwa lugs lha bcu gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig nyin

byed snang ba/ 'jigs byed kyi sbyin sreg las gshin bcu gsum ma'i gtor chog rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ kun rig gi dbang gi mtshams sbyor blo gsal kun dga'/ kun rig gi
sbyin sreg ro sreg tsha tsha'i rab gnas dang bcas pa/ bya spyod kyi thig tshon gyi byin rlabs/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil chog 'chi med grub pa'i lam bzang / mi 'khrugs
pa'i dkyil chog las sgrib rnam sbyong / de'i sbyin sreg bum gter gzhug tshul/ Dombhi he ru ka'i nyin bsrung mtshan bsrung gi byin rlabs kyi tho/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs/
de'i rjes gnang byed tshul/ de'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi yig rnying la mchan bu btab pa/ tshogs bdag gi sgrub thabs/ de'i
rjes gnang gi cho ga thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams su len tshul/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i tho yig mun sel sgron me/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal
gyi sgrub thabs stong mchod rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi sgrub thabs/ bum chog rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ tshe dpag med dkar po'i mngon

pa/ sgrol dkar gyi sgrub thabs de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga gnyan sgrol gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga 'byung 'dul gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga u
tsarYa'i sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga dzam

ser nag gi mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa re re/ mi g.yo pa dkar sngon gyi mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa re re/ so 'brang gi sgrub thabs 'chi
med rang gzungs zhes bya ba lus bsrung ba'i man ngag gi sgom bzlas/ ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i sgo nas 'chi med sgrub pa'i gdams ngag klu sgrub lugs kyi phyag bzhi
pa'i mngon rtogs/ phyag bzhi pa lha mang gi rjes gnang gi cho ga rnam sras kyi gtor chog de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi bslab bya/ yas gtam rin po
che'i phreng ba/ bsngo ba'i bstan bcos rin po che'i me tog mkhas pa blo gros bzang po/ bsam yas lha btsun pa/ kun mkhyen shes rab 'od zer/ zhu ston bkra shis rgya mtsho/
gnas 'ji chos rje/ bla ma byang chub rgyal mtshan/ bshes gnyen bkra shis dpal ldan/ bshes gnyen tshul khrims dpal bzang / chos rje legs blo ba/ rab 'byams pa 'od blo ba/
chos rje grags pa ba/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal/ wa skya chos rje/ chos rje bsam 'phel ba/ shi ri chos rje khu dbon gsum/ ri khrod pa sbyin pa 'od zer rnams la
bstod pa re re/ kun mkhyen shes rab 'od zer la phul ba me tog gi chun po/ lha btsun ma gur rgyal la phul ba chos gtam bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ mi dbang ngag dbang rnam rgyal
la phul ba gzugs kyi me long / de la phul ba'i zhu yig ma mo la spel ba/ sde pa rin chen dbang rgyal la phul ba/ dpal rnam pa lhun grub rtser phul ba gnyis/ shi ri chos
rje/ dpon btsun seng ge rgya

mtsho/ nang so dpal ldan don grub rnams la gdams pa re re/ 'dzam thang sku skye/ gnas 'ji chos rje/ bla ma byang chub rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bkra shis dpal ldan/ rab 'byams pa
shes rab bzang po grogs mched/ glo bo sde pa/ mi chen dpon rnams la phul ba'i zhu yig re re/ ru thog jo bo la phul ba gsum/ dpon chos mdzad la gdams pa/ mngon rtogs ljon
shing las 'phros pa'i dris lan nges don gsal ba/ gsang ba sgo 'byed las 'phros pas dris lan zab don snying po/ a ldong bla ma'i dris lan ngang pa'i pho nya/ gnas brtan
chos skyong dpal gyi dris lan/ kun gzhi'i skabs kyi dka' gnas gsal byed/ brgal lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi don bsdus don tshan brgyad pa/ brgal zhing brtags pa'i lan
mtha' bral bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho/ mdo khams su 'bul bskul gyi yi ge dkar chag gi yi ge ngo mtshar dpal gyi phreng ba/ rnga bo che la bsngags pa'i rab tu byed pa sogs tshigs
bcad thor bu kha yar rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan
snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o/ ! /chos kyi rje rgyal tshab dam pa dkon mchog dpal ldan gyi gsung
rab kyi lung thob pa la rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi rnam thar 'dod dgu'i dpal 'byung gi rnam bshad 'dod dgu'i chu gter blo gsal ngang pa'i bsti gnas/ rdo rje'i

tshigs rkang gi bsdus don tshang bde nyung gsal gyi gsal byed rin chen phreng ba/ tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa'i rgyan gyi go don nor bu'i phreng mdzes blo gsal mgul pa'i rgyan/
dpal kye rdo rje'i phyi bskyed pa'i rim pa'i sems 'dzin gyi sngon 'gro rnal 'byor bcu'i nyams len ku mu ta'i ze'u 'bru 'byed pa/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i bskyed rdzogs kyi
rnam bshad nges don zla ba'i 'od zer rgyas pa/ 'phags pa zhal bcu gcig pa'i snyung gnas kyi cho ga mun pa gsal byed/ dpal ldan lha mo re ma ti'i sgrub thabs gtor chog rjes
gnang dang bcas pa/ bkra shis kyi rgya mtsho spel ba'i phyir bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal tshab dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen kun dga'
bkra shis/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ des bdag sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams la'o// //'dir smras pa/ nanda adbhu ta sya gu Na ni dhi/
kun dga' rmad du byung ba'i yon tan gter/ /sarba pa ri siddha rthadharmA swa mi/ don kun yongs su grub pa chos kyi rje/ /yatpaM sa na yA da yu go da la dhe na/ gang khyod
rtag tu zhabs zung brtan pa yis/ /shAkya sya bhantu da ya shA sa nA ti/ shAkya'i bstan pa shin tu dar gyur cig /bka' gdams bstan pa'i rtsa lag khyed bsngags pas/ /jo bo
yab sras sku mched rnam gsum las/ /bstan 'dzin 'phel ltar bdag la'ang rigs brgyud dang / /chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i slob ma cher 'phel nas/ /kha ba ri yi 'dzin ma'i khyon
'di kun/ /yongs su khyab ste de dang lhan cig tu/ /'gro ba kun la bde skyid dpal 'bar te/ /rdzogs ldan bzhin du yun ring spyod gyur cig /chos kyi rje

dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thob pa'i tshul legs par bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba las/ zab rgyas chos kyi rgya mtsho
sprul pa'i sku spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub kyis rjes su bzung ba'i skabs te bcu gcig pa'o/ /yang smras pa/ buddha trai lokya nA thaM su ra na ra na
mi taM sa ra saM sA ra tI raM/'jig rten gsum gyi mgon po sangs rgyas lha dang mi yi btud pa 'khor ba yi ni pha rol brgal/ /dhi ri gAmbhirYa bantaM sa ka la gu Na ni dhaM
dharmA ra dzya bhi Shikti/brtan cing zab pa dang ldan mtha' dag yon tan gter gyur chos kyi rgyal srid du ni dbang thob pa/ /triShNa mo hanta kA laM ka li ka lu Sha ha raM
kA ma lo bhA de brdzadzi taM/sred dang rmongs pa mthar byed rtsod pa'i dus kyi dri ma 'phrog cing 'dod dang chags sogs spangs pa yi/ /bandaM shAkya siM haM pra Na ma ti
shrI rA sA sarba kA laM na mA mi/btsun pa shAkya seng ge de la spyi bos rab tu btud de dus rnams kun tu phyag bgyi'o/ /ya sya trI kA la dznyA dzi nA nu kampa/gang zhig
dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse rnams/ /kU Tai ka pu Nya dri sa masta ra siM/mtha' dag gcig spungs bsod nams phung po yis/ /pAkSha di bo dzaM ga ma pANDu bhu meHri bo dngos
su rgyu 'dra sa skya pa/ /pA dAbdza tasmai shi rA sA na mA mi/zhabs kyi chu skyes de la spyi bos 'dud/ /shrI shAkya singha sya su bhA Sha sartha/dpal ldan shAkya seng
ge'i legs bshad kun/ /dznyA no mahA bhu ti ba hu shu ta sya/mang thos mkhyen pa'i 'byor pa ches mnga' zhing / /adbhu ta a tstshinna karma wa ti/rmad byung rgyun mi 'chad
pa'i 'phrin las can/ /shrI wansanggu ru sya pA da sya sin ni dhi/dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i zhabs kyi drung / /bai ni ya sA ru sya ba ra swa hi naM/gdul bya mchog dman rang
gi blo 'tshams par/ /dharmA sya a mr-i to sA mi ta shakShya anta/chos kyi bdud rtsis nyer bskyangs

slob bu'i tha/ /shAkya u pA sa ka nanda pu Na ma ma/shAkya'i dge bsnyen kun dga' bsod nams bdag /pra sA da sma re na tsAkSha ba anydza mA ta/bka' drin dran pas mig zum thal
sbyar nas/ /shI ghra shI ghraM sa dAntA shtsa/myur ba myur bar dul ba dang bcas te/ /mu hurmu hurmu mA mi tsa/yang dang yang du phyag ni 'tshal bar bgyi/ /dzanma dzanma
dA yA gr-ihNa/skye ba skye bar brtse bas rjes 'dzin mdzod/ /artha artha ma bharatra tra taM/don de don du gnyer bya'i gtso bo lags/ /sangs rgyas kun las rgyu mtshan du ma
yis/ /bka' drin ches lhag yongs 'dzin mchog rnams las/ /zab dang rgya che'i chos tshul mnos pa rnams/ /snying por dril nas nyams su bla ba'i tshul/ /mdo rgyud lam gyi rim
pa dang mthun par/ /rang dang rang gi rjes 'jug slob tshogs dang / /skal mnyam 'gro ba gzhan la'ang phan pa'i phyir/ /nyung ngus ngag gis brjod la bdag yid spro/ /gang
du gnas na chos brgyad rnam rtog dang / /phyogs rig chags sdang ngang gis 'phel ba'i gzhi/ /grong khyer tshong 'dus pha yul la sogs pa/ /spangs te dgon gnas ri khrod dben
pa bsten/ /der yang chos mthun 'tsho bas chog shes kyis/ /tshe 'di'i phun tshogs bsgrub pa'i blo dor nas/ /blo phugs bla ma dkon mchog la gtad de/ /rang gi sgo gsum bag
yod spyod pa'i gnas/ /mi lus thob cing sangs rgyas bstan dang mjal/ /sgo gsum bkol btub rang dbang yod pa yi/ /'di 'dra'i dus su dam chos mi bsgrub na/ /chos byed dus shig
nam yang rnyed mi 'gyur/ /dang po mngal du zhugs pa nas brtsams te/ /lo zla zhag dang za mas 'chi bar nye/ /de la bros kyang thar pa'i skabs med na/ /chos med shi na

ji 'drar 'gyur snyam bsam/ /tshe 'dir rang gis dge sdig gang bsags pa/ /las de'i dbang gis phyi ma rigs drug lus/ /dbang med blangs nas bde sdug myong 'gyur bas/ /sdig la 'dzems
shing dge la 'bad par rigs/ /skye dang rga dang na dang 'chi ba yi/ /chu chen bzhi 'bab las nyon chu srin brgyas/ /gzir ba'i brgal dka' 'khor ba'i mtsho chen las/ /thar
thabs chos las med pas de la 'bad/ /bde ba'i skabs bral srid pa'i btson ra 'dir/ /bzod med sdug bsngal gyis gzir sems can rnams/ /tshe sngon phan btags pha mar shes
byas nas/ /rgyun chad med par byams dang snying rje bsgom/ /dmigs med snying rje'i dbang gis 'gro ba kun/ /srid dang zhi ba'i 'jigs las bskyab pa'i phyir/ /myur du sangs
rgyas thob 'dod smon pa'i sems/ /kha tsam min pa snying nas yang yang bskyed/ /rgyun chad med par 'khor bar 'khyams pa'i rgyud/ /rang nyid gces 'dzin 'gong po 'di kho na/
/ma gtogs sdug bsngal lan rtsa gzhan med pas/ /bdag 'dzin dgra bo 'dul la 'bad par gces/ /bcos min snying rje chen pos mtshams sbyar nas/ /mkha' khyab 'gro rnams bdag gi
mdun dmigs te/ /de dag sdig sdug bdag la len pa dang / /rang gi bde dge 'gro la gtang bar bya/ /de ltar sangs rgyas bstan pa'i snying po yi/ /nyams len rgyun de rtag tu
dran bya zhing / /rang don g.yo sgyu spangs pa'i bsam sbyor gyis/ /dngos brgyud sgo nas gzhan don ci nus bsgrub/ /kun rdzob byang sems nyams len de lta

bus/ /bdag tu 'dzin pa'i dgra bo'i mgo mnan nas/ /de nyid drungs nas 'byin phyir don dam gyi/ /byang sems zab mo'i nyams len 'di ltar bya/ /nga 'o snyam pa'i 'dzin stangs de'i
gzung byar/ /gyur pa'i bdag de ming lus sems gsum po/ /gang yin ming ni sngon nas med pas na/ /phyis nas btags pa tsam yin lus 'di ni/ /pha ma'i khu khrag las skyes glo
bur ba/ /sems ni skye 'gag med pa nam mkha' dang / /rnam dbyer med pas btsal kyang rnyed mi 'gyur/ /des na ming lus sems gsum bdag min yang / /'khrul pas grib ma 'dre
ru bzung ba ltar/ /rang gi nyer len phung po la dmigs nas/ /nga med nga dang bdag med bdag bzung ba/ /kho nar shes nas gang zag bdag 'dzin spangs/ /de bzhin 'khor 'das chos
kun rmi lam bzhin/ /sems nyid 'khrul snang tsam yin don la med/ /rmi lam 'khrul pa'i phyir na rmi lam nyid/ /rmi ba po yi sems kyang 'khrul snang ste/ /des na gzung 'dzin
so sor ma grub pas/ /gnyis stong sems de'ang gzhi rtsa bral bas na/ /gnyis 'dzin gnyis min la sogs mu bzhi yis/ /stong par shes pas chos kyi bdag 'dzin spangs/ /dgag
bya mtha' bzhi ma grub de yi phyir/ /de bzhi bkag pa'i dbus kyang mi rnyed pas/ /myong yang brjod mi shes pa'i blo 'das kyi/ /gnas lugs dbyings la gsal bzhag med par bzhag
/sems med sems kyis sems la blta shes na/ /mthong med mthong bas sems kyi don mthong 'gyur/ /sgom med bsgom pa'i tshul du bsgom bskyangs pas/ /grol med grol bas sems

nyid grol zhes gsungs/ /de ltar thun mong theg pa'i nyams len rnams/ /shes shing sgom pa'i dpyod ldan skyes bu des/ /dbang gis smin nas dam tshig gzhir bzung ste/ /rdo rje
theg pa'i lta sgom spyod la bslab/ /tshul der rgya cher bsgrub tshul mtha' yas kyang / /snying po'i nyams len bya tshul 'di lta ste/ /dben zhing nyams dga'i bsam gtan spyil
bu ru/ /chos mthun stan la sgo gsum cha mnyam ste/ /nam yang bslu med dkon mchog rnam bzhi la/ /dad shugs drag pos snying nas skyabs 'gro zhing / /mkha' khyab 'gro la
dmigs pa'i snying rje yis/ /bla med byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed bya/ /drin can bla ma spyi bor rtag bsgom la/ /khyed shes khyed mkhyen tshul gyi gsol ba btab/ /mnyam
rjes kun tu snang grags rig gsum 'di/ /lha sngags ye shes rol par dran byas la/ /bdag med gnyis kyis stong pa'i rang gi sems/ /rang rig rang gsal gnyug ma'i rang zhal blta/
/bltas pas ma mthong gsal stong 'gag med dang / /rtog med mkha' khyab mkha' yi rdo rjer bzhag /yid la byar med sgom gyi mchog yin par/ /gsungs pas gzung bya dang ni 'dzin
byed dang / /bsgom bya sgom byed yod med yin min sogs/ /'phro 'du kun spangs mnyam nyid chen por bzhag /shes pa bying na skyabs 'gro gsol gdab 'bad/ /rgod na thar med
'khor ba'i nyes dmigs bsam/ /yang na rnam rtog thol skyes rbad bcad de/ /bying rgod med par dbyings rig bsres la bzhag /phyogs ris med pa'i rang sems gsal stong gi /

chos sku rang la yod kyang ma shes pas/ /thag khra sbrul du 'khrul ltar bdag 'dzin gyis/ /bcings pa'i 'gro la bzod med snying rje bsgom/ /de ltar rang gi dge ba ci bsags pa/
/sems can don du byang chub sar bsngos la/ /spyod lam thams cad sgyu ma rmi lam ltar/ /dran pas bstan 'gro'i don mang ci nus bsgrub/ /mdor na dus rnams kun tu ma brtags
pa'i/ /spyod pa spangs nas brtson ldan dran shes dang / /bag yod blo yis thabs shes zung 'brel gyi/ /lam 'di bsgrubs na byang chub myur thob 'gyur/ /da dung gces pa'i gdams
ngag cung zad bshad/ /chags pa skye ba'i yul la zhen pa spangs/ /zhe sdang skye ba'i yul la byams pa sgoms/ /gti mug skye ba'i yul la rtog dpyod thongs/ /nad dang sdug
bsngal gang byung lam du khyer/ /gdon bgegs lhar sgoms de la dngos grub longs/ /de tsam ma nus phan sems snying rje skyed/ /mi rtag dran pas yang yang lcag gis skul/ /phyi
rol snang ba'i yul la zhen pa thongs/ /nang du rang sems 'dzin pa'i rtsa ba chod/ /bar du rnam smin lus kyi gces 'dzin bshig /srid pa hrul por gtong ba'i thabs mchog
lags/ /skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi bka' drin las/ /zab rgyas chos tshul mnos pa'i snying po'i don/ /nyams su len tshul mdo rgyud dgongs pa bzhin/ /bshad pa 'di la dpyod ldan
kun dges mdzod/ /khungs dang 'brel ba'i zab chos mtha' yas pa/ /thos tshul bstan bcos rta ljang 'di shar bas/ /dam chos rin chen gter mang gsal mthong phyir/ /zab rgyas
chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed

yin/ /'di sbyar dge bas rtsa brgyud bla ma rnams/ /dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su rab rdzogs nas/ /legs byas 'dis mtshon dus gsum dge ba'i mthus/ /bdag gzhan 'gro ba'i sgrib
kun byang gyur cig /de la brten nas bdag cag dpon slob rnams/ /tshe mthar phyin cing lus brtas dbang po gsal/ /bstan pa'i bya ba ma lus mthar phyin te/ /sa skya'i chos srid
dpal 'byor rgyas byed shog /deng sang dus kyi skal bzang las 'phro can/ /dad brtson shes rab snying rje ldan pa yis/ /bstan pa 'dzin nus gang zag thams cad kyang / /zab
rgyas chos kyi 'khor du 'du bar shog /dad pa dman zhing dge ba'i blo gros dman/ /chos la 'jug pa'i skal ba dman rnams kyang / /bdag gi thabs mkhas 'phrin las sna tshogs
kyis/ /kun kyang dbang 'dus dge la sbyor bar shog /ma dad mi bsrun bstan dang 'gro la gnod/ /zhi bas mi thul rnams kyang bdag cag gis/ /ma bcol na yang bka' srung dam can
gyis/ /tshar bcad rnam shes chos dbyings sgrol bar shog /mdor na bdag dang bdag gi slob bu'i tshogs/ /kun gyi sgo gsum bya ba spyod lam rnams/ /bstan dang 'gro la phan
bde'i rgyur gyur nas/ /kun kyang bde skyid dpal la spyod par shog /phyi ma dpon slob lhan cig dag pa'i zhing / /bde ba can du skyes nas rang don rnams/ /mthar phyin gang
'dul sprul pas srid mtha'i bar/ /spyi dang bye brag bstan pa rgyas byed shog /ces chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul legs
par

bshad pa zab rgyas chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di ni/ srid gsum 'gro ba'i bla ma 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo padma'i rnam 'phrul bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga
nas dang / byang chub sems dpa' zhi ba 'tsho'i rnam par sprul pa yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ rigs thams cad dang dkyil 'khor thams cad
kyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje sems dpa' dang dbyer ma mchis pa rgyal ba mus pa chen po rje btsun rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ zab yangs chos kyi spyan ldan
sprul pa'i sku rgyal ba'i sras po spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa'i gter chen nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun bla ma dbang
phyug rab brtan/ chos rje sa paN gyi sdom rgyun 'dzin pa sha chang zhal la mi reg pa sogs sku btsun pa'i mthar thug pas gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po rim gnyis kyi
ting nge 'dzin la thugs brtan pa chos kyi rje nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa/ mdo sngags rig gnas kyis bsdus pa'i shes bya'i gnas thams cad la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes
shing / nang du yang dag pa'i zab bzhes kyi ting nge 'dzin la dbang 'byor bas snyigs dus kyi yongs 'dzin kun gyi gtsug rgyan gcig pu thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen
mkhan chen ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa la sogs te yongs 'dzin 'brel tshad don ldan gyi dam pa mang po'i bka' drin gyis nye bar bskyangs shing thugs brtse ba chen pos rjes
su bzung ba'i skal ba bzang po can/ dpal sa skya pa shAkya'i dge bsnyen paNDi ta mkhas pa sngags 'chang ngag

dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ rigs kyi bu ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug la sogs te rang dang skal ba mnyam pa'i slob ma'i tshogs rnams la
phan par bsams nas/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsan yig so so la gzhi byas/ cung zad mi mthun pa dang the tshom gyi gzhir gyur pa rnams bla ma so so'i rnam thar dang / chos
'byung lo rgyus la sogs pa shes byed kyi khungs rnam par dag pa la gtugs te/ rang gi bgrang gzhi bcu phrag bzhi dang nyag ma brgyad du slebs pa/ 'phags pa'i yul na tA
ra NaHzhes pa sgrol byed ces grags shing / rgya nag lugs la shing pho spre'u'i lo chu stod zla ba'i dkar po'i phyogs kyi tshes bcu bzhi sngon gyi skyes chen 'khon dkon mchog
rgyal po dang / dpal brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po yab sras sogs dang / phyi rabs bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po la sogs te/ sprul
pa'i sku du ma zab mo chos dbyings su mnyam par bzhag pa'i tshul bstan pa'i zla dus kyi dus bzang khyad par can gyi nyin gong ma 'brel tshad don ldan de dag gi dus dran gyi
mchod pa 'bul ba'i tshe/ chos grwa chen po dpal ldan sa skya'i bzhi thog bla brang gi tshoms dmar du/ sa gsum gyi bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i bzhugs
khri padma can gyi drung ga la ba der legs par sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni skyes sbyangs kyi blo gros rab tu gsal bas/ spyir gsung rab mang po la rnam dpyod kyi snang ba ches
cher rgyas shing / khyad par gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs dang / yi ge'i

'du byed la mkhas pa'i phul du phyin pa gdong dga' ba bsam pa don chen gyis gus spro'i sgo nas brtson 'grus chen pos bgyis pa re zhig rdzogs so/ /karma bistar bha wa tu/'phrin
las rgyas par gyur cig swAsti dza yantu/dge legs rgyas par gyur cig oM swAsti shrI dza yantu/dpal bkra shis dge legs rgyas par gyur cig /shu bha mastu sarba dza ga tAM/dge
bar gyur cig 'gro ba thams cad rnams/ /swAsti pra dza bhyaHdge bar gyur cig skye dgu rnams la'o// mangga laM//bkra shis/ //gcig zhus// // ! mkhan chen a pad rin po
che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o//
